tathA avidyAviShayashca pAN^ktaM karma tatphalaM cAnnatrayaM nAmarUpakarmAtmakamiti /
tatrAvidyAviShaye vaktavyaM sarvamuktam /

vidyAviShayastvAtmA kevala upanyasto na nirNItaH /
tannirNayAya ca 'brahma te bravANi'iti prakrAntaM 'j~napayiShyAmi'iti ca /
atastadbrahma vidyAviShayabhUtaM j~nApayitavyaM yAthAtmyataH /
tasya ca yAthAtmyaM kriyAkArakaphalabhedashUnyamatyantavishuddhamadvaitamityetadvivakShitam /
atastadanurUpau prashnAvutthApyete shrutyA 'kvaiSha tadAbhUt' 'kuta etadAgAt'iti /

tatra yatra bhavati tadadhikaraNaM yadbhavati tadadhikartavyam, yatoshcAdhikaraNAdhikartavyayorbhedo dR^iShTo loke /
tathA yata Agacchati tadapAdAnaM ya Agacchati sa kartA tasmAdanyo dR^iShTaH /
tathA AtmA kvApyabhUdanyasminnanyaH kutashcidAgAdanyasmAdanyaH kenacidbhinnena sAdhanAntareNetyevaM lokavatprAptA buddhiH /
sA prativacanena nivartayitavyeti /
nAyamAtmA anyo 'nyatrAbhUdanyo vA

anyasmAdAgataH sAdhanAntaraM vA Atmanyasti /
kiM tarhi? svAtmanyevAbhUt 'svam (AtmAnam) apIto bhavati' 'satA somya tadA sampanno bhavati' 'prAj~nenAtmanA sampariShvaktaH' /
'para Atmani sampratiShThate'ityAdishrutibhyaH /
ata eva nAnyo 'nyasmAdAgacchati /
tacchrutyaiva pradarshyate 'asmAdAtmanaH'iti /
AtmavyatirekeNa vastvantarAbhAvAt /

nanvasti prANAdyAtmavyatiriktaM vastvantaram /
na, prANAdestata eva niShpatteH /
tatkatham? ityucyate, tatra dR^iShTAntaH-


#<sa yathorNavAbhis tantunoccared yathA agneH kShudrA viShphuliN^gA vyuccaranty evam evAsmAd AtmanaH sarve prANAH sarve lokAH sarve devAH sarvANi bhUtAni vyuccaranti |
tasyopaniShat satyasya satyam iti |
prANA vai satyaM teShAm eSha satyam || BrhUp_2,1.20 ||>#

BrhUpBh_2,1.20

sa yathA loka UrNanAbhiH /
UrNanAbhirlUtAkITa eka eva prasiddhaH sansvAtmApravibhaktena tantunoccaredudgacchet /
na cAsti tasyodgamane svato 'tiriktaM kArakAntaram /
yathA caikarUpAdekasmAdagneH shrudrA alpA visphuliN^gAsruTayo 'gnyavayavA vyuccaranti vividhaM nAnA voccaranti /
yathemau dR^iShTAntau kArakabhedAbhAve 'pi pravR^ittiM darshayataH, prAkpravR^itteshca svabhAvata ekatvam, evamevAsmAdAtmano vij~nAnamayasya prAkpratibodhAdyatsvarUpaM tasmAdityarthaH /
sarve prANA vAgAdayaH, sarve lokA bhUrAdayaH, sarvANi karmaphalAni, sarve devAH prANalokAdhiShThAtAro 'gnyAdayaH, sarvANi bhUtAni brahmAdistambaparyantAni prANijAtAni, sarva eta AtmAna ityasminpATha upAdhisamparkajanitaprabudhyamAnavisheShAtmAna ityarthaH, vyuccaranti /

yasmAdAtmanaH sthAvarajabhgamaM jagadidamagnivisphuliN^gavad vyuccaratyanisham, yasminneva ca pralIyate jalabudbudavat, yadAtmakaM ca vartate sthitikAle, tasyAsyAtmano brahmaNaH, upaniShad;upa samIpaM nigamayatItyabhidhAyakaH shabda upaniShadityucatyate, shAsraprAmANyAdetacchabdagato visheSho 'vasIyata upanigamayitR^itvaM nAma /

kAsAvupaniShadityAha-satyasya satyamiti /
sA hi sarvatra copaniShadalaukikArthatvAd durvij~neyArthA, iti tadarthamAcaShTe-prANA vai satyaM teShAmeSha satyamiti /
etasyaiva vAkyasya vyAkhyAnAyottaraM brAhmaNadvayaM bhaviShyati /

bhavatu tAvadupaniShadvyAkhyAnAyottaraM brAhmaNadvayam, tasyopaniShadityuktam, tatra na jAnImaH kiM prakR^itasyAtmano vij~nAnamayasya pANipeShaNotthitasya saMsAriNaH shabdAdibhuja iyamupaniShadAhosvidasaMsAriNaH kasyacit? kiJNcAtaH? yadi saMsAriNastadA saMsAryeva vij~neyaH, tadvij~nAnAdeva sarvaprAptiH /
sa eva brahmashabdavAcyastadvidyaiva brahmavidyeti /
atha asaMsAriNaH, tadA tadviShayA vidyA brahmavidyA /
tasmAcca brahmavij~nAnAtsarvabhAvApattiH /

sarvametacchAsraprAmANyAdbhaviShyati /
kintvasminpakShe"AtmetyevopAsIta" "AtmAnamevAvedahaM brahmAsmi"iti parabrahmaikatvapratipAdikAH shrutayaH kupyeran, saMsAriNashcAnyasyAbhAve upadeshAnarthakyAt /
yata evaM paNDitAnAmapyetanmahAmohasthAnam anuktaprativacanaprashnaviShayam; ato yathAshakti brahmavidyApratipAdakavAkyeShu brahma vijij~nAsUnAM buddhivyutpAdanAya vicArayiShyAmaH /

na tAvadasaMsArI paraH, pANipeShaNapratibodhitAcchabdAdibhujo 'vasthAntaravishiShTAdutpattishruteH /
na prashAsitAshanAyAdivarjitaH paro vidyate, kasmAt? yasmAt 'brahma j~napayiShyAmi' iti pratij~nAya suptaM puruShaM pANipeShaM bodhayitvA tasyaiva svapnadvAreNa suShuptyAkhyamavasthAntaramunnIya tasmAdevAtmanaH suShuptyavasthAvishiShTAd agnivisphuliN^gorNanAbhidR^iShTAntAbhyAmutpattiM darshayati shrutiH"evamevAsmAt"ityAdinA /
na cAnyo jagadutpattikAraNamantarAle shruto 'sti, vij~nAnamayasyaiva hi prakaraNam /
samAnaprakaraNe ca shrutyantare kauShItakinAmAdityAdipuruShAnprastutya"sa hovAca yo vai bAlAka eteShAM puruShANAM kartA yasya vaitatkarma sa vai veditavyaH"iti prabuddhasyaiva vij~nAnamayasya veditavyatAM darshayati, nArthAntarasya /

tathA ca"Atmanastu kAmAya sarvaM priyaM bhavati"ityuktvA, ya evAtmA priyaH prasiddhastasyaiva draShTavyashrotavyamantavyanididhyAsitavyatAM darshayati /
tathA ca vidyopanyAsakAle"AtmetyevopAsIta" "tadetatpreyaH putrAtpreyo vittAt" "tadAtmAnamevAvedahaM brahmAsmi"ityevamAdivAkyAnAmAnulomyaM syAtparAbhAve /
vakShyati ca -"AtmAnaM cedvijAnIyAdayamasmIti pUruShaH"iti /

sarvavedAnteShu ca pratyagAtmavedyataiva pradarshyate 'hamiti, na bahirvedyatA shabdAdivatpradarshyate 'sau brahmeti /
tathA kauShItakinAmeva"na vAcaM vijij~nAsIta vaktAraM vidyAt"ityAdinA vAgAdikaraNairvyAvR^ittasya kartureva veditavyatAM darshayati /

avasthAntaravishiShTo 'saMsArIti cet-athApi syAdyo jAgarite shabdAdibhugvij~nAnamayaH, sa eva suShuptAkhyamavasthAntaraM gato 'saMsArI paraH prashAsitA anyaH syAditi cenna, adR^iShTatvAt /
na hyevandharmakaH padArtho dR^iShTo 'nyatra vainAshikasiddhAntAt /
na hi loke gaustiShThan gacchanvA gaurbhavati, shayAnastvashvAdijAtyantaramiti /
nyAyAcca-yaddharmako yaH padArdhaH pramANenAvagato bhavati, sa deshakAlAvasthAntareShvapi taddharmaka eva bhavati /
sa cettaddharmakatvaM vyabhicarati, sarvaH pramANavyavahAro lupyeta /
tathA ca nyAyavidaH sAN^khyamImAMsakAdayo 'saMsAriNo 'bhAvaM yuktishataiH pratipAdayanti /

saMsAriNo 'pi jagadutpattisthitilayakriyAkartR^itvavij~nAnasyAbhAvAd ayuktamiti cet-yanmahatA prapaJNcena sthApitaM bhavatA, shabdAdibhuksaMsAryevAvasthAntaravishiShTo jagata iha karteti-tadasat; yato jagadutpattisthitilayakriyAkartR^itvavij~nAnashaktisAdhanAbhAvaH sarvalokapratyakShaH saMsAriNaH /
sa kathamasmadAdiH saMsArI manasApi cintayitumashakyaM pR^ithivyAdivinyAsavishiShTaM jagannirminuyAt? ato 'yuktamiti cenna, shAsrAt; shAsraM saMsAriNaH"evamevAsmAdAtmanaH"iti jagadutpattyAdi darshayati /
tasmAtsarvaM shraddheyamiti syAdayamekaH pakShaH /

"yaH sarvaj~naH sarvavit" "yo 'shanAyApipAse atyeti" "asaN^go na hi sajjate" "etasya vA akSharasya prashAsane" "yaH sarveShu bhUteShu tiShThannantaryAmyamR^itaH" "sa yastAnpuruShAnniruhyAtyakrAmat" "sa vA eSha mahAnaja AtmA"

"eSha seturvidharaNaH" "sarvasya vashI sarvasyeshAnaH" "ya AtmApahatapApmA vijaro vimR^ityuH" "tattejo 'sR^ijata" "AtmA vA idameka evAgra AsIt" "na lipyate lokaduHkhena bAhyaH"ityAdishrutishatebhyaH /
smR^iteshca"ahaM sarvasya prabhavo mattaH sarvaM pravartate"iti paro 'styasaMsArI /
shrutismR^itinyAyebhyashca /
sa ca kAraNaM jagataH /
nan"vevamevAsmAdAtmana"iti

saMsAriNa evotpattiM /
darshayatItyuktam /
na /
"ya eSho 'ntarhR^idaya AkAsha"iti parasya prakR^itatvAdasmAdAtmana iti yuktaH parasyaiva parAmarshaH /
"kvaiSha tadAbhUdi"tyasya prashnasya prativacanatvenA'kAshashabdavAcyaH para Atmokto"ya eSho 'ntarhR^idaya AkAshastasmiJNcheta"iti /
"satA somya tadA sampanno bhavatya" "harahargacchantya etaM brahmalokaM na vidanti" "prAj~nenA'tmanA sampariShvaktaH" "para Atmani saMpratiShThate"ityAdishrutibhya AkAshashabdaH para Atmeti nishcIyate /
"daharo 'sminnantarAkAsha"iti prastutya tasminnevA'tmashabdaprayogAcca /
prakuta eva para AtmA /
tasmAdyuktameva asmAdAtmana iti paramAtmana eva sR^iShTiriti /
saMsAriNaH sR^iShTisthitisaMhAraj~nAnasAmarthyAbhAvaM cAvotAma /

atra ca"AtmetyevopAsIta" "AtmAnamevAvedahaM brahmAsmI"ti brahmavidyA prastutA /
brahmaviShayaJNca brahmavij~nAnamiti /
"brahma te bravANI"ti"brahma j~napayiShyAmI"ti prArabdham /
tatredAnImasaMsAri brahma jagataH kAraNamashanAyAdyatItaM nityashuddhabuddhamuktasvabhAvaM tadviparItashca saMsArI tasmAdahaM brahmAsmIti na gR^ihNIyAt /
paraM hi devamIshAnaM nikR^iShTaH saMsAryAtmatvena smarankathaM na doShabhAksyAt /
tasmAnnAhaM brahmAsmIti yuktam /

tasmAtpuShpodakAJNjalistutinamaskArabalyupahArasvAdhyAyadhyAnayogAdibhirAr irAdhayiSheta /
ArAdhanena viditvA sarveshitR^i brahma bhavati /
na punarasaMsAri brahma saMsAryAtmatvena cintayedagnimiva shItatvenA'kAshamiva mUrtimatvena /
brahmAtmatvapratipAdakamapi shAsramarthavAdo bhaviShyati /
sarvatarkashAsralokanyAyaishcaivamavirodhaH syAt /
na, mantrabrAhmaNavAdebhyastasyaiva pravesha shravaNAt /

sharIrendriyamana Atmasu ca pratyekamanumAnakaushalapratyAkhyAne, sharIrendriyamanaHsAdhanA AtmAno vayamanumAnakushalAH, anekakArakasAdhyatvAtkriyANAmiti cet? evaM tarhyanumAnakaushalebhavatAmanekatvaprasaN^gaH; anekakArakasAdhyA hi kriyeti bhavadbhirevAbhyupagatam /

tatra vayamanumAnakushalA ityevaM vadadbhiH-sharIrendriyamanaHsAdhanA AtmAnaH pratyekaM vayamaneka ityabhyupagataM syAt /
aho anumAnakaushalaM darshitamapucchashR^iN^gaistArkikabalIvardaiH /
yo hyAtmAnameva na jAnAti sa kathaM mUDhastadgataM vA jAnIyAt? tatra kimanuminoti? kena vA liN^gena? na hyAtmanaH svato bhedapratipAdakaM kiJNcilliN^gamasti, yena liN^genAtmabhedaM sAdhayet; yAni liN^gAnyAtmabhedasAdhanAya nAmarUpavantyupanyasyanti, tAni nAmarUpagatAnyupAdhaya evAtmano ghaTakarakApavarakabhUcchidrANIvAkAshasya /

yadyatpara AtmadharmatvenAbhyupagacchati, tasya tasya nAmarUpAbhyAM cAtmano 'nyatvAbhyupagamAt,"AkAsho vai nAma nAmarUpayornirvahitA te yadantarA tadbrahma"iti shruteH"nAmarUpe vyAkaravANi"iti ca /
utpattipralayAtmake hi nAmarUpe, tadvilakShaNaM ca brahma-ato 'numAnasyaivAviShayatvAtkuto 'numAnavirodhaH? etenAgamavirodhaH pratyuktaH /

yaduktaM brahmaikatve yasmA upadeshaH, yasya copadeshagrahaNaphalam, tadabhAvAdekatvopadeshAnarthakyamiti, tadapi na, anekakArakasAdhyatvAtkriyANAM kashcodyo bhavati /
ekasminbrahmaNi nirupAdhike nopadeshaH, nopadeShTA, na copadeshagrahaNaphalam; tasmAdupaniShadAM cAnarthakyamityetadabhyupagatameva /
athAnekakArakaviShayAnarthakyaM codyate-na, svato /
¤abhyupagamavirodhAdAtmavAdinAm /

START BrhUp 2,2.1

BrhUpBh_2,2.1

yo ha vai shishuM sAdhAnaM sapratyAdhAnaM sasthUNaM sadAmaM veda, tasyedaM phalam; kiM tat? sapta saptasaMkhyAkAn ha dviShato dveShakartÌn bhrAtR^ivyAn /

idaM pratyAdhAnaM shiraH; pradeshavisheSheShu-prati pratyAdhIyata iti pratyAdhAnam /
prANaH sthUNA annapAnajanitAshaktiH-prANo balamiti paryAyaH /

yathA vatsaH sthUNAvaShTambha evaM sharIrapakShapAtI vAyuH prANaH sthUNeti kecit /
annaM dAma-annaM hi bhuktaM tredhA pariNamate;ya;sthUlaH pariNAmaH, sa etaddvayaM bhUtvA imAmapyeti-mUtraM ca purIShaM ca /
yo madhyamo rasaH sa raso lohitAdikrameNa svakAryaM sharIraM sAptadhAtukamupacinoti;svayonyannAgame hi sharIramupacIyate 'nnamayatvAt;viparyaye 'pakShIyate patati;yastvaNiShTho rasaH-amR^itam UrkprabhAvaH-iti ca kathyate, sa nAbherUrdhvaM hR^idayadeshamAgatya, hR^idayAdviprasR^iteShu dvAsaptatinADIsahasreShvanupravishya yattatkaraNasaN^ghAtarUpaM liN^gaM shishusaJNj~nakam, tasya sharIre sthitikAraNaM bhavati balamupajanayatsthUNAkhyam;tenAnnamubhayataH pAshavatsadAmavat prANasharIrayornibandhanaM bhavati //1//

START BrhUp 2,2.2

START BrhUp 2,3.1

BrhUpBh_2,3.1

START BrhUp 2,3.2

BrhUpBh_2,3.2

tadetanmUrtaM mUrcchitAvayavam itaretarAnupraviShTAvayavaM ghanaM saMhatamityarthaH /

START BrhUp 2,3.3



#<athAmUrtam |
vAyush cAntarikShash ca |

BrhUpBh_2,3.3

athAmUrtam-athAdhunAmUrtamucyate /
vAyushcAntarikShaM ca yatparisheShitaM bhUtadvayam-etadamR^itam, amUrtatvAt;asthitam, ato 'virudhyamAnaM kenacit, amR^itamamaraNadharmi /
etadyatsthitaviparItam, vyApi, aparicchinnam, yasmAt 'yat'etad anyebhyo 'pravibhajyamAnavisheSham, atastyat, 'tyat'iti parokShAbhidhAnArhameva-pUrvavat /

tasyaitasyAmUrtasya tasyAmR^itasyaitasya yata etasya tyasya catuShTayavisheShaNasyAmUrtasyaiSha rasaH;ko 'sau? ya

eSha etasminmaNDale puruShaH-karaNAtmako hiraNyagarbhaH prANa ityabhidhIyate yaH, sa eSho 'mUrtasya bhUtadvayasya rasaH pUrvavatsAriShThaH /

rasaH kAraNaM hiraNyagarbhavij~nAnAtmA cetana iti kecit /
tatra ca kila hiraNyagarbhavij~nAnAtmanaH karma vAyvantarikShayoH prayoktR^i, tatkarma vAyvantarikShAdhAraM sadanyeShAM bhUtAnAM prayoktR^i bhavati;tena svakarmaNA vAyvantarikShayoH prayokteti tayo rasaH kAraNamucyata iti /

tanna, mUrtarasenAtulyatvAt /
mUrtasya tu bhUtatrayasya raso mUrtameva maNDalaM dR^iShTaM bhUtatrayasya raso mUrtameva maNDalaM dR^iShTaM bhUtatrayasamAnajAtIyam, na cetanaH;tathAmUrtayorapi bhUtayostatsamAnajAtIyenaivAmUrtasena yuktaM bhavitum;vAkyapravR^ittestulyatvAt;yathA hi mUrtAmUrte catuShTayadharmavatI vibhajyete, tathA rasarasavatorapi mUrtAmUrtayostulyenaiva nyAyena yukto vibhAgaH, na tvardhavaishasam /

mUrtarase 'pi maNDalopAdhishcetano vivakShyata iti cet? atyalpamidamucyate, sarvatraiva tu mUrtAmUrtayorbrahmarUpeNa vivakShitatvAt /
puruShashabdo 'cetane 'nupapanna iti cet! na, pakShapucchAdivishiShTasyaiva liN^gasya puruShashabdadarshanAt /
"na vA itthaM santaH shakShyAmaH prajAH prajanayitumimAnsapta puruShAnekaM puruShaM karavAmeti ta etAnsapta puruShAnekaM puruShamakurvan"ityAdau annarasamayAdiShu ca shrutyantare puruShashabdaprayogAt /
ityadhidaivatamityuktopasaMhAro 'dhyAtmavibhAgoktyarthaH //3//

#<athAdhyAtmam |

BrhUpBh_2,3.4

athAdhunAdhyAtmaM mUrtAmUrtayorvibhAga ucyate-kiM tanmUrtam? idameva, kiM cedam? yadanyatprANAccavAyoryashcAyamantarabhyantare AtmannAtmanyAkAshaH khaM sharIrasthashca yaH prANa etad dvayaM varjayitvA yadanyaccharIrArambhakaM bhUtatrayam, etanmartyamityAdi samAnamanyatpUrveNa /
etasya sato hyeSha rasaH-yaccakShuriti; AdhyAtmikasya sharIrArambhakasya kAryasyaiSha rasaH sAraH; tena hi sAreNa sAravadidaM sharIraM samastaM yathAdhidaivatamAdityamaNDalena /
prAthamyAcca-cakShuShI eva prathame sambhavataH sambhavata iti /
"tejo raso niranartatAgniH"iti liN^gAt; taijasaM hi cakShuH; etatsAram; taijasaM hi cakShuH; etatsAram AdhyAtmikaM bhUtatrayam; sato hyeSha rasa iti mUrtatvasAratve hetvarthaH //4//

BrhUpBh_2,3.5

START BrhUp 2,3.6

#<tasya haitasya puruShasya rUpam |
yathA mAhArajanaM vAso yathA pANDvAvikaM yathendragopo yathAgnyarcir yathA puNDarIkaM yathA sakR^idvidyuttam |

BrhUpBh_2,3.6

tasya haitasya puruShasya karaNAtmano liN^gasya rUpaM vakShyAmo vAsanAmayaM mUrtAmUrtavAsanAvij~nAnamayasaMyogajanitaM vicitraM paTabhitticitravanmAyendrajAlamR^igatR^iShNikopamaM sarvavyAmohAspadametAvanmAtrameva Atmeti vij~nAnavAdino vainAshikA yatra bhrAntAH, etadeva vAsanArUpaM paTarUpavadAtmano dravyasya guNa iti naiyAyikA vaisheShikAshca sampratipannAH, idamAtmArthaM triguNaM svatantraM pradhAnAshrayaM puruShArthena hetunA pravartata iti sAN^khyAH /

aupaniShadaMmanyA api kecitprakriyAM racayanti-mUrtAmUrtarAshirekaH, paramAtmarAshiruttamaH, tAbhyAmanyo 'yaM madhyamaH kila tR^itIyaH kartrA bhoktrAvij~nAnamayena ajAtashatrupratibodhitena saha vidyAkarmapUrvapraj~nAsamudAyaH;prayoktA karmarAshiH, prayojyaH pUrvokto mUrtAmUrtabhUtarAshiH sAdhanaM ceti /
tatra ca tArkikaiH saha sandhiM kurvanti /
liN^gAshrayashcaiSha karmarAshirityuktvA punastatasrasyantaH sAN^khyatvabhayAt, sarvaH karmarAshiH-puShpAshraya iva gandhaH puShpaviyoge 'pi puTatailAshrayo bhavati, tadvat-liN^gaviyoge 'pi paramAtmaikadeshamAshrayati, sa paramAtmaikadeshaH kilAnyata Agatena guNena karmaNA saguNo bhavati nirguNo 'pi san, sa kartA bhoktA badhyate mucyate ca vij~nAnAtmA - iti vaisheShikacittamapyanusaranti;sa ca karmarAshirbhUtarAsherAgantukaH, svato nirguNa eva paramAtmaikadeshatvAt;svata utthitA avidyA anAgantukApyUSharavadanAtmadharmaH-ityanayA kalpanayA sAN^khyacittamanuvartante /

sarvametattArkikaiH saha sAmaJNjasyakalpanayA ramaNIyaM pashyanti, lopaniShatsiddhAntaM sarvanyAyavirodhaM ca pashyanti;katham? uktA eva tAvatsAva yavatve paramAtmanaH

saMsAritvasavraNatvakarmaphaladeshasaMsAritvasavraNatvakarmaphaladeshasaMsaraNAnupapattyAdayo doShAH;nityabhede ca vij~nAnAtmanaH pareNaikatvAnupapattiH /

liN^gameveti cetparamAtmana upacaritadeshatvena kalpitaM ghaTakarakabhUchidrAkAshAdivat, tathA liN^gaviyoge 'pi paramAtmadeshAshrayaNaM vAsanAyAH /
avidyAyAShca svata utthAnam USharavat-ityAdikalpanAnupapannaiva /
na ca vAsya deshavyatirekeNa vAsanAyA vastvantarasaJNcaraNaM manasApi kalpayituM shakyam /

na ca shrutayo gacchanti"kAmaH saN^kalpo vicikitsA" "hR^idaye hyeva rUpANi" "dhyAyatIva lelAyatIva" "kAmA ye 'sya hR^idi shritAH""tIrNo hi tadA sarvAJNchokAnhR^idayasya"ityAdyAH /
na cAsAM shrutInAM shrutAdarthAntarakalpanA nyAyyA, AtmanaH parabrahmatvopapAdanArthaparatvAdAsAm, etAvanmAtrArthopakShayatvAcca sarvopaniShadAm /
tasmAcchrutyarthakalpanAkushalAH sarva evopaniShadarthamanyathA kurvanti /
tathApi vedArthashcetsyAtkAmaM bhavatu, na me dveShaH /

na ca 'dva vAva brahmaNo rUpe'iti rAshitrayapakShe samaJNjasam;yadA tu mUrtAmUrte tajjanitavAsanAshca mUrtAmUrte dve rUpe, brahma ca rUpi tR^itIyam, na cAnyaccaturthamantarAletadA etadanukUlamavadhAraNam, dve eva brahmaNo rUpe iti;anyathA brahmaikadeshasya vij~nAnAtmano rUpe iti kalpyam, paramAtmano vA vij~nAnAtmadvAreNeti /
tadA ca rUpe eveti dvivacanamasamaJNjasam, rUpANIti vAsanAbhiH saha bahuvacanaM yuktataraM syAt- dve ca mUrtAmUrte vAsanAshca tR^itIyamiti /

atha mUrtAmUrte eva paramAtmano rUpe, vAsanAstu vij~nAnAtmana iti cet-tadA vij~nAnAtmadvAreNa vikriyamANasya paramAtmanaH-itIyaM vAcoyuktiranarthikA syAt, vAsanAyA api vij~nAnAtmadvAratvasya avishiShTatvAt;na ca vastu

vastvantaradvAreNa vikriyata iti mukhyayA vR^ittyA shakyaM kalpayitum;na ca vij~nAnAtmA paramAtmano vastvantaram, tathA kalpanAyAM siddhAntahAnAt /
tasmAd vedArthamUDhAnAM svacittaprabhavA evamAdikalpanA akSharabAhyAH;na hyakSharabAhyo vedArtho vedArthopakArI vA, nirapekShatvAdvedasya prAmANyaM prati;tasmAdrAshitrayakalpanA asamaJNjasA /

'yo 'yaM dakShiNe 'kShanpuruShaH'iti liN^gAtmA prastuto 'dhyAtme, adhidaive ca 'ya eSha etasminmaNDale puruShaH'

iti, 'tasya'iti prakR^itopAdAnAtsa evopAdIyate yo 'sau tyasyAmUrtasya raso na tu vij~nAnamayaH /
nanu vij~nAnamayasyaivaitAni rupANi kasmAnna bhavanti? vij~nAnamayasyApi prakR^itatvAt, 'tasya'iti ca prakR^itopAdAnAt /
naivam, vij~nAnamayasyArUpitvena vijij~nApayiShitatvAt;yadi hi tasyaiva vij~nAnamayasyaitAni mAhArajanAdIni rUpANi syustasyAva 'neti neti'ityanAkhyeyarUpatayAdesho na syAt /
nanvanyasyaivAsAdesho na tu vij~nAnamayasyeti!

na, ShaShThAnte upasaMhArAt-"vij~nAtAramare kena vijAnIyAt"iti vij~nAnamayaM prastutya"sa eSha neti neti"iti"vij~nApayiShyAmi"iti ca pratij~nAyA arthavattvAt /
yadi ca vij~nAnamayasyaiva asaMvyavahAryamAtmasvarUpaM j~nApayitumiShTaM syAtpradhvastasarvopAdhivisheSham, tata iyaM pratij~nArthavatI syAt- yenAsau j~nApito jAnAtyAtmAnamevAhaM brahmAsmIti, shAsraniShThAM prApnoti na bibheti kutashca /
atha punaranyo vij~nAnamayaH, anyaH 'neti neti' iti vyapadishyate-tadAnyadado brahmAnyo 'hamasmIti

viparyayo gR^ihItaH syAt, na 'AtmAnamevAvedahaM brahmAsmi' iti /
tasmAt 'tasya haitasya' iti liN^gapurushasyai vaitAni rUpANi /

satyasya ca satye paramAtmasvarUpe vaktavye niravasheShaM satyaM vaktavyam;satyasya ca visheSharUpANi vAsanAH, tAsAmimAni rUpANyucyante, etasya puruShasya prakR^itasya liN^gAtmana etAni rUpANi;kAni tAni? ityucyante- yathA loke, mahArajanaM haridrA tayA raktaM mAhArajanaM yathA vAso loke, evaM stryAdiviShayasaMyoge tAdR^ishaM vAsanArUpaM raJNjanAkAra mutpadyate cittasya, yenAsau puruSho rakta ityucyate vasrAdivat /

yathA ca loke pANDvAvikam, averidam Avikam UrNAdi, yathA ca tatpANDuraM bhavati, tathAnyadvAsanArUpam /
yathA ca loke indragopo 'tyantarakto bhavati, evamasya vAsanArUpam /
kvacidviShayavisheShApekShayA rAgasya tAratamyam, kvacitpuruShacittavR^ittyapekShayA /
yathA ca loke 'gnyarcirbhAsvaraM bhavati, tathA kvacitkasyacidvAsanArUpaM bhavati /
yathA pumDarIkaM shuklam, tadvadapi ca vAsanArUpaM kasyacidbhavati /
yathA sakR^idvidyuktam, yathA loke sakR^idvidyotanaM sarvataH prakAshakaM bhavati, tathA j~nAnaprakAshavivR^iddhyapekShayA kasyacidvAsanArUpamupajAyate /
naiShAM vAsanArUpANAmAdiranto madhyaM saN^khyA vA, deshaH kAlo nimittaM

vAvadhAryate-asaN^khyeyatvAdvAsanAyAH, vAsanAhetUnAM cAnantyAt /
tathA ca vakShyati ShaShThe-"idaMmayo 'domayaH"ityAdi /

tasmAnna svarUpasaN^khyAvadhAraNArthA dR^iShTAntAH- 'yathA mAhArajanaM vAsaH'ityAdayaH, kiM tarhi? prakArapradarshanArthAH-evamprakArANi hi vAsanArUpANIti /
yattu vAsanArUpamabhihitamante-sakR^idvidyotanamiveti, tatkila hiraNyagarbhasya avyAkR^itAtprAdurbhavataH taDidvatsakR^ideva vyaktirbhavatIti;tattadIyaM vAsanArUpaM hiraNyagarbhasya yo veda tasya sakR^idvidyutteva, ha vai ityavadhAraNArthau, evamevAsya shrIH khyAtirbhavatItyarthaH, yathA hiraNyagarbhasya-evametadyathoktaM vAsanArUpamantyaM yo veda /

evaM niravasheShaM satyasya svarUpamabhidhAya, yattatsatyasya satyamavocAma tasyaiva svarUpAvadhAraNArthaM brahmaNa idamArabhyate-athAnantaraM satyasvarUpanirdeshAnantaram, yatsatyasya satyaM tadevAvashiShyate yasmAdatastasmAtsatyasya satyaM svarUpaM nirdekShyAmaH /
Adesho nirdesho brahmaNaH /
kaH punarasau nirdeshaH? ityucyate-neti netItyevaM nirdeshaH /

nanu kathamAbhyAM 'neti neti'iti shabdAbhyAM satyasya satyaM nirdidikShitam? ityucyate-sarvopAdhivisheShApohena /
yasminna kashcidvisheSho 'sti-nAma vA rUpaM vA karma vA bhedo vA jAtirvA guNo vA;taddvAreNa hi shabdapravR^ittirbhavati /
na caiShAM kashcid visheSho brahmaNyasti;ato na nirdeShTuM shakyate-idaM taditi /
gaurasau spandate shuklo viShANIti yathA loke nirdishyate, tathA;adhyAropitanAmarUpakarmadvAreNa brahma nirdishyate 'vij~nAnamAnandaM brahma' 'vij~nAnaghana eva brahmAtmA'ityevamAdishabdaiH /

yadA punaH svarUpameva nirdidikShitaM bhavati;nirastasarvopAdhivisheSham, tadA na shakyate kenacidapi prakAreNa nirdeShTum;tadA ayamevAbhyupAyaH-yaduta prAptanirdeshapratiShedhadvAreNa 'neti neti'iti nirdeshaH /
idaM ca nakAradvayaM vIpsAvyAptyartham;yadyatprAptaM tattanniShidhyate /
tathA ca sati anirdiShTAshaN^kA brahmaNaH parihR^itA bhavati;anyathA hi nakAradvayena prakR^itadvayapratiShedhe, yadanyatprakR^itAtpratiShiddhadvayAdbrahma tanna nirdiShTam, kIdR^ishaM nu khalu-ityAshaN^kA na nivartiShyate;tathA cAnarthakashca sa nirdeshaH, puruShasya vividiShAyA anivartakatvAt;
'brahma j~napayiShyAmi'iti ca vAkyam aparisamAptArthaM syAt /

yadA tu sarvadikkAlAdivividiShA nivartitA syAt sarvopAdhinirAkaraNadvAreNa tadA saindhavaghanavadekarasaM praj~nAnaghanamanantaramabAhyaM satyasya satyamahaMbrahmAsmIti sarvato nivartate vividiShA, AtmanyevAvasthitA praj~nA bhavati /
tasmAdvIpsArthaM neti netIti nakAradvayam /
nanu mahatA yatnena parikarabandhaM kR^itvA kiM yuktamevaM nirdeshTuM brahma? bADham;kasmAt? na hi-yasmAt, 'iti na, iti na'ityetasmAt-itIti vyAptavyaprakArA nakAradvayaviShayA nirdishyante, yathA grAmo grAmo ramaNIya iti, anyatparaM nirdeshanaM nAsti;tasmAdayameva nirdesho brahmaNaH /

yaduktam- 'tasyopaniShatsatyasya satyam'iti, evaMprakAreNa satyasya satyaM tatparaM brahma;ato yuktamuktaM nAmadheyaM brahmaNaH, nAmaiva nAmadheyam;kiM tat? satyasya satyaM prANA vai satyaM teShAmeSha satyamiti //6//

START BrhUp 2,4.1



AtmetyevopAsIta;tadeva tasminsarvasminpadanIyamAtmatattvam, yasmAtpreyaH putrAdeH-ityupanyastasya vAkyasya vyAkhyAnaviShaye sambandhaprayojane abhihite- 'tadAtmAnamevAvedahaM brahmAsmIti tasmAttatsarvamabhavat'iti;evaM pratyagAtmA brahmavidyAyA viShaya ityetadupanyastam /
avidyAyAshca viShayaH- 'anyo 'sAvanyo 'hamasmIti na sa veda'ityArabhya cAturvarNyapravibhAgAdinimittapAN^ktakarmasAdhyasAdhanalakShaNo bIjAN^kuravadvyAkR^itAvyAkR^itasvabhAvo nAmarUpakarmAtmakaH saMsAraH 'trayaM vA idaM nAma rUpaM karma'ityupasaMhR^itaH /
shAsrIya utkarShalakShaNo brahmalokAnto 'dhobhAvashca sthAvarAnto 'shAsrIyaH pUrvameva pradarshitaH- 'dvayA ha'ityAdinA /
etasmAdavidyAviShayAdviraktasya pratyagAtmaviShayabrahmavidyAyAmadhikAraH kathaM nAma syAditi-tR^itIye 'dhyAye upasaMhR^itaH samasto 'vidyAviShayaH /
caturthe tu brahmavidyAviShayaM pratyagAtmAnam 'brahma te bravANi'iti 'brahma j~napayiShyAmi'iti ca prastutya, tadbrahmaikamadvayaM sarvavisheShashUnyaM kriyAkArakaphalasvabhAvasatyashabdavAcyAsheShabhUtadharmapratiShedhadvAreNa 'neti neti'iti j~nApitam /

asyA brahmavidyAyA aN^gatvena saMnyAso vidhitsitaH, jAyAputravittAdilakShaNaM pAN^ktaM karmAvidyAviShayaM yasmAnnAtmaprAptisAdhanam; anyasAdhanaM hyanyasmai phalasAdhanAya prayujyamAnaM pratikUlaM bhavati /
na hi bubhukShApipAsAnivR^ittyarthaM dhAvanaM gamanaM vA sAdhanam; manuShyalokapitR^ilokadevalokasAdhanatvena hi putrAdisAdhanAni shrutAni, nAtmaprAptisAdhanatvena /
visheShitatvAcca; na ca brahmavido vihitAni, kAmyatvashravaNAt- 'etAvAnvai kAmaH' iti /
brahmavidashcAptakAmatvAdAptakAmasya kAmAnupapatteH /
"yeShAM no 'yamAtmAyaM lokaH"iti ca shruteH /

kecittu brahmavido 'pyeShaNAsambandhaM varNayanti, tairbR^ihadAraNyakaM na shrutam; putrAdyeShaNAnAmavidvadviShayatvam; vidyAviShaye ca-"yeShAM no 'yamAtmAyaM lokaH"ityataH"kiM prajayA kariShyAmaH"ityeSha vibhAgastairna shrutaH shrutyA kR^itaH;  sarvakriyAkArakaphalopamardasvarUpAyAM ca vidyAyAM satyAm, saha kAryeNAvidyAyA anupapattilakShaNashca virodhastairna vij~nAtaH /
vyAsavAkyaM ca tairna shrutam; karmavidyAsvarUpayorvidyAvidyAtmakayoH pratikUlavartanaM virodhaH;
"yadidaM vedavacanaM kuru karma tyajeti ca /
kAM gatiM vidyayA yAnti kAM ca gacchanti karmaNA //
etadvai shrotumicchAmi tadbhavAnprabravItu me /
etAvanyonyavairUpye vartete pratikUlataH /
"ityevaM pR^iShTasya prativacanena - "karmaNA badhyate janturvidyayA ca vimucyate /
tasmAtkarma na kurvanti yatayaH pAradarshinaHþ //

ityevamAdivirodhaH pradarshitaH /
tasmAnna sAdhanAntarasahitA brahmavidyA puruShArthasAdhanam, sarvavirodhAt, sAdhananirapekShaiva puruShArthasAdhanamiti pArivrAjyaM sarvasAdhanasaMnyAsalakShaNamaN^gatvena vidhitsyate /
etAvadeva amR^itatvasAdhanam ityavadhAraNAt, ShaShThasamAptau, liN^gAcca-karmI sanyAj~navalkyaH pravavrAjeti /
maitreyyai ca karmasAdhanarahitAyai sAdhanatvenAmR^itatvasya brahmavidyopadeshAd vittanindAvacanAcca /
yadi hyamR^itatvasAdhanaM karma syAd vittasAdhyaM pAN^ktaM karma, iti tannindAvacanamaniShTaM syAt /
yadi tu paritityAjayiShitaM karma, tato yuktA tatsAdhananindA /

karmAdhikAranimittavarNAshramAdipratyayopamardAcca-"brahma taM parA dAt" "kShatraM taM parAdAt"ityAdeH /
na hi brahmakShatrAdyAtmapratyayopamarde, brAhmaNenedaM kartavyaM kShatriyeNedaM kartavyamiti viShayAbhAvAdAtmAnaM labhate vidhiH /
yasyaiva puruShasyopamarditaH pratyayo brahmakShatrAdyAtmaviShayaH, tasya tatpratyayasaMnyAsAt tatkAryANAM karmaNAM karmasAdhanAnAM ca arthaprAptashca sanyAsaH /
tasmAdAtmaj~nAnAN^gatvena saMnyAsavidhitsayaiva AkhyAyikeyamArabhyate-



#<maitreyIti hovAca yAj~navalkyaH -- udyAsyan vA are 'ham asmAt sthAnAd asmi |
hanta te 'nayA kAtyAyanyAntaM karavANIti || BrhUp_2,4.1 ||>#

BrhUpBh_2,4.1

maitreyIti hovAca yAj~navalkyaH-maitreyIM svabhAryAmAmantritavAnyAj~navalkyo nAma R^iShiH;udyAsyannUrdhvaM yAsyanpArivrAjyAkhyamAshramAntaraM vai /
are iti sambodhanam /
aham, asmAdgArhasthyAt, sthAnAdAshramAt, UrdhvaM gantumicchannasmi

bhavAmi;ato hantAnumatiM prArthayAmi te tava;kiJNcAnyatte tavAnayA dvitIyayA bhAryayA kAtyAyanyAntaM vicchedaM karavANi;patidvAreNa yuvayormayA sambandhasya vicchedaM karavANi dravyavibhAgaM kR^itvA;vittena saMvibhajya yuvAM gamiShyAmi //1//

START BrhUp 2,4.2



#<sA hovAca maitreyI -- yan nu ma iyaM bhagoH sarvA pR^ithivI vittena pUrNA syAt kathaM tenAmR^itA syAm iti |
neti hovAca yAj~navalkyaH |
yathaivopakaraNavatAM jIvitaM tathaiva te jIvitaM syAt |
amR^itatvasya tu nAshAsti vitteneti || BrhUp_2,4.2 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_2,4.2

sA evamuktA hovAca-yadyadi 'nu'iti vitarke, me mama iyaM pR^ithivI, bhagoH-bhagavan, sarvA sAgaraparikShiptA vittena dhanena pUrNA syAt;katham? na kathaJNcanetyAkShepArthaH, prashnArtho vA, tena pR^ithivIpUrNavittasAdhyena karmaNAgnihotrAdinA amR^itA kiM syAmiti vyavahitena sambandhaH /
pratyuvAca yAj~navalkyaH-kathamiti yadyAkShepArtham, anumodanaM neti hovAca yAj~navalkyaH-kathamiti yadyAkShepArtham, anumodanaM neti hovAca yAj~navalkya iti;prashnashcetprativacanArtham;naiva syA amR^itA, kiM tarhi? yathaiva loke upakaraNavatAM sAdhanavatAM jIvitaM sukhopAyabhogasampannam;tathaiva tadvadeva tava jIvitaM syAt;amR^itatvasya tu nAshA manasApyasti vittena vittasAdhyena karmaNeti //2//

START BrhUp 2,4.3



#<sA hovAca maitreyI -- yenAhaM nAmR^itA syAM kim ahaM tena kuryAm |
yad eva bhagavAn veda tad eva me brUhIti || BrhUp_2,4.3 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_2,4.3

sA hovAca maitreyI;evamuktA pratyuvAca maitreyI-yadyevaM yenAhaM nAmR^itA syAm, kimahaM tena vittena kuryAm? yadeva bhagavAnkevalamamR^itatvasAdhanaM veda, tadevAmR^itatvasAdhanaM me mahyaM brUhi //3//

START BrhUp 2,4.4



#<sa hovAca yAj~navalkyaH -- priyA batAre naH satI priyaM bhAShase |
ehy Assva |
vyAkhyAsyAmi te |
vyAcakShANasya tu me nididhyAsasveti || BrhUp_2,4.4 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_2,4.4

sa hovAca yAj~navalkyaH /
evaM vittasAdhye 'mR^itatvasAdhane pratyAkhyAte, yAj~navalkyaH svAbhiprAyasampattau tuShTa Aha;sa hovAca-priyeShATA, batetyanukampyAha, are maitreyi no 'smAkaM pUrvamapi priyA satI bhavantI idAnIM priyameva cittAnukUlaM bhAShase;ata ehyAHsvopavisha vyAkhyAsyAmi-yatte tava iShTam amR^itatvasAdhanam Atmaj~nAnaM

kathayiShyAmi /
vyAcakShANasya tu me mama vyAkhyAnaM kurvato nididhyAsasva vAkyAnyarthato nishcayena dhyAtumiccheti //4//

START BrhUp 2,4.5



#<sa hovAca -- na vA are patyuH kAmAya patiH priyo bhavaty Atmanas tu kAmAya patiH priyo bhavati |
na vA are jAyAyai kAmAya jAyA priyA bhavaty Atmanas tu kAmAya jAyA priyA bhavati |
na vA are putrANAM kAmAya putrAH priyA bhavanty Atmanas tu kAmAya putrAH priyA bhavanti |
na vA are vittasya kAmAya vittaM priyaM bhavaty Atmanas tu kAmAya vittaM priyaM bhavati |
na vA are brahmaNaH kAmAya brahma priyaM bhavaty Atmanas tu kAmAya brahma priyaM bhavati |
na vA are kShatrasya kAmAya kShatraM priyaM bhavaty Atmanas tu kAmAya kShatraM priyaM bhavati |
na vA are lokAnAM kAmAya lokAH priyA bhavanty Atmanas tu kAmAya lokAH priyA bhavanti |
na vA are devAnAM kAmAya devAH priyA bhavanty Atmanas tu kAmAya devAH priyA bhavanti |
na vA are bhUtAnAM kAmAya bhUtAni priyANi bhavanty Atmanas tu kAmAya bhUtAni priyANi bhavanti |
na vA are sarvasya kAmAya sarvaM priyaM bhavaty Atmanas tu kAmAya sarvaM priyaM bhavati |
AtmA vA are draShTavyaH shrotavyo mantavyo nididhyAsitavyo maitreyi |
Atmano vA are darshanena shravaNena matyA vij~nAnenedaM sarvaM viditam || BrhUp_2,4.5 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_2,4.5

sa hovAca-amR^itatvasAdhanaM vairAgyamupadidikShurjAyApatiputrAdibhyo virAgamutpAdayati tatsaMnyAsAya /
na vai-vaishabdaH prasiddhasmaraNArthaH;prasiddhamevaitalloke;patyurbhartuH kAmAya prayojanAya jAyAyAH patiH priyo na bhavati, kiM tarhyAtmanastu kAmAya prayojanAyaiva bhAryAyAH patiH priyo bhavati /
tathA na vA are jAyAyA ityAdi samAnamanyat, na vA are putrANAm, na vA are vittasya, na vA are brahmaNaH, na vA are kShatrasya, na vA are devAnAm, na vA are bhUtAnAm, na vA are sarvasya, pUrvaM pUrvaM yathAsanne prItisAdhane vacanam;tatra tatreShTataratvAdvairAgyasya;sarvagrahaNamuktAnuktArtham /

tasmAllokaprasiddhametat-Atmaiva priyaH, nAnyat /
'tadetatpreyaH putrAt'ityupanyastam, tasyaitad vR^ittisthAnIyaM prapaJNcitam /
tasmAdAtmaprItisAdhanatvAdgauNI anyatra prItiH, Atmanyeva mukhyA /
tasmAdAtmA vai are draShTavyo darshanArhaH, darshanaviShayamApAdayitavyaH;shrotavyaH pUrvamAcAryata Agamatashca;pashcAnmantavyastarkataH;tato nididhyAsitavyo nishcayena dhyAtavyaH;evaM hyasau dR^iShTo bhavati shravaNamanananididhyAsanasAdhanairnirvartitaiH /
yadaikatvamatAnyupagatAni, tadA samyagdarshanaM brahmaikatvaviShayaM prasidati, nAnyathA shravaNamAtreNa /
yadbrahmakShatrAdi karmanimittaM varNAshramAdilakShaNam AtmavidyAdhyAropitapratyayaviShayaM kriyAkArakaphalAtmakamavidyApratyayaviShayam-rajjavAmva sarpapratyayaH, tadupamardanArtham Aha-Atmani khalvare maitreyi dR^iShTe shrute mate vij~nAte idaM sarvaM viditaM vij~nAtaM bhavati //5//




nanu kathamanyasminvidite 'nyadviditaM bhavati? naiSha doShaH;na hi AtmavyatirekeNAnyatkiJNcidasti ;yadyasti na tadviditaM syAt;na tvanyadasti;Atmaiva tu sarvam;tasmAtsarvamAtmani vidite viditaM syAt /
kathaM punarAtmaiva sarvamityetacchrAvayati-

START BrhUp 2,4.6



#<brahma taM parAdAd yo 'nyatrAtmano brahma veda |
kShatraM taM parAdAd yo 'nyatrAtmanaH kShatraM veda |
lokAs taM parAdur yo 'nyatrAtmano lokAn veda |
devAs taM parAdur yo 'nyatrAtmano devAn veda |
bhUtAni taM parAdur yo 'nyatrAtmano bhUtAni veda |
sarvaM taM parAdAd yo 'nyatrAtmanaH sarvaM veda |
idaM brahmedaM kShatram ime lokA ime devA imAni bhUtAnIdaM sarvaM yad ayam AtmA || BrhUp_2,4.6 ||>#

BrhUpBh_2,4.6

brahma brAhmaNajAtistaM puruShaM parAdAtparAdadhyAtparAkuryAt;kam? yo 'nyatrAtmana AtmasvarUpavyatirekeNa-Atmaiva na bhavatIyaM brAhmaNajAtiriti-tAM yo veda, taM parAdadhyAtsA

brAhmaNajAtiranAtmasvarUpeNa mAM pashyatIti;paramAtmAhi sarveShAmAtmA /
tathA kShatraM kShatriyajAtiH, tathA lokAH, devAH, bhUtAni, sarvam /
idaM brahmeti-yAnyanukrAntAni tAni sarvANi, Atmaiva, yadayamAtmA-yo 'yamAtmA draShTavyaH shrotavya iti prakR^itaH;yasmAdAtmano jAyata Atmanyeva lIyata AtmamayaM ca sthitikAle, AtmavyatirekeNAgrahaNAt, Atmaiva sarvam //6//




kathaM punaridAnImidaM sarvamAtmaiveti grahItuM shakyate? cinmAtrAnugamAtsarvatra citsvarUpataiveti gamyate /
tatra dR^iShTAnta ucyate /
tatra dR^iShTAnta ucyate-yatsvarUpavyatirekeNAgrahaNaM yasya, tasya tadAtmatvameva loke dR^iShTam /

START BrhUp 2,4.7



#<sa yathA dundubher hanyamAnasya na bAhyA¤ chabdA¤ chaknuyAd grahaNAya |
dundubhes tu grahaNena dundubhyAghAtasya vA shabdo gR^ihItaH || BrhUp_2,4.7 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_2,4.7

sa yathA-sa iti dR^iShTAntaH, loke yathA dundubherbheryAdeH, hanyamAnasya tADyamAnasya daNDAdinA, na, bAhyAJNchabdAn bahirbhUtAJNchabdavisheShAn dundubhishabdasAmAnyAnniShkR^iShTAn dundubhishabdavisheShAn na shaknuyAd grahaNAya grahItum;dundubhestu grahaNena, dundubhishabdA eta iti, shabdavisheShA gR^ihItA bhavanti, dundubhishabdasAmAnyavyatirekeNAbhAvAtteShAm /

dundubhyAghAtasya vA, dunduberAhananam AghAtaH, dundubhyAghAtavishiShTasya shabdasAmAnyasya grahaNena tadgatA visheShA gR^ihItA

bhavanti, na tu ta eva nirbhidya grahItuM shakyante, visheSharUpeNAbhAvAtteShAm /
tathA praj~nAnavyatirekeNa svapnajAgaritayorna kashcidvastuvisheSho gR^ihyate;tasmAtpraj~nAnavyatirekeNa abhAvo yuktasteShAm //7//

START BrhUp 2,4.8



#<sa yathA shaN^khasya dhmAyamAnasya na bAhyA¤ chabdA¤ chaknuyAd grahaNAya shaN^khasya tu grahaNena shaN^khadhmasya vA shabdo gR^ihItaH || BrhUp_2,4.8 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_2,4.8

tathA sa yathA shaN^khasya dhmAyamAnasya shabdena saMyojyamAnasya ApUryamANasya na bAhyAJNchabdAJNchaknuyAdityevamAdi pUrvavat //8//

START BrhUp 2,4.9



#<sa yathA vINAyai vAdyamAnAyai na bAhyA¤ chabdA¤ chaknuyAd grahaNAya vINAyai tu grahaNena vINAvAdasya vA shabdo gR^ihItaH || BrhUp_2,4.9 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_2,4.9

tathA vINAyai vAdyamAnAyai-vImAyA vAdyamAnAyAH /
anekadR^iShTAntopAdAnamiha sAmAnyabahutvakhyApanArtham-aneke hi vilakShaNAshcetanAcetanarUpAH sAmAnyavisheShAH-teShAM pAramparyagatyA yathaikasminmahAsAmAnye 'ntarbhAvaH praj~nAnaghane, kathaM nAma pradarshayitavya iti;dundubhishaN^khavINAshabdasAmAnyavisheShANAM yathA shabdatve 'ntarbhAvaH, evaM sthitikAle tAvatsAmAnyavisheShAvyatirekAd brahmaikatvaM shakyamavagantum //9//

START BrhUp 2,4.10


evamutpattikAle prAgutpatterbrahmaiveti shakyamavagantum /
yathAgnervisphuliN^gadhUmAN^gArArciShAM prAgvibhAgAdagnireveti bhavatyagnyekatvam, evaM jagannAmarUpavikR^itaM pragutpatteH praj~nAnaghana eveti yuktaM grahItumityetaducyate-


#<sa yathArdraidhAgner abhyAhitAt pR^ithag dhUmA vinishcaranty eva vA are 'sya mahato bhUtasya niHshvasitam etad yad R^igvedo yajurvedaH sAmavedo 'tharvAN^girasa itihAsaH purANaM vidyA upaniShadaH shlokAH sUtrANy anuvyAkhyAnAni vyAkhyAnani |
asyaivaitAni nishvasitAni || BrhUp_2,4.10 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_2,4.10

sa yathA-ArdraidhAgneH, Ardrairedhobhiriddho 'gnirArdraidhAgniH, tasmAt, abhyAhitAtpR^ithagdhUmAH, pR^ithagnAnAprakAram, dhUmagrahaNaM visphulihgAdipradarshanArtham, dhUmavisphuliN^gAdayo vinishcaranti vinirgacchanti /
evam-yathAyaM dR^iShTAntaH, are maitreyyasya paramAtmanaH prakR^itasya mahato bhUtasya nishvasitametat, nishvasitamiva nishvasitam;yathA aprayatnenaiva puruShanishvAso bhavatyevaM vA are /
kiM tannishvasitamiva tato jAtamityucyate-yadR^igvedo yajurvedaH sAmavedo 'tharvAN^girasaH-caturvidhaM mantrajAtam, itihAsa ityurvashIpurUravasoH saMvAdAdiH-"urvashIhApsarAH"ityAdibrAhmaNameva, purANam"asadvA idamagra AsIt"ityAdi, vidyA devajanavidyA vedaH so 'yamityAdyA, upaniShadaH"priyamityetadupAsIta"ityAdyAH, shlokA brAhmaNaprabhavA mantrAH"tadete shlokAH"ityAdayaH; sUtrANi vastusaN^graha vAkyAni vede yathA-"AtmetyevopAsIta"ityAdIni, anuvyAkhyAnAni mantravivaraNAni, vyAkhyAnAnyarthavAdAH, athavA vastusaN^grahavAkyavivaraNAnyanuvyAkhyAnAni, yathA caturthAdhyAye 'AtmetyevopAsIta' ityasya, yathA vA 'anyo 'sAvanyo 'hamasmIti na sa veda yathA pashurevam' ityasyAyamevAdhyAyasheShaH, mantravivaraNAni vyAkhyAnAni, evamaShTavidhaM brAhmaNam /
evaM mantrabrAhmaNayoreva grahaNam, niyataracanAvato vidyamAnasyaiva vedasyAbhivyaktiH puruShanishvAsavat, na ca puruShabuddhiprayatnapUrvakaH; ataH pramANaM nirapekSha eva svArthe; tasmAdyattenoktaM tattathaiva pratipattavyam, AtmanaH shreya icchadbhiH j~nAnaM vA karma veti /
nAmaprakAshavashA hi rUpasya vikriyAvyavasthA /
nAmarUpayoreva hi paramAtmopAdhibhUtayorvyAkriyamANayoH salilaphenavattattvAnyatvenAnirvaktavyayoH sarvAvasthayoH saMsAratvam-ityato nAmna eva nishvasitatvamuktam, tadvacanenaivetarasya nishvasitatvasiddheH /
athavA sarvasya dvaitajAtasya avidyAviShayatvamuktam-"brahma taM parAdAt.....idaM sarvaM yadayamAtmA"iti /
tena vedasyAprAmANyamAshaN^kyate /
tadAshaN^kAnivR^ittyarthamidamuktam? puruShanishvAsavadaprayatnotthitatvAtpramANaM vedaH, na yathA anyo grantha iti //10//



kiJNcAnyat, na kevalaM sthityutpattikAlayoreva praj~nAnavyatirekeNAbhAvAjjagato brahmatvam, pralayakAle ca /
jalabudbudaphenAdInAmiva salilavyatirekeNAbhAvaH, evaM praj~nAnavyatirekeNa tatkAryANAM nAmarUpakarmaNAM tasminneva lIyamAnAnAmabhAvaH /
tasmAdekameva brahma praj~nAnaghanamekarasaM pratipattavyamityata Aha /
pralayapradarshanAya dR^iShTAntaH-

START BrhUp 2,4.11



#<sa yathA sarvAsAm apAM samudra ekAyanam |
evaM sarveShAM sparshAnAM tvag ekAyanam |
evaM sarveShAM gandhAnAM nAsike ekAyanam |
evaM sarveShAM rasAnAM jihvaikAyanam |
evaM sarveShAM rUpANAM cakShur ekAyanam |
evaM sarveShaM shabdAnAM shrotram ekAyanam |
evaM sarveShAM saMkalpAnAM mana ekAyanam |
evaM sarvAsAM vidyAnAM hR^idayam ekAyanam |
evaM sarveShAM karmaNAM hastAv ekAyanam |
evaM sarveShAm AnandAnAm upastha ekAyanam |
evaM sarveShAM visargANAM pAyur ekAyanam |
evaM sarveShAm adhvanAM pAdAv ekAyanam |
evaM sarveShAM vedAnAM vAg ekAyanam || BrhUp_2,4.11 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_2,4.11

sa iti dR^iShTAntaH;yathA yena prakAreNa, sarvAsAM nadIvApItaDAgAdigatAnAmapAm, samudro 'bdhirekAyanam, ekagamanamekapralayo 'vibhAgaprAptirityarthaH;yathAyAM dR^iShTAntaH, evaM sarveShAM sparshAnAM mR^idukarkashakaThinapicchilAdInAM vAyorAtmabhUtAnAM tvagekAyanam, tvagiti tvagviShayaM sparshasAmAnyamAtram, tasminpraviShTAH sparshavisheShAH-Apa iva samudram-tadvyatirekeNAbhAvabhUtA bhavanti;tasyaiva hi te saMsthAnamAtrA Asan /
tathA tadapi sparshasAmAnyamAtraM tvakchabdavAcyaM manaHsaN^kalpe manoviShayasAmAnyamAtre, tvagviShaya ivasparshavisheShAH, praviShTaM tadvyatirekeNAbhAvabhUtaM bhavati;evaM manoviShayo 'pi buddhiviShayasAmAnyamAtre praviShTastadvyatirekeNAbhAvabhUto bhavati;vij~nAnamAtrameva bhUtvA praj~nAnaghane pare brahmaNyApa iva samudre pralIyate /

evaM paramparAkrameNa shabdAdau saha grAhakeNa karaNena pralIne praj~nAnaghane upAdhyabhAvAtsaindhavaghanavat praj~nAnaghanamekarasamanantamapAraM nirantaraM brahma vyavatiShThate /
tasmAdAtmaiva ekamadvayamiti pratipattavyam /

tathA sarveShAM gandhAnAM pR^ithivIvisheShANAM nAsike ghrANaviShayasAmAnyam, tathA sarveShAM rasAnAmabvisheShANAM cakShushcakShurviShayasAmAnyam, tathA shabdAnAM shrotraviShayasAmAnyaM pUrvavat /
tathA shrotrAdiviShayasAmAnyAnAM manoviShayasAmAnye saN^kalpe;manoviShayasAmAnyasyApi buddhiviShayasAmAnye vij~nAnamAtre;vij~nAnamAtraM bhUtvA parasminpraj~nAnaghane pralIyate /
tathA karmendriyANAM viShayA vadanAdAnagamanavisargAnandavisheShAH tattatkriyAsAmAnyeShveva praviShTA na vibhAgayogyA bhavanti, samudra ivAbvisheShAH; tAni ca sAmAnyAni prANamAtram, prANashca praj~nAnamAtrameva /
"yo vai prANaH sA praj~nA yA vai praj~nA sa prANaH"iti kauShItakino 'dhIyate /
nanu sarvatra viShayasyaiva pralayo 'bhihitaH, na tu karaNasya;tatra ko 'bhiprAya iti? bADham;kintu viShayasamAnajAtIyaM karaNaM manyate shrutiH, na tu jAtyantaram;viShayasyaiva svAtmagrAhakatvena saMsthAnAntaraM karaNaM nAma-yathA rUpavisheShasyaiva saMsthAnaM pradIpaH karaNaM sarvarUpaprakAshane, evaM sarvaviShayavisheShANAmeva svAtmavisheShaprakAshakatvena saMsthAnAntarANi karaNAni pradIpavat /
tasmAnna karaNAnAM pR^ithakpralaye yatnaH kAryaH,
viShayasAmAnyAtmakatvAdviShayapralayenaiva pralayaH siddho bhavati karaNAnAmiti //11//



tatra 'idaM sarvaM yadayamAtmA' iti pratij~nAtam, tatra heturabhihitaH-AtmasAmAnyatvam, Atmajatvam, AtmapralayatvaM ca /
tasmAdutpattisthitipralayakAleShu praj~nAnavyatirekeNAbhAvAt"praj~nAnaM brahma" "AtmaivedaM sarvam"iti pratij~nAtaM yat, tattarkataH sAdhitam /
svAbhAviko 'yaM pralaya iti paurANikA vadanti /
yastu buddhipUrvakaH pralayo brahmavidAM brahmavidyAnimittaH, ayamAtyantika ityAcakShate-avidyAnirodhadvAreNa yo bhavati; tadartho 'yaM visheShArambhaH-

START BrhUp 2,4.12



#<sa yathA saindhavakhilya udake prAsta udakam evAnuvilIyeta na hAsyodgrahaNAyeva syAt |
yato-yatas tv AdadIta lavaNam |
evaM vA ara idaM mahad bhUtam anantam apAraM vij~nAnaghana eva |
etebhyo bhUtebhyaH samutthAya tAny evAnuvinashyati |
na pretya saMj~nAstIty are bravImi |
iti hovAca yAj~navalkyaH || BrhUp_2,4.12 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_2,4.12

tatra dR^iShTAnta upAdIyate-sa yatheti /
saindhavakhilyaH- sindhorvikAraH saindhavaH, sindhushabdenodakamabhidhIyate, syandanAtsindhurudakam, tadvikArastatra bhavo vA saindhavaH saindhavashcAsau khilyashceti saindhavakhilyaH, khila eva khilyaH svArthe yatpratyayaH, udeka sindhau svayonauprastaH prakShiptaH, udakameva vilIyamAnamanuvilIyeta;yattadbhaumataijasasamparkAtkAThinyaprAptiH /
khilyasya svayonisamparkAdapagacchati tadudakasya vilayanam, tadanu saindhavakhilyo vilIyata ityucyate /
tadetadAha udakamevAnuvilIyeteti /

na ha naiva asya khilyasyodgrahaNAyoddhR^itya pUrvavadgrahaNAya grahItuM naiva samarthaH kashcitsyAtsunipuNo 'pi /
ivashabdo 'narthakaH /
grahaNAya naiva samarthaH;kasmAt? yato yato yasmAdyasmAddeshAtadudakamAdadIta gR^ihItvA svAdayet, lavaNAsvAdameva tadudakaM na tu khilyamAvaH /

yathAyaM dR^iShTAntaH, evameva vA are maitreyidaM paramAtmAkhyaM mahadbhUtam-yasmAnmahato bhUtAdavidyayA paricchinnA satI kAryakaraNopAdhisambandhAtkhilyamAvamApannAsi, martyA janmamaraNAshanAyApipAsAdisaMsAradharmavatyasi, nAmarUpakAryAtmikA-amuShyAnva yAhamiti, sa khilyabhAvastava kAryakaraNabhUnopAdhisamparkabhrAntijanito mahati bhUte svayonau mahAsamudrasyAnIye paramAtmani ajare 'mare 'bhaye shudve saindhavavanavadekarase praj~nAnaghane 'nante 'pAre nirantare 'vidyAjanitabhrAntimedavarjite praveshitaH /
tasminpraviShTe svayonigraste khilyabhAve 'vidyAkR^ite bhedabhAve praNAshite-idamekamadvaitaM mahadbhUtam mahacca tad bhUtaM ca mahadbhUtaM sarvamahattaratvAdAkAshAdikAraNatvAcca /
bhUtaM viShvapi kAlepu svarUpAdhyabhicArAtsarvadaiva pariniShpannamiti vaikAliko niShThApratyayaH /

athavA bhUtashabdaH paramArthavAcI, mahacca pAramArthikaM cetyarthaH;laukikaM tu yadyapi mahadbhavati, svapnamAyAkR^itaM himavadAdiparvatopamaM na paramArthavastu;ato vishinaShTi--idaM tu mahacca tadabhUtaM ceti /
anantaM nAsyAnto vidyata ityanantam;kadAcidApekShikaM syAdityato vishinaShTayapAramitivij~naptirvij~nAnam, vij~nAnama ca tadghanashceti vij~nAnaghanaH, ghanashabdojAtyantarapratiShedhArthaH-yathA suvarNaghano 'yoghana iti;

evashabdo 'vadhAraNArthaH-nAnyaJNjAtyantaramantarAle vidyata ityarthaH /
yadIdamekamadvaitaM paramArthataH svacchaM saMsAraduHkhAsampR^ittkam, kinnimito 'yaM khilyabhAva Atmano jAto mR^itaH sukhI duHkhyahaM mametyevamAdilakShaNo 'nekasaMsAradharmopadrutaH? ityucyate--
etebhyo bhUtebhyo yAnyetAni kAryakaraNavipayAkArapariNatAni nAmarUpAtmakAni salliphenavudvudopamAnisvacchasya paramAtmanaH salilopamasya, yepAM viShayaparyantAnAM praj~nAnaghane brahmaNi paramArthavivekaj~nAnena pravilApanamuttakaM nadIsamudravata--etabhyo hetubhUtebhyo bhUtebhyaH satyashabdavAcyebhyaH samutthAya saindhavakhilyavat-yathA adbhayaH sUryacandrAdipratibimbaH, yathA vA svacchasya sphaTikasya alattakAdyupAdhibhyo rattkAdibhAvaH, evaM kAryakaraNabhUtabhUtopAdhibhyo vishepAtmakhilyabhAvena samutthAya samyagutthAya--yebhyo bhUtebhya utthitaH tAni yadAkAryakaraNaviShayAkArapariNatAni bhUtAnyAtmano vishepAtmakhilyahetubhUtAni shAstrAcAryopadeshena brahmavidyAyA nadIsamudravatpravilApitAni vinashyanti, salilaphenabudbudAdivatteShu vinashyatsu anvevaiSha visheShAtmakhilyabhAvo vinashyati;yathA udakAlattphakAdihetvapanaye sAryacandrasphaTikAdipratibimbo vinashyati, candrAdi svarUpameva paramArthato vyavatiShThate, tadvatpraj~nAnaghanamanantamapAraM svacchaM vyavatiShThate /
na tatra pretya vishepasaMj~nAsti kAryakaraNasaN^ghAtebhyovimuttkasya-ityevamare maitreyi bravImi nAsti visheShasaMj~neti--ahamasAvamuShya putro mamedaM kShetraM dhanaM sukhI duHkhItyevamAdilakShaNA, avidyAkR^itatvAttasyAH;avidyAyAshcabrahmavidyayA niranvayato nAshitatvAtkuto visheShasaMj~nAsambhavo brahmavidashcaitanyasvabhAvAvasthitasya? sharIrAvasthitasyApi visheShasaMj~nA nopapadyate kimuta kAryakaraNavimuttkasya sarvataH? iti hovAcottkavAnkila paramArthadarshanaM maitreyyai bhAryAyai yAj~navalkyaH //12 //



evaM pratibodhitA--

#<sA hovAca maitreyI -- atraiva mA bhagavAn amUmuhan na pretya saMj~nAstIti |

BrhUpBh_2,4.13

sA ha kilovAcottkavatI maitreyI--atraiva etasmitreva ekasminvastuni brahmaNi virudvadharmavattavamAcakShaNena bhagavatA mama moha kR^itaH;tadAha--atraiva mA bhagavAnpUjAvAnamUmuhanmohaM kR^itacAn /
kathaM tena virudvadharmavattvam utkamityucyate--pUrva vij~nAnaghana eveti pratishAya punarna pretya saMshAstIti;kathaM vij~nAnaghana eva? kathaM vA na pretya saMj~nAstIti? na hyuShNaH shItashcAgnirevaiko bhavati /
ato mUDhAsmyatra /

sa hovAca yAj~navalkyaH-na vA are maitreyyahaM mohaM bravImi mohanaM vAkyaM na bravImityarthaH /
nanu kathaM virudvadharmatvamavocaH-vij~nAna ghanaM saMj~nAbhAvaM ca ? na mayedamekasminvamiMNyamihitam, tvayaivedaM virudvadharmatvenaikaM vastu parigR^ihItaM bhrAntyA, na tu mayottkam /
mayA tvidamuttkam--yastvavidyApratyupasyApitaHkAryakaraNasambandhI AtmanaH khilyabhAvaH, yasminvidyayA nAshite, tannimittA yA visheShasaMj~nA sharIrAdisambandhinI anyatvadarshanalakShaNA, sA kAryakaraNasaN^ghAtopAdhau pravilApite nashyati hetvabhAvAd udakAdyAdhAranAshAdiva candrAdipratibimba stannimittashca prakAshAdiH; na punaH paramArthacandrAdityasvarUpAnAshavadasaMsAribrahmasvarUpasya vij~nAnaghanasya nAshaH; tadvij~nAghana ityuttkam; sa AtmA sarvasya jagataH, paramArthato bhUtanAshAnna vinAshI /
vinAshI tvavidyakR^itaH khilyabhAvaH,"vAcArambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyam"(chA0 u0 6 /1 /4) iti shrutyantarAt /
ayaM tu pAramArthikaH-avinAshI vA are 'yamAtmA, ato 'laM paryAptaM vai are idaM mahadbhUtamanantamapAraM ya yAvyAkhyAtaM vij~nAnAya vij~nAtum /

BrhUpBh_2,4.14

kathaM tarhi pretya saMj~nA nAstItyucyate /
shR^iNu /
yatra yasminnavidyAkalpite kAryakaraNasaMghAtopAdhijanite visheShAtmani khilyabhAve hi yasmAdaddvaitamiva pAramArthato 'dvaite brahmaNi dvaitamiva bhinnamiva vastvantaramAtmana upalakShyate /
nanu dvaitenopamIyamAnatvAddvaitasya pAramArthikatvamiti /
na /
'vAcA'rambhaNaM vikAro nAmadheyami'ti shrutyantarA 'dekamevA'dvitIyamAtmaivedaM sarvAmiti ca /
tattatra yasmAddvaitamiva tasmAdevetaro 'sau paramAtmanaH khilyabhUta AtmAparamArthashcandroderivodakacandrAdipratibimba itaro ghrAtetareNa dhrANenetaraM ghrAtavyaM jighrati /
itara itaramiti kArakapradarshanArthaM jighratIti kriyAphalayorabhidhAnam /
yathA chinttIti yathodyamyodyamya nipAtanaM chedasya ca dvaidhIbhAva ubhayaM chinattItyekenaiva shabdenAbhidhIyate kriyAvasAnatvAtkriyAvyatirekeNa ca tatphalasyAnupalambhAt /
itaro ghrANetareNa ghrANenetaraM ghratavyaM jighrati tathA sarvaM pUrvavadvijAnAti /
iyamavidyAvadavasthA /

yatra tu brahmavidyayAvidyA nAshamupagamitA tatrA'tmavyatirekeNAnyasyAbhAvaH /
yatra vA asya brahmavidaH sarvaM nAmarUpAdyAtmanyeva pravilApitamAtmaiva saMvR^ittaM yatraivamAtmaivAbhUttatra kena karaNena kaM dhrAtavyaM ko jighrettathA pashyodvijAnIyAt /
sarvatra hi kArakasAdhyA kriyA /
ataH kArakAbhAve 'nupapattiH kriyAyAH kriyAbhAve ca phalAbhAvaH /
tasmAdavidyAyAmeva satyAM kriyAkArakaphalavyavahAro na brahmavidaH /
AtmatvAdeva sarvasya nA'tmavyatirekeNa kArakaM kriyAphalaM vAsti /
nacAnAtmA sansarvamAtmaiva bhavati kasyacit /
tasmAdavidyayaivAnAttmatvaM parikalpitaM na tu paramArthata AtmavyatirekeNAsti kiJNcit /
tasmAtparamArthAtmaikatvapratyaye kriyAkArakaphalapratyayAnupapattiH /
ato virodhAdbrahmavidaH kriyANAM tatsAdhanAnAM cAntyantameva nivR^ittiH /
kena kimiti kShepArthaM vacanaM prakArAntarAnupapattidarshanArtham /
kenacidapi prakAreNa kriyAkaraNAdikArakAnupapatteH /
kenatcitkaJNcitkAshcitkathaM cinna jivredevetyarthaH /

yatrApyavidyAvasthAyAmanyo 'nyaM pashyati tatrApi yenedaM sarvaM vijAnAti taM kena vijAnIyAdyena vijAnAti tasya karaNasya

vij~neye viniyuktatvAt /
j~nAtushva j~neya eva hi jij~nAsA nA'tmani /
na cAgnerivA'tmA'tmano viShayo na cAviShaye j~nAturj~nAnamupapadyate /
tasmAdyenedaM vijAnAti taM vij~nAtAraM kena karaNena ko vAnyo vijAnIyAt /
yadA tu punaH paramArthavivekino brahmavido vij~nAtaiva kevalo 'dvayo vartate taM vij~nAtAramare kena vijAnIyAditi //4//

#<iyaM pR^ithivI sarveShAM bhUtAnAM madhu |

BrhUpBh_2,5.1

iyaM pR^ithivI prasiddhA sarveShAM bhUtAnAM madhu sarveShAM brahmAdistambaparyantAnAM bhUtAnAM prANinAM madhu kAryaM madhviva madhu yathaiko madhvapUpo 'nekairmadhukarairnirvartita evamiyaM pR^ithivI sarvabhUtanirvartitA /

START BrhUp 2,5.15



#<sa vA ayam AtmA sarveShAM adhipatiH sarveShAM bhUtAnAM rAjA |

BrhUpBh_2,5.15

yasminnAtmani parishiShTo vij~nAnamayo 'mAtmA /
tasminnavidyAkR^itakAryakaraNasaN^ghAtopadhivishiShTe brahmavidyAyA paramArthAtmani praveshite, sa evamuttko 'nantaro 'bAhyaH kR^itastraH praj~nAnaghanabhUtaH sarveShAM bhUtAnAmayamAtmA sarvairUpAsyaH sarveShAM bhUtAnAmadhipatiH sarvabhUtAnAM svatantro na kumAramAtyavat, kiM tarhi? sarveShAM bhUtAnAM rAjA /
rAjatvavisheShaNamadhipatiriti;bhavati kashcidrAjocitaShTattimAshritya rAjA, na tvadhipatiH, ato vishinaShTyadhipatiriti /
evaM sarvabhUtAtmA vidvAn brahmavinmuttko bhavati /

yaduttkam 'brahmavidyayA sarvaM bhaviShyanto manuShyA manyante kimu tadbrahmAvedyasmAttatsarvamabhavat'itIdaM tad vyAkhyAtam /
evamAtmAnabheva sarvAtmatvena AcAryagamAbhyAM shrutvA, matvA tarkato vij~nAya sAkShAdevaM yathA madhubrAhmaNe darshitaM tathA, tasmAdbrahmavij~nAnAdevaMlakShaNAt pUrvamapibrahemaiva sadavidyayA abrahmAsIt, sarvabheva ca sadasarvamAsIt tAntvavidyAmasmAdvij~nanAttiraskR^itya brahmavidbrahmaiva san brahmAbhavat sarvaH sa sarvamabhavat /

parisamAptaH shAstrArtho yadarthaH prastutaH /
tasminnetasmin sarvAtmabhUte brahmavidi sarvAtmani sarvaM jagat samarpitamityetasminnarthe dR^iShTAnta upAdIyate-tadyathA rathanAbhau ca rathenemau cArAH sarve samarpitA iti prasidvor'thaH, evamevAsminnAtmani paramAtmabhUte brahmavidi sarvANi bhUtAni brahmAdistambaryantAni, sarve devA agnyAdayaH, sarve lokA

bhUrAdayaH, sarve praNA vAgAdayaH, sarva eta AtmAno jalacandravat pratisharIrAnupraveshino 'vidyAkalpitAH, sarvaM jagadasmin samarpitam /

yaduttkaM brahmavidvAmadevaH pratipede-'ahaM manurabhavaM sUryashca'iti, sa eSha sarvAtmabhAvo vyAkhyAtaH /
sa eSha vidvAn brahmavit  sarvopAdhiH sarvAtmA sarvo bhavati /
nirupAdhirnirupAkhyaH anantaro 'bAhyaH kR^itsnaH praj~nAnaghano 'jAjaro 'mR^itobhayo 'calo neti netyasthUlo 'naNurityevaMvisheShaNo bhavati /

tametamarthamajAnantastArkikAH kecit paNDitaMmanyAshcAgamavidaH shAstrArtha virudvaM manyamAnA vikalpayanto mohamagAdhamupayAnti /
tametamarthametau manetrAvanuvadataH--"anejadekaM manaso javIyaH" "tadejati tannaijati"iti /
tathA ca taittirIyake--"yasmAtparaM nApAramasti kiJNcat""etatsAma gAyannAste" "ahamannamahamannamahamannam"ityAdi /
tathA ca cchAndogye"jakShat krIDanramamANaH" "sayadi pitR^ilokakAmaH" "sarvagandhaH sarvarasaH"ityAdi /
AyarvaNe ca"sarvaj~naH sarvavit""dUrAta sudUre tadihAntike ca /
"kaThavallIShvapi"aNoraNIyAn mahato mahIyAn" "kastaM madAmadaM devam" "tadvAvato 'nyAnatyeti tiShThat"iti ca /
tathA gItAsu"ahaM kraturahaM yaj~naH" "pitAhamasya jagataH" "nAdatte kasyacit pApam" "samaM sarveShu bhUteShu" "avimattkaM vibhattkepu" "grasiShNu prabhaviShNu ca"ityevamAdyAgamArtha virudvamiva

pratibhAntaM manyamAnAH svacittasAmarthyAdarthanirNayAya vikalpayantaH, astyAtmA nAstyAtmA kartAkartA muttko badvaH kShaNiko vij~nAnamAtraM shUnyaM cetyevaM vikalpayanto na pAramadhigacchantyavidyAyAH, virudvarrmadarshitvAt sarvatra /

tasmAttatra ya eva shrutyAcAryadarshitamArgAnusAriNaH, ta evAvidyAyAH pAramadhigacchanti /
ta eva vAsmAnmohasamudrAdagAdhAduttariShyanti, netare svavudvikaushalAnusAriNaH //15 //

START BrhUp 2,5.16



parisamAptA brahmavidyAmR^itatvasAdhanAbhUtA, yAM maitreyI pR^iShTavatI bhartAram 'yadeva bhagavAnamR^itatvasAdhanaM veda tadeva me brUhi'iti /
etasyA brahmavidyAyAH stutyartheyamAkhyAyikAyAH saN^kShepator'thaprakAshanArthAvetau mantrau bhavataH /
evaM hi mantrabrAhmaNAbhyAM stutatvAt amR^itatvasarvaprAptisAdhanatvaM brahmavidyAyAH prakaTIkR^itaM rAjamArga mupanItaM bhavati--yathAditya udyaJNchalArvaraM tamo 'panayatIti tadvat /

api caivaM stutA brahmavidyAyA indrarakShitA sA duShprApyA devairapi;.smAdashcibhyAmapidevabhipagbhyAmindrarakShitA vidyA mahatAyAsena prAptA /
brAhmaNasya shirashchittvAshvayaM shiraH pratisandhAya tasminnindreNacchinne punaH svashira eva pratisandhAya tena brAhmaNasya svashirasaivottkAsheShA brahmavidyA shrutA /
tasmAttataH parataraM kiJNcit puruShArthasAdhanaM na bhUtaM na bhAvi vA, kuta eva vartamAnam, iti nAtaH parAstutirasti /

api caivaM stUyate brahmavidyAsarvapuruShArthAnAM karma hi sAdhanamiti loke prasidvam /
tacca karma vittasAdhyam,

tenAshApinAstyamR^itatvasya /
tadidamamR^itatvaM kevalayAtmavidyayA karmanirapekShayA prApyate;yasmAt karmaprakaraNe vaktuM prAptapi kevalaprakaraNe, karmaprakaraNAduttIrta karmaNA virudvatvAt kevalasaMnyAsasahitA abhihitA amR^itatvasAdhanAya /
tasmAnnAtaH paraM puruShArthasAdhanamasti /

api caivaM stutA brahmavidyA sarvo hi loko dvandvArAmaH"sa vai naiva reme tasmAdekAkI na ramate"iti shruteH /

api caivaM stutA brahmavidyA yasmAdyAj~navalkyenasaMsAramArgad vyuttiShThatApi priyAyai bhAryAyai protyarthameMvAmihitA,"priyaM bhApasa ehyAHsva"iti liN^gAt /

tatreyaM stutyarthAkhyAyiketyavocAma /
kA punaH sA AkhyAyikA? ityucyate---



#<idaM vai tan madhu dadhyaÇÇ AtharvaNo 'shvibhyAm uvAca |
tad etad R^iShiH pashyann avocat -- tad vAM narA sanaye daMsa ugram AviSh kR^iNomi tanyatur na vR^iShTim |
dadhyaÇ ha yan madhv AtharvaNo vAm ashvasya shIrShNA pra yad Im uvAceti || BrhUp_2,5.16 ||>#

BrhUpBh_2,5.16

idamityanantaranirdiShTaM vyapadishati, budvau sannihitatvAt /
vaishabdaH smaraNArthaH /

tadityAkhyAyikAnirvR^ittaMprakaraNAntarAbhihitaM parokShaM vaishabdena smArayanniha vyapadishati /
yattat pravargyaprakaraNe mUcitam, nAviShkR^itaM madhu, tadidaM madhvihAnantaraM nirdiShTam-'iyaM pR^ithivI'ityAdinA /

kathaM tatra prakaraNAnte sUcitam-dadhyaÇ ha vA AbhyAmAtharvaNo madhu nAma brAhmaNamuvAca /
tadenayoH priyaM dhAma tadevainayoretenopagacchati /
sa hovAcendreNa vA uttko 'smayetaccedanyasmA anuvrUyAstata eva te shirashchindyAmiti /
tasmAdvai bibhemi, yadvai me sa shiro na chindyAt tadvAmupaneShya iti /
tau hocaturAvAM tvA tasmAt trAsyAvahe iti kathaM mA trAsyethe? iti /
yadA nAvupaneShyase;atha te shirashchittvA anyatrAhratyopanidhAsyAvaH;athAshvasya shira Ahratya tatte pratidhAsyAvaH;tena nAvanuvakShyasi /
yadA nAvanuvakShyasi, atha te tadindraH shirashchetsyati;atha te svaM shira Ahratya tatte pratidhAsyAva iti /

tatheti tau hopaninye /
tau yadopaninye, athAsya shiracchittvAnyatropanidadhutuH;athAshvasya shira Ahratya tadvAsya pratidadhatuH /
tena hAbhyAmanuvAca /
sa yadA AbhyAmanuvAcAthAsya tadindraH shirashciccheda /
athAsya svaM shira Ahratya tadvAsya pratidadhaturiti /

yAvattu pravargyakarmAN^gabhUtaM madhu tAvadeva tatrAbhihitam, na tu kakShyamAtmAj~nAnAkhyam /
tatra yA AkhyAyikAbhihitA seha stutyarthA pradarshyate /
idaM vai tanmadhu dadhyaÇÇAtharvaNo 'nena prapaJNcenAshvibhyAmuvAca /

tadetadR^ipiH-tadetat karma, shR^ipirmantraH, pashyannupalabhamAnaH, avocat-uttkavAn /
katham? taddaMsa iti vyavahitena sambandhaH /
daMsa iti karmaNo nAmadheyam /
tacca daMsaH kivishiShTam? ugraM krUram /
vAM yuvayoH /
he narA narAkArAvashvinau /
tacca karma kinnimitam? sanaye lAbhAya !lAmalubdho hi loke 'pi krUraM karmAcarati, tathaivaitAvupalabhyete yathA soke /

tadAviH prakAshaM kR^iNomi karomi yadrahasi bhavadbhayAM kR^itam, kimiva? ityucyate--tanyatuH parjanyaH, na iva /
nakArastUpariShTAdupacAra upamArthIyo vede, na pratipedhArthaH;yathAshvaM na /
ashvamiveti yadvat /
tanyaturiva vR^irShTi yathA parjanyo vR^irShTi prakAshayati stanayitnvAdishabdaiH, tadvadahaM yuvayoH krUraM karma AviShkR^iNomIti sambandhaH /
nanvashvinoH stutyarthau kathamimau mantrau syAtAM nindAvacanau hImau /

naipa doShaH;stutirevaiShA, na nindAvacanau /
yasmAdIdR^ishamapyatikrUraM karma kurvatoryuvayorna loma ca mIyata iti /
na cAnyatkiJNcidvIyata eveti /
stutAvetau bhavataH /
nindAM prashaMsAM hi laukikAH smaranti /
tathA prashaMsArUpA ca nindA loke prasidvA /

dadhyaÇnAma AtharvaNaH /
hetyanarthako nipAtaH /
yanmadhukakShyamAtmaj~nAnalakShaNamAthavaNo vAM yukAbhyAmashvasya shIrShNA shirasA prayat Im uvAca yat provAca madhu /
Imityanarthako nipAtaH //16//

START BrhUp 2,5.17



#<idaM vai tan madhu dadhyaÇÇ AtharvaNo 'shvibhyAm uvAca |

BrhUpBh_2,5.17

idaM vai tanmadhvityAdi pUrvavanmantrAntaradarshanArtham /
tathAnyo mantrastAmeva AkhyAyikAmanusaratisma /
AtharvaNo dadhyaÇnAma, AtharvaNo 'nyo vidyata ityato vishinaShTi dadhyaÇnAmAtharvaNaH /

tasmai dadhIca AtharvaNAya he 'shvinAviti mantradR^isho vacanam, ashvyama shvasya svabhUtaM shiraH, brAhmaNasya shirasicchinne 'shvasya shirashchittvedR^ishamatikrUraM karma kR^itvA ashvayaM shiro brAhmaNaM prati erayataM gamitavantau yuvAm /
sa cAtharvaNo vAM yuvAbhyAM tanmadhu pravocad yat pUrvaM pratij~nAtaM vakShyAmIti /

sa kimarthamevaM jIvitasandehamAruhya pravocat? ityucyate /
shR^itAyan yata pUrvaM pratij~nAtaM satyaM tat paripAlayitumicchan /
jIvitAdapi hi satyadharmaparipAlanA gurutaretyesya liN^gametat /

ki tanmadhu pravocat? ityucyate-tvAShTram, tvaShTA Adityastasya sambandhi, yaj~nasya shirashchinnaM tvaShTAbhavat,

tatpratisandhAnArtha pravargya karma /
tatra pravargyakarmAN^gabhUtaM yad vij~nAnaM tattvAShTraM madhu-yaj~nasya shirashchedanapratisandhAnAdiviShayaM darshanaM tattvAShTraM yanmadhu he dastro, dastrAviti parabalAnAmupakShapayitArau shatrUNAM vA

hiMsitArau, api ca na kevalaM tvAShTrameva madhu karmasambandhiyuvAbhyAmavocat, api ca kakShyaM gopyaM rahasyaM paramAtmasambandhi yad vij~nAnaM madhu madhubrAhmaNenottkamadhyAyadvayaprakAshitam, tacca vAM yuvAbhyAM pravocadityanuvartate //17//

START BrhUp 2,5.18



#<idaM vai tan madhu dadhyaÇÇ AtharvaNo 'shvibhyAm uvAca |

BrhUpBh_2,5.18

idaM vai tanmadhviti  pUrvavat /
uttkau dvau mantrau pravargyasambandhyAkhyAyikopasaMhartArau /
dvayoH pravargyakarmArthayoradhyAyayorartha AkhyAyikAbhUtAbhyAM mantrAbhyAM prakAshitaH /
brahmavidyArthayostvadhyAyayorarthauttarAbhyAmR^igbhyAM prakAshayitavyaH, ityataH pravartate /
yat kakShyaM ca madhuttkavAnAtharvaNo yuvAbhyAmityuttkam /
kiM punasdanmadhu? ityucyate-

purashcakre puraH purANi sharIrANi yata iyamacyAkR^itavyAkaraNaprakriyA sa parameshvaro nAmarUpe avyAkrate vyAkurvANaH prathamaM bhUrAdIM llokAn sR^iShTvA cakre kR^itavAna dvipado dvipAdapalakShitAni manuShyasharIrANi pakShisharIrANi /
tavA puraH sharIrANi cakre catuShpadashcatuShpAdupalakShitAni pashusharIrANi /

puraH purastAn sa IshvaraH pakShI liN^gasharIraM bhUtvA puraH sharIrANipuruSha AvishadityasyArthamAcaShTe shrutiH-sa vA ayaM puruShaH sarvAsuyUrShu sarvasharIreShu purishayaH, purisheta iti purishayaH san puruSha ityucyate /
nainenAnena ki¤acana kiJNcidapyanAvR^itamanAcchaditam /
tathA nainena kiJNcanAsaMvR^itamantarananupraveshitaM bAhyabhUtenAntarbhUtena ca na anAvR^itam /
evaM sa eva nAmakhyAtmanA antarvahirbhAvena  kAryakaraNarUpeNa vyavasthitaH /
purashcakre ityAdimantraH saN^kShepata AtmaikatvamAcaShTaityarthaH //18//

START BrhUp 2,5.19



#<idaM vai tan madhu dadhyaÇÇ AtharvaNo 'shvibhyAm uvAca |
tad etad R^iShiH pashyann avocat -- rUpaMrUpaM pratirUpo babhUva tad asya rUpaM praticakShaNAya |
indro mAyAbhiH pururUpa Iyate yuktA hy asya harayaH shatA dasheti |

BrhUpBh_2,5.19

idaM vai tanmadhvityAdi pUrvavat /
rUpaM rUpaM pratirUpo rUpAntaraM babhUvetyarthaH /
pratirUpo 'nurUpo vA yAdR^iksaMmathAnau mAtApitarau tatsaMsthAnastadanurUpa eva putro jAyate /
na hi catuShpado dvipAjjAyate dvipado vA catuShpAt /
sa eva hi parameshvaro nAmarUpe vyAkurvANo rUpaM rUpaM pratirUpo babhUva /

kimartha punaH pratirUpamAgamanaM tasya? ityucyate--tadasyAtmano rUpaM praticakShaNAya pratikhyApanAya /
yadi hi nAmarUpe na vyAkriyete, tadA asyAtmano nirUpAdhikaM rUpaM praj~nAnaghanAkhyaM na pratikhyAyeta /
yadA punaH kAryakaraNAtmanA nAmarUpe vyAka-te bhavataH, tadAsya rUpaM pratikhyAyeta /

indraH parameshvaro mAyAbhiH praj~nAbhiH nAmarUpabhUtakR^itamithyAbhimAnairvA, na tu paramArthataH; pururUpo bahurUpa Iyate gabhyate, ekarUpa eva praj~nAnaghanaH sannavidyApraj~nAbhiH /
kasmAt punaH kAraNAt? yuttkA ratha iva vAjinaH svavipayaprakAshanAya, hi yasmAndasya harayo haraNAdindriyANi, shatA shatAni, dasha ca prANibhedabAhulyAcchatAna dasha ca bhavanti /
tasmAdindriyavipayabAhulyAttatprakAshanAyeva ca yuttkAna tAni na AtmaprakAshanAya /
"parAJNci khAni vyatR^iNat svayambhUH"iti hi kAThake /
tasmAtaireva vipayasvarUpairIyate na praj~nAnaghanaikarasena svarUpeNa /

evaM tahi ayamanyaH parameshvaro 'nye haraya ityevaM prApte ucyate-ayaM vai harayo 'yaM vai dasha ca sahasrANi bahUni cAnantAni ca prANibhedasyAnantyAt /
kiM bahunA, tadetadbrahma ya AtmA /
apUrvaM nAsya kAraNaM pUrva vidyata ityapUrvam /
nAsyAparaM kAryaM vidyata ityanaparam /
nAsya jAtyantaramantarAle vidyata ityanaltaram /
tathA bahirasya na vidyata ityavAhyam /
kiM punastannirantaraM brahma? ayamAtmanA /
ko 'sau? yaH pratyagAtmA draShTA shrotA mantA bodvA vij~nAtA sarvAnubhUH, sarvAtmanA sarvamanubhavatIti sarvamanubhUH /
ityetadanushAsanaM sarvavedAntopadeshaH /
eSha sarvavedAntAnAmupasaMhrator'thaH /
etadamR^itamabhayam /
parisamAptashca shAstrArthaH //19 //

#<ghR^itakaushikAt |
ghR^itakaushikaH prAsharyAyaNAt |
pArasharyAyaNaH pArAsharyAt |
pArAsharyo jAtUkarNyAt |
jAtUkarNya AsurAyaNAc ca yAskAc ca |
AsurAyaNas traivaNeH |
traivaNir aupajandhaneH |
aupajandhanir AsureH |
Asurir bhAradvAjAt |
bhAradvAja AtreyAt |
Atreyo mANTeH |
mANTir gautamAt |
gautamo vAtsyAt |
vAtsyaH shANDilyAt |
shANDilyaH kaishoryAt kApyAt |
kaishoryaH kApyaH kumArahAritAt |
kumArahArito gAlavAt |
gAlavo vidarbhIkauNDinyAt |
vidarbhIkauNDinyo vatsanapAto bAbhravAt |
vatsanapAd bAbhravaH pathaH saubharAt |
panthAH saubharo 'yAsyAd AN^girasAt |
ayAsya AN^girasa AbhUtes tvAShTrAt |
AbhUtis tvAShTro vishvarUpAt tvAShTrAt |
vishvarUpas tvAShTro 'vshibhyAm |
ashvinau dadhIca AtharvaNAt |
dadhyaÇÇ AtharvaNo 'tharvaNo daivAt |
atharvA daivo mR^ityoH prAdhvaMsanAt |
mR^ityuH prAdhvaMsanaH pradhvaMsanAt |
pradhvaMsana ekarSheH |
ekarShir vipracitteH |
vipracittir vyaShTer |
vyaShTiH sanAroH |
sanAruH sanAtanAt |
sanAtanaH sanagAt |
sanagaH parameShThinaH |
parameShThI brahmaNaH |
brahma svayaMbhu |
brahmaNe namaH || BrhUp_2,6.3 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_2,6.3

ayedAnIM brahmavidyArthasya madhukANDasya vaMshaH stutyartho brahmavidyAyAH /
mantrashcAyaM svAdhyAyArtho japArthashca /
tatra vaMsha iva vaMshaH yathA veNurvaMshaH parvaNaH parvaNo hi bhidyate tadvadagratprabhR^iti AmUlaprApterayaM vaMshaH /
adhyAyacatuShTayasya AcAryaparamparAkramo vaMsha ityucyate /
tatra prathamAntaH shiShyaH paJNcamayantaH AcAryaH /
parameShThI virAT, brAhmaNo hiraNyagarbhAt /
tataH paramAcAryaparamparAnAsti /
yatpunarbrahma tannityaM svayambhU, tasmai brahmaNai svayambhuve namaH //1-3//


#<iti ShaShThaM brAhmaNam >#//

ADHYAYA 3


janako ha vaideha ityAdi yAj~navalkoyaM kANDamArabhyate /
upapattipradhAnatvAdatikrAntena madhukANDena samAnArthatve 'pi sati na punaruktatA /
madhukANDaM hyAgemapradhAnam /
AgamopapattI hyAtmaikatvaprakAshanAya pravR^itte shaknutaH karatalagatabilvamiva darshayitum /
shrotavyo mantavya iti hyuktam /
tasmAdAgamArthasyaiva parIkShApUrvakaM nirdhAraNAya yAj~navalkIyaM kANDamupapattipradhAnamArabhyate /
AkhyAyikA tu vij~nAnastutyarthopAyavidhiparA vA /
prasiddho hyupAyo vidvadbhiH shAstreShu ca dR^iShTo dAnam /
dAnena hR^iyupanamante prANinaH /
prabhUtaM hiraNyaM gosahasradAnaM cehopalabhyate /
tasmAdanyapareNApi shAstreNa vidyAprAptyupAyadAnapradarshanArthA'khyAyikA'rabdhA /
api ca tadvidyasaMyogastaishva saha vAdakaraNaM vidyAprAptyupAyo nyAyavidyAyAM dR^iShTaH /
taccAsminnadyAye prAbalyena pradarshyate /
pratyakShA ca vidvatsaMyoge praj~nAvR^iddhiH /
tasmAdvidyAprAptyupAyapradarshanArthaivAkhyAyikA /

START BrhUp 3,1.1

#<janako ha vaideho bahudakShiNena yaj~neneje |
tatra ha kurupaJNcAlAnAM brAhmaNA abhisametA babhUvuH |
tasya ha janakasya vaidehasya vijij~nAsA babhUva -- kaH svid eShAM brAhmaNAnAm anUcAnatama iti |
sa ha gavAM sahasram avarurodha |
dashadasha pAdA ekaikasyAH shR^iN^gayor AbaddhA babhUvuH || BrhUp_3,1.1 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,1.1 janako nAma ha kila samrADrAjA babhUva videhAnAM tatra bhavo vaidehaH /
sa ca bahudakShiNena yaj~nena shAkhAntaraprasiddho vA bahudakShiNo nAma yaj~no 'shvamedho vA dakShiNAbAhulyAdbahudakShiNa ihocyate teneje 'yajat /
tatra tasminyaj~ne nimantritA darshanakAmA vA kurUNAM deshAnAM paJNcAlAnAM ca brAhmaNAsteShu hi viduShAM bAhulyaM prasiddhamabhisametA abhisaMgatA babhUvuH /
tatra mahAntaM vidvatsamudAyaM dR^iShTvA tasya ha kila janakasya vaidehasya yajamAnasya ko nu khalvatra brahmiShTha iti visheSheNa j~nAtumicchA vijij~nAsA babhUva /
kathaM, kaHsvitko nu khalveShAM brAhmaNAnAmanUcAnatamaH sarva ime 'nUcAnAH kaHsvideShAmatishayenAnUcAna iti /
sa hAnUcAnatamaviShayotpannijij~nAsaH saMstadvij~nAnopAyArthaM gavAM sahasraM prathamavayasAmavarurodha goShThe 'varodhaM kArayAmAsa /
kiMvishiShTAstA gAvo 'varuddhA ityucyate /
palacaturthabhAgaH pAdaH suvarNasya /
dasha dasha pAdA ekaikasyA goH shR^iN^gayorAbaddhA babhUvuH /
paJNca paJNca pAdA ekaikasmi¤shR^iN^ge //1//


_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 3,1.2

#<tAn hovAca -- brAhmaNA bhagavanto yo vo brahmiShThaH sa etA gA udajatAm iti |
te ha brAhmaNA na dadhR^iShuH |
atha ha yAj~navalkyaH svam eva brahmacAriNam uvAca -- etAH saumyodaja sAmashravA3 iti |
tA hodAcakAra |
te ha brAhmaNAsh cukrudhuH: -- kathaM nu no brahmiShTho bruvIteti |
atha ha janakasya vaidehasya hotAshvalo babhUva |
sa hainaM papraccha -- tvaM nu khalu no yAj~navalkya brahmiShTho 'sI3 iti |
sa hovAca -- namo vayaM brahmiShThAya kurmo gokAmA eva vayaM sma iti |
taM ha tata eva praShTuM dadhre hotAshvalaH || BrhUp_3,1.2 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,1.2 gA evamavarudhya brAhmaNAMstAnhovAca /
he brAhmaNA bhagavanta ityAmantratha yo vo yuShmAkaM brahmiShThaH sarve yUyaM brahmANo 'tishayena yuShmAkaM brahmA yaH sa etA gA udajatAmutkAlayatu svagR^ihaM prati /
te ha brAhmaNA na dadhR^iShuH ha kilaivamuktA brAhmaNA brahmiShThatAmAtmanaH pratij~nAtuM na dadhR^ipurna pragalbhAH saMvR^ittAH /
apragalbhabhUteShu brAhmaNeShvatha ha yAj~navalkyaH svamAtmIyameva brahmacAriNamantevAsinamuvAca- etA gA he somyodajodgamayAsmadgR^ihAn prati, he sAmashravaH- sAmavidhiM hi shR^iNotyator'yAccaturvedo yAj~navalkyaH /
tA gA hodAcakArotkAlitavAnAcAryagR^ihaM prati /
yAj~navalkyena brahmiShThapaNasvIkaraNena Atmano brahmiShThatA pratij~nAtA, iti te ha cukrudhuH kruddhavanto brAhmaNAH /
teShAM krodhAbhiprAyamAcaShTe- kathaM no 'smAkaM ekaikapradhAnAnAM brahmiShTho 'smIti bruvIteti /
atha haivaM kruddheShu brAhmaNeShu janakasya yajamAnasya hotA R^itvigashvalo nAma babhUva AsIt /
sa enaM yAj~navalkyam, brahmiShThAbhimAnI rAjAshrayatvAccadhR^iShTaH, yAj~navalkyaM papraccha pR^iShTavAn /
katham? tvaM nu khalu no yAj~navalkya brahmiShTho 'sI 3 iti /
plutirbhartsanArthA /
sa hovAca yAj~navalkyaH- namaskarmo vayaM brahmiShThAya, idAnIM gokAmAH smo vayamiti /
taM brahmiShThapratij~naM  santaM tata eva brahmiShThapaNasvIkaraNAt praShTuM dadhre dhR^itavAn mano hotA ashvalaH //2//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 3,1.3

#<yAj~navalkyeti hovAca -- yad idaM sarvaM mR^ityunAptaM sarvaM mR^ityunAbhipannaM kena yajamAno mR^ityor Aptim atimucyata iti |
hotrartvijAgninA vAcA |
vAg vai yaj~nasya hotA |
tad yeyaM vAk so 'yam agniH sa hotA sA muktiH sAtimuktiH || BrhUp_3,1.3 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,1.3 yAj~navalkyeti hovAca /
tatra madhukANDe pADaktena karmaNA darshanasaptuccitena yajamAnasya mR^ityoratyayo vyAkhyAta udgIthaprakaraNe saN^kShepataH /
tasyaiva parIkShAviShayo 'yamititadgatadarshanavisheShArtho 'yaM vistara Arabhyate /
yadidaM sAdhanajAtam asya karmaNa R^itvigagnyAdi mR^ityunA karmalakShaNena svAbhAvikAsaN^gasahitena AptaM jyAptam, na kevalaM vyAptamabhiShannaM ca mR^ityunA bashIkR^itaM ca /
kena darshanalakShaNena sAdhanena yajamAno mR^ityorAptimati mR^ityugacaratvam atikramya mucyate svatantro mR^ityoravasho bhavatItyarthaH /
nanUdgItha evAbhihitaM yenAtimucyatemukhyaprANAtmadarshaneneti /
bADhamuktam, yo 'nukto visheShastatra, tadartho 'yamArambha ityadoShaH /
hotrartvijAgninA vAcetyAha yAj~navalkyaH /
etasyArthaMvyAcaShTe /
kaH punarhetA yena mR^ityumatikAmati? ityucyate-vAgvai yaj~nasya yajamAnasya"yaj~no vai yajamAnaH"iti shruteH /
yaj~nasya yajamAnasya yAvAksaiva hotAdhiyaj~ne /
katham? tatatrayeyaMvanga yaj~nasyayajamAnasya so 'yaM prasiddho 'gniradhidaivatam /
tadetatvyannaprakaraNevyAkhyAtam /
sa cAgnirhetA"agnirvai hotA"iti shruteH /
yadetad yaj~nasya sAdhanadvayamhotA catviN^g adhiyaj~nam, adhyAtmaM ca vAk etadubhayaM sAdhanadvayaM paricchinnaM mR^ityunA AptaM svAbhAvikAj~nAnAsaN^gaprayuktena karmaNA mR^ityunA pratikShaNamanyathAtvamApadyamAnaM vashIkR^itam /
tad anenAdhidaivatarUpeNAgninA'dR^ishyamAnaM'yajamAnasya yaj~nasya sR^ityoratimuktaye bhavati /
tadetadAha-sa muktiH sa hotA agnirmuktiH, agnisvarUpadarshanameva muktiH /
yadaiva sAdhanadvayamagnirUpeNa gashyati, tadAnImeva hi svAbhAvikAdAsaN^gAnmR^ityorvimucyate AdhyAtmikAt paricchinnarUpAdAdhibhautikAcca /
tasmAt sa hotA agnirUpeNa dR^iShTo muktirmuktisAdhanaM yajamAnasya /
sA atimuktiH-yaiva ca muktiH sAtimuktiH, atimuktisAdhanamityarthaH /
sAdhanadvayasya paricchinnasya yA adhidevatArUpeNAparicchinnenAgnirUpeNa dR^iShTiH, sA muktiH /
yAsau muktiradhidevatAdR^iShTiH saiva, adhyAtmAdhibhUtaparicchedaviShayAsaN^gAspadaM mR^ityumatikramya adhidevatAtvasyAgnibhAvasya prAptiryA phalabhUtA, sA atimuktirityucyate /
tasyA atimuktermuktireva sAdhanamiti kR^itvA sA atimuktirityAha /
yajamAnasya hyatimuktirvAgAdInAmagnyAdibhAva ityudgIthaprakaraNe vyAkhyAtam /
tatra sAmAnyena mukhyaprANadarshanamAtraM muktisAdhanamuktam, na tadvisheShaH /
vAgAdInAm agnyAdidarshanamiha visheSho varNyate /
mR^ityuprAptyatimuktistu saiva phalabhUtA, yodgIthabrAhmaNena vyAkhyAtA -'mR^ityupratikrAnto dIpyate'(1 / 3 / 12) ityAdyA //3//

START BrhUp 3,1.4

#<yAj~navalkyeti hovAca -- yad idaM sarvam ahorAtrAbhyAm AptaM sarvam ahorAtrAbhyAm abhipannaM kena yajamAno 'horAtrayor Aptim atimucyata iti |
adhvaryuNartvijA cakShuShAdityena |
cakShur vai yaj~nasyAdhvaryuH |
tad yad idaM cakShuH so 'sAv AdityaH |
so 'dhvaryuH sA muktiH sAtimuktiH || BrhUp_3,1.4 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,1.4 yAj~navalkyeti hovAca /
svAbhAvikAdaj~nAnAsaN^gaprayuktAt karmalakShaNAnmR^ityoratimuktirvyAkhyAtA /
tasya karmaNaH sAsaN^gasya mR^ityorAshrayabhUtAnAM darshapUrNamAsAdikarmasAdhanAnAM yo vipariNAmahetuH kAlaH, tasmAt kAlAt pR^ithagatinuShThAnavyatirekeNApi prAgUrdhvaM ca kriyAyAH sAdhanavipariNAmahetutvena vyApAradarshanAt kAlasya /
tasmAt pR^ithakkAlAdatimuktirvaktavyetyata Aha- yadidaM sarvamahorAtrAbhyAmAptam, sa ca kAlo dvirUpaH - ahorAtrAdilakShaNAH, tithyAdilakShaNashca /
tatrAhorAtrAdilakShaNAttAvadatimuktimAha - ahorAtrAbhyAM hi sarvaM jAyate vardhate vinashyati ca, tathA yaj~nasAdhanaM ca /
yaj~nasya yajamAnasya cakShuradhvaryushca /
shiShTAnyakSharANi pUrvavanneyAni /
yajamAnasya cakShuradhvaryushca sAdhanadvayamadhyAtmAdhibhUtaparicchedaM hitvA adhidaivatAtmanA dR^iShTaM yat sa muktiH so 'dhvaryurAdityabhAvena dR^iShTo muktiH /
saiva muktirevAtimuktiriti /
pUrvavat AdityAtmabhAvamApannasya hi nAhorAtre sambhavataH //4//

idAnIM tithyAdilakShaNAdatimuktirucyate- 



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 3,1.5

#<yAj~navalkyeti hovAca -- yad idaM sarvaM pUrvapakShAparapakShAbhyAm AptaM sarvaM pUrvapakShAparapakShAbhyAm abhipannaM kena yajamAnaH pUrvapakShAparapakShayor Aptim atimucyata iti |
udgAtrartvijA vayunA prANena |
prANo vai yaj~nasyodgAtA |
tad yo 'yaM prANaH sa vAyuH sa udgAtA |
sa muktiH sAtimuktiH || BrhUp_3,1.5 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,1.5 idAnIM tithyAdilakShaNAdatimuktirUcyate-yadidaM sarvam - ahorAtrayoravishiShTayorAdityaH kartA, na prati padAdInAM tithInAm;tAsAM tu vR^iddhikShayopagamanenapratipatprabhR^itInAM candramAH kartA /
atastadApAcyA pUrvapakShAparapakShAtyayaH, AdityApacyA ahorAtrAtyayavat /
tatra yajamAnasya prANo vAyuH, sa evaudgAtA - ityudgIthabrAhmaNe 'vagatam'vAcA ca hyeva sa prANena codagAyat'iti ca nirdhAritam /
'athaitasya prANasyApaH sharIraM jyotIrUpamasau candraH'iti ca /
prANAvAyucandramasAmekatvAccandramasA vAyunA copasaMhAre na kashcid visheShaH /
evaM manyamAnA shrutirvAyunA adhidaivatarUpeNopasaMharati /
api ca vAyunimittau hi vR^iddhikShayau candramasaH /
tena tithyAdilakShaNasya kAlasya karturapi kArayitA vAyuH /
ato vAyurUpApannastithyAdikAlAdatIto bhavatItyupapannataraM bhavati /
tena shrutyantare candrarUpeNa dR^iShTirmuktiratimuktishca /
iha tu kANvAnAM sAdhanadvayasya tatkAraNarUpeNa vAyvAtmanA dR^iShTirmuktiratimuktishceti na shrutyorvirodhaH //5//

START BrhUp 3,1.6

#<yAj~navalkyeti hovAca -- yad idam antarikSham anArambaNam iva kenAkrameNa yajamAnaH svargaM lokam Akramata iti |
brahmaNartvijA manasA candreNa |
mano vai yaj~nasya brahmA |
tad yad idaM manaH so 'sau candraH sa brahmA sa muktiH sAtimuktir ity atimokShA |
atha saMpadaH || BrhUp_3,1.6 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,1.6 mR^ityoH kAlAdatimuktirvyAkhyAtA yajamAnasya /
so 'timucyamAnaH kenAvaShTambhena paricchedaviShayaM mR^ityumatotya phalaM prApnotyatimucyata ityucyate /
yadidaM prasiddhamantarikShamAkAsho 'nArambaNamanAlambanamivashabdAdastyeva tatrA'lambanaM tattu na j~nAyata ityabhiprAyaH /
yattu tadaj~nAyamAnamAlambanaM tatsarvanAmnA keneti pR^icchyate /
anyathA phalaprApterasaMbhavAt /
yenAvaShTambhenA'krameNa yajamAnaH karmaphalaM pratipadyamAno 'timucyate kiM taditi prashnaviShaya /
kenA'krameNa yajamAnaH svargaM lokamAkramata iti svargaM lokaM phalaM prApnotyatimucyata ityarthaH /
brahmaNartvijA manasA candreNetyakSharanyAsaH pUrvavat /
tatrAdhyAtmaM yaj~nasya yajamAnasya yadidaM prasiddhaM manaH so 'sau candro 'dhidaivatam /
mano 'dhyAtmaM candramA adhidaivatamiti hi prasiddham /
sa eva candramA brahmartviktenAdhibhUtaM brAhmaNaH paricchinnaM rUpamadhyAtmaM ca manasa etaddvayamaparicchinnena candramaso rUpeNa pashyati /
tena candramasA manasAvalambanena karmaphalaM svargaM lokaM prApnotyatimucyata ityabhiprAyaH /
itItyupasaMhArAthaM vacanam /
ityevaMprakArA mR^ityoratimokShAH /
sarvAMNi hi darshanaprakArANi yaj~nAN^gaviShayANyasminnavasara uktAnIti kR^itvopasaMhAra ityatimokShAH /
evaMprakArA atimokShA ityarthaH /
atha saMpadaH /
athAdhunA saMpada ucyante /
saMpannAma kenacitsAmAnyenAgnihotrAdInAM karmaNAM mahatAM phalavatAM tatphalAya saMpAdanaM saMpat /
phalasyaiva vA sarvotsAhena phalasAdhanAnuShThAne prayatatAM kenacidvaiguNyenAsaMbhavaH /
tadidAnImAhitAgniH sanyatkiJNcitkarmAgnihotrAdInAM yathAsaMbhavamAdAyA'lambanIkR^itya karmaphalavidvattAyAM satyAM yatkarmaphalakAmo bhavati tadeva saMpAdayati /
anyathA rAjasUyAshvamedhapuruShamedhasarvamedhalakShaNAnAmadhikR^itAnAM traivarNikAnAmapyasaMbhavasteShAM tatpAThaH svAdhyAyArtha eva kevalaH syAt /
yadi tatphalaprAptyupAyaH kashcana na syAt /
tasmAtteShAM sepadaiva tatphalaprAptistasmAtsaMpadAmapi phalavattvamataH saMpada Arabhyante //6//
