START BrhUp 3,1.7

#<yAj~navalkyeti hovAca -- katibhir ayam adyargbhir hotAsmin yaj~ne kariShyatIti |
tisR^ibhir iti |
katamAs tAs tisra iti |
puronuvAkyA ca yAjyA ca shasyaiva tR^itIyA |
kiM tAbhir jayatIti |
yat kiJNcedaM prANabhR^id iti || BrhUp_3,1.7 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,1.7 yAj~navalkyeti hovAca abhimukhIkaraNAya /
katibhirayamadyargbhirhetAsmin yaj~ne katibhiH katisaN^khyAbhirR^igbhirR^igjAtibhiH ayaMhotartvigasmin yaj~ne kariShyati shastraM shaMsati /
AhetaraH-tisR^ibhirR^igjAtibhiH /
ityukkavantaM pratyA hetaraH-katamAstAstistra iti /
saN^khyeyaviShayo 'yaM prashnaH, pUrvastu saN^khyAviShayaH /
puronuvAkyAca-prAgyAgaphAlAd yAH prayujyante R^icaH, sA R^igjAtiH puronuvAkyetyucyate /
yAgArthaM yAH prayujyante R^icaH, sA R^igjAtiryAjyA /
shastrArthaM yAH prayujyante R^icaH, sA R^igjAtiH shasyA /
sarvAstu yAH kAshcana R^icaH;tAH stotriyA vA anyA vA sarvA etAsveva tisR^iShu R^igjAtiShvantarbhavanti /
kiM tAbhirjayatIti yatkiJNcedaM prANabhR^iditi-atashcasaN^khyAsAmAnyAd yatkiJNcitprANabhR^ijjAtama, tat sarvaM jayati tat sarvaM phalajAtaM sampAdayati saN^khyAdisAmAnyena //7//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 3,1.8

#<yAj~navalkyeti hovAca -- katy ayam adyAdhvaryur asmin yaj~na AhutIr hoShyatIti |
tisra iti |
katamAs tAs tisra iti |
yA hutA ujjvalanti yA hutA atinedanti yA hutA adhisherate |
kiM tAbhir jayatIti |
yA hutA ujjvalanti devalokam eva tAbhir jayati |
dIpyata iva hi devaloko |
yA hutA atinedante pitR^ilokam eva tAbhir jayati |
atIva hi pitR^ilokaH |
yA hutA adhisherate manuShyalokam eva tAbhir jayatyi |
adha iva hi manuShyalokaH || BrhUp_3,1.8 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,1.8 yAj~navalkyeti hovAveti pUrvavat /
katyayamadyAdhvaryurasmin yaj~na AhutIrheShyatIti, katyAhutiprakArAH? tastra iti, katamAstAstistra iti pUrvavat /
itara Aha-yA hUtA ujjvalanti samidAjyAhutayaH yA hutA atinedante 'tIva shabdaM kuvanti mAsAdyAhutayaH, yA hutA adhisherate 'dhyAdho gatvA bhUmeradhisherate payaHsomAhutayaH /
kiM tAbhirjayatIti, tAbhirevaM nirvartitAbhirAhutibhiH kiM jayatIti /
yA Ahutayo hutA ujjvalantyujjvalanayuktA Ahutayo nirvartitAH, phalaM ca devalokAkhyamujjvalameva, tena sAmAnyena yA mayatA ujjvalantya Ahutayo nirvartyamAnAstA etAH sAkShAddevalokasya karmaphalasyarUpaM devalokAkhyaM phalameva mayA nirvartyata ityevaM sampAdayati /
yA hutA atinedante AhutayaH pitR^ilokameva tAbhirjayati kutsitashabdakartR^itvasAmAnyena /
pitR^ilokameva tAbhirjayati kutsitashabdakartR^itvasAmAnyena /
pitR^ilokasambaddhAyAM hi saMyamanyAM puryAM vaivasvatena yAtyamAnAnAM'hA hatAH sma muJNca muJNca'iti shabdobhavati /
tathAvadAnAhutayaH tena pitR^ilokasAmAnyAt pitR^iloka eva mayA nirvartyata iti sampAdayati /
yA hutA adhisherate manuShyalokameva tAmijayati bhUmyupari sambandhasAmAnyAt /
adha iva hyagha eva hi manuShyalokaH uparitanAn sAdhyAMllokAnapekShya, athavAdhogamanamapekShya /
ato manuShyaloka eva mayA nirvartyata iti sampAdayati /
yA hutA adhisherate manuShyalokameva tAbhijayati bhUmyupari sambandhasAmAnyAt /
adha iva hyadha eva hi manuShyalokaH uparitanAn sAdhyAMllokAnapekShya, athavAdhogamanamapekShya /
ato manuShyaloka eva mayA nirvartyata iti sampAdayati payaHsomAhutinirvartanakAle //8//

START BrhUp 3,1.9

#<yAj~navalkyeti hovAca -- katibhir ayam adya brahmA yaj~naM dakShiNato devatAbhir gopAyatIti |

BrhUpBh_3,1.9 yAj~navalkyeti hovAceti pUrvavat /
ayamR^itvigbrahmA dakShiNato brahmAsane sthitvA yaj~naM gopAyati /

evaM j~nAte bahuvacanena prashno nopapadyate svayaM jAnatastasmAtpUrvayoH kaNDikayoH prashnaprativacaneShu katibhiH kati tisR^ibhististra iti prasaN^gaM dR^iShTvehApi bahuvacanenaiva prashnopakramaH kriyate /

itara AhaikayetyekA sA devatA yayA dakShiNataH sthitvA brahmA'sane yaj~naM gopAyati /

manasA hi brahmA vyApriyate dhyAnenaiva /

tena mana eva devatA tayA manasA hi gopAyati brahmA yaj~nam /
tacca mano vR^ittibhedenAnantam /
vaishabdaH prasiddhAvadyotanArthaH /
prasiddhaM manasa  Anantyma /
tadAnantyAbhimAnino devAH,"sarve devA yatraikaM bhavanti"ityAdishrutyantarAt /
tenAnantyasAmAnyAdanantameva sa tena lokaM jayati //9//

START BrhUp 3,1.10

#<yAj~navalkyeti hovAca -- katy ayam adyodgAtAsmin yaj~ne stotriyAH stoShyatIti |
tisra iti |

puronuvAkyA ca yAjyA ca shasyaiva tR^itIyA |

BrhUpBh_3,1.10 yAj~navalkyeti hovAceti pUrvavat /
kati stotriyAH stopyatItyayamudgAtA /
stotriyA nAma R^iksAmasamudAyaH katipayAnAmR^icAm /
stotriyAvAshamyAvAyAH kAshcana R^icaH, tA sarvAstistra evetyAha /
tAshca vyAkhyAtAH- muronuvAkyA ca yAjyA ca shasyaiva tR^itIyeti /
tatra pUrvamuktam - yatkiJNcedaM prANabhR^ita sarve jayatIti tat kena sAmAnyena? ityucyate - katamAstAstistra R^ico yA adhyAtmaM bhavantIti /
prANa eva puronuvAkyA, pashabdasAmAnyAt /
avAno yAjyA, AnantaryAt /

kiM tAbhirjayatIti vyAkhyAtam /

tato ha tasmAdAtmanaH prashnanirNayAdasau hotA ashvala upararAma nAyamasmadgecara iti //10//

#<iti tR^itIyAdhyAye prathamamashvalabrAhmaNam //1//>#


AkhyAyikAsambandhaH prasiddha eva /
mR^ityoratimuktirvyAkhyAtA kAlalakShaNAt karmalakShaNAcca /
kaH punarasau mR^ityuryasmAdatimuktirvyAkhyAtA? sa ca svAbhAvikAj~nAnAsaN^gAspado 'dhyAtmAdhibhUtAviShayaparicchinno grahAtigrahalakShaNo mR^ityuH /
tasmAt paricchinnarUpAnmR^ityoratimuktasya rUpANyaganyAdityAdInyudgIthaprakaraNe vyAkhyAtAni /
ashvalaprashnecatadgato visheShaH kashcit /
taccaitat karmaNAM j~nAnasahitAnAM phalam /
etasmAt sAdhyasAdhanarUpAt saMsArAnmokShaH kartavya ityatobandhanarUpasyamR^ityoH svarUpamucyate /
baddhasya hi mokShaH kartavyaH /
yadapyatimuktasya svarUpamuktaM tatrApi grahAtigrahAbhyAmavinirmukta eva mR^ityurUpAbhyAm /
tathA coktaM"ashanAyAhimR^ityuH"(bR^i.u.1 / 2 / 1) "eSha eva mR^ityuH"iti /
AdityasthaM puruShamaN^gIkR^ityAha"eko mR^ityurvahavA"iti ca /
tadAtmabhAvApanno hi mR^ityorAptimatimucyata ityucyate /
na ca tatra grahAtigrahau mR^ityurUpau nastaH /
"athaitasya manaso dyauH sharIraM jyotIrUpamasAvAdityaH"(bR^i. u. 1 / 5 / 12) 'manashva'grahaH sa kAmenAtigrAheNa gR^ihItaH"(3 / 2 / 7) iti, vakShyati"prANo vai grahaH so 'pAnenAtigrAheNa"(3 / 2 / 2) iti,"vAgvai grahaH sa nAmnAtigrAheNa"(3 / 2 / 3) iti ca /
tathA vyannavibhAge vyAkhyAtamasmAbhiH /
suvicAritaM caitad yadeva pravR^ittikAraNaM tadeva nivR^ittikAraNaM na bhavatIti /
kecittu sarvameva nivR^ittikAraNaM manyante /
ataH kAgNAt pUrvasmAtpUrvasmAnmR^ityormucyate uttaramuttaraM pratipadyamAno vyAvR^ittyarthameva prati padyate na tu tAdarthyam, ityata A dvaitakShayAta sarvaM mR^ityuH, dvainakShaye tu paramArthatA mR^ityorAptimatimucyate /
atashca ApekShikI gauNI muktirantarAle /
sarvametad evat abArhadAraNyakam /
nanu sarvaikatvaM mokShaH"tasmAttatsarvamabhavat"(bR^i. u. 1 / 4 / 10) iti shruteH /
bADhaM bhavatyetadapi, natu"grAmakAmo yajeta, pashukAmo yajeta"ityAdishrutInAM tAdarthyam /
yadi hyadvaitArthatvameva AsAM grAmapashusvargAdyarthatvaM nAstIti grAmapashusvargAdayo na gR^ihyeran, gR^ihyante tu karmaphalavaicitryavisheShAH /
yadi ca vaidikAnAM karmaNAM tAdarthyameva, saMsAra eva nAbhaviShyat /
atha tAdarthye 'pi anuniShpAditapadArthasvabhAvaH saMsAra iti cet /
yathA ca rUpadarshanArtha Aloke sarvo 'pi tatrasthaH prakAshyata eva /
na;pramANAnupapatteH /
advaitArthatve vaidikAnAM karmaNAM vidyAsahitAnAm anyaspAnuniShpAditatve pramANAnupapattiH /
na pratyakShaM nAnumAnamata eva ca nAgamaH /
ubhayam ekena vAkyena pradarshyata iti cet kulyApraNayanAlokAdivat /
tannevam;vAkyadharmAnupapatteH /
na ca ekavAkyagatasyArthasya pravR^ittinivR^ittisAdhanatvamavagantuM shakyate /
kulyApraNayanAlokAdAvarthasya pratyakShatvAdadoShaH /
yadapyucyate mantrA asminnartheH dR^iShTA iti /
ayameva tu tAvadarthaH pramANAgamyaH /
mantrAH punaH kim asminnartha Ahosvidanyasminnartha iti mR^igyametat /
tasmAd grahAtiprahalakShaNo mR^ityurbandhaH, tasmAnbhokSho vaktavya ityata idamArabhyate na ca jAnImo viShayasandhAvivAntarAle 'vasthAnamardhajaratIyaM kaushalam /
yattu mR^ityoratimucyata ityukatvA grahAtigrahAvucyete, tacvarthasambandhAt /
sarvo 'yaM sAdhyasAdhanalakShaNo bandhaH, grahAtigrahAvinirmokAt /
nigaDe hi nirj~nAte nigaDitasya mokShAya yatnaH kartavyo bhavati;tasmAtAdarthyenArambhaH /

BrhUpBh_3,2.10 upasaMhR^iteShu grahAtigraheShvAha punaH - yAj~navalkyeti hovAca /

START BrhUp 3,2.13

#<yAj~navalkyeti hovAca -- yatrAsya puruShasya mR^itasyAgniM vAg apyeti vAtaM prANash cakShur AdityaM manash candraM dishaH shrotraM pR^ithivIM sharIram AkAsham AtmauShadhIr lomAni vanaspatIn keshA apsu lohitaM ca retash ca nidhIyate kvAyaM tadA puruSho bhavatIti |

BrhUpBh_3,2.13 grahAtigraharUpaM bandhanamuktaM mR^ityurUpaM tasya ca mR^ityormR^ityusadbhAvAnmokShashcopapadyate /
sa ca mokSho grahAtigraharUpANAmihaiva pralayaH pradIpanirvANavat /
yadvadgrahAtigrahAkhyaM bandhanaM mR^ityurUpaM tasya yatprayojakaM tatsvarUpanirdhAraNArthamidamArabhyate /

atra kecidvarNayanti grahAtigrahasya saprayojakasya vinAshe 'pi kila na mucyate /
nAmAvashiShTo 'vidyayoSharasthAnIyayA svAtmaprabhavayA pa mAtmanaH paricchinno bhojyAcca jagato vyAvR^itta ucchinna kAmakarmAntarAle vyavatiShThate /
tasya paramAtmaikatvadarshane dvaitadarshanamapanetavyamityataH paraM paramAtmadarshanamArabdhavyamityevamapavargAkhyAmantarAlAvasthAM parikalyottaragranthasaMbandhaM kurvanti /
tatra vaktavyaM vishIrNeShu karaNeShu videhasya paramAtmadarshanashravaNamanananididhyAsanAni kathamiti /
samavanItaprANasya hi nAmamAtrAvashiShTasyeti tairucyate /
mR^itaH sheta iti hayuktam /
na manorathenApyetadupapAdayituM shakyate /
atha jIvannevAvidyAmAtrAvashiShTo bhojyAdapAvR^itta iti parikalpyate tattu kiMnimittamiti vaktavyam /
samastadvaitaikatvAtmaprAptinimittamiti yadyucyate tatpUrvameva nirAkR^itam /
karmasahitena dvaitaikatvAtmadarshanena sampanno vidvAnmR^itaH samavanItaprANo jagadAtmatvaM hiraNyagarbhasvarUpaM vA prApnuyAdasamavanItaprANo bhojyAjjIvanneva vyAvR^itto viraktaH paramAtmadarshanAbhimukhaH syAt /
na cobhayamekaprayatnaniShpAdyena sAdhanena labhyam /
hiraNyagarbhaprAptisAdhanaM cenna tato vyAvR^ittisAdhanam /
paramAtmAbhimukhIkaraNasya bhojyAdvayAvR^itteH sAdhanaM cenna hiraNyagarbhaprAptisAdhanam /
na hi yadgatisAdhanaM tadgatinivR^itterapi /
atha mR^itvA hiraNyagarbhaM prApya tataH samavanItaprANo nAmAvashiShTaH paramAtmaj~nAne 'dhikriyate /
tato 'smadAdyarthaM paramAtmaj~nAnopadesho 'narthakaH syAt /
sarveShAM hi brahmavidyA puruShArthAyopadishyate"tadyo yo devAnAm"ityAdyayA shrutyA /
tasmAdatyantanikR^iShTA shAstrabAhyaiveyaM kalpanA /
prakR^itaM tu vartayiShyAma /
tatra kena prayuktaM grahAtigrahalakShaNaM bandhanamityetannirdidhArayiShayA'ha-yatrAsya puruShasyAsamyagdarshinaH shiraHpANyAdimato mR^itasya vAgagnimapyeti vAtaM prANo 'pyeti cakShurAdityamapyetIti sarvatra sambadhyate /
manashcandraM dishaH shrotraM pR^ithivIM sharIramAkAshamAtmetyatrA'tmAdhiShThAnaM hR^idayAkAshamucyate /
sa AkAshamapyeti /
oShadhIrapiyati lomAni /
vanaspatInapiyanti keshAH /
apsu lohitaM ca retashca nidhIyata iti punarAdAnaliN^gam /
sarvatra hi vAgAdishabdena devatAH parigR^ihyante na tu karaNAnyevApakrAmanti prAÇmokShAt /
tatra devatAbhiranadhiShThitAni karaNAni nyastadAtrAdyupamAnAni videhashca kartA puruSho 'svatantraH kimAshrito bhavatIti pR^icchayate-kvAyaM tadA puruSho bhavatIti /
kimAshritastadA puruSho bhavatIti /
yamAshrayamAshritya punaH kAryakaraNasaMghAtamupAdatte yena grahAtigrahalakShaNaM bandhanaM prayujyate tatkimiti prashnaH /
atrocyate-svabhAvayadR^icchAkAlakarmadaivavij~nAnamAtrashUnyAni vAdibhiH parikalpitAni /
ato 'nekavipratipattisthAnatvAnnaiva jalpanyAyena vastunirNayaH /
atra vastunirNayaM cedicchasyAhara sobhya hastasArtabhAga ha AvAmevaitasya tvatpR^iShTasya veditavyaM yattadvediShyAvo nirUpayiShyAvaH /
kasmAt /
na nAvAvayoretadvastu sajane janasamudAye nirNetuM shakyate /
ata ekAnta gamiShyAvo vicAraNAya /
tau hetyAdi shrutivacanam /
tau yAj~navalkyArtabhAgAvekAntaM gatvA kiM cakraturityucyate-tau hotkramya sajanAddeshAnmantrayAJNcakrAte /
Adau laukikavAdipakShANAmekaikaM parugR^ihya vicAritavantau /
tau ha vicArya yadUcaturapohya pUrvapakShAnsarvAneva tacchR^iNu /
karma haivA'shrayaM punaH punaH kAryakaraNopAdAnahetuM tattatrocaturuktavantau /
na kevalaM kAlakarmadaiveshvareShvabhyupagateShu hetuShu yatprashashaMsatustau karma haiva tatprashashaMsatuH /
yasmAnnirdhAritametatkarmaprayuktaM grahAtigrahAdikAryakaraNopAdAnaM punaH punastasmAtpuNyo vai shAstravihitena puNyena karmaNA bhavati tadviparotena viparIto bhavati pApaH pApenetyevaM yAj~navalkyena prashneShu nirNIteShu tato 'shakyaprakampyatvAdyAj~navalkyasya ha jaratkArava ArtabhAga upararAma //13//

#<iti tR^itIyAdhyAye dvitIyamArtabhAgabrAhmaNam //2//>#

START BrhUp 3,3.1

#<atha hainaM bhujyur lAhyAyaniH papraccha -- yAj~navalkyeti hovAca -- madreShu carakAH paryavrajAma |
te pataJNcalasya kApyasya gR^ihAn aima |
tasyAsId duhitA gandharvagR^ihItA |
tam apR^icchAma ko 'sIti |
so 'bravIt sudhanvAN^girasa iti |
taM yadA lokAnAm antAn apR^icchAma |
athainam abrUma -- kva pArikShitA abhavann iti |
kva pArikShitA abhavan |
sa tvA pR^icchAmi yAj~navalkya |
kva pArikShitA abhavann iti || BrhUp_3,3.1 ||>#

BrhUpBh_3,3.1 atha hainaM bhujyurlAhyAyaniH papraccha /
grahAtigrahalakShaNaM bandhanamuktam /
yasmAtsaprayojakAnmukto mucyate yena vA baddhaH saMsarati sa mR^ityuH /
tasmAcca mokSha upapadyate /
yasmAnmR^iyormR^ityurasti /
muktasya ca na gatiH kvacit /
sarvotsAdo nAmamAtrAvasheShaH pradIpanirvANavaditi cAvadhR^itam /
tatra saMsaratAM mucyamAnAnAM ca kAryakaraNAnAM svakAraNasaMsarge samAne muktAnAmatyantameva punaranupAdAnam /
saMsaratAM tu punaH punarupAdAnaM yena prayuktAnAM bhavati tatkarmetyavadhAritaM vicAraNApUrvakam /
tatkShaye ca nAmAvasheSheNa sarvotsAdo mokShaH /
tacca puNyapApAkhyaM karma /
puNyo vai puNyena karmaNA bhavati pApaH pApenetyavadhAritatvAt /
etatkR^itaH saMsAraH /
tatrApuNyena sthAvarajaN^gameShu svabhAvaduHkhabahuleShu narakatiryakpretAdiShu ca duHkhamanubhavati punaH punarjAyamAno mriyamANashcetyetadrAjavartmavatsarvalokaprasiddham /
yattu shAstrIyaM puNyo vai puNyena karmaNA bhavati tatraivAdaraH kriyata iha shrutyA /
puNyameva ca karma sarvapuruShArthasAdhanamiti sarve shrutismR^itivAdAH /
mokShasyApi puruShArthatvAttatsAdhyatA prAptA /
yAvadyAvatpuNyotkarShastAvattAvatphalotkarShaprAptiH /
tasmAduttameva puNyotkarSheNa mokSho bhaviShyatItyAshaN^kA syAt /
sA nivartayitavyA j~nAnasahitasya ca prakR^iShTasya karmaNa etAvatI gatiH /
vyAkR^itanAmarUpAspadatvAtkarmaNastatphalasya ca /
na tvakArye nitye 'vyAkR^itadharmiNyanAmarUpAtmake kriyAkArakaphalasvabhAvavarjite karmaNo vyApAro 'sti /
yatra ca vyApAraH sa saMsAra evetyasyArthasya pradarshanAya brahmaNamArabhyate /
yattu kaishciducyate vidyAsahitaM karma nirabhisaMdhi mantrasharkarAdiyuktaviShadadhyAdivatkAryAntaramArabhata iti /
tanna /
anArabhyatvAnmokShasya /
bandhanAsha eva hi mokSho na kAryabhUtaH bandhanaM cAvidyetyavocAma /
avidyAyAshca na karmaNA nAsha upapadyate /
dR^iShTaviShayatvAcva karmasAmarthyasya /
utpattyAptivikArasaMskArA hi karmasAmarthyasya viShayAH /
utpAdayituM prApayituM vikartuM ca sAmarthyaM karmaNo nAto vyatiriktaviShayo 'sti karmasAmarthyasya /
loke 'prasiddhatvAt /
na ca mokSha eShAM padArthAnAmanyatamaH /
avidyAmAtravyavahita ityavocAma /
bADham /
bhavatu kevalasyaiva karmaNa evaMsvabhAvatA /
vidyAsaMyuktasya tu nirabhisaMdherbhavatyanyathA svabhAvaH /
dR^iShTaM hyanyashaktitvena nirj~nAtAnAmapi padArthAnAM viShadadhyAdInAM vidyAmantrasharkarAdisaMyuktAnAmanyaviShaye sAmathyam /
tathA karmaNo 'pyastviti cet /
na /
pramANAbhAvAt /
tatra hi karmaNa uktaviShayavyatirekeNa viShayAntare sAmarthyAstitve pramANaM na pratyakShaM nAnumAnaM nopamAnaM nArthApattirna shabdo 'sti /
nanu phalAntarAbhAve codanAnyathAnupapattiH pramANamiti /
na hi nityAnAM karmaNAM vishvajinnyAyena phalaM kalpyate /
nApi shrutaM phalamasti /
codyante ca tAni /
pArisheShyAnmokShasteShAM phalamiti gamyate /
anyathA hi puruShA na pravarteran /
nanu vishvajinnyAya evA'yAto mokShasya phalasya kalpitatvAt /
mokShe vAnyasminvA phale 'kalpite puruShA na pravarteranniti mokShaH phalaM kalpyate shrutArthApattyA yathA vishvajiti /
nanvevaM sati kathamucyate vishvajinnyAyo na bhavatIti /
phalaM ca kalpyate vishvajinnyAyashca na bhavatIti vipratiShiddhamabhidhIyate /
mokShaH phalameva na bhavatIti cet /
na /
pratij~nAhAnAt /
karma kAryAntaraM viShadadhyAdivadArabhata iti hi pratij~nAtam /
sa cenmokShaH karmaNaH kAryaM phalameva na bhavatIti sA pratij~nA hIyeta /
karmakAryatve ca mokShasya svargAdiphalebhyo visheSho vaktavyaH /
atha karmakAryaM na bhavati nityAnAM karmaNAM phalaM mokSha ityasyA vacanavyakteH kor'tha iti vaktavyam /
na ca kAryaphalashabdabhedamAtreNa visheShaH shakyaH kalpayitum /
aphalaM ca mokSho nityaishca karmabhiH kriyate nityAnAM karmaNAM phalaM na kAryamiti caiShor'tho vipratiShiddho 'bhidhIyate yathAgniH shIta iti /
j~nAnavaditi cet /
yathA j~nAnasya kAryaM mokSho j~nAnenAkriyamANo 'pyucyate tadvatkarmakAryatvamiti cet /
na /
aj~nAnanivartakatvAjj~nAnasya /
aj~nAnavyavadhAnanivartakatvAjj~nAnasya mokSho j~nAnakAryamityupacaryate /
na tu karmaNA nivartayitavyamaj~nAnam /
na cAj~nAnavyatirekeNa mokShasya vyavadhAnAntaraM kalpayituM shakyam /
nityatvAnmokShasya sAdhakasvarUpAvyatirekAcca, yatkarmaNA nivartyeta /
aj~nAnameva nivartayatIti cet /
na /
vilakShaNatvAt /
anabhivyaktiraj~nAnamabhivyaktilakShaNena j~nAnena virudhyate /
karma tu tAj~nAnena virudhyate tena j~nAnavilakShaNaM karma /
yadi j~nAnAbhAvo yadi saMshayaj~nAnaM yadi viparItaj~nAnaM vocyate 'j~nAnamiti sarvaM hi tajj~nAnenaiva nivartyate /
na tu karmaNAnyatamenApi virodhAbhAvAt /
athAdR^iShTaM karmaNAmaj~nAnanivartakatvaM kalpyamiti cet /
na /
j~nAnenAj~nAnanivR^ittau gamyamAnAyAmadR^iShTanivR^ittikalpanAnupapatteH /
yathAvaghAtena vrIhINAM tuShanivR^ittau gamyamAnAyAmagnihotrAdinityakarmakAryAdR^iShTA na kalpyate tuShanivR^ittiH /
tadvadaj~nAnanivR^ittirapi nityakarmakAryAdR^iShTA na kalpyate /
j~nAnena viruddhatvaM cAsakR^itkarmaNAmavocAma /
yadaviruddhaM j~nAnaM karmabhistaddevalokaprAptinimittamityuktaM"vidyayA devalokaH"iti shruteH /
kiJNcAnyatkalpye ca phale nityAnAM karmaNAM shrutAnAM yatkarmabhirvirudhyate dravyaguNakarmaNAM kAryameva na bhavati, kiM tatkalpyatAmiti? yasminkarmaNaH sAmarthyameva na dR^iShTam, kiMvA yasmindR^iShTaM sAmarthyaM yacca karmaNAM phalamaviruddhaM tatkalpyatAmiti /
puruShapravR^ittijananAyAvashyaM cetkarmaphalaM kalpayitavyam karmAviruddhaviShaya eva shrutArthApatteH kShINatvAnnityo mokShaH phalaM kalpayituM na shakyastadvyavadhAnAj~nAnanivR^ittirvA /
aviruddhatvAddR^iShTasAmarthyaviShayatvAcceti /
pArisheShyanyAyAnmokSha eva kalpayitavya iti cet /
sarveShAM hi karmaNAM sarvaM phalam na cAnyaditarakarmaphalavyatirekeNa phalaM kalpanAyogyamasti /
parishiShTashca mokShaH /
sa ceShTo vedavidAM phalam /
tasmAtsa eva kalpayitavya iti cet /
na /
karmaphalavyaktonAmAnantyAtpArisheShyanyAyAnupapatteH /
nahi puruShecchAviShayANAM karmaphalAnAmetAvattvaM nAma kenacidasarvaj~nenAvadhR^itaM tatsAdhanAnAM vA puruShecchAnAM vAniyatadeshakAlanimittatvAtpuruShecchAviShayasAdhanAnAM ca puruSheShTaphalaprayuktatvAt /
pratiprANi cecchAvaicitryAtphalAnAM tatsAdhanAnAM cA'nantyasiddhiH /
tadAnantyAccAshakyametAvattvaM puruShairj~nAtum /
aj~nAte ca sAdhanaphalaitAvattve kathaM mokShasya parisheShasiddhiriti /
karmaphalajAtipArisheShyamiti cet /
satyapIcchAviShayANAM tatsAdhanAnAM cA'nantye karmaphalajAtitvaM nAma sarveShAM tulyam /
mokShasatvakarmaphalatvAtparishiShTaH syAt /
tasmAtparisheShAtsa eva yuktaH kalpayitumiti cet /
na /
tasyApi nityakarmaphalatvAbhyupagame karmaphalasamAnajAtIyatvopapatteH parisheShAnupapattiH /
tasmAdanyathApyupapatteH kShINA shrutArthApattiH /
utpattayAptivikArasaMskArANAmanyatamapi nityAnAM karmaNAM phalamupapadyata iti kShINA shrutArthApattiH /
caturNAmanyatama eva mokSha iti cet /
na tAvadutpAdyo nityatvAt /
ata evAvikAryo 'saMskAryashcAta eva, asAdhanadravyAtmakatvAcca /
sAdhanAtmakaM hi dravyaM saMskriyate /
yathA pAtrAjyAdi prokShaNAdinA /
na ca saMskriyamANaH saMskAranirvartyo vA yUpAdivat /
pArisheShyAdApyaH syAt /
nA'pyo 'pyAtmasvabhAvatvAdekatvAcca /
itaraiH karmabhirvailakShaNyAnnityAnAM karmaNAM tatphalenApi vilakShaNena bhavitavyamiti cet /
na /
karmatvasAlakShaNyAtsalakShaNaM kasmAtphalaM na bhavatItarakarmaphalaiH /
nimittavailakShaNyAditi cet /
na /
kShAmavatyAdibhiH samAnatvAt /
yathA hi gR^ihadAhAdau nimitte kShAmavatyAdIShTiryathA bhinne juhoti skanne juhotItyevamAdau naimittikeShu karmasu na mokShaH phalaM kalpyate /
taishcAvisheShAnnaimittikatvena jIvanAdinimitte ca shravaNAt /
tathA nityAnAmapi na mokShaH phalam /
Alokasya sarveShAM rUpadarshanasAdhanatva ulUkAdaya Alokena rUpaM na pashyantItyulukAdicakShuSho vailakShaNyAditaralokacakShurbhirna rasAdiviShayatvaM parikalpyate rasAdiviShaye sAmarthyasyAdR^iShTatvAt /
sudUramapi gatvA yadviShaye dR^iShTaM sAmarthyaM tatraiva kashcidvisheShaH kalpayitavyaH /
yatpunaruktaM vidyAmantrasharkarAdisaMyuktaviShadadadhyAdivannityAni kAryAntaramArabhanta iti /
ArabhyatAM vishiShTaM kAryaM tadiShTatvAdavirodhaH /
nirabhisaMdheH karmaNo vidyAsaMyuktasya vishiShTakAryAntarArambhe na kashcidvirodhaH /
devayAjyAtmayAjinorAtmayAjino visheShashravaNAddevayAjinaH'shreyAnAtmayAjI'tyAdau'yadeva vidyayA karotI'tyAdau ca /
yastu paramAtmadarshanaviShaye manunokta AtmayAjishabdaH'samaM pashyannAtmayAjI'tyatra samaM pashyannAtmayAjI bhavatItyarthaH /
athavA bhUtapUrvagatyA /
AtmayAjyAtmasaMskArArthaM nityAni karmANi karoti"idaM me 'nenAN^ga saMskriyate"iti shruteH /
tathA gArbhairhemairityAdiprakaraNe kAryakaraNasaMskArArthatvaM nityAnAM karmaNAM darshayati /
saMskR^itashca ya AtmayAjI taiH karmabhiH samaM draShTuM samartho bhavati /
tasyeha vA janmAntare vA samamAtmadarshanamutpadyate samaM pashyansvArAjyamadhigacchatItyeShor'thaH /
AtmayAjishabdastu bhUtapUrvagatyA prayujyate /
j~nAnayuktAnAM nityAnAM karmaNAM j~nAnotpattisAdhanatvapradarshanArtham /
kiJNcAnyat- brahmA vishvasR^ijo dharmo mahAnavyaktameva ca /
uttamAM sAttvikImetAM gatimAhurmanIShiNaH //
iti ca devasArShTivyatirekeNa bhUtApyayaM darshayati bhUtAnyapyeti paJNca vai /
bhUtAnyatyetIti pAThaM ye kurvanti teShAM vedaviShaye paricchinnabuddhitvAdadoShaH /
na cArthavAdatvamadhyAyasya brahmAntakarmavipAkArthasya tadvayatiriktAtmaj~nAnArthasya ca karmakANDopaniShadbhayAM tulyArthatvadarshanAt /
vihitAkaraNapratiShiddhakarmaNAM ca sthAvarashvasUkarAdiphaladarshanAt /
vAntAshyAdipretadarshanAcca /
na ca shrutismR^itivIrItapratiShiddhavyatirekeNa vihitAni vA pratiShiddhAnivA karmANi kenacidavagantuM shakyante /
yeShAmakaraNAdanuShThAnAcca pretashvasUkarasthAvarAdIni karmaphalAni pratyakShAnumAnAbhyAmupalabhyante /
na caiShAmakarmaphalatvaM kenacidabhyupagamyate /
tasmAdvihitAkaraNapratiShiddhasevAnAM yathaite karmavipAkAH pretatiryaksthAvarAdayastathotkR^iShTeShvapi brahmAnteShu karmavipAkatvaM veditavyam /
tasmAt"sa Atmano vapAmudakhidat" "so 'rodIdi"tyAdivannAbhUtArthavAdatvam /
tatrApyabhUtArthavadatvaM mA bhUditi cet /
bhavatvevam /
na caitAvatAsya nyAyasya bAdho bhavati /
na cAsmatpakSho vA duShyati /
na ca"brahmA vishvasR^ija"ityAdInAM kAmyakarmaphalatvaM shakyaM vaktum /
teShAM devasArShTitAyAH phalasyoktatvAt /
tasmAtsAbhisaMdhInAM nityAnAM karmaNAM sarvamedhAshvamedhAdInAM ca brahmatvAdIni phalAni /
yeShAM punarnityAni nirabhisaMdhInyAtmasaMskArArthAni teShAM j~nAnotpattyarthAni tAni /
"brAhmIyaM kriyate tanuH"iti smaraNAt /
teShAmArAdupakArakatvAnmokShasAdhanAnyapi karmANi bhavantIti na virudhyate /
yathA cAyamarthaH ShaShThe janakAkhyAyikAsamAptau vakShyAmaH /
yattu viShadadhyAdivadityuktaM tatra pratyakShAnumAnaviShayatvAdavirodhaH /
yastvatyantashabdagamyor'thastatra vAkyasyAbhAve tadarthapratipAdakasya na shakyaM kalpayituM viShadadhyAdisAdharmyam /
na ca pramANAntaraviruddhArthaviShaye shruteH prAmANyaM kalpyate yathA shIto 'gniH kledayatIti /
shrute tu tAdarthye vAkyasya pramANAntarasyA'bhAsatvama /
yathA khadyoto 'gniriti talamalinamantarikShamiti bAlAnAM yatpratyakShamapi tadviShayapramANAntarasya yathArthatve nishcite nishcitArthamapi bAlapratyakShamAbhAsIbhavati /
tasmAdvedaprAmANyasyAvyabhicArAttAdarthye sati vAkyasya tathAtvaM syAt /
na tu puruShamatikaushalam /
nahi puruShamatikaushalAtsavitA rUpaM na prakAshayati /
tathA vedavAkyAnyapi nAnyArthAni bhavanti /
tasmAnna mokShArthAni karmANIti siddham /
ataH karmaphalAnAM saMsAratvapradarshanAyaiva brAhmaNamArabhyate /
athAnantaram uparate jAratkArave, bhujyuriti nAmato lahyasyApatyaM lAhyastadapatyaM lAhyAyaniH papraccha /
yAj~navalkyeti hovAca /
AdAbuktamashvamedhadarshanam;samaShTivyaShTiphalashcAshvamedhakratuH, j~nAnasamuccito vA kevalaj~nAnasampAdito vA, sarvakarmaNAM parA kAShThA;bhraNahatyAshvamedhAbhyAM na paraM puNyapApayoriti hi smaranti;tena hi samaShTiM vyaShTIshca prApnoti;tatra vyaShTayo nirj~nAtA antaraNDaviShayA ashvamedhayAgaphalabhUtAH;'mR^ityurasyAtmA bhavatyetAsAM devatAnAmekA bhavati'(1 / 2 / 7) ityuktam /
mR^ityushcAshanAyAlakShaNo buddhayAtmA samaShTiH prathamajo vAyuH sUtraM satyaM hiraNyagarbhaH;tasya vyAkR^ito viShayaH-yadAtmakaM sarvaM dvaitaikatvam /
yaH sarvabhUtAntarAtmA liN^gam amUrtaraso yadAshritAni sarvabhUtakarmANi, yaH karmaNAM karmasambaddhAnAM ca vij~nAnAnAM parA gatiH paraM phalam, tasya kiyAn gocaraH kiyati vyAptiH sarvataH parimaNDalIbhUtA, sA vaktavyA;tasyAm uktAyAM sarvaH saMsAro bandhagocara ukto bhavati /
tasya ca samaShTivyaShTyAtmadarshanasya alaukikatvapradarshanArthamAkhyAyikAmAtmano vR^ittAM prakurute;tena ca prativAdibuddhiMvyAmohayiShyAmIti manyate /
madreShu madrA nAma janapadAsteShu, carakA adhyayanArthavratacaraNAccarakA adhvaryavo vA, paryavrajAma paryaTitavantaH;te pataJNcalasya nAmataH, kApyasya kapigotrasya, gR^ihAn aima gatavantaH /
tasyAsId duhitA gandharvagR^ihItA-gandharveNa amAnuSheNa sacvena kenacidAviShTA;gandharvo vA dhiShNyo 'gnirR^itvigadevatA vishiShTavij~nAnatvAdavasIyate;na hi sacvamAtrasyedR^ishaM vij~nAnamupapadyate /
taM sarve vayaM parivAritAH santo 'pR^icchAma-ko 'sIti, kastvamasi kinnAmA kiMsatacvaH /
so 'bravId gandharvaH sudhanvA nAmataH, AN^giraso gotrataH /
taM yadA yasmin kAle lokAnAmantAn paryavasAnAni apR^icchAma athainaM gandharvamabrUma-bhUvanakoshaparimANaj~nAnAya pravR^itteShu sarveShvAtmAnaM shlAghayantaH pR^iShTavanto vayam;katham? kva pArikShitA abhavanniti /
sa ca gandharvaH sarvamasmabhyabravIt /
tena divyebhyo mayA labdhaM j~nAnam, tattava nAsti, ato nigR^ihIto 'si, ityabhiprAyaH /
so 'haM vidyAsampanno labdhAgamo gandharvAt tvA tvAM pR^icchAmi yAj~navalkya-kva pArikShitA abhavantat tvaM kiM jAnAsi? he yAj~navalkya'kathaya pR^icchAmi kva pArikShitA abhavanniti //1//

START BrhUp 3,3.2

#<sa hovAca -- uvAca vai saH |
agacchan vai te tad yatrAshvamedhayAjino gacchantIti |
kva nv ashvamedhayAjino gacchantIti |
dvAtriMshataM vai devarathAhnyAny ayaM lokaH |
taM samantaM pR^ithivI dvistAvat paryeti |
tAM samantaM pR^ithivIM dvistAvat samudraH paryeti |
tad yAvatI kShurasya dhArA yAvad vA makShikAyAH pattraM tAvAn antareNAkAshaH tAn aindraH suparNo bhUtvA vAyave prAyacchat |
tAn vAyur Atmani dhitvA tatrAgamayad yatrAshvamedhayAjino 'bhavann iti |
evam iva vai sa vAyum eva prashashaMsa tasmAd vAyur eva vyaShTir vAyuH samaShTiH |
apa punarmR^ityuM jayati ya evaM veda |
tato ha bhujyur lAhyAyanir upararAma || BrhUp_3,3.2 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_3,3.2 sa hovAca yAj~navalkya uvAca vai saH /
vaishbdaH smaraNArthaH /
uvAca vai sa gandharvastubhyam /
agacchanvai te pArikShitAstattatra kva? yatra yasminnashvamedhayAjino gacchantIti /
nirNote prashna Aha-kva nu kasminnashvamedhayAjino gacchantIti /
teShAM gativivakShayA bhuvanakoshaparimANamAha-dvAtriMshataM vai dve adhike triMshaddvAtriMshataM vai devarathAhrayAni deva Adityastasya ratho devarathastasya rathasya gatyAhrA yAvatparicchidyate deshaparimANa taddevarathAhrayaM taddvAtriMshadguNitaM devarathAhrayAni tAvatparimANo 'yaM loko lokAlokagiriNA parikShiptaH /
yatra vairAjaM sharIraM yatra ca karmaphalopabhogaH prANinAM sa eSha loka etAvAMlloko 'taH paramalokastaM lokaM samantaM samantato lokavistArAddviguNaparimANavistAreNa parimANena taM lokaM parikShiptA paryeti pR^ithivI /
tAM pR^ithivIM tathaiva samantaM dvistAvaddviguNena parimANena samudraH paryeti yaM ghanodamAcakShate paurANikAH /
tatraNDakapAlayorvivaraparimANamucyate /
yena vivareNa mArgeNa vahirnirgacchanto vyApnuvantyashvamedhayAjinaH /
tatra yAvatI yAvatparimANa kShurasya dhArAgraM yAvadvA saukShmyeNa yuktaM makShikAyAH patraM tAvAMstAvatparimANo 'ntareNa madhye 'NDakapAlayorAkAshchidraM tenA'kAshenetyetat /
tAnpArikShitAnashvamedhayAjinaH prAptAnidraH parameshvaro yo 'shvameve 'gnishcitaH suparNo yadviShayaM darshanamuktaM tasya prAci divishara ityAdinA suparNaH pakShI bhUtvA pakShapucchAdyAtmakaH suparNo bhUtvA vAyave prAyacchanmUrtatvAnnAstyAtmano gatistatreti /
tAnpArikShitAnvAyurAtmani dhitvA sthApayitvA svAtmabhUtAnkR^itvA tatra tasminnagamayat /
kva /
yatra pUrve 'tikrAntAH pArikShitA ashvamedhayAjino 'bhavanniti /
evamiva vA evameva sa gandharvo vAyumeva prashashaMsa pArikShitAnAM gatim /
samAptA'khyAyikA /
AkhyAyikAnirvR^ittaM tvarthamAkhyAyikAto 'pasutya shrutiH svamukhenaivA'caShTe 'smabhyam /
yasmAdvAyuH sthAvarajaN^gamAnAM bhUtAnAmantarAtmA bahishca sa eva tasmAdadhyAtmAdhibhUtAdhidaivabhAvena vividhA yAShTirvyAptiH sa vAyureva /
tathA samaShTiH kevalena sUtrAtmanA vAyureva /
evaM vAyumAtmAnaM samaShTivyaShTirUpAtmakatvenopagacchati ya evaM veda /
tasya kiM phalamityAhi-apa punarmR^ityuM jayati sakR^itmR^itvA punanaM mriyate /
tata AtmanaH prashnanirNayAdbhujyurlAhyAyanirupararAma //2//

#<iti bR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadbhAShye tR^itIyAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaM brAhmaNam //3//>#

START BrhUp 3,4.1

#<atha hainam uShastash cAkrAyaNaH papraccha |
yAj~navalkyeti hovAca -- yat sAkShAd aparokShAd brahma ya AtmA sarvAntaras taM me vyAcakShveti |
eSha ta AtmA sarvAntaraH |
yaH prANena prANiti sa ta AtmA sarvAntaraH |
yo 'pAnenApAniti sa ta AtmA sarvAntaraH |
yo vyAnena vyaniti sa ta AtmA sarvAntaraH |
ya udAnenodaniti sa ta AtmA sarvAntaraH |
eSha ta AtmA sarvAntaraH || BrhUp_3,4.1 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,4.1 atha hainamuShastashcAkrAyaNaH papraccha /
puNyapApaprayuktairgrahAtigrahairgR^ihItaH punaH punargrahAtigrahAMstyajannupAdadatsaMsaratItyuktam /
puNyasya ca para utkarSho vyAkhyAto vyAkR^itaviShayaH samaShTivyaShTirUpo dvaitaikatvAtmaprAptiH /
yastu grahAtigrahairgrastaH saMsarati so 'sti vA nAstyastitve ca kiMlakShaNa ityAtmana eva vivekAdhigamAyoShastaprashna Arabhyate /
tasya ca nirupAdhisvarUpasya kriyAkArakavinirmuktasvabhAvasyAdhigamAdyathoktAdvandhanAdvimucyate saprayojakAt /
AkhyAyikAsaMbandhastu prasiddhaH /
atha hainaM prakR^itaM yAj~navalkyamuShasto nAmatashcakrasyApatyaM cAkrAyaNaH papraccha /
yadbrahma sAkShAdavyavahitaM kenaciddraShTuraparokShAdagauNam /
na shrotrabrahmAdivat /
kiM tat /
ya AtmA /
Atmashabdena pratyagAtmocyate /
tatrA'tmashabdasya prasiddhatvAt /
sarvasyAbhyantaraH sarvAntaraH yadyaHshabdAbhyAM prasiddha AtmA brahmeti /
tamAtmAnaM me mahyaM vyAcakShveti /
viShpaShTaM shR^iN^ge gR^ihItvA yathA gAM darshayati tathA'cakShva so 'yamityevaM kathayasvetyarthaH /
evamuktaH pratyAha yAj~navalkyaH-eShu te tavA'tmA sarvAntaraH sarvasyAbhyantaraH /
sarvavisheShaNopalabhaNArtha sarvAntaragrahaNam /
yatsAkShAdavyavahitamaparokShAdagauNaM brahma bR^ihattamamAtmA sarvasyAbhyantara etairguNaiH samastairukta eShaH /
ko 'sau tavA'tmA /
yo 'yaM kAryakaraNasaMghAtastava yenA'tmanA'tmavAnsa eSha tavAtmA /
tava kAryakaraNasaMghAtasyetyarthaH /
tatra piNDastamyAbhyantare liN^gAtmA karaNasaMghAtastR^itIyo yashca saMdihyamAnasteShu katamo mamA'tmA sarvAntarastvayA vivakShita ityukta itara Aha-yaH prANena mukhanAsikAsaMcAriNA prANiti prANaceShTAM karoti yena prANaH praNIyata ityarthaH /
sa te taba kAryakaraNasaMghAtasyA'tmA vij~nAnamayaH /
samAnamanyat /
yo 'pAnenApAnIti /
yo vyAnena vyAnItIti cchAndasaM dairdhyam /
sarvAH kAryakaraNasaMghAtagatAH prANanAdiceShTA dAruyantrasyeva yena kriyante /
nahi cetanAvadanadhiShThatasya dAruyantrasyeva prANanAdiceShTA vidyante /
tasmAdvij~nAnamayenAdhiShThitaM vilakShaNena dAruyantravatprANanAdiceShTAM pratipadyate /
tasmAtso 'sti kAryakaraNasaMghAtavilakShaNo yashciShTayati //1//

START BrhUp 3,4.2

#<sa hovAcoShastash cAkrAyaNaH -- yathA vai brUyAd asau gaur asAv ashva ity evam evaitad vyapadiShTaM bhavati |
yad eva sAkShAd aparokShAd brahma ya AtmA sarvAntaras taM me vyAcakShveti |
eSha ta AtmA sarvAntaraH |
katamo yAj~navalkya sarvAntaraH |
na dR^iShTer draShTAraM pashyeH |
na shruteH shrotAraM shR^iNuyAH |
na mater mantAraM manvIthA |
na vij~nAter vij~nAtAraM vijAnIyAH |
eSha ta AtmA sarvAntaraH |
ato 'nyad Artam |
tato hoShastash cAkrAyaNa upararAma || BrhUp_3,4.2 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,4.2 sa hovAcoShastashcAkrAyaNo yathA kashcidanyathA pratij~nAya pUrvaM punarvipratipanno brUyAdanyathAsau gaurasAvashvo yashcalati dhAvatIti vA pUrvaM pratyakShaM darshayAmiti pratij~nAya pashcAccalanAdiliN^gairvyapadishatyevamevaitadbrahma prANanAdiliN^gairvyapadiShTaM bhavati tvayA /
kiM bahunA tyaktvA gotR^iShNAnimittaM vyAjaM yadeva sAkShAdaparokShAdbrahma ya AtmA sarvAntarastaM me vyAcakShveti /
itara Aha-yathA mayA prathamaM pratij~nAtastavA'tmava (tmA vi) lakShaNa iti tAM pratij~nAmanuvarta eva /
tattathaiva yathokta mayA /
yatpunaruktaM tamAtmAnaM ghaTAdivadviShayIkurviti tadashakyatvAnna kriyate /
kasmAtpunastadashakyamiti /
Aha /
vastusvAbhAvyAt /
kiM punastadvastusvAbhAvyam /
dR^iShTayAdidraShTR^itvam /
dR^iShTerdraShTA hyAtmA /
dR^iShTiriti dvividhA bhavati laukikI pAramArthikI ceti /
tatra laukikI cakShuHsaMyuktAntaHkaraNavR^ittiH /
sA kriyata iti jAyate vinashyati ca /
yA tvAtmano dR^iShTiragnyuShNaprakAshAdivatsA ca draShTaH svarUpatvAnna jAyate na vinashyati ca /
sA kriyamANayopAdhibhUtayA saMsR^iShTeveti vyapadishyate draShTeti bhedavacca draShTA dR^iShTiriti ca /
yAsau  laukikI dR^iShTishcakShurdvArA rUpoparaktA jAyamAnaiva nityayA'tmadR^iShTyA saMsR^iShTeva tatpraticchAyA tayA vyAptaiva jAyate tathA vinashyati ca tenopacaryate draShTA sadA pashyannapi pashyati na pashyati ceti /
na tu punardraShTurdR^iShTeH kadAcidapyanyathAtvam /
tathA ca vakShyati ShaShThe-dhyAyatIva lelAyatIva /
nahi draShTurdR^iShTerviparilopo vidyata iti ca /
tamimamarthamAha-laukikyA dR^iShTeH karmabhUtAyA draShTAraM svakIyayA nityayA dR^iShTyA vyAptAraM na pashyeH /
yAsau laukikI dR^iShTiH karmabhUtA sA rUpoparaktA rUpAbhivyaJNjikA nA'tmAnaM svAtmano vyAptAraM pratyaJNcaM vyApnoti /
tasmAttaM pratyagAtmAnaM dR^iShTedraShTAraM na pashyeH /
tathA shruteH shrotAraM na shR^iNuyAH /
tathA matermanovR^itteH kevalAyA vyAptAraM na manvIthAH /
tathA vij~nAteH kevalAyA buddhivR^ittervyAptAraM na vijAnIyAH /
eSha vastunaH svabhAvo 'to naiva darshayituM shakyate gavAdivat /
na dR^iShTerdraShTAramityatrAkSharANyanyathA vyAcakShate kecit /
na dR^iShTerdraShTAraM dR^iShTeH kartAraM dR^iShTibhedamakR^itvA dR^iShTimAtrasya kartAraM na pashyeriti /
dR^iShTeriti karmaNi ShaShThI /
sA dR^iShTiH kriyamANA ghaTavatkarma bhavati /
draShTAramiti tR^ijantena draShTurdR^iShTikartR^itvamAcaShTe /
tenAsau dR^iShTerdraShTA dR^iShTeH karteti vyAkhyAtR^iNAmabhiprAyaH /
tatra dR^iShTeriti ShaShThyantena dR^iShTigrahaNaM nirarthakamiti doShaM na pashyanti pashyatAM vA punaruktamasAraH pramAdapATha iti vA nA'daraH /
kathaM punarAdhikyaM tR^ijantenaiva dR^iShTikartR^itvasya siddhatvAddR^iShTeriti nirarthakam /
tadA draShTAraM na pashyerityetAvadeva vaktavyam /
yasmAddhAtoH parastR^icchUyate taddhAtvarthakartari hi tR^icsmaryate /
gantAraM bhattAraM vA nayatItyetAvAneva hi shabdaH prayujyate /
na tu gatergantAraM bhiderbhettAramityasatyarthavisheShe prayoktavyaH /
na cArthavAdatvena hAtavyaM satyAM gatau /
na ca pramAdapAThaH /
sarveShAmavigAnAt /
tasmAdvyAkhyAtR^iNAmeva buddhidaurbalyaM nAdhyetR^ipramAdaH yathA tvasmAbhirvyAkhyAtaM laukikadR^iShTervivicya nityadR^iShTivishiShTa AtmA pradarshayitavyastathA kartR^ikarmavisheShaNatvena dR^iShTishabdasya dviHprayoga upapadyata AtmasvarUpanirdhAraNAya /
'nahi draShTurdR^iShTeri'ti ca pradeshAntaravAkyenaivaikavAkyatopapannA bhavati /
tathA ca"cakShUMShi pashyati""shrotramidaM shrutam"iti shrutyantareNaikavAkyatopapannA /
nyAyAcca /
evameva hyAtmano nityatvamupapadyate vikriyAbhAve vikriyAvacca nityamiti ca vipratiShiddham /
"dhyAyatIva lelAyatIva" "nahi draShTurdR^iShTerviparilopo vidyate" "eSha nityo mahimA brAhmaNasya"iti ca shrutyakSharANyanyathA na gacchanti /
nanu draShTA shrotA mantA vij~nAtetyevamAdInyapyakSharANyAtmano 'vikriyatve na gacchantIti /
na /
yathAprAptalaukikavAkyAnuvAditvAtteShAm /
nA'tmatattvanirdhAraNArthAni tAni /
dR^iShTerdraShTAramityevamAdInAmanyArthAsambhavAdyathoktArthaparatvamavagamyate /
tasmAdanavabodhAdeva hi visheShaNaM parityaktaM dR^iShTerdraShTAramityevamAdInAmanyArthAsambhavAdyathoktArthaparatvamavagamyate /
tasmAdanavabodhAdeva hi visheShaNaM parityaktaM dR^iShTeriti /
eSha te tavA'tmA sarvairuktairvisheNaNairvishiShTaH /
ata etasmAdAtmano 'nyadArta kArya vA sharIraM karaNAtmakaM vA liN^gam /
etadevaikamanArtamavinAshi kUTastham /
tato hoShastashcAkrAyaNa upararAma //2//

iti bR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadbhAShye tR^itIyAdhyAyasya caturtha brAhmaNam //4//

START BrhUp 3,5.1

#<atha hainaM kaholaH kauShItakeyaH papraccha -- yAj~navalkyeti hovAca |
yad eva sAkShAd aparokShAd brahma ya AtmA sarvAntaras taM me vyAcakShveti |
eSha ta AtmA sarvAntaraH |
katamo yAj~navalkya sarvAntaraH |
yo 'shanAyApipAse shokaM mohaM jarAM mR^ityum atyeti |
etaM vai tam AtmAnaM viditvA brAhmaNAH putraiShaNAyAsh ca vittaiShaNAyAsh ca lokaiShaNAyAsh ca vyutthAyAtha bhikShAcaryaM caranti |
yA hy eva putraiShaNA sA vittaiShaNA yA vittaiShaNA sA lokaiShaNA |
ubhe hy ete eShaNe eva bhavataH |
tasmAd brAmaNaH pANDityaM nirvidya bAlyena tiShThAset |
bAlyaM ca pANDityaM ca nirvidyAtha muniH |
amaunaM ca maunaM ca nirvidyAtha brAhmaNaH |
sa brAhmaNaH kena syAd yena syAt tenedR^isha eva |
ato 'nyad Artam |
tato ha kaholaH kauShItakeya upararAma || BrhUp_3,5.1 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,5.1 vandhanaM saprayojakamuktam /
yashca baddhastasyApyastitvamadhigataM vyatiriktatvaM ca /
tasyedAnIM bandhamokShasAdhanaM sasaMnyAsamAtmaj~nAnaM vaktavyamiti kaholaprashna Arabhyate-atha hainaM kaholo nAmataH kuShItakasyApatyaM kauShItakeyaH papraccha yAj~navalkyeti hovAceti pUrvavat /
yadeva sAkShAdaparokShAdbrahma ya AtmA sarvAntarastaM me vyAcakShveti /
yaM viditvA bandhanAtpramucyate /
yAj~navalkya Aha-eSha te tavA'tmA /
kimuShastakaholAbhyAmeka AtmA pR^iShTaH kiMvA bhinnAvAtmAnau tulyalakShaNAviti /
bhinnAviti yuktaM prashnayorapunaruktatvopapatteH /
yadi hyeka AtmoShastakaholaprashnayorvivakShitastatraikenaiva prashnenAdhigatatvAttadviShayo dvitoyaH prashno 'narthakaH syAt /
na cArthavAdarUpatvaM vAkyasya /
tasmAdbhinnAvetAvAtmAnau kShetraj~naparamAtmAkhyAviti kecidvyAcakShate /
tanna /
ta iti pratij~nAnAt /
eSha ta Atmeti hi prativacane pratij~nAtam /
na caikasya kAryakaraNasaMghAtasya dvAvAtmAnAvupapadyete /
eko hi kAryakaraNasaMghAta ekenA'tmanA'tmavAn /
na coShastasyAnyaH kaholasyAnyo jAtito bhinna AtmA bhavati /
dvayoragauNatvAtmatvasarvAntaratvAnupapatteH /
yadyekamagauNaM brahma dvayoritareNavashyaM gauNena bhavitavyaM tathA'tmatvaM sarvAntaratvaM ca /
viruddhatvAtpadArthAnAm /
yadyekaM sarvAntaraM brahmA'tmA mukhya itareNAsarvAntareNAnAtmanAmukhyenAvashyaM bhavitavyam /
tasmAdekasyaiva dviHshravaNaM visheShavivakShayA /
yattu pUrvoktena samAnaM dvitIye prashnAntara uktaM tAvanmAtraM pUrvasyaivAnuvAdastasyaivAnuktaH kashcidvisheSho vaktavya iti /
kaH punarasau visheSha iti /
ucyate-pUrvasminprashne 'sti vyatirikta AtmA yasyAyaM saprayojako bandha ukta iti /
dvitIye tu tasyaivA'tmano 'shanAyAdisaMsAradharmAtItatvaM visheSha ucyate /
yadvisheShaparij~nAnAtsaMnyAsasahitAtpUrvoktAdvandhanAdvimucyate /
tasmatprashnaprativacanayoreSha ta AtmetyevamantayostulyArthataiva /
nanu kathamekasyaivA'tmano 'shanAyAdyatItatvaM tadvatvaM ceti viruddhadharmasamavAyitvamiti /
na /
parihR^itatvAt /
nAmarUpavikarakAryakaraNalakShaNasaMghAtopAdhibhedasaMparkajanitabhrAntimAtraM hi saMsAritvamityasakR^idavocAma /
viruddhashrativyAkhyAnaprasaN^gena ca /
yathA rajjushuktikAgaganAdayaH sarparajatamalinA bhavanti parAdhyAropitadharmavishiShTAH svataH kevalA eva rajjushuktikAgaganAdayaH /
na caivaM viruddhadharmasamavAyitve padArthAnAM kashcana virodhaH /
nAmarUpopAdhyastitve"ekamevAdvitIyam" "neha nAnAsti kiJNcana"iti shrutayo virudhyeranniti cet /
na /
salilaphenadR^iShTAntena parihR^itatvAnmR^idAdihaShTAntaishca /
yadA tu paramArthadR^iShTyA paramAtmatattvAcchratyanusAribhiranyatvena nirupyamANe nAmarUpe mR^idAdivikAravadvastvantare tattvato na staH salilaphenaghaTAdivikAravadeva tadA tadapekShya'ekamevAdvitIyaM'neha nAnAsti kiJNcane tyadiparamArthadarshanagocaratvaM pratipadyate /
yadA tu svAbhAvikyAvidyayA brahmasvarUpaM rajjushuktikAgaganasvarUpavadeva svena rUpeNa vartamAnaM kenacidaspR^iShTasvabhAvamapi sannAmarUpakR^itakAryakaraNopAdhibhyo vivekena nAvadhAyate nAmarUpopAdhidR^iShTireva ca bhavati svAbhAvikI tadA sarvo 'yaM vastvantarAstitvavyavahAraH /
asti cAyaM bhedakR^ito mithyAvyavahAro yeShAM brahmatattvAdanyatvena vastu vidyate yeShAM ca nAsti /
paramArthavAdibhistu shrutyanusAreNa nirUpyamANe vastuni kiM tattvato 'sti vastu kiMvA nAstIti brahmaikamevAdvitIyaM sarvasaMvyahArashUnyamiti nirdhAryate tena na kashcidvirodhaH /
nahi paramArthAvadhAraNaniShThAyAM vastvantarAstitvaM pratipadyAmahe /
"ekamevAdvitIyam" "anantaramabAhyam"iti shruteH /
na ca nAmarUpavyavahArakAle tvavivekinAM kriyAkArakaphalAdisaMvyavahAro nAstIti pratiShidhyate /
tasmAjj~nAnAj~nAne apekShya sarvaH saMvyavahAraH j~nAstrIyo laukikashca /
ato na kAcana virodhashaN^kA /
sarvavAdinAmapyaparihAryaH paramArthasavyavahArakR^ito vyavahAraH /
tatra paramArthAtmasvarUpamapekShya prashnaH punaH katamo yAj~navalkya sarvAntara iti /
pratyAhetaro yo 'shanAyApipAso /
ashitumicchAshanAyA pAtumicchA pipAsA /
te ashanAyApipAse yo 'tyetIti vakShyamANena sambandhaH /
avivekibhistalamalavadiva gaganaM gamyamAnameva talamale atyeti paramArthatastAbhyAmasaMsR^iShTasvabhAvatvAt /
tathA mUDhairashanAyApipAsAdimadbrahma gamyamAnamapi kShudhito 'haM pipAsito 'hamiti te atyetyeva paramArthatastAbhyAmasaMsR^iShTasvabhAvatvAt /
"na lipyate lokaduHkhena bAhyaH"iti shruteH /
avidvallokAdhyAropitaduHkhenetyarthaH /
prANaikadharmatvAtsamAsakaraNamashanAyApipAsayoH /

na;vidhitsitavij~nAnena samAnakartR^ikatvashravaNAt /

yat punaruktaM vartamAnApadeshAdarthavAdamAtramiti - na, audumbarayUpAdividhisamAnatvAdadoShaH /
'vyutthAya bhikShAcaryaM caranti'ityanena pArivrAjyaM vidhIyate, pArivrAjyAshrame ca yaj~nopavItAdisAdhanAni vihitAni, liN^gaM ca shrutibhiH smR^itishca /
atastad varjayitvA anyasmAd vyutthAnam eShaNAtve 'pIti cet? na, vij~nAnasamAnakartR^ikAt pArivrAjyAdeShaNAvyutthAnalakShaNAt pArivrAjyAntaropapatteH;yaddhi tadeShaNAbhyo vyutthAnalakShaNaM pArivrAjyaM tadAtmaj~nAnAN^gam, Atmaj~nAnavirodhyeShaNAparityAgarUpatvAt, avidyAviShayatvAccaiShaNAyAH, tadvyatirekeNa cAstyAshramarUpaM pArivrAjyaM brahmalokAdiphalaprAptisAdhanam, yadviShayaM yaj~nopavItAdisAdhanavidhAnaM siN^gavidhAnaM ca /
na ca eShaNArUpasAdhanApAdAnasya AshramadharmamAtreNa pArivrAjyAntare viShaye sambhavati sati, sarvopaniShadvihitasya Atmaj~nAnasya bAdhanaM yuktam, yaj~nopavItAdyavidyAviShayaiShaNArUpasAdhanopAditsAyAM cAvashyam asAdhanaphalarUpasya ashanAyAdisaMsAradharmavarjitasya ahaM brahmAsmi, ithi vij~nAnaM bAdhyate, na ca tadrAdhanaM yuktam. sarvopaniShadAM tadarthaparatvAt /
'bhikShAcaryaM caranti'ityeShaNAM grAhayantI shrutiH svayameva bAdhata iti cet? athApi syAdeShaNAbhyo vyutthAnaM vidhAya punareShaNakadeshaM bhikShAcaryagrAhayantI tatsambaddhamanyadapi grAhayatIti cet? na, bhikShAcaryasyAprayojakatvAd hutvottarakAlabhakShaNAt /
sheShapratipattikarmatvAdaprayojakaM hi tat, asaMskAramapi syAt, na tu bhikShAcaryam;niyamAdR^iShTasyApi brahmavido 'niShTatvAt /
niyamAdR^iShTasyAniShTatve kiM bhikShAcaryeNeti cet! na, anyasAdhanAd vyutthAnasya vihitatvAt /
tathApi kiM teneti cet? yadi syAt, bAdhamabhyupagamyate hi tat /
yAni pArivrAjye 'bhihitAni vacanAni'yaj~nopavItyevAdhIyIta'ityAdIni, tAnyavidvatpArivrAjyamAtraviShayANIti parihR^itAni;itarathA Atmaj~nAnabAdhaH syAditi hyuktam,"nirAshiShamanArambhaM nirnamastAramastutim /
akShINaM kShINakarmANaM taM devA brAhmaNe viduH"iti sarvakarmAbhAvaM darshayati smR^itirviduShaH,"vidvAMliN^go dharmaj~naH"iti ca /
tasmAt paramahaMsapArivrAjyameva vyutthAnalakShaNaM pratipadyetAtmavit sarvakarmasAdhanaparityAgarUpamiti /
yasmAt pUrve brAhmaNA etamAtmAnam asAdhanaphalasvabhAvaM viditvA sarvasmAt sAdhanaphalasvarUpAdeShaNAlakShaNAd vyutthAya bhikShAcaryaM caranti sma, dR^iShTAdR^iShTArthaM karma tatsAdhanaM ca hitvA, tasmAd adyatve 'pi brAhmaNo brahmavit pANDityaM paNDitabhAvam, etadAtmavij~nAnaM pANDityam, nirvidya niHsheShaM viditvA Atmavij~nAnaM niravasheShaM kR^itvetyarthaH - AcAryata Agamatashca, eShaNAbhyo vyutthAya-eShaNAvyutthAnAvasAnameva hi tat pANDityam eShaNAtiraskArodbhavatvAdeShaNAvirudvatvAt;eShaNAmatiraskR^itya na hyAtmaj~nAnenaiva vihitameShaNAvyutthAnam Atmaj~nAnasamAnakartR^ikatvApratyayopAdAnaliN^gashrutyAd daDhIkR^itam /
tasmAdepaNAbhyo vyutthAya j~nAnabanabhAvena bAlyena tiShThAset sthAtumicchet /
sAdhanaphalAshrayaNaM hi balamitareShAmanAtmavidAm, tad balaM hitvA vidvAn asAdhanaphalasvarUpAtmavij~nAnameva balaM tadbhAvameva kevalamAshrayet, tadAshrayaNe hi karaNAnyeShaNAvipaye enaM hratvA sthApayituM nItsahante;j~nAnabalahInaM hi mUDhaMd daShTAdR^iShTaviShayAyAm eShaNAyAmevainaM karaNAni niyojayanti;balaM nAma AtmavidyayAsheShaviShayadR^iShTitiraskaraNam;atastadbhAvena bAlyena tiShThAset;tathA"AtmanA bindate vIryam"iti shrutyantarAt /
"nAyamAtmA balahInena labhyaH"iti ca /
bAlyaM ca pANDityaM ca nirvidya niHsheShaM kR^itvAtha  mananAnmuniryogI bhavati;etAvadvi brAhmaNena kartavyam, yaduta sarvAnAtmapratyayatiraskaraNam;etat kR^itvA kR^itakR^ityo yogI bhavati /
amaunaM ca Atmaj~nAnAnAtmapratyayatiraskArau pANDityabAlyasaMj~nakau niHsheShaM kR^itvA, maunaM nAma anAtmapratyayatiraskaraNasya parthavasAnaM phalam, tacca nirvidyAtha brAhmaNaH kutakR^ityo bhavatibrahmaiva sarvamiti pratyaya upajAyate /
sa brAhmaNaH kutakR^ityaH, ato brAhmaNaH, nirUpacaritaM hi tadA tasya brAhmaNyaM prAptam;kena syAt kena caraNena bhavet? yena syAd yena caraNena bhavet, tenedR^isha evAyam-yena kenaciccaraNena syAt tenedR^isha eva uktalakShaNa eva brAhmaNo bhavati;yena kenaciccaraNeneti stutyartham-yeyaM brAhmaNyAvasthA seyaM stUyate, na tu caraNe 'nAdaraH /
ata etasmAd brAhmaNyAvasthAnAda ashanAyAdyatItAtmasvarUpAd nityatR^iptAd anyad avidyAvipayam eShaNAlakShaNaM vastvantaram, Arta vinAshi ArtiparigR^ihItam, svapnamAyAmarIcyudakasamam asAram, AtmaivAkaH kevalo nityamukta iti /
tato ha kaholaH kaupAtakeyaH upararAma //1//

yat sAkShAdaparokShAd brahma sarvantara Atmetyuktam, tasya sarvAntarasya svarUpAdhigamAya A shAkalyabrAhmaNAd grantha Arabhyate /

START BrhUp 3,6.1

#<atha hainaM gArgI vAcaknavI papraccha -- yAj~navalkyeti hovAca |
yad idaM sarvam apsv otaM ca protaM ca kasmin nu khalv Apa otAsh ca protAsh ceti |
vAyau gArgIti |

BrhUpBh_3,6.1 atha hainaM gArgI nAmataH, vAcaknavIvacakrorduhitA, papraccha;yAj~navalkyeti hovAca;yadidaM sarvaM pArthivaM dhAtujAtam apsUdake otaM ca protaM ca, otaM dIrghapaTatantuvat protaM tiryaktantuvad viparItaM vA-adbhiH sarvato 'ntarbahirbhUtAbhirvyAptamityarthaH, anyathA saktumuShTivad vishIryeta /
idaM tAvadanumAnamupanyastam-yat kAryaM paricchinnaM sthUlam, kAraNenAparicchinnena sUkShmeNa vyAptamitid daShTam-yathA pR^ithivI adbhiH, tathApUrvaM pUrvamuttareNottareNa vyApinA bhavitavyam, ityeSha A sarvAntarAdAtmanaH prashnArthaH /
tatra bhUtAni paJNca saMhatAnyevottaramuttaraM sUkShamabhAvena vyApakena kAraNarUpeNa ca vyavatiShThante, na ca paramAtmanor'vAk tadvayatirekeNavastvantaramasti"satyasya satyam"iti shruteH /
satyaM ca bhUtapaJNcakam satyasya satyaM ca para AtmA /
kasminnu khalvApa otAshcaprotAshceti-tAsAmapi kAryatvAt sthUlatvAt paricchinnatvAcca kacidvi otaprotabhAvena bhavitavyam;kva tAsAmetayotabhAva iti /
evamutarottaraprakShaNasaN^goyojayitavyaH /
vAyau gArgIti /
nanvagnAviti vaktavyam!naipa doShaH, agneH pArthivaM vA ApyaM vA dhAtumanAshritya itarabhUtavat svAtantryeNa AtmalAbho nAstIti tasminnotaprotabhAvo nopadishyate /
kasminnu khalu vAyurotashca protashcetyantarikShalokeShu gArgIti tAnyeva bhUtAni saMhatAnyantarikShalokAH, tAnyapi gandharvalokeShu, gandharvalokA AdityalokeShu, AdityalokAshcandralokeShu, candralokA nakShatralokeShu, nakShatralokA devalokeShu, devalokA indralokeShu, indralokA virATsharIrAraMmakeShu bhUteShu prajApatilokeShu, prajApatilokA brahmalokeShu /
brahmalokA nAma aNDAraMmakANi bhUtAni;sarvatra hi sUkShmatAratamyakrameNa prApyubhogAshrayAkArapariNatAni bhUtAni saMhatAni tAnyeva paJNceti bahuvacanamAJNji /
kasminnu khalu brahmalokA otAshca protAshceti-sa hovAca yAj~navalkyo he gArgI mAtiprAkShIH svaM prashnam, nyAyaprakAramatItya Agamena praShTabyAM devatAmanumAnena mA prAkShIrityarthaH, pR^icchantyAshca mA te tava mUrdhA shiro vyapatad vispaShTaM patet;devatAyAH svaprashna AgamaviShayaH;taM prashnaviShayamatikrAnto gArgyAH prashnaH;AnumAnikatvAt sa yasyA devatAyAH prashnaH sAtiprashnyA, nAtiprashnyAnatiprashnyA, svaprashraviShayaiva, kevalAgamagamyetyarthaH, tAmanatiprashnyAM vai devatAmatipR^icchasi /
ato gArgi mAtiprAkShIH, martuM cennecchasi /
tato ha gArgI vAcaknavI upararAma //1//

START BrhUp 3,7.1

#<athainam uddAlaka AruNiH papraccha -- yAj~navalkyeti hovAca |
madreShv avasAma pataJNcalasya kApyasya gR^iheShu yaj~nam adhIyAnAH |
tasyAsId bhAryA gandharvagR^ihItA |
tam apR^icchAma -- ko 'sIti |

so 'bravIt pataJNcalaH kApyo nAhaM tad bhagavan vedeti |
so 'bravIt pataJNcalaM kApyaM yAj~nikAMsh ca |

yo vA idaM kashca brUyAd veda vedeti yathA vettha tathA brUhIti || BrhUp_3,7.1 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,7.1 atha hainamuddAlako nAmataH, aruNasyApatyamAruNiH papraccha;yAj~navalkyeti hovAca;madreShu desheShvavasAmoShitavantaH, pataJNcalasya-pataJNcalo nAmatastasyaiva kapigotrasya kApyasya gR^iheShu yaj~namadhIyAnA yashashAstrAdhyayanaM kurvANAH /
tasyAsId bhAryA gandharvagR^ihItA;tamapR^icchAma-ko 'sIti;so 'bravIt kabandho nAmataH, atharvaNo 'patyamAtharvaNa iti /
so 'bravId gAndharvaH pataJNcalaM kApyaM yAj~nikAMshca tacchipyAn-vettha nu tvaM he kApya jAnIShe tat sUtram? kiM tat? yena sUtreNAyaM ca leka idaM ca janma, parashca lokaH paraM ca pratipattavyaM janma, sarvANi ca bhUtAni brahmAdistambaparyantAni, sandR^ibdhAni saN^grathitAni sragiva sUtreNa viShTabdhAni bhavanti yena-tat kiM sUtraM vettha? so 'bravIdevaM pR^iShTaH kApyaH-nAhaM tad bhagavan vedeti, tat sUtraM nAhaM jAne he bhagavanniti sampUjayannAha /
so 'bravIt punargandharva upAdhyAyamasmAMshca-vettha na tvaM kApya tamantaryAmiNam? antaryAmIti visheShyate-ya imaM ca lokaM paraM ca lokaM sarvANi ca bhUtAni yo 'ntarAbhyantaraH san yamayati niyamayati,  dAruyantramiva brAmayati, svaM svamucitavyApAraM kArayatIti /
so 'bravIdevamuktaH pataJNcalaH kApyaH-nAhaM taM jAne bhagavanniti sampUjayannAha /
so 'bravIt punargandharvaH;sUtratadantargatAntaryAmiNorvij~nAnaM stUyate-yaH kashcid vai tat sUtraM he kApya bavidyAd vijAnIyAt taM cAntaryAmiNaM sUtrAntargataM tasyaiva sUtrasya niyantAraM vidyAt yaH-ityevamuktena prakAreNa, sa hi brahmavita paramAtmavit sa lokAMshca bhUrAdInantaryAmiNA niyamyamAnAMllokAn vetti, sa devAMshcAgnyAdIMllokino jAnAti, vedAMshca sarvapramANabhUtAn vetti, bhUtAni ca brahmAdIni sUtreNa dhiyamANAni tadantargatenAntaryAmiNA niyamyamAnAni vetti, sa AtmAnaM ca kartR^itvabhoktR^itvavishiShTaM tenaivAntaryAmiNA niyamyamAnaM vetti, sarvaM ca jagata tathAbhUtaM vettIti /
evaM stute sUtrAntaryAmivij~nAne pralubdhaH kApyo 'bhimukhIbhUtaH, vayaM ca;tebhyashcAsmabhyamabhimukhIbhUtebhyobravId gandharvaH sUtramantaryAmiNaM ca;tadahaM sUtrAnitaryAmivij~nAnaM veda gandharvAllabdhAgamaH san /
tacced yAj~navalkya sUtraM taM cAntaryAmiNamavidvAMshcebrahmavit san yadi brahmagavIrudajatase brahmavidAM svabhUtA gA udajase unnayasi tvam anyAyena, tato macchApadagdhasya mUrdhA shiraste tava vispaShTaM ShatiShyati /
evamukto yAj~navalkya Ahaveda jAnAmyahaM he gautameti gotrataH, tat sUtraM yad gandharvastubhyamuktavAn yaM cAntaryAmiNaM gandharvAd viditavanto yUyam, taM cAntaryAmiNaM vedAhamiti /
evamukto pratyAha gautamaH-yaH kashcit prAkR^ita idaM yattavayoktaM brUyAt-katham? veda vedeti-AtmAnaM shlAghayan, kiM tena garjitena kAryeNa darshaya;yathA vetya tathA brUhIti //1//

START BrhUp 3,7.2

#<sa hovaca -- vAyur vai gautama tat sUtram |
vAyunA vai gautama sUtreNAyaM ca lokaH parash ca lokaH sarvANi ca bhUtAni saMdR^ibdhAni bhavanti |
tasmAd vai gautama puruShaM pretam Ahur vyasraMsiShatAsyAN^gAnIti |
vAyunA hi gautama sUtreNa samdR^ibdhAni bhavantIti |
evam evaitad yAj~navalkya |
antaryAmiNaM brUhIti || BrhUp_3,7.2 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,7.2 sa hovAca yAj~navalkyaH /
brahmalokA yasminnotAshca protAshca vartamAnekAle, yathA pR^ithivyapsu, tat sUtram AgamagamyaM vattavyamiti tadarthaM prashnAntaramutthApitam;atastannirNayAyAha-vAyurvai gautama tat sUtram, nAnyat;vAyuriti sUkShmamAkAshavadviShTambhakaM pR^ithivyAdInAm, yadAtmakaM saptadashavidhaM liN^gaM karmavAsanAsamavAyi prANinAm, yattat samaShTivyaShTyAtmakam, yasya bAhyA medAH saptasapta marudraNAH samudrasyevormayaH, tadetad vAyavyaM tattvaM sUtrAmityabhidhIyate /
vAyunA vai gautama sUtreNAyaM ca lokaH parashca lokaH sarvANi ca bhUtAni sandR^ibdhAni bhavanti saÇprathitAni bhavantIti prasiddhametat /
asti ca loke prasiddhiH, katham? yasmAd vAyuH sUtram, vAyunA vidhR^itaM sarvam, tasmAd vai gautama puruShaM pretamAhuH kathayanti - vyasraMsipata visrastAnyasyapuruShasyAN^gAnIti;sUtrApagame hi maNyAdInAM protAni yad yasyAN^gAni syustato yuktametad vAyvapagame 'vasraMsanamaN^gAnAm ato vAyunA hi gautama sUtreNa sandR^ibdhAni bhavantIti nigamayati /
evamevaitad yAj~navalkya samyaguktaM sUtram;tadantargataM tvidAnIM tasyaiva sUtrasya niyantAramantaryAmiNaM brUhItyukta Aha //2//

START BrhUp 3,7.3

#<yaH pR^ithivyAM tiShThan pR^ithivyA antaro yaM pR^ithivI na veda yasya pR^ithivI sharIraM yaH pR^ithivIm antaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH || BrhUp_3,7.3 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,7.3 yaH pR^ithivyAM tiShThan bhavati, so 'ntaryAmI, sarvaH pR^ithivyAM tiShThatIti sarvatra prasaN^go mA bhUditi vishinaShTi - pR^ithivyA antaro 'bhyantaraH /
tatraitat syAt pR^ithivIdevataiva antaryAmItyata Aha - yamantaryAmiNaM pR^ithivI devatApi na veda mayyanyaH kashcidvartata iti /
yasya pR^ithivI sharIram-yasya ca pR^ithivyeva sharIram, nAnyat-pR^ithivIdevatAyA yaccharIram, tadeva sharIraM yasya, sharIragrahaNaM copalakShaNArtham, karaNaM ca pR^ithivyAH, tasya svakarmaprayuktaM hi kAryaM ca pR^ithivIdevatAyAH, tadasya svakarmAbhAvAdantaryAmiNo nityamuktatvAt /
parArthakartavyatAsvabhAvatvAt parasya yat kAryaM karaNaM ca tadevAsya, na svataH, tadAha-yasya pR^ithivI sharIramiti /
devatAkAryakaraNasyeshvarasAkShimAtrasAnnidhyena hi niyamenapravR^ittinivR^ittI syAtAm;ya IdR^igIshvaro nArAyaNAkhyaH, pR^ithirvI pR^ithivIdevatAm, yamayati niyamayati svavyApAre, antaro 'bhyantarastiShThan, eSha ta AtmA, te tava, mama ca sarvabhUtAnAM cetyupalakShaNArthametat;antaryAmI yastvayApR^iShTaH, amR^itaH sarvasaMsAradharmavarjita ityetat //3//

START BrhUp 3,7.4-14

#<yo 'psu tiShThann adbhyo 'ntaro yam Apo na vidur yasyApaH sharIraM yo 'po 'ntaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH || BrhUp_3,7.4 ||>#


#<yo 'gnau tiShThann agner antaro yam agnir na veda yasyAgniH sharIraM yo 'gnim antaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH || BrhUp_3,7.5 ||>#


#<yo 'ntarikShe tiShThann antarikShAd antaro yam antarikShaM na veda yasyAntarikShaM sharIraM yo 'ntarikSham antaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH || BrhUp_3,7.6 ||>#


#<yo vAyau tiShThan vAyor antaro yaM vAyur na veda yasya vAyuH sharIraM yo vAyum antaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH || BrhUp_3,7.7 ||>#


#<yo divi tiShThan divo 'ntaro yaM dyaur na veda yasya dyauH sharIraM yo divam antaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH || BrhUp_3,7.8 ||>#


#<ya Aditye tiShThann AdityAd antaro yam Adityo na veda yasyAdityaH sharIraM ya Adityam antaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH || BrhUp_3,7.9 ||>#

#<yash candratArake tiShTha¤ candratArakAd antaro yaM candratArakaM na veda yasya candratArakaM sharIraM yash candratArakam antaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH || BrhUp_3,7.11 ||>#


#<ya AkAshe tiShThann AkAshAd antaro yam AkAsho na veda yasyAkAshaH sharIraM ya AkAsham antaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH || BrhUp_3,7.12 ||>#


#<yas tamasi tiShThaMs tamaso 'ntaro yaM tamo na veda yasya tamaH sharIraM yas tamo 'ntaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH || BrhUp_3,7.13 ||>#


#<yas tejasi tiShThaMs tejaso 'ntaro yaM tejo na veda yasya tejaH sharIraM yas tejo 'ntaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH || BrhUp_3,7.14 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,7.4-14 samAnamanyat /
yo 'psu tiShThan-agnau, antarikShe, vAyau, divi, Aditye, yastamasyAvaraNAtmake bAhye tamasi, tejasi tadviparIte prakAshasAmAnye ityevamadhidaivatam antaryAmiviShayaM darshanaM devatAsu /
athAdhibhUtaM bhUteShu brahmadistambaparyanteShu antaryAmidashanamadhibhUtam // 4 -14 //

#<athAdhibhUtam | 
yaH sarveShu bhUteShu tiShThan sarvebhyo bhUtebhyo 'ntaro yaM sarvANi bhUtAni na vidur yasya sarvANi bhutAni sharIraM yaH sarvANi bhUtAny antaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH |
ity adhibhUtam || BrhUp_3,7.15 ||>#

#<yo manasi tiShThan manaso 'ntaro yaM mano na veda yasya manaH sharIraM yo mano 'ntaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH || BrhUp_3,7.20 ||>#


#<yas tvaci tiShThaMs tvaco 'ntaro yaM tvaÇ na veda yasya tvak sharIraM yas tvacam antaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH || BrhUp_3,7.21 ||>#


#<yo vij~nAne tiShThan vij~nAnAd antaro yaM vij~nAnaM na veda yasya vij~nAnaM sharIraM yo vij~nAnam antaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH || BrhUp_3,7.22 ||>#


#<yo retasi tiShThaM retaso 'ntaro yaM reto na veda yasya retaH sharIraM yo reto 'ntaro yamayaty eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH |
adR^iShTo draShTAshrutaH shrotAmato mantAvij~nato vij~nAtA |
nAnyo 'to 'sti draShTA nAnyo 'to 'sti shrotA nAnyo 'to 'sti mantA nAnyo 'to 'sti vij~nAtA |
eSha ta AtmAntaryAmy amR^itaH |
ato 'nyad Artam |
tato hoddAlaka AruNir upararAma || BrhUp_3,7.23 ||>#

BrhUpBh_3,7,15-23 athAdhyAtmam-yaH prANe prANavAyusahite ghrANe, yo vAci, cakShuShi, shrotre, manasi, tvaci, vij~nAne, budvau, retasi prajanane /
kasmAt punaH kAraNAt pR^ithivyAdidevatA mahAbhAgAH satyo manuShyAdivadAtamani tiShThantamAtmano niyantAramantaryAmiNaM na vidurityata Aha-adR^iShTenad daShTo na viShayIbhUtaH cakShurdarshanasya kasyacit, svayaM tu cakShuShi sannihitatvAdd dashisvarUpa iti draShTA /
tathAshrutaH shrotragocaratvamanApannaH kasyacit, svayaM tvaluptashravaNashaktiH sarvashrotreShu sannihitatvAchracotA /
tathAmato manaHsaN^kalpaviShayatAmanApannaH;dR^iShTashrute eva hi sarvaH saN^kalpayati;uddR^iShTatvAdakShutatvAdevAmataH;allaptamananashaktitvAt sarvamanaHsu sannihitatvAcca mantA /
tathAvij~nAto nishcayagocaratAmanApannorUpAdivat lasukhAdivadvA, svayaM tvaluptavij~nAnashaktitvAttatsannidhAnAcca vij~nAtA /
tatra yaM pR^ithivI na veda yaM sarvANi bhUtAni na viduriti cAnye niyantavyA vij~nAtAro 'nyo niyantA antaryAmIti prAptam, tadanyatvAshaN^kAnivR^ittyarthamucyate - nAnyo 'taH, nAnyaH ato 'smAdantaryAmiNo nAnyo 'sti draShTA, tathA nAnyo 'to 'sti mantA, nAnyo 'to 'sti shrotA, nAnyo 'to 'sti mantA, nAnyo 'to 'sti vij~nAtA /
yasmAt paro nAsti draShTA shrotA mantA vij~nAtA, yo 'dR^iShTo draShTA, ashrutaH shrotA, amato mantA, avij~nAto vij~nAtA, amR^itaH sarvasaMsAradharmavarjitaH sarvasaMsAriNAM karmaphalavibhAgakartA - eSha te AtmAntaryAmyamR^itaH asmAdIshvarAdAtmano 'nyadArtam /
tato hi uddAlaka AruNirupararAma //15//

START BrhUp 3,8.1

#<atha ha vAcaknavy uvAca -- brAhmaNA bhagavanto hantAham imaM dvau prashnau prakShyAmi |
tau cen me vivakShyati |
na vai jAtu yuShmAkam imaM kashcid brahmodyaM jeteti |
pR^iccha gArgIti || BrhUp_3,8.1 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,8.1 atha ha vAcaknavyuvAca /
sarvaM yAj~navalkyena niShiddhA mUrdhapAtabhayAduparatA satI punaH praShTuM brAhmaNAnuj~nAM prArthayate - he brAhmaNA bhagavantaH pUjAvantaH shR^iNuta mama vacaH;hantAhamimaM yAj~navalkyaM punardvai prashnau prakShyAmi, yadyanumatirbhavatAmasti;tau prashnau cedyadi vakShyati kathayiShyati me, kathaJNcinna vai jAtu kadAcid yuShmAkaM madhye imaM yAj~navalkyaM kashcid brahmodyaM brahmavadanaM prati jetA na vai kashcid bhavediti /
evamuktA brAhmaNA anuj~nAM pradaduH - pR^iccha gArgIti //1//

START BrhUp 3,8.2

#<sA hovAca -- ahaM vai tvA yAj~navalkya yathA kAshyo vA vaideho vograputra ujjyaM dhanur adhijyaM kR^itvA dvau bANavantau sapatnAtivyAdhinau haste kR^itvopottiShThed evam evAhaM tvA dvAbhyAM prashnAbhyAm upodasthAm |
tau me brUhIti |
pR^iccha gArgIti || BrhUp_3,8.2 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,8.2 labdhAnuj~nA ha yAj~navalkyaM sA hovAca - ahaM vai tvA tvAM dvau prashnau prakShyAmItyanuShajyate;kau tAviti jij~nAsAyAM tayorduruttaratvadyotayituM dR^iShTAntapUrvakaM tAvAha - he yAj~navalkya yathA loke kAshyaH kAshiShu bhavaH kAshyaH, prasiddhaM shauryaM kAshye, vaideho vA videhAnAM vA rAjA, ugraputraH shUrAnvaya ityarthaH, ujjyam avatAritajyAkaM dhanuH punaradhijyam AropitalyAkaM kR^itvA dvau bANavantau bANashabdena sharAgre yo vaMshakhaNDaH saMdhIyate, tena vinApi sharo bhavatItyato vishinaShTi bANavantAviti - dvau bANavantau sharau, tayoreva visheShaNaM sapatnAtivyAdhinau shatroH pIDAkarAvatishayena, haste kR^itvopottiShThet samIpata AtmAnaM darshayet evamevAhaM tvA tvAM sharasthAnIyAbhyAM prashnAbhyAM dvAbhyAmupodasthAM utthitavatyasmi tvatsamIpe /

START BrhUp 3,8.3

#<sA hovAca -- yad UrdhvaM  yAj~navalkya divo yad avAk pR^ithivyA yad antarA dyAvApR^ithivI ime yad bhUtaM ca bhavac ca bhaviShyac cety AcakShate kasmiMs tad otaM ca protaM ceti || BrhUp_3,8.3 ||>#

START BrhUp 3,8.5

START BrhUp 3,8.7

#<sa hovAca -- yad UrdhvaM gArgi divo yad avAk pR^ithivyA yad antarA dyAvApR^ithivI ime yad bhUtaM ca bhavac ca bhaviShyac cety AcakShata AkAsha eva tad otaM ca protaM ceti |

BrhUpBh_3,8.7 sarvaM yathoktaM gArgyA pratyuccArya tameva pUrvoktamarthamavadhAritavAnAkAsha eveti yAj~navalkyaH /
gArgyAha-kasminnu khalvAkAsha otashca protashceti /
AkAshameva tAvat kAlatrayAtItatvAd durvAcyam, tato 'pi kaShTataramakSharam yasminnAkAshamotaM ca protaM ca, ato 'vAcyamitikR^itvA, na pratipadyate sA apratipattirnAma nigrahasthAnaM tArkikasamaye;athAvAcyamapi vakShyati, tathApi vipratipattirnAma nigrahasthAnam;virudvA pratipattirhi sA, yadavAcyasya vadanam;ato durvacanaM prashnaM manyate gArgI // 7 // tad doShadvayamapi parijihIrpannAha-

START BrhUp 3,8.8

#<sa hovAca -- etad vai tad akSharaM gArgi brAhmaNA abhivadanty asthUlam anaNv ahrasvam adIrgham alohitam asneham acchAyam atamo 'vAyv anAkAsham asaN^gam arasam agandham acakShuShkam ashrotram avAg amano 'tejaskam aprANam amukham agAtram anantaram abAhyam (VAR for agAtram: amAtram) |
na tad ashnAti kiM cana |
na tad ashnAti kash cana || BrhUp_3,8.8 ||>#

__________


BrhUpBh_3,8.8 sa hovAca yAj~navalkyaH-etad vai tad yat pR^iShTavatyasi kasminnu khalvAkAsha otashca protashceti, kiM tat? akSharam-yanna kShIyate na kSharatIti vAkSharam-tadakSharaM he gArgi brAhmaNA brahmavido 'bhivadanti /
brahmaNAbhivadanakathanena-nAhamavAcyaM vakShyAmi na cana pratipadyeyam-ityevaM dopadrayaM pariharati /
evamapAkute prashne punargArgyAH prativacanaM draShTavyam-brUhi kiM tadakSharam? yad brAhmaNA abhivadanti, ityukta Aha-prasthUlaM tat sthUlAdanyat, evaM tarhyaNu? anaNu, astu tarhi hasvam, ahasvam;evaM tarhi dIrgham, nApi dIrghamadIrgham;evametaishcaturbhiH parimANapratiShedhairdravyadharmaH pratiShidvaH, na dravyaM tadakSharamityarthaH /
astu tarhi lohito guNaH, tato 'pyanyadalohitam;Agneyo guNo lohitaH;bhavatu tarhyapyAM snehanam, na, asnehanam;astu tarhicchAyA, sarvathApyanirdeshyatvAt, chAyAyA apyanyadacchAyam;astu tarhi tamaH, atamaH;bhavatu vAyustarhi, avAyuH;bhavettarhyAkAsham, anAkAsham;bhavatu tarhi saN^gAtmakaM jatuvat, asaN^gam'raso 'stu tarhi, arasam';tathA gandho 'stvagandham;astu tarhi cakShuH, acakShuShkam-na hi cakShurasya karaNaM vidyate 'to 'cakShuShkam;"pashyatyacakShuH"iti mantravarNAt /
tathAshrotram;"sa shR^iNotyakarNaH"iti;bhavatu tarhi vAgavAk;tathAmanaH;tathAtejaskam-avidyamAnaM tejo 'sya tadatejaskam;na hi tejo 'gnyAdiprakAshavadasya vidyate;aprANam-AdhyAtmiko vAyuHpratiShidhyate 'prANamiti;mukhaM tarhi dvAraM tadamukham;amAnnam-mIyate yena tanmAtram amAtraM mAtrArUpaM tanna bhavati, na tena kiJNcinmIyate;astu tarhicchidravat, anantaram-nAsyAntaramasti;sambhavet tarhi bahistasya, abAhyam;astu tarhi bhakShayitR^i tat na tadashnAti kJNcina;bhavettarhi bhakShyaM kasyacit, na tadashnAti kashcana;sarvavisheShaNarahitamityarthaH;ekamevAdvitIyaM hi tat kena kiM vishiShyate // 8 //  anekavisheShaNapratiShedhaprayAsAdastitvaM tAvadakSharasyopagamitaM shrutyA;tathApi lokabudvimapekShyA shaN^kyate yataH, ato 'stitvAyAnumAnaM pramANamupanyasyati-

START BrhUp 3,8.9

#<etasya vA akSharasya prashAsane gArgi sUryacandramasau vidhR^itau tiShThataH |

BrhUpBh_3,8.9 etasya vA akSharasya;yadetadadhigatamakSharaM sarvAntaraM sAkShAdaparokShAdbrahma, ya AtmA ashanAyAdidharmAtItaH, etasya vA akSharasya prashAsane-yathA rAj~naH prashAsane rAjyamasphuTitaM niyataM vartate, evamatasyAkSharasya prashAsane he gArgi sUryAcandramaso ahorAtrayorlokapradIpau, tAdarthyena prashAsitrA tAbhyAM nirvatyamAnalokaprayojanavij~nAnavatA nirmitau ca, syAtAM sAdhAraNasarvaprANiprakAshopakArakatvAllaukikapradIpavat /
tasmAdasti tad yena vidhR^itAvIshvarau svatantrau sastau nirmitau tiShThato niyatadeshakAlanimittodayAstamayavR^iddhikShayAbhyAM vartete;tadastyevametayoH prashAsitrakSharam, pradIpakartR^ividhArayitR^ivat /
etasya vA akSharasya prashAsane gArgI dyAvApR^ithivI ca sAvayavatvAt sphuTanasvabhAve api satyau gurutvAt patanasvabhAve saMyuktatvAd viyogasvabhAve cetanAvadabhimAnidevatAdhiShThitatvAt svatantre api etasyAkSharasya prashAsane vartete vidhR^ite tiShThataH;etaddhyakSharaM sarvavyavasthAsetuH sarvamaryAdAvidharaNam, ato nAsyAkSharasya prashAsanaM dyAvApR^ithivyAvatikrAmataH;tasmAt siddhamasyAstitvamakSharasya avyabhicAri hi talliN^gam, yad dyAvApR^ithivyau niyate vartete;cetanAvantaM prashAsitAramasaMsAriNamantareNa naitad yuktam /
"yena dyaurugrA pR^ithivI ca dR^iShTA"iti mantravarNAt /
etasya vA akSharasya prashAsane gArgi, nimeShA muhUrtA ityete kAlAvayavAH sarvasya atItAnAgatavartamAnasya janimataH kalayitAraH - yathA loke prabhuNA niyato gaNakaH sarvamAyaM vyayaM cApramatto gaNayati, tathA prabhusthAnIya eShAM kAlAvayavAnAM niyantA /
tathA prAcayaH prAgaJNcanAH pUrvadiggamanA nadyaH syandante sravanti shvetebhyo himavadAdibhyaH parvatebhyo giribhyo gaN^gAdyA nadyastAshca yathA pravartitA eva niyatAH pravartante 'nyathApi pravartitumutsahantyaH, tadetalliN^gaM prashAstuH /
pratIcyo 'nyAH pratIcIM dishamaJNcanti sindhvAdyA nadyaH, anyAshca yAM yAM dishamanupravR^ittAstAM tAM na vyabhicaranti;tacca siN^gam /
kiJNca dadato hiraNyAdIn prayacchata AtmapIDAM kurvato 'pi pramANaj~nA api manuShyAH prashaMsanti;tatra yacca dIyate, ye ca dadati, ye ca pratigR^ihmanti, teShAmihaiva samAgamo vilayashcAnvakSho dR^ishyate;adR^iShTastu paraH samAgamaH, tathApi manuShyA dadatAM dAnaphalena saMyogaM pashyantaH pramANaj~natayA prashaMsanti; tacca, karmaphalena saMyojayitari kartuH karmaphalavibhAgaj~ne prashAstaryasati na syAt;dAnakriyAyAH pratyakShavinAshitvAt;tasmAdasti dAnakartR^iNAM phalena saMyojayitA /
apUrvamiti cet? tatsadbhAve pramANAnupapatteH prashasturapIti cet /
na, AgamatAtparyasya siddhatvAt;avocAma dyAgamasya vastuparatvAt /
kiJNcAnyat, apUrvakalpanAyAM cArthApatteH, kShayo 'nyathaivopapatteH /
sevAphalasya sevyAt prAptidarshanAt /
sevAyAshca kriyAtvAt, tatsAmAnyAcca vAgadAnahomAdInAM sevyAd IshvarAdeH phalaprAptirupapadyate dR^iShTakriyAdharmasAmarthyamaparityajyaiva phalaprAptikalpanopapattau dR^iShTakriyAdharmasAmarthyaparityAgo na nyAyyaH /
kalpanAdhikyAcca, IshvaraH kalpvo 'pUrvA vA? tatra kriyAyAshca svabhAvaH sevyAt phalaprAptirdR^iShTA na tvapUrvAt;na cApUrvaM dR^iShTam;tatrApUrvamadR^iShTaM kalpayitavyaM tasya ca phaladAtR^itve sAmarthyam, sAmarthye ca sati dAnaM cAbhyadhikamiti /
iha tu Ishvarasya sevyasya sadbhAvamAtraM kalpyam, na tu phaladAnasAmarthyaM dAtR^itvaM ca, sevyAt phalaprAptidarshanAt /
anumAnaM ca darshitam -'dyAvApR^ithivyau vidhR^ite tiShThataH'ityAdi /

tathA pitaro 'pi tadarthaM darvI darvIhomamanvAyattA anugatA ityarthaH, samAnaM sarvamanyat //9//

START BrhUp 3,8.10

BrhUpBh_3,8.11 tad vA etadakSharaM gArgi adR^iShTaM na kenacid dR^iShTam, aviShayatvAt svayaM tu draShTR^i dR^iShTisvarUpatvAt /

START BrhUp 3,8.12

#<sA hovAca -- brAhmaNA bhagavantas tad eva bahu manyadhvaM yad asmAn namaskAreNa mucyedhvam |

BrhUpBh_3,9.7 katame ShaDiti;ta evAgnyAdayo vasutvena paThitAshcandramasaM nakShatrANi ca varjayitvA ShaD bhavanti - ShaTasaMkhyAvishiShTAH, trayastriMshadAdi yaduktamidaM sarvam, eta eva ShaD bhavanti sarvo hi vasvAdivistara eteShveva ShaTasvantarbhavatItyarthaH //7//

BrhUpBh_3,9.8 katame te trayo devA iti;ima eva trayo lokA iti - pR^ithivImagniM caikokR^ityaiko devaH, antarikShaM vAyuM caikIkR^itya tR^itIyaH - te eva trayo devA iti /
eShu. hi yasmAt, triShu deveShu sarve devA antarbhavanti tena ta eva devAstrayaH - ityeSha nairuktAnAM keShAJNcit pakShaH /

START BrhUp 3,9.9

BrhUpBh_3,9.9 tattatrAhushcodayanti - yadayaM vAyureka ivaiva eka eva pavate ;atha kathamadhyardha iti? yadasminnidaM sarvamadhyArdhnot-asmin vAyau satIdaM sarvamadhyArdhnodadhi R^iddhiM prApnoti, tenAdhyardha iti /

START BrhUp 3,9.10

#<pR^ithivy eva yasyAyatanam agnir loko mano jyotir yo vai taM puruShaM vidyAt sarvasyAtmanaH parAyaNaM sa vai veditA syAt |

BrhUpBh_3,9.10 pR^ithivyeva yasya devasyAyatanamAshrayaH, agnirloko yasya - lokayatyaneneti lokaH, pashyatIti - agninA pashyatItyarthaH /
manojyotiH manasA jyotiShA saMkalpavikalpAdikAryaM karoti yaH, so 'yaM manojyotiH /
pR^ithivIsharIro 'gnidarshano manasA saMkalpayitA pR^ithivyabhimAnI kAryakaraNasaMghAtavAn deva ityarthaH /
ya evaM vishiShTaM vai taM puruShaM vidyAd vijAnIyAt sarvasyAtmana AdhyAtmikasya kAryakaraNasaMghAtasya AtmanaH paramayanaM para AshrayastaM parAyaNam /
mAtR^ijena tvaÇmAMsarudhirarUpeNa kShetrasthAnIyena bIjasthAnIyasya pitR^ijasya asthimajjAshukrarUpasya paramayanam, karaNAtmanashca, sa vai veditA syAt /
ya etadevaM vetti sa vai veditA paNDitaH syAdityAbhiprAyaH /
yAj~navalkya tvaM tamajAnanneva paNDitAbhimAnItyamiprAyaH /
yadi tadvij~nAne pANDityaM labhyate, veda vai ahaM taM puruShaM sarvasyAtmanaH parAyaNaM yamAttha yaM kathayasi tamahaM veda /
tatra shAkalyasya vacanaM draShTyam-yadi tvaM vettha taM puruSham, brUhikiMvisheShaNo 'sau? saH-ya evAyaM shArIraH- pArdhivAMshe sharIre bhavaH shArIro mAtR^ijakoshatrayarUpa ityarthaH, sa e, devaH, yastvayA pR^iShTaH, he shAkalya /
kintvasti tatra vaktavyaM visheShaNAntaram, tad vadaiva pR^icchaivetyarthaH, he shAkalya /
sa evaM prakShobhito 'marpavashaga Aha-tottrAdinta iva gajaH- tasya devasya sharIrasya kA devatA? yasmAnniShpadyate yaH sA tasya devatetyasmin prakaraNe vivakShitaH;amR^itamiti hovAca /
amR^itamiti yo bhuktasyAnnasya raso mAtR^ijasya lohitasya niShpattihetuH /
tasmAdvayannarasAllohitaM niShpadyate striyAM shritam, tatashca lohitamayaM sharIraM bIjAshrayam /
samAnamanyat //10//

BrhUpBh_3,9.20 kindevataH kA devatAsya tava digbhR^itasya /

BrhUpBh_3,9.24 kindevato 'syAM dishyasIti /
meroH samantato vasatAmavyabhicArAdUrdhvA dig dhruvetyucyate /
agnidevata iti - UrdhvAyAM hi prakAshabhUyastvam, prakAshashcAgniH /
so 'gniH kasmin pratiShThita iti? vAcIti /
kasminni vAk pratiShThiteti? hR^idaya iti /
tatra yAj~navalkyaH sarvAsu dikShu vipasR^itena hR^idayena sarvAM disha AtmatvenAbhisampannaH;sadevAH sapratiShThitA disha AtmabhUtAstasya nAmarUpakarmAtmabhUtasya yAj~navalkyasya /
yad rUpaM tat prAcyA dishA saha hR^idayabhUtaM yAj~navalkyasya /
yat kevalaM karma putrotpAdanalakShaNaM ca yAnasahitaM ca sahaphenAdhiShThAtrIbhishca devatAbhirdakShiNApratIcyudIcyaH karmaphalAtmikA hR^idayameva ApannAstasya, dhruvayA dishA saha nAma sarvaM vAgdvAreNa hR^idayameva Apannam /
etAvaddhIdaM sarvam, yaduta rUpaM vA karma vA nAma veti tat sarvaM hR^idayameva, tat sarvAtmakaM hR^idayaM pR^icchyate - kasminnu hR^idayaM pratiShThitamiti //24//

START BrhUp 3,9.25

#<ahalliketi hovAca yAj~navalkyaH |

__________


BrhUpBh_3,9.25 ahalliketi hovAca yAj~navalkyaH, nAmAntareNa sambodhanaM kR^itavAn /

START BrhUp 3,9.26

#<kasmin nu tvaM cAtmA ca pratiShThitau stha iti |
prANa iti |
kasmin nu prANaH pratiShThita iti |
apAna iti |
kasmin nv apAnaH pratiShThita iti |
vyAna iti |

na riShyati |
etAny aShTAv AyatanAny aShTau lokA add. aShTau devA aShTau puruShAH |

__________


BrhUpBh_3,9.26 kasminnu tvaM ca sharIramAtmA ca tava hR^idayaM pratiShThitau stha iti? prANa iti;dehAtmAnau prANe pratiShThitau syAtAM prANavR^ittau /
kasminnu prANAH pratiShThita iti apAna iti - sApi prANavR^ittiH prAgeva preyAt apAnavR^ittyA cenna nigR^ihyeta /
kasminnvapAnaH pratiShThita iti? vyAna iti - sApyapAnavR^ittiradha eva yAyAt prANavR^ittishca prAgeva, madhyasthayA cedvyAnavR^ittyA na nigR^ihyeta /
kasminnu vyAnaH pratiShThita iti? udAna iti - sarvAstisro 'pi vR^ittaya udAne kIlasthAnIye cenna niruddhA, viShvageveyuH /
kasminnUdAnaH pratiShThita iti? samAna iti - samAnapratiShThA hyetAH sarvA vR^ittayaH /
etaduktaM bhavati - sharIrahR^idayavAyavo 'nyonyapratiShThAH, saN^ghAtena niShatA vartante vij~nAnamayArthaprayuktA iti /
sarvametad yena niyataM yasmin pratiShThitamAkAshAntamotaM ca protaM ca, tasya nirupAdhikasya sAkShAdaparokShAd brahmaNo nirdeshaH katavya ityayamArambhaH /
sa eShaH - sayo netinetIti nirdiShTo madhukANDe, eSha saH /
so 'yamAtmAgR^ihyo na gR^ihyaH /
katham? yasmAt sarvakAryadharmAtItaH, tasmAdagR^ihyaH /
kutaH? yasmAnna hi gR^ihyate /
yaddhi karaNagocaraM vyAkR^itaM vastu, tad grahaNagocaram. idaM tu tadviparItamAtmatattvam /
tathAshIryaH;yaddhi mUrtaM saMhataM sharIrAdi tacchIryate;ayaM tu tadviparIto 'to na hi shIryate /
tathAsaN^go mUrto mUrtAntareNa sambadhyamAnaH sajyate 'yaM ca tadviparIto 'to na hi sajyate /
tathAsito 'baddhaH, yaddhi mUrta tad vadhyate;ayaM tu tadviparItatvAdabaddhatvAnna vyathate, ato na riShyati - grahaNavisharaNasambandhakAryadharmarahitatvAnna riShyati na hiMsAmApadyate na vinashyatItyarthaH /
kramamatikramya aupaniShadasya puruShasya AkhyAyikAto 'pasR^itya shrutyA svena  rUpeNa tvarayA nirdeshaH kR^itaH, tataH punarAkhyAyikAmevAshrityAha - etAni yAnyuktAnyaShTAvAyatanAni'pR^ithivyeva yasyAyatanam'ityevamAdIni, aShTau lokA agnilokAdayaH, aShTau devAH amR^itamiti hovAca ityevamAdayaH, aShTau puruShAH sharIraH puruShaH, ityAdayaH, sa yaH kashcit tAn puruShA¤shArIraprabhR^itIn niruhya nishcayenohya garmayitvAShTacatuShkabhedena lokasthitimupapAdyaH, punaH prAcIdigAdidvAreNa pratyuhya upasaMhR^itya svAtmani hR^idaye 'tyakrAmadatikrAntavAnupAdhidharma hR^idayAdyAtmatvam;svenaivAtmanA vyavasthito ya aupaniShadaH puruSho 'shanAyAdivarjitaH upaniShatsveva vij~neyo nAnyapramANagamyaH, taM tvA tvAM vidyAbhimAninaM puruShaM pR^icchAmi /
taM ced yadi me na vivakShyasi vispaShTaM na kathayiShyasi, mUrdhA te vipatiShyatItyAha yAj~navalkyaH /
taM tvaupaniShadaM puruShaM shAkalyo na mene ha na vij~nAtavAn kila tasya ha mUrdhA vipapAta vipatitaH /
samAptAkhyAyakA /
shrutevacanaM taM ha na mena ityAdi /
kiM cApi hAsya parimoShiNastaskarA asthInyapi saMskArArtha shiShyenIyamAnAni gR^ihAn pratyapajahaH-apahratavantaH kinnimittam? anyad dhanaM nIyamAnaM manyamAnAH /
pUrvavR^ittA hyAkhyAyikeha sUcitA /
aShTAdhyAya kila shAkalyena yAj~navalkyasya samAnAnta eva kila saMvAdo nivR^ittaH;tatra yAj~navalkyena shApo dattaH-pure 'tithye mariShyasi na te 'sthIni ca na gR^ihAn prApsyantIti /
sa ha tathaiva mamAra /
tasya hApyanvaH manyamAnAH parimoShiNo 'thInyapajahaH;tasmAnnopavAdI syAduta hyevaMvit paro bhavatIti /
saipA AkhyAyikA AcArArtha sUcitA vidyAstutaye ceha //26//

yasya neti, netItyanyapratiShedhadvAreNa brahmaNo nirdeshaH kR^itaH, tasya vidhimukhena kathaM nirdeshaH kartavyaH, iti punarAkhyAyikAmeva AshrityAha mUlaM ca jagato vaktavyamiti /
AkhyAyikAsambandhastvavrahyavido brAhmaNAJNjitvA godhanaM irtavyamiti /
nyAyaM matvAha--

START BrhUp 3,9.27

#<atha hovAca -- brAhmaNA bhagavanto yo vaH kAmayate sa mA pR^icchatu |

BrhUpBh_3,9.27 atha hovAca /

START BrhUp 3,9.28:1

#<tAn haitaiH shlokaiH papraccha --

BrhUpBh_3,9.28:3 evaM mAMsAnyasya puruShasya, vanaspatesyAni shakarANi shakalAnItyarthaH /
kinATaM vR^ikShasya, kinATaM nAma shakalebhyo 'bhyantaraM valkalarUpaM kAShThasaMlagnam, tat snAva puruShasya;tat sthiram-tacca kinATaM snAvavad dR^iDhaM hi tat;asthIni puruShasya, snAvno 'ntarato 'sthIni bhavanti;tathA kinATasyAbhyantarato dAruNi kAShThAni;majjA, majjeva vanaspateH puruShasya ca majjopamA kR^itA, majjAyA upamAmajjopamA, nAnyo visheSho 'stItyarthaH;yathA vanaspatermajjA tathA puruShasya, yathA puruShasya tathA vanaspateH //3//

BrhUpBh_3,9.28:4 yad yadi vR^ikSho vR^ikNashchinno rohati punaH punaH prarohatiprAdurbhavati mUlAt punarnavataraH pUrvasmAdabhinavataraH;yadetasmAd visheNAt prAg vanaspateH puruShasya ca, sarvaM sAmAnyamavagatam;ayaM tu vanaspatau visheSho dR^ishyate yacchinnasyaprarohaNam;na tu puruShe mR^ityunA vR^ikNe punaH prarohaNaM dR^ishyate;bhavitavyaM ca kutashcitprarohaNena;tasmAda vaH pR^icchAmi-martyo manuShyaH svinmR^ityunA vR^ikNaH kasmAnmUlAt prarohati? mR^itasya puruShasya kutaH prarohaNamityarthaH //4//

START BrhUp 3,9.28:7-8

#<jAta eva na jAyate ko nv enaM janayet punaH |

#<jAta eva na jAyate ko nv enaM janayet punaH |
