BrhUpBh_3,9.28:7-8. jAta eveti manyadhvaM yadi kimanna praShTavyamiti-aniShyamANasya hi sambhavaH praShTavyaH, na jAtasya, ayaM tu jAta evAtopasmin viShaye prashna eva nopa'dyata iti cet-na, kiM tarhi? mR^itaH punarapi jAyata evAnyathAkR^itAbhyAgamakR^itanAshaprasaN^gAt;ato vaH pR^icchAmi-ko nvenaM mR^itaM punarjanayet? tatra vijaj~nurbrAhmaNAH-yato mR^itaH punaH prarohati jagato mUlaM na vij~nAtaM brAhmaNaiH;ato brahmiShThatvAd hratA gAvaH;yAj~navalkyena jitAbrAhmaNAH /
samAptA AkhyAyikA /
yajjagato mUlam, yena ca shabdena sAkShAd vyapadishyate brahma, yad yAj~navalkyo brAhmaNAn pR^iShTavAMstat svena rUpeNa shrutirasyabhyamAha-vij~nAnaM vij~naptirvij~nAnam, tacca Anandam, na viShayavij~nAnavad duHkhAnuvidvam, kiM tarhi? prasannaM shivamatulamanAyAsaMnityatR^iptame karasamityarthaH. kiM tad brahma umayavisheNavad rAtiH-rAteH paShThayatha prathamA, dhanasyetyarthaH, dhanasya dAtuH karmakR^ito yajamAnasya parAyaNaM parA gatiH karmaphalasya pradAtR^i /
kiJNca vyutthAyaiShaNAbhyasyasminneva brahmANi tiShThatyakarmakR^it, tad brahma vettIti tadvicca;tasya-tiShThamAnasya ca tadvidaH, brahmavida ityarthaH, parAyaNamiti /
atredaM vicAryate-Anandashabdo loke sukhavAcI prasidvaH, atra ca brahmaNo visheShaNatvena AnandashabdaH shrUyate-AnandaM brahmeti /
shrutyantare ca-"Anando brahmeti vyajAnAt""AnandaM brahmaNo vidvAn" "yadeSha AkAsha Anando na syAta" "yo vai bhUmA tat sukham"iti ca;"eSha parama AnandaH"ityevamAdyAH /
saMvedye ca sukhe AnandashabdaH prasidvaH brahmAnandashca yadi saMvedyaH syAd yuktA ete brahmaNyAnandashabdAH /
nanu ca shrutiprAmANyAt saMvedyAnandasvarUpameva brahma, kiM tatra vicAryam? iti na, virudvashrutivAkyadarshanAt--satyam, Anandashabdo brahmaNi shrUyate, vij~nAnapratiShedhashcaikatve--"yatra tvasya sarvamAtmaivAbhUttatkena kaM pashyettatkena kaM vijAnIyAt" "yatra nAnyat pashyati nAnyacchR^iNoti nAnyadvijAnAti sa bhUmA" "prAj~nenAtmanA sampariShvakto na bAhyaM kiJNcana veda"ityAdi;virudvashrutivAkyadarshanAt tena kartavyo vicAraH;tasmAd yuktaM vedavAkyarthanirNayAya vicArayitum /
mokShavAdivipratipatteshca-sAMkhyA vaisheShikAshca  mokShavAdino nAsti mokShe sukhaM saMvedyamityevaM vipratipannAH;anye nigtishayaM sukhaM svasaMvadyamiti;kiM tAvad yuktam? AnandAdishravaNAt"jakShatakrIDan ramamANaH"'sayAda pitR^ilokakAmo bhavata' "yaH sarvaj~naH sarvavit""sarvAn kAmAn samashnute"ityAdishrutibhyo mokShe sukhaM saMvedyamiti /
nanvekatve kArakavimAgamAvAd vij~nAnAnupapattiH, kriyAyAshcAne kakArakrasAdhyAtvAd vij~nAnasya ca kriyAtvAt /
naiSha doShaH;shabdaprAmANyAd bhaved vij~nAnamAnandaviShaye;"vij~nAnamAnandam"ityAdIni AnandasvarUpasyAsaMvedyatve 'nupapannAni vacanAnItyavocAma /
nanu vacanenApyagneH shaityamudakasya cauShbhyaM na kriyate eva, j~nApakatvAd vacanAnAm /
na ca deshAntare 'gniH shIta iti shakyate j~nApayitum;agamye vA deshAntare uShNamudakamiti /
na, pratyagAtmanyAnandavij~nAnadarshanAt;na'vij~nAnamAnandam'itvevamAdInAM vacanAnAM shIto 'gnirityAdivAkyavat pratyakShAdivirudvArthapratipAdakatvAm /
anubhUyate tvavirudvArthatA;sukhyahamiti sukhAtmakamAtmAnaM svayameva vedayate;tasmAt sutarAM pratyakShAvirudvArthatA;tasmAdAnandaM brahma vij~nAnAtmakaM sat svayameva vedayate /
tathA AnandapratipAdikAH shrutayaH samaJNjasAH syuH'jakShat krIDan ramamANaH' ityevamAdyAH pUrvoktAH /
na, kAryakaraNAbhAve 'nupapattervij~nAnasya-sharIraviyogo hi mokSha AtyantikaH;sharIrabhAve ca karaNAnupapattiH, AshrayAbhAvAt;tatashca vij~nAnAnupattiH, AkAryakaraNatvAt;dehadyabhAve ca vij~nAnotpattau sarveShAM kAryakaraNopAdAnAnarthakyaprasaN^gaH /
ekatvavirodhAcca-paraM ced brahma AnandAtmakamAtmAnaM nityavij~nAnatvAnnityameva vijAnIyAt, tanna, saMsAryapi saMsAravinirmuktaH svAbhAvyaM pratipadyeta;jalAshaya ivodakAJNjaliH kShipto na pR^ithaktvena vyavatiShThate AnandAtmakabrahmavij~nAnAya, tadA mukta AnandAtmakamAtmAnaM vedayate ityetadanarthakaM vAkyam /
atha brahmAnandamanyAH san mukto vedayate, pratyagAtmAnaM ca, ahamasmyAnandasvarUpa iti, tadaikatvavirodhaH, tathA ca sati sarvashrutivirodhaH, tR^itIyA ca kalpanA nopapadyate /
kiJNcAnyat, brahmaNashca nirantarAtmAnandavij~nAne vij~nAnAvij~nAnakalpanAnarthakyam;nirantaraM cedAtmAnandaviShayaM brahmaNo vij~nAnam, tadeva tasya svabhAva ityAtmAnandaM vijAnAtIti kalpanAnupapannA;atadvij~nAnaprasaN^ge hi kalpanAyA arthavattvam, yathA AtmAnaM paraM ca vettIti, na hIShvAdyAsaktamanaso nairantaryeNoShuj~nAnAj~nAnakalpanAyA arthavattvam /
atha vicchinnamAtmAnandaM vijAnAti-vij~nAnasya  Atmavij~nAnacchidre anyaviShayatvaprasaN^gaH;Atmanashya vikriyAvattvaM tatashcAnityatvaprasaN^gaH;tasmAd vij~nAnamAnandamiti svarUpAnvAkhyAnaparaiva shrutiH, nAtmAnandasaMvedyatvArtha /
'jakShat krIDan'ityAdishrutivirodho 'saMvedyatva iti cet! na;sarvAtmaikatve yathAprAptAnuvAditvAt-muktasya sarvAtmabhAve sati yatra kvacid yogiShu deveShu vA jakShaNAdi prAptam, tad yathAprAptamevAnUdyate-tattasyaiva sarvAtmabhAvAditi sarvAtmabhAvamokShastutaye /
yathAprAptAnuvaditve duHkhitvamapIti cet-yogyAdiShu yathAprAptajakShaNAdivat sthAvarAdiShu yathAprAptaduHkhitvamapIti cet! na, nAmarUpakR^itakAryakaraNopAdhisamparkajanitabhrAntyadhyAropitatvAt sukhitvaduHkhitvAdivisheShasyeti parihratametat sarvam /
virudvashrutInAM ca viShayamavocAma /
tasmAt"eSho 'sya parama AnandaH"itivat sarvAShyAnandavAkyAni draShTavyAni //28//

iti tR^itIyAdhyAye navamaM shAkalyabrAhmaNam //1 //
iti bR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadbhAShye tR^itIyo 'dhyAyaH //3//

ADHYAYA 4





janako ha vaideha AsAJNcakre /
asya sambandhaH-  sharIrAdyAnaShTau puruShAnniruhya, pratyuhya punarhR^idaye, digbhedanena ca punaH paJNcadhA vyAhya, hR^idaye pratyUhya, hR^idayaM sharIraM ca punaranyonyapratiShThaM prANAdipaDhtavR^ityAtmake samAnAkhye jagadAtmanu sUtra upasaMhR^itya, jagadAtmani sUtra upasaMhR^itya, jagadAtmAnaMsharIrahR^idayasUtrAvasthamatikrAntavAn ya aupaniShadaH puruSho neti netIti vyapadiShTaH, sa sAkShAJNcopAdAnakAraNasvarUpeNa ca nirdiShTaH 'vij~nAnamAnandam' iti /
tasyaiva vAgAdidevatAdvAreNa punaradhigamaH kartavya ityadhigamanopAyAntarArtho 'yamArambho brAhmaNadvayasya /
AkhyAyikA tvAcArapradarshanArthA-



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 4,1.1

#<janako ha vaideha AsAM cakre |
atha ha yAj~navalkya AvavrAja |
taM hovAca -- yAj~navalkya kim artham acArIH pashUn icchan aNvantAnIti |
ubhayam eva saMrAD iti hovAca || BrhUp_4,1.1 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,1.1 janako ha vaideha AsAJNcakre AsanaM kR^itavAnAsthAyikAM dattavAnityarthaH, darshanakAmebhyo rAj~naH /
atha ha tasminnavasare yAj~navalkyaH AvavrAja-AgatavAnAtmano yogakShemArtham, rAj~no vA vivadiShAM dR^iShTvAnugrahArtham /
tamAgataM yaj~navalkyaM yathAvat pUjAM kR^itvovAca hoktavAJNjanakaH he yAj~navalkya kimartham acArIH-Agato 'si? kiM pashUnicchan punarapi, AhosvidaNvantAn sUkShmAntAn sUkShmavastunirNayAntAn prashnAn mattaH shrotumicchanniti /
ubhayameva pashUn prashnAMshca he samrAT-samrADiti vAjapeyayAjino liN^gam ; yashca Aj~nayA rAjyaM prashAsti, samrAT ; tasyA mantraNaM he samrADiti ; samastasya vA bhAratasya varShasya rAjA //4,1.1//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 4,1.2

#<yat te kashcid abravIt tac chR^iNavAmeti |
abravIn me jitvA shailiniH -- vAg vai brahmeti |
yathA mAtR^imAn pitR^imAn AcAryavAn brUyAt tathA tac chailinir abravId vAg vai brahmeti |
avadato hi kiM syAd iti |
abravIt tu te tasyAyatanaM pratiShThAm |
na me 'bravId iti |
ekapAd vA etat samrAD iti |
sa vai no brUhi yAj~navalkya |
vAg evAyatanam AkAshaH pratiShThA praj~nety enad upAsIta |
kA praj~natA yAj~navalkya |
vAg eva samrAD iti hovAca |
vAcA vai samrAD bandhuH praj~nAyate |
R^igvedo yajurvedaH sAmavedo 'tharvAN^girasa itihAsaH purANaM vidyA upaniShadaH shlokAH sUtrANy anuvyAkhyAnAni vyAkhyAnAnIShTaM hutam AshitaM pAyitam ayaM ca lokaH parash ca lokaH sarvANi ca bhUtAni vAcaiva saMrAT praj~nAyante |
vAg vai samrAT paramaM brahma |
nainaM vAg jahAti |
sarvANy enaM bhUtAny abhikSharanti |
devo bhUtvA devAn apyeti |
ya evaM vidvAn etad upAste |
hastyR^iShabhaM sahasraM dadAmIti hovAca janako vaidehaH |
sa hovAca yAj~navalkyaH -- pitA me 'manyata nAnanushiShya hareteti || BrhUp_4,1.2 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,1.2 kintu yatte tubhyaM kashcidabravIdAcAryo 'nekAcAryo 'nekAcAryasevI hi bhavAMstacchR^iNavAmeti /
itara Aha - abravadIduktavAnme mamA'cAryo jitvA nAmataH shilinasyApatyaM shailinirvAgvai brahmeti vAgdevatA brahmeti /
Ahetapo yathA mAtR^imAnmAtA yasya vidyate putrasya samyaganushAstryanushAsanakartrI sa mAtR^imAn /
ata UrdhvaM pitA yasyAnushAstA sa pitR^imAn /
upanayanAdUrdhvamA samAvartanAdAcAryo yasyAnushAstA sa AcAryavAn /
evaM shuddhitrayahetusaMyuktaH sa sAdhAdAcAryaH svayaM na kadAcidapu prAmANAdvyabhicarati sa yathA brUyAcchiShyAya tathAsau jitvA shailiniruktavAnvAgvai brahmeti /
avadato hi kiM syAditi /
na hi mUkasyehArthamamutrArthaM vA kiJNcana syAt /
kintvabravIduktavAste tubhyaM tasya brahmaNa AyatanaM pratiShThAM ca /
AyatanaM nAma sharIram /
pratiShThA triShvapi kAleShu ya AshrayaH /
Ahetaro na me 'bravIditi /
itara Aha-yadyevamekapAdvA etadekaH pAdo yasya brahmaNastadidamekapAdbrahma tribhiH pAdaiH shUnyamupAsyamAnamapi na phalAya bhavatItyarthaH /
yadyevaM sa tvaM vidvAnsanno 'smabhyaM brUhi he yAj~navalkyeti /
sa cA'ha-vAgevA'yatanaM vAgdevasya brahmaNo vAgeva karaNamAyatanaM sharIramAkAsho 'vyAkR^itAkhyaH pratiShThotpattisthitilayakAleShu /
praj~netyenadupAsIta praj~netIyamupaniShadbrahmaNashcaturthaH pAdaH praj~neti kR^itvainadbrahmopAsIta /
kA praj~natA yAj~navalkya ki svayameva praj~nota praj~nAnimittam /
yathA'yatanapratiShThe brahmaNo vyatirikte tadvatkim /
na, katha tarhi, vAgeva samrADiti hovAca vAgeva praj~neti hovAcoktavAnna vyatiriktA praj~nAti /
kathaM punarvAgeva praj~neti, ucyate-vAcA vai samrADbandhuH praj~nAyate 'smAkaM bandhurityukte praj~nAyakate bandhustathargvaidAdi /
iShTaM yAganimitta dharmajAtaM hutaM homanimittaM ca /
AshitamannadAnimittaM pAyitaM pAnadAnanimittamayaM ca loka idaM ca janma parashca lokaH pratipattavyaM ca janma sarvANi ca bhUtAni vAcaiva samrATpraj~nAyante 'to vAgvaisamrATparamaM brahma nAnaM yathoktabrahmavidaM vAgjahAti /
sarvANyenaM bhUtAnyabhikSharanti balidAnAdibhiriha /
devo bhUtvA punaH sharIrapAtottarakAlaM devAnapyetyapigacchati ya evaM vidvAnetadupAste vidyAniShkriyArthaM hastitulya R^iShabho hastyR^iShabho yasmingosahasretaddhastR^iShabhaM sahasraM dadAmIti hovAca janako vaidehaH /
sa hovAca yAj~navalkyaH /
ananushiShya shiShyaM kR^itArthamakR^itvA shiShyAddhanaM na hareteti me mama pitAmanyata mamApyayamevAbhiprAyaH //4,1.2//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 4,1.3

#<yad eva te kashcid abravIt tac chR^iNavAmeti |
abravIn ma udaN^kaH shaulbAyanaH |
prANo vai brahmeti |
yathA mAtR^imAn pitR^imAn AcAryavAn brUyAt tathA tac chaulbAyano 'bravIt prANo vai brahmeti |
aprANato hi kiM syAd iti |
abravIt tu te tasyAyatanaM pratiShThAm |
na me 'bravId iti |
ekapAd vA etat samrAD iti |
sa vai no brUhi yAj~navalkya |
prANa evAyatanam AkAshaH pratiShThA |
priyam ity enad upAsIta |
kA priyatA yAj~navalkya |
prANa eva samrAD iti hovAca |
prANasya vai samrAT kAmAyAyAjyaM yAjayati |
apratigR^ihyasya pratigR^ihNAti |
api tatra vadhAshaN^kA bhavati yAM disham eti prANasyaiva samrAT kAmAya |
prANo vai samrAT paramaM brahma |
nainaM prANo jahAti |
sarvANy enaM bhUtAny abhikSharanti |
devo bhUtvA devAn apyeti |
ya evaM vidvAn etad upAste |
hastyR^iShabhaM sahasraM dadAmIti hovAca janako vaidehah |
sa hovAca yAj~navalkyaH -- pitA me 'manyata nAnanushiShya hareteti || BrhUp_4,1.3 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,1.3 yadeva te kashcidabravIdudaN^ko nAmataH shulbasyApatyaM shaulbasyApatyaM shaulbAyano 'bravItprANo vai brahmeti prANo vAyurdevatA pUrvavat /
prANa evA'yanamAkAshaH pratiShThopaniShatpriyamityenadupAsIta /
kathaM punaH priyatvaM, prANasya vai he samrATkAmAya prANasyArthAyAyAjyaM yAjayati patitAdikamapyapratigR^ihyasyApyugrAdeH pratigR^ihNAtyapi tatra tasyAM dishi vadhanimittamAshaN^kaM vadhAshaN^ketyartho yAM dishameti taskarAdyAkIrNAM ca tasyAM dishi ba dhAshahkA taccaitatsarvaM prANasya priyatve bhavati prANasyaiva samrATkAmAya /
tasmAtprANo vai samrATparamaM brahma nainaM prANo jahAti /
samAnamanyat //4,1.3//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 4,1.4

#<yad eva te kashcid abravIt tac chR^iNavAmeti |
abravIn me barkur vArShNaH |
cakShur vai brahmeti |
yathA mAtR^imAn pitR^imAn AcAryavAn brUyAt tathA tad vArShNo 'bravIc cakShur vai brahmeti |
apashyato hi kiM syAd iti |
abravIt tu te tasyAyatanaM pratiShThAm |
na me 'bravId iti |
ekapAd vA etat samrAD iti |
sa vai no brUhi yAj~navalkya |
cakShur evAyatanam AkAshaH pratiShThA |
satyam ity etad upAsIta |
kA satyatA yAj~navalkya |
cakShur eva samrAD iti hovAca |
cakShuShA vai samrAT pashyantam Ahur adrAkShIr iti |
sa AhAdrAkSham iti tat satyaM bhavati |
cakShur vai samrAT paramaM brahma |
nainam cakShur jahAti |
sarvANy enaM bhUtAny abhikSharanti |
devo bhUtvA devAn apyeti |
ya evaM vidvAn etad upAste |
hastyR^iShabhaM sahasraM dadAmIti hovAca janako vaidehaH |
sa hovAca yAj~navalkyaH -- pitA me 'manyata nAnanushiShya hareteti || BrhUp_4,1.4 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,1.4 yadeva te kashcidbarkuriti nAmato vR^iShNasyApatyaM vArShNashcakShurvai brahmetyAdityo devatA cakShuShyupaniShatsatyam /
yasmAcchrotreNa shrutamanR^itamapi syAnna tu cakShuShA dR^iShTam /
tasmAdvai samrATpashyantamAhuradrAkShIstvaM hastinamiti sa cedadrAkShamityAhatatsatyameva bhavati /
yastvanyau brUyadahamashrauShamiti /
tadvyabhicarati /
yattu cakShuShA dR^iShTaM tadavyabhicAritvAtsatyameva bhavati //4,1.4//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 4,1.5

#<yad eva te kashcid abravIt tac chR^iNavAmeti |
abravIn me gardabhIvipIto bhAradvAjaH |
shrotraM vai brahmeti |
yathA mAtR^imAn pitR^imAn AcAryavAn brUyAt tathA tad bhAradvAjo 'bravIc chrotraM vai brahmeti |
ashR^iNvato hi kiM syAd iti |
abravIt tu te tasyAyatanaM pratiShThAm |
na me 'bravId iti |
ekapAd vA etat samrAD iti |
sa vai no brUhi yAj~navalkya |
shrotram evAyatanam AkAshaH pratiShThAnantam ity enad upAsIta |
kAnantatA yAj~navalkya |
disha eva samrAD iti hovAca |
tasmAd vai samrAD api yAM kAJNca dishaM gacchati naivAsyA antaM gacchati |
anantA hi dishaH |
disho vai samrAT shrotram |
shrotraM vai samrAT paramaM brahma |
nainaM shrotraM jahAti |
sarvANy enaM bhUtAny abhikSharanti |
devo bhUtvA devAn apyeti |
ya evaM vidvAn etad upAste |
hastyR^iShabhaM sahasraM dadAmIti hovAca janako vaidehaH |
sa hovAca yAj~navalkyaH -- pitA me 'manyata nAnanushiShya hareteti || BrhUp_4,1.5 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,1.5 yadeva te gardabhIvipIta iti nAmato bhAradvAjo gotrataH shrotraM vai brahmeti /
shrotre digdevatAnanta ityenadupAsIta /
kAnantatA shrotrasya /
disha eva shrotrasyA'nantyaM yasmAttasmAdvai samrATprAcImudIcAM vA yAM kAJNcidapi dishaM gacchati naivAsyA antaN^gacchati kaJNcidapu /
ato 'nantA hi dishaH /
disho vai samrATshrotram /
tasmAddigAnantyameva shrotrasyA /
Sha'nantyam //4,1.5//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 4,1.6

#<yad eva te kashcid abravIt tac chR^iNavAmeti |
abravIn me satyakAmo jAbAlaH -- mano vai brahmeti |
yathA mAtR^imAn pitR^imAn AcAryavAn brUyAt tathA taj jAbAlo 'bravIn mano vai brahmeti |
amanaso hi kiM syAd iti |
abravIt tu te tasyAyatanaM pratiShThAm |
na me 'bravId iti |
ekapAd vA etat samrAD iti |
sa vai no brUhi yAj~nAvalkya |
mana evAyatanam AkAshaH pratiShThAnanda ity enad upAsIta |
kAnandatA yAj~navalkya |
mana eva samrAD iti hovAca manasA vai samrAT striyam abhi hAryati tasyAM pratirUpaH putro jAyate |
sa AnandaH |
mano vai samrAT paramaM brahma |
nainaM mano jahAti |
sarvANy enaM bhUtAny abhikSharanti |
devo bhUtvA devAn apyeti |
ya evaM vidvAn etad upAste |
hastyR^iShabhaM sahasraM dadAmIti hovAca janako vaidehaH |
sa hovAca yAj~navalkyaH -- pitA me 'manyata nAnanushiShya hareteti || BrhUp_4,1.6 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,1.6 satyakAma iti nAmato jabAlAyA apatyaM jAbAlaH /
candramA manasi devatA /
Ananda ityupaniShati /
yasmAnmana evA'nandastasmAnmanasA vai samrATastriyamabhikAmayamAno 'bhihAryate prArthayata ityarthaH /
tasmAdyAM striyamabhikAmayamAno 'bhihAryate tasyAM pratirUpo 'nurUpaH putro jAyate sa AnandahetuH sa yena manasA nirvartyate tanmana AnandaH //4,1.6//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 4,1.7

#<yad eva te kashcid abravIt tac chR^iNavAmeti |
abravIn me vidagdhaH shAkalyaH |
hR^idayaM vai brahmeti |
yathA mAtR^imAn pitR^imAn AcAryavAn brUyAt tathA tac chAkalyo 'bravId dhR^idayaM vai brahmeti |
ahR^idayasya hi kiM syAd iti |
abravIt tu te tasyAyatanaM pratiShThAm |
na me 'bravId iti |
ekapAd vA etat samrAD iti |
sa vai no brUhi yAj~navalkya |
hR^idayam evAyatanam AkAshaH pratiShThA |
sthitir ity enad upAsIta |
kA sthititA yAj~navalkya |
hR^idayam eva samrAD iti hovAca |
hR^idayaM vai samrAT sarveShAM bhUtAnAm Ayatanam |
hR^idayaM vai samrAT sarveShAM bhUtAnAM pratiShThA |
hR^idaye hy eva samrAT sarvANi bhUtAni pratiShThitAni bhavanti |
hR^idayaM vai samrAT paramaM brahma |
nainaM hR^idayaM jahAti |
sarvANy enaM bhUtAny abhikSharanti |
devo bhUtvA devAn apyeti |
ya evaM vidvAn etad upAste |
hastyR^iShabhaM sahasraM dadAmIti hovAca janako vaidehaH |
sa hovAca yAj~navalkyaH -- pitA me 'manyata nAnanushiShya hareteti || BrhUp_4,1.7 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,1.7 vidagdhaH shAkalyo hR^idayaM vai brahmeti /
hR^idayaM vai samrATsarveShAM bhUtAnAmAyatanam /
nAmarUpakarmAtmakAni hi bhUtAni hR^idayAshrayANItyavocAma shAkalyabAhmaNe hR^idayapratiShThAnu ceti /
tasmAdvadhR^itaye hyeva samrATsravANi bhUtAni pratiShThitAni bhavanti /
tasmAddhR^idayaM sthitirityupAsIta hR^idaye ca prajApatirdevatA //4,1.7//

iti bR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadbhAShye caturthAdhyAyasya prathamaM brAhmaNam //1//

atha caturthAdhyAyasya dvitIyaM brAhmaNam

START BrhUp 4,2.1

#<janako ha vaidehaH kUrcAd upAvasarpann uvAca -- namas te 'stu yAj~navalkya |
anu mA shAdhIti |
sa hovAca yathA vai samrAN mahAntam adhvAnam eShyan rathaM vA nAvaM vA samAdadItaivam evaitAbhir upaniShadbhiH samAhitAtmAsi |
evaM vR^indAraka ADhyaH sann adhItaveda uktopaniShatka ito vimucyamAnaH kva gamiShyasIti |
nAhaM tad bhagavan veda yatra gamiShyAmIti |
atha vai te 'haM tad vakShyAmi yatra gamiShyasIti |
bravItu bhagavAn iti || BrhUp_4,2.1 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,2.1 janako ha vaidehaH /
yasmAtsavisheShaNAni sarvANi brahmANi jAnAti yAj~navalkyastasmAdAcAryakatvaM hitvA janakaH kUrcAdAsanavisheShAdutthAyopa samIpamavasarpanyAdayornipatannityarthaH /
uvAcoktavAnnamaste tubhyamastu he yAj~navalkyAnu mA shAdhyanushAdhi mAmityarthaH /
itishabdo vAkyaparisamAptyarthaH /
sa hovAca yAj~navalkyo yathA vai loke he samrADmahAntaM dIrghamadhvAnameShyangamiShyanrathaM vA sothalena gamiShyannAvaM vA jalena gamiShyansamAdadIta /
evamevaitAni brahmANyetAbhirupaniShadbhiryuktAnyupAsInaH samAhitatmAsyatyantametAbhirupaniShadbhiH saMyuktAtmAsi na kevalamupaniShatsamAhita evaM vR^indArakaH pUjyashcA'Dhyashceshvaro na daridra ityarthaH /
adhItavedo 'dhIto vedo yena sa tvamadhItaveda uktAshcopaniShada AcAryaistubhyaM sa tvamuktopaniShatka evaM sarvavibhUtatisaMpanno 'pi sanbhayayamadhyashcha eva paramAtj~nAnena vinAkR^itArtha evatAvadityarthaH /
yAvatparaM brahma na vetsi /
ito 'smAddehAdimucyamAna etAbhirtorathasthAnIyAbhiH samAhitaH kva kasmingamiShyasi kiM vastu prApsyasIti /
nAhaM tadvastu bhagavanpUjAvanveda jAne yatra gamiShyAmIti /
atha yadyevaM na jAnIShe yatra gataH kR^itArthaH syA ahaM vai tubhyaM tadvakShyAmi yatra gamiShyasIti /
bravItu bhagavAniti, yadi prasanno mAM prati /
shR^iNu //4,2.1//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 4,2.2

#<indho ha vai nAmaiSha yo 'yaM dakShiNe 'kShan puruShaH |
taM vA etam indhaM santam indra ity AcakShate parokSheNaiva |
parokShapriyA iva hi devAH pratyakShadviShaH || BrhUp_4,2.2 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,2.2 indho ha vai nAma /
indha ityevaMnAmA /
yashcakShurvai brahmeti purokta AdityAntaragta puruShaH sa eSha yo 'yaM dakShiNe 'kShannakShaNi visheSheNa vyavasthitaH /
sa ca satyanAmA /
taM vA etaM puruShaM dIptiguNatvAtpratyakShaM nAmAsyendha iti tamindhaM santamindra ityAcakShateparokSheNa /
yasmAtparokShapriyA iva hi devAH pratyakShadviShaH pratyakShanAmagrahaNaM dviShanti /
eSha tvaM vaishvAnaramAtmAnaM saMpanno 'si //4,2.2//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 4,2.3

#<athaitad vAme 'kShaNi puruSharUpam eShAsya patnI virAT |
tayor eSha saMstAvo ya eSho 'ntar hR^idaya AkAshaH |
athainayor etad annaM ya eSho 'ntar hR^idaye lohitapiNDaH |
athainayor etat prAvaraNaM yad etad antar hR^idaye jAlakam iva |
athainayor eShA sR^itiH saMcaraNI yaiShA hR^idayAd UrdhvA nADy uccarati |
yathA keshaH sahasradhA bhinna evam asyaitA hitA nAma nADyo 'ntar hR^idaye pratiShThitA bhavanti |
etAbhir vA etad Asravad Asravati |
tasmAd eSha praviviktAhAratara iva bhavaty asmAc chArIrAd AtmanaH || BrhUp_4,2.3 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,2.3 athaitadvAme 'kShaNi puruSharUpameShAsya patnI yaM tvaM vaishvAnaramAtmAnaM saMpanno 'si tasyAsyendrasya bhokturbhogyaiShA patnI virADannaM bhogyatvAdeva tadetadannaM cAttA caikaM mithunaM svapne /
ko 'sau /
ya eSho 'ntarahR^idaya AkAsho 'ntarhR^idaye hR^idayasya mAMsapiNDasya madhye /
athainayoretadvakShyamANamannaM bhojyaM sthitihetuH /
kiM tat /
ya eShe 'ntarhR^idaye lohitapiNDo lohita eva piNDAkArApannA lohitapiNDaH /
annaM jagdhaM dvedhA pariNamate yatsthUlaM tadadho gacchati /
yadanyattatpunarAgninA pacyamAnaM dvedhA pariNamate /
yo madhyamo rasaH sa lohitAdakrameNa pAJNcabhautikaM piNDaM sharIramupacinoti /
yo 'NiShTho rasaH sa eSha lohitapiNDa indrasya liN^gAtmano hR^idaye mithunIbhUtasya /
yaM taijasamAcakShate sa tayorindrendrANyorhR^idaye mithunIbhUtayoH sUkShmAsu nADIShvanupraviShTaH sthitiheturbhavati /
tadetaducyate 'thainayoretadannamityAdi /
kiJNcAnyat /
athainayoretatpravAraNam /
bhuktavatoH svapatoshca prAvaraNaM bhavati loke tatsAmAnyaM hi kalpayati shrutiH /
ki tadiha prAvaraNam /
yadetadantarhR^idaye jAlakamivAnekanADIchidrabahulatvAjjAlakamiva /
athainayoreShA sR^itirmArgaH saMcanarato 'nayeti saMcaraNI svapnajjAgaritadeshAgamanamArgaH /
kA sA sR^itiH /
yaiShA hR^idayAdahR^idayadeshAdUrdhvAbhimukhI satyuccarati nADI /
tasyAH parimANamidamucyate /
yathA loke keshaH sahasradhA bhinno 'tyantasUkShmo bhavatyevaM sUkShmA asya dehasya saMbandhinyo hitA nAma hitA ityevaM khyAtA nADyAstAshcAntarhR^idaye mAsaMpiNDe pritiShThitA bhavanti hR^idayAdviprarUDhAstAH sarvatra kadambakesapavadetAbhirnADobhiratyantasUkShmAbhiretadannamAsravadgacchadAsravati gacchati /
tadetaddevatAsharIramanenAnnena dAmabhUtenopacIyamAnaM tiShThati /
tasmAdyasmAtsthUlenAnnenopacitaH piNDa idaM tu devatAsharIraM liN^gaM sUkShmeNAnnenopacitaM tiShThati /
piNDopacayakaramapyannaM praviviktameva mUtrapurIShAdisthUlamapekShya liN^gasthitikaraM tvannaM tato 'pisAkShmataram /
ataH praviviktAhAraH piNDaH /
tasmAtpraviviktAhArAdapi praviviktAhAratara eSha liN^gAtmevaiva bhavatyasmAccharIrAcchArIrameva shArIraM tasmAcchArIrAt /
Atmano vaishvAnarAttaijasaH sUkShmAnnopacito bhavati //4,2.3//

START BrhUp 4,2.4

#<tasya prAcI dik prAJNcaH prANAH |
dakShiNA dig dakShiNe prANAH |
pratIcI dik pratyaJNcaH prANAH |
udIcI dig udaJNcaH prANAH |
UrdhvA dig UrdhvAH prANAH |
avAcI dig avAJNcaH prANAH |
sarvA dishaH sarve prANAH |
sa eSha neti nety AtmA |
agR^ihyo na hi gR^ihyate |
ashIryo na hi shIryate |
asaN^go na hi sajyate |
asito na vyathate |
na riShyati |
abhayaM vai janaka prApto 'sIti hovAca yAj~navalkyaH |
sa hovAca janako vaideho 'bhayaM tvA gacchatAd yAj~navalkya yo no bhagavann abhayaM vedayase |
namas te 'stu |
ime videhA ayam aham asmIti || BrhUp_4,2.4 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,2.4 sa eSha hR^idayabhUtastaijasaH sUkShmabhUtena prANena vidhriyamANaH prANa eva bhavati /
tasyAsya viduShaH krameNa vaishvAnarAttaijasaM prAptasya hR^idayAtmAnamApannasya hR^idayAtmanashca prANAtmAnamApannasya prAcI dikprAJNcaH prAggatAH prANAH.tathA dakShiNA digdakShiNe prANAH /
sarvA dishaH sarve prANAH /
evaM vidvAnkreNa sarvAtmakaM prANamAtmatvenopagato bhavati /
taM sarvAtmAnaM pratyagAtmanyupasaMhR^itya draShTurhi draShTubhAvaM neti netItyAtmAnaM turIyaM pratipadyate /
yameSha vidvAnanena krameNa pratipadyate sa eSha neti netyAtmetyAdi na riShyatItyantaM vyAkhyAtametat /
abhayaM vai janmamaraNAdinimittabhayashUnyaM he janaka prApto 'sIti haivaM kilovAcoktavAnyAj~navalkyaH /
tadetaduktamatha vai te 'haM tadvakShyAmi yatra gamiShyasIti /
sa hovAca janako vaideho 'bhayameva tvA tvAmapi gacchatAdgacchatu yastvaM no 'smAnhe yAj~navalkya bhagavAnpUjAvannabhayaM brahma vedayase j~nApayasi prApitavAnupAdhikR^itAj~nAnavyavadhAnApanayanenetyarthaH /
kimanyadahaM vidyAniShkriyArthaM prayacchAmi sAkShAdAtmAnameva dattavate /
ato namaste 'stvime videhAstava yatheShTaM bhujyantAmayaM cAhamasmi dAsabhAve sthito yatheShTaM mAM rAjyaM ca pracatipadyasvetyarthaH //4,2.4//

iti bR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadi caturthAdhyAyasya dvitIyaM brAhmaNam //2//



atha caturthAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaM brAhmaNam //

START BrhUp 4,3.1

#<janakaM ha vaidehaM yAj~navalkyo jagAma |
sam enena vadiShya iti |
atha ha yaj janakash ca vaideho yAj~navalkyash cAgnihotre samUdAte |
tasmai ha yAj~navalkyo varaM dadau |
sa ha kAmaprashnam eva vavre |
taM hAsmai dadau |
taM ha samrAD eva pUrvaH papraccha || BrhUp_4,3.1 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,3.1 janakaM ha vaidehaM yAj~navalkyo jagAmetyasyAbhisaMbandhaH /
vij~nAnamaya AtmA sAkShAdaparokShAdbrahma sarvAntaraH para eva /
"nAnyo 'to 'sti draShTA nAnyadato 'sti draShTi"tyAdishrutibhyaH /
sa eSha iha praviShTo vadanAdiliN^go 'sti vyatirikta iti madhukANDe 'jAtashatrusaMvAde prANAdikartR^itvabhoktR^itvapratyAkhyAnenAdhigato 'pi satpunaH prANanAdiliN^gamupanyasyauShastaprashne prANanAdiliN^go yaH sAmAnyenAdhigataH prANena prANitItyAdinA dR^iShTerdraShTetyAdinAluptashaktisvabhAvo 'dhigataH /
tasya ca paropAdhinimittaH saMsAro yathA rajjUSharashuktikAgaganAdiShu sarpedakarajamalinatvAdi parAdhyAropaNanimittameva na svatastathA nirupAdhiko nirupAkhyo neti netIti vyapadeshyaH sAkShAdaparokShAtsarvAntara AtmA brahmAkSharamantaryAmI prashastaupaniShadaH puruSho vij~nAnamAnandaM brahmetyadhigatam /
tadeva punarindhasaj~naH praviviktAhArastato 'ntarhR^idaye liN^gAtmA praviviktAhAratarastataH pareNa jagadAtmA prANopAdhistato 'pi pravilApya jagadAtmAnamupAdhibhUtaM rajjvAdAviva sarpAdikaM vidyayA sa eSha neti netIti sAkShAtsarvAntaraM brahmAdhigatam /
evamabhayaM pariprApito janako yAj~navalkyenA'gamataH saMkShepataH /
atra ca jAgratsvapna suShuptaturIyANyupanyanyaprasaN^genendhaH praviviktAhArataraH sarve prANAH sarve prANAH sa eSha neti netIti /
idAnIM jAgratsvapnAdvAreNAva mahatA tarkeNa vistarato 'dhigamaH kartavyaH /
abhayaM prApayitavyaM /
sadbhAvAshcA'tmano vipratipattyAshaN^kAnirAkaraNadvAreNa /
vyatiriktatvaM shuddhatvaM svayaJNjyotiShTvamaluptashaktisvarUpatvaM niratishayAnandasvAbhAvyamadvaitatvaM cAdhigantavyamitIdamArabhyate /
AkhyAyayikA tu vidyAsaMpradAnagrahaNavidhiprakAshanArthA /
vidyAstutaye ca visheShataH /
varadAnAdisUcanAt /
janakaM ha vaidehaM yAj~navalkyo jagAma /
sa ca gacchannevaM mene cintitavAnna vadiShye kiJNcidapu rAj~ne /
gamanaprayojanaM tu yogakShemArtham /
na vadiShya ityevaMsaMkalpo 'pi yAj~navalkyo yadyajjanakaH pR^iShTavAMstattatpratipede tatra ko hetuH saMkalpitasyAnyathAkaraNa ityatrA'khyAyikAmAcaShTe /
pUrvatra kila janakayAj~navalkyoH saMvAda AsIdagnihotre nimitte /
tatra janakasyAgnihotraviShayaM vij~nAnamupalabhya parituShTo yAj~navalkyastasmai janakAya ha kila varandadau /
sa ca janako ha kAmaprashnameva varaM vavre vR^itavAMstaM ca varaM hAsmai dadau yAj~navalkyaH /
tena varapradAnasAmarthyenAvyAcikhyAsumapidAviti /
yAj~navalkyaM tUShNaiM sthitamapi samrADeva janakaH pUrvaM papraccha /
tatraivAnuktirbrahmavidyAyAH karmaNA viruddhatvAt /
vidyAyAshca svAtantryAt /
svatantrA hi brahmavidyA sahakArisAdhanAntaranirapekShA puruShArthasAdhaneti ca //4,3.1//

START BrhUp 4,3.2
#<
yAj~navalkya kiMjyotir ayaM puruSha iti |
AdityajyotiH samrAD iti hovAca |
AdityenaivAyaM jyotiShAste palyayate karma kurute vipalyetIti |
evam evaitad yAj~navalkya || BrhUp_4,3.2 ||>#

BrhUpBh_4,3.2 he yAj~navalkyetyevaM saMbodhyAbhimukhIkaraNAya kiJNjyotirayaM puruSha iti kimasya puruShasya jyotiryena jyotiShA vyavaharati so 'yaM kiJNjyotirayaM prAkR^itaH kAryakaraNasaMghAtarUpaH shiraHpANyAdimAnpuruShaH pR^icchyate /
kimayaM svAvayavAsaMghAtabAhyena jyotirantareNa vyavaharatyAhosvitsvAvayavasaMghAtamadhyapAtinA jyotiShA jyotiShkAryamayaM puruSho nirvartayatItyetadabhipretya pR^icchati /
kiJNcAto yadi vyatiriktena yadi vAvyatiriktena-jyotiShA jyotiShkAryaM nirvartayati /
shR^iNu tatra kAraNam yadi vyatiriktenaivajyotiShA jyotiShkAryanirvartakatvamasya svabhAvo nirdhArito bhavati tato 'dR^iShTajyotiShkAryaviShaye 'pyanumAsyAmahe vyatiriktajyotirnimittamevedaM kAryamiti /
athAvyatiriktenaiva svAtmanA jyotiShA vyavaharati tato 'pratyakShe 'pi jyotiShi jyotiShkAryadarshane 'byatiriktameva jyotiranumeyam /
athAniyama eva vyatiriktamavyatiriktaM vA jyotiH puruShasya vyavahArahetustato 'nadhyavasAya eva jyotirviShaya ityevaM manvAnaH pR^icchati janako yAj~navalkyaM kiJNjyotirayaM puruSha iti /
nanvevamanumAnakaushale janakasya kiM prashnena svayameva kasmAnna pratipadyata iti /
satyametat /
tathApi liN^galiN^gisaMbandhavisheShANAmatyantasaukShmyAdduravabodhyatAM  manyate bahUnAmapu paNDitAnAM kimutaikasya /
ata eva hi dharmasUkShmanirNaye pariShadvyApAra iShyate /
puruShavisheShashcApekShyate /
dashAvarA pariShattrayo vaiko veti /
tasmAdyadyapyanumAnakaushalaM rAj~nastathApi tu yukto yAj~navalkyaH praShTum /
vij~nAnakaushalatAratamyopapatteH puruShANAm /
athavA shrutiH svayamevA'khyAyikAvyAjenAnumAnamArgamupanyasyAsmAnbodhayati puruShamatimanusartI /
yAj~navalkyo 'pi janakAbhiprAyabhij~natayA vyatiriktamAtmajyotirbodhayiShyaJNjanakaM vyatiriktapratipAdakameva liN^gaM pratipede yathA prasiddhamAdityajyotiH samrADiti hovAca /
katham /
Adityenaiva svAvayavasaghAtavyatiriktena cakShuSho 'nugrAhakeNa jyotiShAyaM prAkR^itaH puruSha Asta upavishati palyayate prayeti kShetramaraNyaM vA tatra gatvA karma bAhyanekajyotiHpradarshanaM ca liN^gasyAvyabhicAritvadarshanArtham /
evamevaitadyAj~navalkya //4,3.2//

START BrhUp 4,3.5

#<astamita Aditye yAj~navalkya candramasy astamite shAnte 'gnau kiMjyotir evAyaM puruSha iti |
vAg evAsya jyotir bhavatIti |
vAcaivAyaM jyotiShAste palyayate karma kurute vipalyeti |
tasmAd vai samrAD api yatra svaH pANir na vinirj~nAyate 'tha yatra vAg uccaraty upaiva tatra nyetIti |
evam evaitad yAj~navalkya || BrhUp_4,3.5 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,3.5 shAnte 'gnau vAgjyotiH vAgiti shabdaH parigR^ihyate /
shabdena viShayeNa shrotramindriyaM dIpyate /
shrotrendriye saMpradIpte manasi viveka upajAyate /
tena manasA bAhyAM ceShTAM pratipadyate /
"manasA hyova pashyati manasA shR^iNotI"ti brAhmaNam /
kathaM purvAgjyotiriti vAcojyotiShTvamaprasiddhamityata Aha-tasmAdvai samrADyasmAdvAcA jyotiShAnugR^ihIto 'yaTaM puruSho vyavaharati tasmAtprasiddhametadvAco jyotiShTvam /
kathamapi yatra yasminkAle prAvR^iShi prAyeNa medhAndhakAre sarvajyotiHpratyastamaye svo 'pi prANirhasto na vispaShTaM nirj~nAyate /
atha tasminkAle sarvaceShTAnirodhe prApte bAhyajyotiSho 'bhAvAdyatra vAguccarati shvA vA bhaShati gardabho vA rautyupaiva tatra nyeti tena shabdena jyotiShA shrotramanasornairantayaM bhavati tena jyotiShkAryatvaM vAkpratipadyeta tena vAcA jyotiShopanyetyevopagacchatyeva tatra sannihito bhavatItyarthaH /
tatra ca karma kurute vipalyeti /
tatra vAgyotiSho grahaNaM gandhAdInAnupalakShaNArtham /
gandhAdibhirapi hi ghrANAdiShvanugR^ihIteShu pravR^ittinivR^ityAdayo bhavanti /
tena tairapyanugraho bhavati kAryakaraNasaMghAtasya /
evamevaitadyAj~navalkya //4,3.5//

START BrhUp 4,3.6

#<astamita Aditye yAj~navalkya candramasy astamite shAnte 'gnau shAntAyAM vAci kiMjyotir evAyaM puruSha iti |
AtmaivAsya jyotir bhavatIti |
AtmanaivAyaM jyotiShAste palyayate karma kurute vipalyetIti || BrhUp_4,3.6 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,3.6 shAntAyA punarvAci gandhAdiShvapi ca shAnteShu /
bAhyeShvanugrAhakeShu sarvapravR^ittinirodhaH prApto 'sya puruShasya /
etaduktaM bhavati /
jAgradviShaye bahirmukhAnu karaNAni cakShurAdInyAdityAdijyotirbhiranugR^ihyAmANAni yadA tadA sphuTataraH saMvyavahAro 'sya puruShasyadR^iShTA /
tasmAtte vayaM manyAmahe sarvabAhyajyotiHpratyastamaye 'pi svapnasuShuptakAle jAgarite ca tAdR^igavasthAyAM svAvayavasaMghAtavyatiriktenaiva jyotiShA jyotiShkAryasiddhirasyeti /
dR^ishyate ca svapne jyotiShkAryasiddhirbandhusaMgamanaviyogadarshanaM deshAntragamanAdi ca /
suShuptaccotthAnaM sukhamahamasvApsaM na kiJNcidavediShamiti /
tasmAdasti vyatiriktaM kimapi jyotiH /
kiM punastacchAntAyAM vAci jyotirbhavatIti /
ucyate - AtmaivAsya jyotirbhavatIti /
Atmeti kAryakaraNasvAvayavasaMghAtavyatiriktaM kAryakaraNAvabhAsakamAdityAdibAhyajyotirvatsvayamanyenAnavabhAsyamAnamabhidhIyate jyotirantaHsthaM ca tatpArisheShyAt /
kAryakaraNavyatiriktaM taditi tAvatsiddham /
yacca kAryakaraNavyatiriktaM kAryakaraNasaMghAtAnugrAhakaM ca jyotistadbAhyaishcakShurAdikaraNairupalabhyamAnaM dR^iShTaM na tu tathA taccakShurAdibhirupalabhyata AdityAdijyotiHShUparateShu /
kAryaM tu jyotiSho dR^ishyote yasmAttasmAdAtmanaivAyaM jyotiShA'ste palyayate karma kurute vipalyetIti /
tasmAnnUnamantaraHsthaM jyotirityavagamyate /
kiJNcA'dityAdijyotirvilakShaNaM tadabhautikaM ca sa eva heturyaccakShurAdyagrAhyamAdityAdivat /
na /
samAnajAtIyenaivA /
AdityAdijyotiShA kAryakaraNasaMghAtasya bhautikasya bhautikenaivopakAraH kriyamANo dR^ishyate /
yathAduShTaM cedamanumeyam /
yadi nAma kAryakaraNAdarthAntaraM tadupakArakamAdityAdivajjyotisthApi kAryakaraNasaMghAtasamAnajAtIyamevAnumeyaM kAryakaraNasaghAtopakArakatvAdAdityAdijyotirvat /
yatpunarantaHsthatvAdapratyakShatvAcca vailakShaNyamucyate taccakShurAdijyotirbhiranaikAntikam /
yato 'pratyakShANyantaHsthAni ca cakShurAdijyotIMShi bhautikAnyeva /
tasmAttava manorathamAtraM vilakShaNamAtmajyotiH siddhamiti /
kAryakaraNasaMghAtabhAvabhAvitvAcca saMghAtadharmatvamanumIyate jyotiShaH sAmAnyato dR^iShTasya cAnumAnasya vyabhicAritvAdaprAmANyam /
sAmAnyato dR^iShTabalena hi bhavAnAdityAdivadvyatiriktaM jyotiH sAdhayati kAryakaraNebhyaH /
na ca pratyakShamanumAnena bAdhituM shakyate /
ayameva tu kAryakaraNasaMghAtaH pratyakShaM pashyati shR^iNoti manute vijAnAti ca /
yadi nAma jyotirantaramasyopakArakaM syAdAdityAdivanna tadA'tmA syajyotirantaramAdityAdivadeva /
ya eva tu pratyakShaM darshanakriyAM karoti sa evA'tmA syAtkAryakaraNasaMghAto nAnyaH /
pratyakShavirodhe 'numAnasyAprAmANyAt /
nanvayameva ceddarshanAdikrAyakartA'tmA saMghAtaH kathamavikalasyaivAsya darshanAdikriyAkartR^itvaM kadAcidbhavati kadAcinneti /
naiSha doSho dR^iShTatvAt /
nahi dR^iShTe 'nupapannaM nAma /
nahi khadyote prakAshAprakAshatvena dR^ishyamAne kAraNAntaramanumeyam /
anumeyatve ca kenacitsAmAnyAtsarvaM sarvatrAnumeyaM syAt /
taccAniShTam /
na ca padArthasvabhAvo nAsti na hyagneruShNasvAbhAvyamanyanimittamudakasya vA shaityam /
prANidharmAdharmAdyapekShamiti cet /
dharmAdharmAdernimittAntarApekShasvabhAvaprasaN^gaH /
astviti cenna tadanavasthAprasaN^gaH /
sa cAniShTaH /
na /
svapnasmR^ityordR^iShTasyaiva darshanAt /
yaduktaM svabhAvavAdinA dehasyaiva darshanAdikriyA na vyatiriktasyeti /
tanna /
yadi hi dehasyaiva darshanAdikriyA svapne dR^iShTasyaiva darshanaM na syAt /
andhaH svapnaM pashyandR^iShTapUrvameva pashyati na shAkadvIpAdigatamadR^iShTarUpam /
tatashcetatsiddhaM bhavati yaH svapne pashyati dR^iShTapUrvaM vastu sa eva pUrvaM vidyamAne cakShuShyadrAkShInna deha iti /
dehashceddraShTAsa yenAdrAkShIttasminnuddhR^ite cakShuShi svapne tadeva dR^iShTapUrvaM na pashyet /
asti ca loke prasiddhiH pUrvaM dR^iShTaM mayA himavataH shR^iN^gamadyAhaM svapne 'drAkShamityuddhR^itacakShuShAmandhAnAmapu /
tasmAdanuddhR^ite 'pi cakShuShiH yaH svapnadR^iksa eva draShTA na deha ityavagamyate /
tathA smR^itau dR^iShTR^ismartrorekatve  sati ya eva draShTAsa eva smartA yadA caivaM tadA nimIlitAkSho 'pi smandR^iShTapUrvaM yadrUpaM taddR^iShTavadeva pashyatIti /
tasmAdyannimIlitaM tanna draShTR^iyannimIlite cakShuShi smaradrUpaM pashyati tadevAnimIlite 'pi cakShuShi draShTrAsIdityavagamyate /
mR^ite ca dehe 'vikalasyaiva ca rUpAdidarshanAbhAvAt /
devasyaiva draShTrutve mR^ite 'pi darshanAdi kriyA syAt /
tasmAdyapAye dehe darshanaM na bhavati .dbhAve ca bhavati taddarshanAdikriyAkartR^i na deva ityavagamyate /
cakShurAdInyeva darshanAdikriyAkartÌNIti cet /
na /
yadahamadrAkShaM tatspR^ishAmIti bhinnakartR^ikatve pratisaMghAnAnupapatteH /
manastarhIti cet /
na /
manaso 'pi viShayatvAdrUpAdivaddR^iShTR^itvAdyanupapatti /
tasmAdantaHsthaM vyatiriktamAdityAdivaditi siddham /
yaduktaM kAryakaraNasaMghAtasamAnajAtIyameva jyotirantaramanumeyam /
AdityAdibhistatsamAnajAtIyairevopakriyamANatvAditi /
tadasat /
upakAryopakArakabhAvasyAniyamadarshanAt /
kathaM pArthivairindhanaiH pArthavatvasamAnajAtIyaistR^iNolapAdibhiragneH prajvalanopakAraH kriyamANo dR^ishyate /
na ca tAvatA tatsamAnajAtIyairevAgneH prajvanopakAraH sarvatrAnumeyaH syAt /
yenodakenApi prajvalanopakAro bhinnajAtIyona vaidyutasyAgnerjATharasya ca kriyamANo dR^ishyate /
tasmAdupakAryopakArakabhAve samAnajAtIyAsamAnajAtIyaniyamo nAsti /
kadAcitsamAnajAtIyA manuShyA manuShyairevopakriyante kadAcitsthAvarapashvAdibhishca bhinnajAtIyaiH /
tasmAdahetuH kAryakaraNasaMghAtamAnajAtIyairevA'dityAdijyotirbhirupakriyamANatvAdit i /
yatpunarAttha cakShurAdibhirAdityAdijyotirvadadR^ishyatvAdityayaM heturjyotirantarasyAntaHsthatvaM vailakShaNyaM ca na sAdhayati cakShurAdibhiranaikAntikatvAditi /
tadasat /
cakShurAdikaraNebhyo 'nyatve satIti hetorvisheShaNatvopapatteH /
kAryakaraNasaMghAtadharmatvaM jyotiSha iti yaduktaM tanna /
anumAnavirodhAt /
AdityAdijyotirvatkAryakaraNasaMghAtAdarthAntaraM jyotiriti hyanumAnamuktaM tena virudhyata iyaM pratij~nA kArayakaraNasaMghAtadharmatvaM jyotiSha iti /
tadbhAvabhAvitvaM tvasiddhaM mR^ite dehe jyotiSho 'darshanAt /
sAmAnyato dR^iShTasyAnumAnasyAprAmANye sati pAnabhojanAdisarvavyavahAralopaprasaN^gaH /
sa cAniShTaH /
pAnabhojanAdiShu hi kShutpipAsAdinivR^ittimupalabdhavasastatsAmAnyAtpAnabhojanAdyupAdAnaM dR^ishyamAnaM loke na prApnoti /
dR^ishyante hyupalabdhapAnabhojanAH  sAmAnyataH punaH pAnabhojanAntaraiH kShutpipAsAdinivR^ittimanuminvantastAdartheyana pravartamAnAH /
yaduktamayameva tu deho darshanAdikriyAkarteti tatprathamameva parihR^itaM svapnasmR^ityordehAdarthAntarabhUto draShTeti /
anenaiva jyotirantarasyAtmatvamapi pratyuktam /
yatpunaH khadyotAdeH kAdAcitkaM prakAshAprakAshatvaM sadasat /
pakShAdyavayavasaMkocavikAsanimitittatvAtprakAshAprakAshatvasya /
yatpunaruktaM dharmAdharmayoravashyaM phaladAtR^itvaM svabhAvo 'bhyupagantavya iti /
tadabhyubagame bhavataH siddhAntahAnAt /
etenAnavasthAdoShaH pratyuktaH /
tasmAdasti vyatiriktaM cAntaHsthaM jyotirAtmeti //4,3.6//

START BrhUp 4,3.7

#<katama Atmeti -- yo 'yaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu hR^idy antarjyotiH puruShaH |

sa hi svapno bhUtvemaM lokam atikrAmati add. mR^ityo rUpANi || BrhUp_4,3.7 ||>#

BrhUpBh_4,3.7 yadyapi vyatiriktatvAdi siddhaM tathApi samAnajAtIyAnugrAhakatvadarshananimittabhrAntyA karaNAnAmevAnyatamo vyatirikto vetyavivekataH pR^icchati-katama iti /
nyAyasUkShmatAyA durvij~neyatvAdupapadyate bhrAntiH /
athavA sharIravyatirikte siddhe 'pi karaNAnu sarvANi vij~nAnavantIva vivekata Atmano 'nupalabdhatvAt /
ato 'haM pR^icchAmi katama Atmeti /
katamo 'sau dehendriyaprANamanaHsu yastvayokta AtmA /
yena jyotiShA'sta ityuktam /
athavA yo 'yamAtmA tvayAbhipreto vij~nAnamayaH /
sarva ime prANA vij~nAnamayA ivaiShu prANeShu katamaH /
yathA samuditeShu brAhmaNeShu sarva ime tejasvinaH katama eShu ShaDaN^gaviditi /
pUrvasminvyAkhyAne katama AtmetyetAvadeva prashnavAkyaM vij~nAnamayo hR^idyantarjyotiH puruShaHkatama ityedatantam /
yo 'yaM vij~nAnamaya ityetasyashabdasya sarvameva prashnavAkyaM vij~nAnamayo hR^idyantarjyotiH puruShaH katama ityedatantam /
yo 'yaM vij~nAnamaya ityetasya shabdasya nirdhAritArthavisheShaviShayatvaM katama AtmetItishabdasya prashnavAkyaparisamAptyarthatvaM vyavahitasaMbandhamantareNa yuktamiti kR^itvA katama Atmetyevamantameva prashnavAkyaM yo 'yamityAdi paraM sarvameva  prativacanamiti nishcIyate /
yo 'yamityAtmanaH pratyakShatvAnnirdeshaH /

"manasA hyeva pashyati manasA shR^iNotI"ti hyuktam /

dvAramAtrANi tvanyAni karaNAnu buddheH /
tasmAttenaiva visheShyate vij~nAnamaya iti /
yeShAM paramAtmavij~naptivikAra iti vyAkhyAnaM teShAM vij~nAnamayo manomaya ityAdau vij~nAnamayashabdasyAnyArthadarshanAdashrautArthatAvasIyate /
saMdigdhashca padAratho 'nyatra nishcitaprayogadarshanAnnirdhArayituM shakyo vAshyasheShAt /
nishcatanyAyabalAdvA /
sadhIriti cottaratra pAThAt /
hR^idyantariti vacanAdyuktaM vij~nAnaprAyatvameva /
prANeShviti vyatirekapradarshArthA saptamI yathA vR^ikSheShu pAShANa iti sAmIpyalakShaNA /
prANeShu hi vyAtirekAvyatirekatA saMdihyata AtmanaH /
prANeShu prANebhyo vyatirikta ityarthaH /
yo hi yeShu bhavati sa tadvyatirikto bhavatyeva /
yathA pAShANeShu vR^ikShaH /
hR^idi tatrAtatsyAtprANeShu prANajAtIyaiva buddhiH syAdityata Aha-hR^idyantariti /
hR^idacchabdena puNDarIkAkAro mAMsapuNDastAtthyAdbuddhirhR^ittasyA hR^idi buddhau /
antariti buddhivR^ittivyatirekapradarshanArtham /
jyotiravabhAsAtmakatvAdAtmocyate /
tena hyavabhAsakenA'tmanA jyotiShA'ste palyayate karma kurute cenAvAniva hyayaM kAryakaraNapiNDo yathA'dityaprakAshastho ghaTo yathA marakatAdirmaNiH kShIrAdidravye prakShiptaH parIkShaNAyAtmacchAyameva tatkShIrAdirdvyaM karoti tAdR^igedAtmajyetipabuddherapi hR^idayAtsUkShmatvAddhR^idyantaHsthamapi hR^idayAdikaM kAryakaraNasaMghAtaM caikIkR^ityA'tmajyotishchAyaM karoti /
pAramparyeNa sUkShmasthIlatAratamyAtsarvAntaratamatvA /
buddhastAvatsvacchatvAdAnantaryAccA'tmacaitanyajyotiH praticchAyA bhavati /
tena hi vivekinAmapu tatrA'tmAbhimAnabuddhiH prathamA /

tata indriyeShu /
manaH saMyogAt /
tato 'nantaraM sharIre /
indriyasaMparkAt /

tathA ca bhagavatoktaM gItAsu-"yathA prakAshayatyekaH kR^itsnaM lokamimaM raviH /
kShetraM kShetrI tathA kR^itsnaM prakAshayati bhArati" //
"yadAdityagataM tejaH"ityAdi ca /

tenAyaM hR^idyantarjyotiH /
puruSha AkAshavatsarvagatvAtpUrNa iti puruShaH niratishayaM cAsya svayaJNjyotiShTvaM sarvAvabhAsakatvAtsvayamanyAnavabhAsyatvAcca /

kena /
prakR^itatvAtsannihitatvAcca hR^idayena /

tasmAttayaivA sAmAnyam /
kiM punaH sAmAnyamashvamahiShavadvivekato 'nupalabdhiH avabhAsyA buddhirabhAsakaM tadAtmajyotirAlokavat /
avabhAsyAvabhAsakayorvivekato 'nupalabdhiH prasiddhA /
vishuddhatvAddhyAloko 'vabhAsyena sadR^isho bhavati /
yathA raktamavabhAsayanraktasadR^isho raktAkAro bhavati /

sarvamaya iti cAta eva vakShyati /
tenAsau kutashcitpravabhajya muJNjeShIkAvatsvena jyotIrUpeNa darshayituM na shakyata iti sarvavyApAraM tatrAdhyAropya nAmarUpagataM jyotirdharmaM ca nAmarUpayornAmarUpe cA'tmajyotiShi sarvo loko momugyate 'yamAtmA nAyamAmtaivandharmA naivadharmA kartAkartA shuddho 'shuddho baddho muktaH sthito gata Agato 'sti nAstItyAdivikalpaiH /
ataH samAnaH mannubhau lokau pratipannapratipattavyAvihalokaparalokAvupAttadehendriyAdi- saN^ghAtatyAgAnyopAdAnAstAnaprabandhashatasannipAtairanukrameNa saJNcarati /
dhIsAdR^ishyamevobhayalokasaMcaraNaheturna svata iti /

dA dhIrjajAgariShati tadAsAvapyata Aha-svapno bhUtvA svapnavR^ittimavabhAsayandhiyaH svApavR^ityAkAro bhUtvema lokaM jAgaritavyavahAralakShaNaM kAryakaraNasaN^ghAtAtmakaM laukikashAstrIyavyavahArAspadamatikrAmatyatItya krAmati viviktena svenA'tmajyotiShA svapnAtmikA dhIvR^ittamavabhAyannavatiShThate yasmAttasmAtsvayaJNjyotaHsvabhAva evAsau vishuddhaH sa kartR^ikriyAkArakaphalashUnyaH /

dhIreva hi citsvarUpAvabhAsakatvenasvAkArA viShayAkArA ca /

anyo 'nyo hi ghaTAdirutpadyate /
vij~nAnamAtrameva sAlokaghaTAdiviShayAkAramavabhAsate /

tasyApu shAntiM kecidicchanti /

sarvA etAH kalpanA buddhavij~nAnAvabhAsakasya vyatiriktasyA'tmajyotiSho 'pahnavAdasya shreyomArgasya pratipakShabhUtA vaidikasya /

na svAtmAvabhAsakatvaM ghaTAdeH /

avabhAsyatvAvisheShAt /

kasmAt /

kR^itteShu punarutthiteShu /
ca keshanakhAdiShu keshanakhatvAjAterekeshanakhatvapratyayastannimitto 'bhrAnta e /
na hi dR^ishyamAnalUnotthitakeshanakhAdiShu vyaktinimittaH sa eveti pratyayo bhavati /
kasyaciddIrkhakAlavyavahitadR^iShTeShu sa eveti pratyayaH /
tasmAnna samo dR^iShTAntaH /
pratyakSheNa hi pratyabhij~nAyamAne vastuni tadeveti na cAnyatvamanumAtuM yuktaM pratyakShavirodhe liN^gasyA'bhAsatvopapatteH /
sAdR^ishyapratyayAnupapatteshca /
j~nAnasya kShaNikatvAt /
ekasya hi vastudarshino vastvantaradarshane sAdR^ishyapratyayaH syAt /
na tu vastudarshyeko vastvantaradarshanAya kShaNAntaramavatiShThate /
vij~nAnasya kShaNikatvAtsakR^idvastudarshanenaiva kShayopapatteH /
tenedaM sadR^ishamiti hi sAdR^ishyapratyayo bhavati /
teneti  dR^iShTasmaraNam imiti vartamAnapratyayaH /
teneti dR^iShTaM smR^itvA yAvadidimiti vartamAnakShaNakAlamavatiShTheta tataH kShaNikavAdahAniH /
atha tenetyavopakShINaH smArtaH pratyaya idamiti cAnya eva vArtamAnikaH pratyayaH kShIyate tataH sAdR^ishyapratyatAnupapattistenedaM sadR^ishamiti /
anekadarshina ekasyAbhAvAt /
vyapadeshAnupapattishca draShTavyadarshanenaivopakShayAdvij~nAnasyedaM pashyAmyado 'drAkShamitivyapadeshAnupapaccardR^iShTavato vyapadeshakShaNAnavasthAnAt /
athAvatiShTeta kShaNikavAdahAniH /
athAdR^iShTavato vyapadeShaH sAdR^ishyapratyayashca tadAnUM jAtyandhasyeva rUpavisheShavyapadeshastatsAdR^ishyapratyayashca sarvamandhaparampareti prasajyeta sarvaj~nashAstrapraNayanAdi /
na caitadiShyate /
akR^itAbhyAgamakR^itavipraNAshadoShau tu prasiddhatarau kShaNavAde /
dR^iShTavyapadeshahetuH pUrvettarasahita eka eva hi shR^iN^galAvatpratyayo jAyata iti cet /
tenedaM sadR^ishamiti ca /
na /
varmAnAtItayorbhinnakAlatvAt /
tatra vartamAnapratyaya ekaH shR^iN^galAvayavasthAnIyo 'tItashcAparastau pratyayau bhinnakAlau tadubhayapratyayaviShayaspR^ikcecchR^iN^khalApratyayastataH kShaNadvayAvyApitvAdekasya vij~nAnasya punaH kShaNavAdahAniH /
mamatavatAdivisheShAnupapatteshca sarvasaMvyavahAraloprasaN^gaH /
sarvasya ca svasaMvedyavij~nAnamAtratve vij~nAnasya ca svacchAvabodhAbhAsamAtrasvAbhAvyAbhyupagamAttaddarshinashcAnyasyAbhAve 'nityaduHkha- shUnyAnAtmatvAdyanekakalpanAnupattiH /
na ca dADimAderiva viruddhAnekAMshavatvaM vij~nAnasya /
svacchAvabhAsasvAbhAvyAddvij~nAnasya /
anityaduHkhAdInAM vij~nAnAMshatve ca satyanubhIyamAnatvAdvyatiriktaviShayatvaprasaN^gaH /
athAnityaduHkhAdyAtmaikatvameva vij~nAnasya tadA tadviyogAdvishuddhikalpanAnupapattiH /
saMyogimalavigAddhi vishuddharbhavati /
yathA'darshaprabhR^itInAm /
na tusvAbhAvikena raktatvAdInAM dravyAntarayogena viyojanaM dR^ishyate tatrApi saMyogapUrvatvamanumIyate /
bIjabhAvanayA puShpaphalAdInAM guNAntarotpattidarshanAt /
ato vij~nAnasya vishuddhikalpanAnupapattiH /
ato vij~nAnasya vishuddhikalnAnupattiH /
viShayaviShayyAbhAsatvaM ca yanmalaM parikalpyate vij~nAnasya tadapyanyasaMsargAbhAvAdAnupapannam /
na hyavidyamAnena vidyamAnasya saMsargaH syAt /
asati cAnyasaMsargeyo dharmo yasya dR^iShTaH sa tatsvabhAtvAnna tena viyogamarhati /
yathAgnerauShNyaM saviturvA prabhA /
tasmAdanityasaMsargeNa malinatvaM tadvishuddhishca vij~nAnasyetIyaM kalpanAndhaparamparaiva pramANashUnyetyavagamyate /
yadapi tasya vij~nAnasya nirvANaM puruShArthaM kalpayanti tatrApi phalAshrayAnupapattiH /
kaNTakaviddhasya hi kaNTakavedhajanitaduHkhanivR^ittiH phalaM na tu kaNTakaviddhamaraNe tadduHkhanivR^ittaphalasyA'shraya upapadyate /
tadvatsarvanirvANe 'sati ca phalAshraye puruShArthakalpanA vyarthaiva /
yasya hi puruShashabdavAcyasya satvasyAtmano vij~nAnasya cArthaH parikalpyate tasya punaH puruShasya nirvANe kasyArthaH puruShArtha iti syAt /
yasya punarastyanekArthadashIM vij~nAnavyatirikta AtmA tasya dR^iShTasmaraNadukhasaMyogaviyogAdi sarvamevopapannamanyasaMyoganimittaM kAluShyaM tadviyoganimittA ca vishuddhiriti /
shUnyavAdipakShastu sarvapramANavipratiShiddha iti tannirAkaraNAya nA'daraH kriyate //4,3.7//

START BrhUp 4,3.8

#<sa vA ayaM puruSho jAyamAnaH sharIram abhisampadyamAnaH pApmabhiH saMsR^ijyate |

__________



BrhUpBh_4,3.8 yathaivehaikasmindehe svapno bhUtvA mR^ityo rUpANi kAryakaraNAnyatikramya svapne sva AtmajyetiShyAsta evaM sa vai prakR^itaH puruSho 'jAyamAnaH /

sa evotkrAmaJNcharIrAntaramUrdhaMva krAmangacchanmriyamANa ityetasya vyAkhyAnamutkrAmanniti /
tAneva saMshliShyAnpApmarUpakAryakaraNopAdAnaparityAgAbhyAmanavaracaM saMcarati dhiyA samAnaH san, tathA so 'yaM puruSha ubhAvihalokaparokau janmamaraNAbhyAM kAryakaraNopAdAnaparityAgAvanavarataM pratipadyamAna A saMsAramokShAtsaMcarati /

na hi taddharmatve sati taireva saMyogo viyogo vA yuktaH //4,3.8//

START BrhUp 4,3.9

#<tasya vA etasya puruShasya dve eva sthAne bhavataH |
idaM ca paralokasthAnaM ca |
sandhyaM tR^itIyaM svapnasthAnam |
tasminsandhye sthAne tiShThan ubhe sthAne pashyatIdaM ca paralokasthAnaM ca |

atrAyaM puruShaH svayaMjyotir bhavati || BrhUp_4,3.9 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,3.9 nanu na syo 'syobhau lokau yau janmamaraNAbhyAmanukrameNa saMcarati svapnajAgarite iva /
svapnajAgarite tu pratyakShamavagamyete na tvihalokaparalokau kenacitpramaNena /
tasmAdete eva svapnajAgagarite ihalokaparalokAviti /
ucyate-tasyaitasya puruShasya vai dve e sthAne bhavato na tR^itacIyaM caturthaM vA /
ke te /
idaM ca .tpratipannaM vartamAnaM janma sharIrenjadriyaviShayavedanAvishiShTaM sthAnaM pratyakShato 'nubhUyamAnam /

na /
kathaM tarhi /
saMdhyaM tat /
ihalokaparalokayoryaH saMdhistasminbhavaM saMdhyaM yattR^itIyaM tatsvapnasthAnam /

ke te ubhe /
idaJNca paralokasthAnaM ca /
tasmAtstaH svapnajAgaritavyatirekeNobhau lokau yo dhiyA samAnaH sannanusaMcarati janmamaraNasaMtAnaprabandhena /
kathaM punaH svapne sthitaH lokau pashyati /
kimAshrayaH kena vidhineti /
ucyete-atha kathaM pashyatIti shR^iNu /
yathAkrama akrAmatyanenetyAkrama Ashrayo 'vaShTambha ityarthaH /
yAdR^isha Akmayo 'sya so 'yaM yathAkramaH /
ayaM puruShaH paralokasthAne pratipattavye nimitte yathAkramo bhavati yAdR^ishenaparalokapratipattisAdhanena vidyAkarmapUrvapraj~nAnalakShaNena yukto bhavatItyarthaH /
tamAkramaM paralokasthAnAyonmukhIbhUtaM prAptAN^kurIbhAvamiva bIjaM tamAkramyAvaShTabhyA'shrityobhayAnpashyati bahuvacanaM dharmAdharmaphalonekatvAdubhayaprakArAnityarthaH /
kAMstAnpApmanaH pApaphalAni /
na tu punaH sAkShAdeva pApmanAM darshanaM saMbhavati tasmAtpApaphalAni duHkhAnItyarthaH /
AnandAMshca dharmaphalAni sukhAnItyetat /
tAnubhayAnpApmana AnandAMshca pashyati janmAntaradR^iShTavAsanAmayAt /
yAni ca pratipattavyajanmaviShayANi kShudradharmAdharmaphalAni dharmAdharmaprayukto devatAnugrahAdvApashyati /
tatkathamavagamyate paralokasthAnasaMbandhipApmAnAndadarshanaM svapna iti /
ucyate-yasmAdiha janmanyananubhAvyamapi pashyati bahu /
na ca svapno nAmApUrvaM darshanam /
pUrvadR^iShTasmR^itirhi svapnaH prAyeNa /
tena svapnjAgaritasthAnavyatirekeNa sta ubhau lokau /
yadAdityAdibAhyajyotiShAmabhAve 'yaM kAryakAraNasaMgAtaH puruSho yena vyatiriktenA'tmanA jyotiShA vyavaharatItyuktam tadeva nAsti /
yadA'dityAdijyotiShAmabhAvagamanaM yatredaM viviktaM svayaJNjyotirupalabhyota /

tasmAdasatsamo 'sanneva vA svena viviktasvabhAvena jyotIrUpeNA'tmeti /
atha kvacidviviktaH svena jyotIrUpeNopalabhyeta bAhyAdhyAtmikabhUtabhautikasaMsargashUnyastato yathoktaM sarvaM bhaviShyatItyedarthamAha-sa yaH prakR^ita AtmA yatra yasminkAle prasvapiti prakarSheNa svApamanubhavati tadA kimupAdAnaH kena vidhinA svapiti saMdhyaM sthAnaM pratipadyata ityacyate /
asya dR^iShTasya lokasyajAgaritalakShaNasya sarvAvataH sarvamavatIti sarvAvAnayaM lokaH kAryakaraNasaMghAto viShayavedanAsaMyuktaH /
sarvAvatvamasya vyAkhyAtamannatrayaprakaraNe 'tho ayaM vA AtmetyAdinA /
sarvA vA bhUtabhautikamAtrA asya saMsargakANabhUtA vidyanta iti sarvavAnsarvAneva sarvAvAMstasya sarvAvato mAtrAmekadeshamavayavamapAdAyApacchidyA'dAya gR^ihItvA dR^iShTajanmavAsanAvAsitaH sannityarthaH /
svayamAtmanaiva vihatya dehaM pAtayitvA niHsaMbodhamApAdya /
jAgarite hyodityAdInAM cakShurAdiShvanugraho dehavyavavahArArthaH /
dehavyavahArashcA'tmano dharmAdharmaphalopabhogaprayuktastaddharmAdharmaphalopabhogoparamaNamasmindeha AtmakarmoparamakR^itamityAtmAsya vihantetyucyate /
svayaM nirmAya nirmANaM kR^itvA vAsanAmayaM svapnadehaM mAyAmayamiva /
nirmANamapi tatkarmApekShatvAtsvayaN^kartR^ikamucyate /
svenA'tmIyena bhAsA mAtropAdAnalakShaNena bhAsA dIptyA prakAshena sarvavAsanAtmakenAntaHkaraNavR^ikkiprakAshenetyarthaH /
sA hi tatra viShayabhUtA sarvavAsanAmayI prakAshate /
sA tatra svayaM bhA ucyate /
tena svena bhAsA viShayabhUtena svena ca jyotiShA tadviShayiNA viviktarUpeNAluptadR^iksvabhAvena tadbhAvarUpaM vAsanAtmakaM viShayIkurvanprasvapiti /
yadevaM vartanaM tatprasvapitItyucyate /
atraitasyAmavasthAyAmetasminkAle 'yaM puruSha AtmA svayameva vivaktajyotirbhavati /
bAhyAdhyAtmikabhUtabhautikasaMsargarahitaM jyotirbhavati /
nanvasya lokasyamAtropAdAnaM kR^itaM kathaM tasminsatyatrAyaM puraShaH svayaJNjyotirbhavatItyucyate /
naiSha doShaH /
viShayabhUtameva hi tat /
tenaiva cAtrAyaM puruShaH svayaM jyotirdarshayituM shakyaH /
na tvanyathAsati viShaye kasmiMshcitsuShuptakAla iva /

tenAtrAyaM purushaH svayaJNjyotirbhavatIti siddham //4,3.9//

START BrhUp 4,3.10

#<na tatra rathA na rathayogA na panthAno bhavanti |
atha rathAn rathayogAn pathaH sR^ijate |
na tatrAnandA mudaH pramudo bhavanti |
athAnandAn mudaH pramudaH sR^ijate |

BrhUpBh_4,3.10 nanvatra kathaM puruShaH svayaJNjyotiryena jAgarata iva grAhyagrAhakAdilakShaNaH sarve vyavahAro dR^ishyate /
cakShurAdyanugrAhakAshcA'dityAdyA lokAstathaiva dR^ishyante yathA jAgarite /
tatra kathaM visheShAvadhAraNaM kriyate 'trAyaM puruShaH svayaM jyotirbhavatIti /
ucyate-vailakShaNyAtsvapnadarshanasya /
jAgaritaM hIndriyabuddhamana AlokAdivyApArasaMkIrNamAtmajyotiH /
iha tu svapn indriyAbhAvAttadanugrAhakAdityAdyAlokAbhAvAcca viviktaM kevalaM bhavati /
tasmAdvilakShaNam /
nanu tathaiva viShayA upalabhyante svapne 'pi yathA jAgarite tatra kathamindrAyAbhAvAdvailakShamyamucyate iti /
shR^iNu-  na tatra liShayAH svapne rathAdilakShaNAH /
tathA na rathayogA ratheShu yujyanta iti rathayogA ashvAdayastatra na vidyante /
na ca panthAno rathamArgA bhavanti /
atha rathAnrathayogAnpathashca sR^ijate svayam /
kathaM punaH sR^ijate rathAdisAdhanAnAM vR^ikShAdInAMmabhAve /
ucyete-nanUktamasya lokasya sarvAvato mAtrAmapAdAya svayaM vihatya svayaM nirmAyetyantaHkaraNavR^ittirasya lokasya vyavatiShThate taducyate svayaM nirmAyeti /
tadevA'ha-rathAdInsR^ijata iti /
natu tatra karaNaM vA karaNAnugrAgakANivA'dityAdijyotIMShi tadavabhAsyA vA rathAdayo viShayA vidyante /
tadvAsanAmAtraM tu kevalaM tadupalabdhikarmanimittacoditodbhUtAntaHkaraNavR^ityAshrayaM dR^ishyate /
tadyasya jyotiSho dR^ishyate 'luptadR^ishastadAtmajyotiratra kevalamasiriva koshAdvivivaktam /
tathA na tatrA'nandAH sukhavisheShA mudo harShA putrAdilAbhanimittAH pramudasta eva prakorShopetAH /
atha cA'nandAdInsR^ijate /
tathA na tatra veshAntAH palvalAHpuShkariNyastaDAgAH sravantyo nadyo bhavanti /
atha veshAntAdInsR^ijate vAsanAmAtrarUpAn /
yasmAtsa hi kartA /
tdavAsanAshracittavR^ityudbhavanimittakarmahetutvenetyavocAma /
tasya kartR^itvaM na tu sAkShAdeva tatra kriyA saMbhavati sAdhanAbhAvAt /
na hi kArakamantareNa kriyA saMbhavati /
na ca tatra hastapAdAdIni kriyAkArakANi saMbhavanti /
yatka tu tAni vidyante jAgarite tatrA'tmajyotiravabhAsitaiHkAryakaraNai rathAdivAsanAshrayAntaHkaraNavR^ityudbhavanimittaM karma nivartyate tenocyate sa  hi karteti /
taduktamAtmanaivAyaM jyotiShA'ste palyayate karma kuruta iti /
tatrApi na paramArthataH svataH kartR^itvaM caitanyajyotiSho 'vabhAsakatvavyatirekeNa /
yaccaitanyAtmajyotiShAntaHkaraNadvAreNAvabhAsayati kAryakaraNAni sadavabhAsitAni karmasu vyApriyante kAryakaraNAni tatra kartR^itvamupacaryata AtmanaH /
yaduktaM dhyAyatIva lelAyatIveti tadevAnUdyate /
sa hi kartetIha hetvartham //4,3.10//

#<tad ete shlokA bhavanti  --

START BrhUp 4,3.14

#<ArAmam asya pashyanti na taM pashyati kash caneti |

BrhUpBh_4,3.14 ArAmamAramaNamAkrIDAmanena nirmitAM vAsanArUpAmasyA'tmanaH pashyanti sarve janAH /
grAmaM nagaraM striyamannAdyamityAdivAsanAnirmitamAkrIDanarUpam /
na te pashyati taM na pashyati kashcana /

taM nA'yataM  bodhayedityAhuH /
prasiddhirapi loke vidyate svapna AtmajyotiSho vyatiriktatve /
kAsau /
tamAtmAnaM suptamAyataM sahasA bhR^ishaM na bodhayedityAhurevaM kathayanti cikatsakAdayo janA loke /
nUnaM te pashyanti jAgraddehAdindriyadvArato 'pasR^itya kevalo bahirvartata iti yata AhustaM nA'yataM bodhayediti /
tatra ca doShaM pashyantibhR^ishaM hyasau bodhyamAnastAnIndriyadvArANi sahasA pratibodhyamAno na pratipadyata iti /
tadetadAha-durbhiShajyaM hAsmai bhavati yameSha na pratipadyate yamindriyadvAradeshaM yasmAddeshAcchukramAdAyapasR^itastamindriyadeshameSha AtmA punarna pratipadyate /
kadAcidvyatyAsenendriyamAtrAH praveshayati /
tata AndhyabAdhiryAdidoShaprAptau durbhaShajyo duHkhabhiShakvarmatA hAsmai dehAya bhati duHkhena cikitsanIyo 'sau deho bhavatItyarthaH /
tasmAtprasiddhdhyApi svapne svayaM jyotiShTvAmasya gamyate /
svapno bhUtvAtikrAnto mR^ityo rUpANIti tasmAtsvapne svayojyotirAtmA /
atho api khalvanya AhurjAgaritadesha evAsyaiSha yaH svaraH /
na saMdhyaM sthAnAntaramihalokaparalokAbhyAM vyatiriktaM kiM tarhIhaloka eva jAgaritadeshaH /
yadyevaM, kiJNcAtaH /
shR^iNvato yadbhavati, yadA jAgaritadesha evAyaM svapnastadAyamAtmA kAryakaraNebhyo na vyAvR^ittastairmishrIbhUtaH /
ato na svayaJNjyotirAtmetyataH svayaJNjyotiShTvabAdhanAyAnya AhurjAgaritadesha evAsyaiSha iti /
tatra ca hetumAcakShate jAgaritadeshatve yAni hi yasmAddhastyAdIni padArthajAtAni jAgrajjAgaritadeshe pashyati laukikastAnyeva supto 'pi pashyatIti /
tadasat /
indriyoparamAt /
uparateShu hIndriyeShu svapnAnpashyati /
tasmAnnAnyasya jyotiShastatra saMbhavo 'sti /
taduktaM na tatra rathA na rathayogA ityAdi /
tasmAdatrAyaM puraShaH svayaJNjyotirbhavatyeva /
svayaJNjyotirAtmAstIti svapnanidarshenapradarshitam /
atikrAmati mR^ityo rUpANIti ca /
krameNasaMcarannigalokaparalokAdInihalokaparalokAdivyatiriktaH /
tathA jAgratsvapnakulAyAbhyAM vyatiriktaH /
tatra ca kAmasaMcArAnnityashcetyetatpratipadAditaM yAj~navalkyena /
ato vidyAniShkriyArthaM sahasraM dadAmItyAha janakaH so 'hamevaM bodhitastvayAbhagavate tubhyaM sahasraM dadAmi /
vimokShashca kAmaprashno mayAbhipretaH /
tadupayogyayaM tadArthyAttadekadesha eva /
itastvAM niyokShyAmi samastakAmaprashnanirNayashravaNena vimokShAyAta UrdhvaM brUhIti /
yena saMsArAdvipramucyeyam, tvatprasAdAt /
vimokShapadArthaikadeshanirNayahetoH sahasradAnam //4,3.14//

START BrhUp 4,3.15

#<sa vA eSha etasmin saMprasAde ratvA caritvA dR^iShTvaiva puNyaM ca pApaM ca punaH pratinyAyaM pratiyony Adravati svapnAyaiva |
sa yat tatra kiJNcit pashyaty ananvAgatas tena bhavati |

ata UrdhvaM vimokShAyaiva brUhIti || BrhUp_4,3.15 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,3.15 yatprastutamAtmanaivAyaM jyotiShA'sta iti /
tatpratyakShataH pratipAditamatrAyaM puruShaH svayaJNjyotirbhavatIti svapne /
yattUktaM svpano bhUtvemaM lokamatikrAmati mR^ityo rUpANIti /
tatraitadAshaN^kayte mR^ityo rUpANyevAtikrAmati na mR^ityum /
pratyakShaM hyetatsvapne kAryarakaraNavyAvR^ittasyApu modatrAsAdidarshanam /
tasmAnnUnaM naivAyaM mR^ityumatikrAmati /
karmaNo hi mR^ityoH kAryaM modatrAsAdi dR^ishyate /
yadi ca mR^ityunA baddha evAyaM svabhAvatastato vimokSho nopapadyate /
na hi svabhAvastato vimokSho nopapadyate /
na hi svabhAvAtkashcidvimucyate /
atha svabhAvo na bhavati mR^ityustatastasmAnmokSha upapatsyate /
yathAsau mR^ityurAtmAyo dharmo na bhavati tathA pradarshanAyAta UrdhvaM vimokShAya brUhItyevaM janakena paryanuyukto yAj~navalkyastaddidarshayiShayA pravavR^ite - sa vai prakR^itaH svayaJNjyotiH puruShaH /
eSha yaH svapne pradarshita etasminsaMprasAde samyakprasIdatyasminniti saMprasAdaH /
jAgarite dehendriyavyApArashatasaMnipAtajaM hitvA kAluShyaM tebhyo vipramukta IShatprasIdati svapne /
iha tu suShupte samyakprasIdatItyataH suShuptaM saMprasAda ucyate /
"tIrNo hi tadA sarvAn shokAn""salila eko draShTe"ti vakShyati suShuptasthamAtmAnam /
sa vA eSha etasminsaMprasAde krameNa saMprannaH sansuShupte sthitvA /
kathaM saMprasannaH /
svapnAtsuShuptaM pravivikShuH svapnAvastha eva ratvA ratimanubhUya mitrabandhujanadarshanAditA taritvA vihR^ityAnekadhA caraNaphalaM shramamupalabhyetyarthaH /
dR^iShTvaiva na kR^itvetyarthaH puNyaM ca puNyaphalaM pApaM ca pApaphalam /
na tu puNyapApayoH sAkShAddadarshanamastItyavocAma /
tasmAnna puNyapApAbhyAmanu baddhaH /
yo hi karoti puNyapApe sa tAbhyAmanubadhyate /
na hi darshanamAtreNa tadanubaddhaH syAt /
tasmAtsvapno bhUtvA mR^ityumatikrAmatyeva na mR^ityumatikrAmatyeva na mR^ityurUpANyeva kevalam /
ato na mR^ityorAtmasvabhAvatvAshaN^kA /
mR^ityushcetsvabhAvo 'stha svapne 'pi kuryAt /
na tu karoti /
svabhAvashcetkriyA syAdanirmokShataiva syAva /
na tu svabhAvaH svapne 'bhAvAt /
ato vimokSho 'syopapadyate mR^ityoH puNyapApAbhyAm /
nanu jAgarite 'sya svabhAva eva /
na /
buddhyAdyupAdhikR^itaM hi tat /
tacca pratipAditaM sAdR^ishyAddhyAyatIva lelAyatIveti /
tasmAdekAntenaiva svapne mR^ityurUpAtikramaNAnna svAbhAvikatvashaN^kAnirmokShatA vA /
tatra caritveti caraNaphalaM shramamupalabhyetyarthaH /
tataH saMprasAdAnuvabhottarakAlaM punaH pratinyAyaM yathAnyAyaM yathAgataM nishcita Ayo nyAyaH /
ayanamAyo nirgamanaM punaH pUrvagamanaparItyena yadAgamanaM sa pratinyAyaH /
yathAgataM punarAgacchatItyarthaH /
pratiyoni yathAsthAnam /
svapnasthAnAddhi suShuptaM pratipannaH sanyathAsthAnameva punarAgacchati /
pratiyonyAdravati svapnAyaiva svapnasthAnAyaiva /
nanu svapne na karoti puNyapApe tayoH phalameva kathamavagamyate tathA jAgarite yathA karotyeva svapne 'pi tulyatvAddarshanasyeti, ata Aha sa AtmA yatkiJNcittatra svapne pashyati puNyapApaphalamanvAgato 'nanubaddhastena iShTena bhavati naivAnubaddho bhavati /
yadi hi svapne kR^itameva tena syAttenAnubadhyeta /
svapnAdutthito 'pi samanvAgataH syAt /
na ca talloke svapnakR^itakarmaNAnvAgataprasiddhiH /
na hi svapnakR^itenA'gasA'gaskAriNamAtmAnaM manyate kashcit /
na ca svapnadR^ishaH AgaH shrutvA lokastaM garhati pariharati vA /
ato 'nanvAgata eva tena bhavati /
AkhyAtArashcasvapnal sahevashabdenA'cakShate hastino 'dya ghaTIkR^itA dhAvantIva mayA dR^iShTA iti /
ato na tasya kartR^itvamiti /
kathaM punarasyArtR^itvamiti /
kAryakaraNairmUrtaiH saMshleSho mUrtasya sa tu kriyAheturdR^iShTaH /
nahyamUrtaH kashcitkriyAvAndR^ishyate 'mUrtashcA'tmAto 'saN^gaH /
yasmAccAsaN^go 'yaM purushastasmAdananvAgatastena svapnadR^iShTena /
ata eva na kriyAkartR^itvamasya kathaJNcidupapadyate /
kAryakaraNasaMshleSheNa hi kartR^itvaM syAtsa ca sashleShaH saN^go 'sya nAsti yato 'saN^go hyayaM puruShaH /
tasmAdamR^itaH /
evamevaitadyAj~navalkya /
so 'haM bhagavate sahasraM dadAmyata UrdhvaM vimokShAyaiva brUhi /
mokShapadArthakadeshasya karmapravivekasya samyagdarshutatvAt /
ata UrdhvaMvimokShAyaiva brUhIti //4,3.15//

START BrhUp 4,3.16

#<sa vA eSha etasmin svapne ratvA caritvA dR^iShTvaiva puNyaM ca pApaM ca punaH pratinyAyaM pratiyony Adravati buddhAntAyaiva |

START BrhUp 4,3.17

#<sa vA eSha etasmin buddhAnte ratvA caritvA dR^iShTvaiva puNyaM ca pApaM ca punaH pratinyAyaM pratiyony Adravati svapnAntAyaiva || BrhUp_4,3.17 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,3.17 yathAsau svapne 'saN^gatvAtsvapnasaN^gajairdeShairjAgarite pratyAgato na lipyata evaM jAgaritasaN^gajairapu doShAnra lipyata eva buddhAntena tadetaducyate-  sa vA eSha etasminbuddhAnte jAgarite ratvA caritvetyAdi pUrvavat /

nanu dR^iShTvaiveti kathamavadhAryate karoti ca tatra puNyapApe tatphalaM ca pashyati /
kArakAvabhAsakatve kartR^itvopapatteH /
AtmanaivAyaM jyotiShA'sta ityAdinA'tmajyotiShAvabhAsitaH kAryakaraNasaN^ghAto vyavaharati tenAsya kartR^itvamupacaryate na svataHkartR^itvam /

iti //

START BrhUp 4,3.18

#<tad yathA mahAmatsya ubhe kUle anusaMcarati pUrvaM cAparaM ca |

BrhUpBh_4,3.18 evamayaM puruSha AtmA svayaJNjyotiH kAryakaraNavilakShaNastatprayojakAbhyA kAmakarmabhyAM vilakSha No yasmAdasaN^go hyayaM puruSho 'saÇtvAdityayamarthaH"sa vA eSha etasminsaMprasAda"ityAdyAbhistasR^ibhiH kaNDakAbhiH pratipAditaH /

START BrhUp 4,3.19

#<tad yathAsminn AkAshe shyeno vA suparNo vA viparipatya shrAntaH saMhatya pakShau saMlayAyaiva dhriyate |
evam evAyaM puruSha etasmA antAya dhavati |
yatra supto na kaM cana kAmaM kAmayate na kaM cana svapnaM pashyati || BrhUp_4,3.19 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,3.19 atra ca sthAnatrayAnusaMtAreNa svayaJNjyotiSha AtmanaH kAryakaraNasaMghAtavyatiriktasya kAmakarmabhyAM vivaktatoktA svato nAyaM saMsAradharmavAnupAdhinimittameva tvasya saMsAritvamavidyAdhyAropitamityeSha samudAyArtha uktaH /

yathA'kAshe 'sminvihR^itya viparipatya shrAnto nAnAparipatanalakShaNena karmaNA parikhinnaH saMhR^itya pakShau saMgamayya pakShau samyaglIyate 'sminniti saMlayo nIDo nIDAyaiva dhriyate svAtmanaiva dhrAyate svayameva /
yathAyaM dR^iShTAnta evamevAyaM puruSha etasyA etasmai antAya dhAvati /

tathA ca na kaJNcana svapnaM pashyati /
na kaJNcana kAmiti svapnbuddhAntayoravisheSheNa sarvaH kAmaH pratiShidhyate /
kaJNcanetyavasheShitAbhidhAnAt /
tathA na kaJNcana svapnamiti /

yathA dR^iShTAnte pakShiNaH paripatanajashramApanupattaye svanIDaupasarpaNamevaM jAgratsvapnayoH kAryakaraNasaMyogajakriyAphalaiH saMyujyamAnasya pakShiNaH paripatanaja iva shramo bhavaci tacchmApanuttaye svAtmano nIDAmAyatanaM sarvasaMsAradharmavilakShaNaM sarvakriyAkArakaphalAyAsashUnyaM svamAtmAnaM pravishati //4,3.19//

START BrhUp 4,3.20

#<tA vA asyaitA hitA nAma nADyo yathA keshaH sahasradhA bhinnas tAvatANimnA tiShThanti |
shuklasya nIlasya piN^galasya haritasya lohitasya pUrNAH |
atha yatrainaM ghnantIva jinantIva hastIva vicchAyayati gartam iva patati |
yad eva jAgrad bhayaM pashyati tad atrAvidyayA manyate |
atha yatra deva iva rAjevAham evedaM sarvo 'smIti manyate |
so 'sya paramo lokaH || BrhUp_4,3.20 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,3.20 yadyasyAyaM svabhAvaH sarvasaMsAradharmashUnyatA paropAdhinimittaM cAsya saMsAradharmitvam /
yannimittaM cAsya paropAdhikR^itaM saMsAradharmitvaM sA cAvidyA /
tasyA avidyAyA kiM svAbhAvikatvamAhosvitkAmakarmAdivadAgantukatvam /
yadi cA'gantukatvaM tato vimokSha upapadyate /
tasyAshcA'gantukatve kopapattiH kathaM vA nA'tmadharmo 'vidyeti, sarvAnarthabIjabhUtAyA avidyAyAH satatvAvadhAraNArthaM parA kaNDikA'rabhyate-  tA vA asya shiraHpANyAdilakShaNasya puruShasyaitA hitA nAma nADyo yathA keshaH sahasradhA bhinnastAvatA tAvatparimANenANimnANutvena tiShThanti /
tAshTa shuklasya rasasya nIlasya piN^galasya haritasya lohitasya pUrNA etaiH shuklatvAdibhI rasavisheShaiH pUrNA ityarthaH /
ethe ca rasAnAM varNavisheShA vAtapittashleShmaNAmitaretarasaMyogavaiShamyavisheShAdvicitrA bahavashca bhavanti /
tAsvevavidhAsu nADIShu sUkShmAsu bAlAgrasahasrabhedaparimANAsu shuklAdirasapUrNAsu saraladehavyApinIShu saptadashakaM liN^gaM vartate /
tadAshritAH sarvA vAsanA uccAvacasaMsAradharmAnubhavajanitAH /
talliN^gaM vAsanAshrayaM sUkShmatvAtsvacchaM sphaTikamaNikalpaM nADIgatarasopAdhisaMsargavashAddharmAdharmapreritodbhUtavR^ittivisheShaM strIrathahastyAdyAkAravisheShairvAsanAbhiH pratyavabhAsate /
athaivaM sati yatra yasminkAle kecana shatravo 'nye vA taskarA mAmAgatya ghnantIti mR^iShaiva vAsanAnimittaH pratyayo 'vidyAkhyo jAyate tadetaducyata enaM svapnadR^ishaN^ghnantIveti /
tathA hastIvainaM vicchAyayati vicchAdayati vidrAvayati dhAvayatIvetyarthaH /
gartamiva patati gartaM jIrNakUpAdikamiva patantamAtmAnamupalakShayati /
tAdR^ishI hyasya mR^iShA vAsanodbhavatyatyantanikR^iShTAdharmodbhAsitAntaHkaraNavR^ityAshrayA duHkhasvarUpavR^ityAshrayA duHkhasvarUpatvAt /
kiMbahunA yadeva jAgradbhayaM hastyAdilakShaNaM tadeva bhayarUpamatrAsminsvapne vinaiva hastyAdirUpaM bhayamavidyAvAsanayA mR^iShaivodbhUtayA manyate /
atha punaryatrAvidyApakR^iShyamANA vidyA cotkR^iShyamANA kiMviShayA kiMlakShaNA cetyucyate-atha punaryatra yasminkAle deva iva svayaM bhavati /
devatAviShayA vidyA yadodbhUtA jAgaritakAle tadodbhUtayA vAsanayA devamivA'tmAnaM manyate /
svapne 'pi taducyate deva iva rAjeva rAjyastho 'bhiShiktaH svapne 'pi rAjAhamiti manyate rAjavAsanAvAsitaH /
evamatyantaprakShIyamANAvidyodbhUtA ca vidyA sarvAtmaviShayA yadA yadA svapne 'pi tadbhAvito 'hamevedaM sarvo 'smIti manyate /

BrhUpBh_4,3.21 idAnIM yo 'sau sarvAtmabhAvo mokSho vidyAphalaM kriyAkArakaphalashUnyaM sa pratyakShato nirdishyate yatrAvidyAkAmakarmANi na santi /

ayaM tu svena sarvAtmanA saMpiShvaktaH svena pareNa prAj~nenA'tmanA priyayeva puruShaH /
tena na pR^ithaktvena vyavasthitAni karaNAni viShayAshca /
tadabhAvAdvisheShadarshanaM nAsti /
karaNAdikR^itaM hi tannA'tmakR^itam /
AtmakR^itamiva pratyavabhAsate /
tasmAttakR^iteyaM bhrAntirAtmano dR^iShTiH parilupyataca iti //4,3.23//

BrhUpBh_4,3.32 yatra punaH sAvidyA suShupte vastvantarapratyupasthApikA shAntA tenAnyatvenAvidyApravibhaktasya vastuno 'bhAvAtkena kaM pashyejjighredvijAnIyAdvA /

START BrhUp 4,3.34

START BrhUp 4,3.35

tatra caitanyAtmajyotiShA bhAsye liN^ge prANapradhAne gacchati tadupAdhirapyAtmA gacchatIva /

ata evoktaM prAj~nenA'tmanAnvArUTha iti /

ucyate-yatraitadbhavati /
etaditi kriyAvisheShaNam /
UrdhvocchvAsI yatrordhvocchAsitatvamasya bhavatItyarthaH /
dR^ishyamAnasyApyanuvadanaM vairAgyagahetoH IdR^ishaH kaShTaH khalvayaM saMsAraH yenotkrAntikAle marmasUtkR^ityamAneShu smR^itilopo duHkhavedanArtasya puruShArthasAdhanapratipattau cAsAmarthyaM paravashIkR^itacittasya /

START BrhUp 4,3.36

#<sa yatrAyam aNimAnaM nyeti jarayA vopatapatA vANimAnaM nigacchati |

BrhUpBh_4,3.36 tadasyordhvocchvAsitvaM kasminkAle kiMnimittaM kathaM kimarthaM vA  syAdityetaducyate-so 'yaM prAkR^itaH shiraH pANyAdimAnpiNDo yatra yasminkAle 'yamaNimAnamaNorbhAvamaNutvaM kArshyamityarthaH /

kimartham /

START BrhUp 4,3.37

START BrhUp 4,4.1

#<sa yatrAyam AtmAbalyaM nyetya saMmoham iva nyeti |

BrhUpBh_4,4.1 sa yatrAyamamAtmA /

ucyate-sa AtmaitAstejomAtrAstejaso mAtrAstejomAtrAstejovayavA rUpAdiprakAshakatvAccakShurAdIni karaNAnItyarthaH /
tA etAH samabhyAdadAnaH samyaÇnirlepenAbhyAdadAna AbhimukhyenA /
¤a'dadAnaH saMharamANastatsvapnApekShayA visheShaNaM samiti /
na tu svapne nirlepena samyAgAdAnam /
asti tvAdAnamAtram /

uc.te-sa yatraiSha cakShuShi bhavashcAkShuSha- puruSha jAdityAMsho bhoktuH karmaNA prayukto yAdavaddehadhAraNaM tAvaccakShuSho 'nugrahaM kurvanvartate /

START BrhUp 4,4.2

#<ekIbhavati na pashyatIty AhuH |
ekIbhavati na jighratIty AhuH |

ekIbhavati na vadatIty AhuH |

BrhUpBh_4,4.2 ekIbhavati karaNajAtaM svena liN^gAtmanA /
tadaivana pArshvasthA Ahurna pashyatIti /

samAnamanyat /
jihvAyAM somo varuNo vA devatA tannivR^ityapekShayA na rasayata ityAhuH /
tathA na vadati na shR^iNoti na manute na spR^ishati na vijAnAtItyAhuH /

tatra hR^idaya upasaMhR^iteShu karaNeShu yo 'ntarvAyapAraH sa kathyate-tasya haitasya prakR^itasya hR^idayasya hR^idayacchidrasyetyetat /

AdityalokaprAptinimittaM j~nAnaM karma vA yadi syAt /
mUrdhno vA brahmalokaprAptinimittaM cet /
anyebhyo vA sharIradeshebhyaH sharIrAvayavebhyo yathAkarma yathAshrutam /

taM ca prANamanUtkrAmantaM vAgAdayaH sarve prANAM anUtkrAmanti /
yathApradhAnAnvAcikhyAseyaM na tu krameNa sArthavadgmanamiha vivakShitam /
tadaiSha AtmA savij~nAno bhavati svapn iva visheShavij~nAnavAnbhavati karmavashAnn svatantraH svAtantryeNa hi savij~nAnatve sarvaH kR^itakR^ityaH syAt /
naiva tu tallabhyate /
ata evA'ha vyAsaH"sadA tadbhAvabhAvitaH"iti /
karmaNA tUdbhAvyamAnenAntaHkaraNavR^ittivisheShAshritavAsanAtmakavisheShavij~nAnena sarvo loka etasminkAle savij~nAno bhavati /
savij~nAnameva ca gantavyamanvavakrAmatyagacchati visheShavij~nAnodbhAsitamevetyarthaH /
tasmAttatkAle svAtantryArthaM yogadharmAnusevanaM parisaMkhyAnAbhyAsashca vishiShTapuNyopayashca shraddhadhAnaiH paralokArthibhirapramattaiH kartavya iti /
sarvashAstrANAM yatnato vidheyor'tho dushcaritAccoparamaNam /
na hi tatkAle shakyate kiJNcitsampAdayitum /
karmaNA nIyamAnasya svAtantryAbhAvAt /
'puNyo vai puNyena karmaNA bhavati pApaH pApena'tyuktam /
etasya hyanarthasyopashamopAyavidhAnAyA sarvashAkhopaniShadaH pravR^ittAH /
na hi tadvihitopAyAnusevanaM muktvA'tyantiko 'syAnarthasyopashamopAyo 'sti /
tasmAdatraivopaniShadvihitopAye yatnaparairbhavitavyamityeSha prakaraNArthaH /
shakaTavastaMbhR^isaMbhAraM utsarjanyAtItyuktaM, kiM punastasya paralokAya pravR^ittasya pathdanaM shAkaTikasaMbhArasthAnIyaM gatvA vA paralokaM yadbhuN^kte sharIrAdyArambhakaM ca yattatkimiti /
ucyate-taM paralokAya gacchantamAtmAnaM vidyAkarmaNI vidyA ca karma ca vidyAkarmaNI vidyA sravaprakArA vihitA pratiShiddhA cAvihitApratiShiddhA ca /
tathA karma vihitaM pratiShiddhaM cAvihitapratiShiddhaM ca samanvArabhete samyaganvArabhete anvAlabhete anugacchataH pUrvapraj~nA ca pUrvAnubhUtaviShayA praj~nApUrvapraj~nAtItakarmaphalAnubhavavAsanetyarthaH /
sA ca vAsanApUrvakarmarambhe karmavipAke cAN^gaM bhavati /
tenAsAvapyanvApabhate /
na hi tayA vAsanayA vinA karma kartuM phalaM copabhoktuM shakyate /
na hyanabhyaste viShaye kaushalamindrayANAM bhavati /
pUrvAnubhavavAsanApravR^ittAnAM tvindriyANAmihAbhyAsamanantareNa kaushalamupapadyate /

tasmAdetattrayaM shAkaTikasambhArasthAnIyaM paralokapathyadana vidyAkarmapUrvapraj~nAkhyam /

START BrhUp 4,4.3
#<tad yathA tR^iNajalAyukA tR^iNasyAntaM gatvAnyam Akramam AkramyAtmAnam upasaMharati |

BrhUpBh_4,4.3 evaM vidyAdisambArasamphR^ito dehAntaraM pratipadyamAno muktvA pUrvaM dehaM pakShIva vR^ikShAntaraM dehAntaraM pratipadyate /

yathA yena prakAreNa tR^iNajalAyukA tR^iNajalUkA tR^iNasyAntamavasAnaM gatvA prApyAnyaM tR^iNAntaramAkramamAkramyata ityAkramastamAkramamAkramyA'shcityA'tmAnamAtmanaH pUrvavayavamupasaMharatyantyAvayavasthAne /

START BrhUp 4,4.4

#<tad yathA peshaskArI peshaso mAtrAm apAdAyAnyan navataraM kalyANataraM rUpaM tanute |

__________



BrhUpBh_4,4.4 tatra dehAntarArambhe nitthopAttamevopAdAnamupamR^idyopamR^idya dehAntaramArabhata AhostidapUrvameva punaH punarAdatta iti /
atrocyate dR^iShTAntaH-tattatretasminnarthe--yathA peshaskArI peshaH suvarNa tat karotIti peshaskArI suvarNakAraH, peshasaH suvarNasya mAtrAmapAdAyApicchidya gR^ihItvA anyat pUrvasmAd racanAvisheShAnnavataramabhinavataraM kalyANAt kalyANataraM rUpaM tanute nirminoti /
evamevAyamAtmetyAdi pUrvavat /
nityopAttAnyeva pR^ithivyAdInyAkAshAntAni paJNca bhUtAni yAni 'dve vAva brahmaNo rUpe' iti caturthe vyAkhyAtAni peshaHsthAnAyAni,tAnyevopamR^idyopamR^idya, anyadanyacca dehAntaraM navataraM kalyANataraM rUpaM saMsthAnavesheShaM vA pitR^ibhyo hitaM pitR^ilokopabhogayogyamityarthaH, gAndharvaM gandharvANAmupabhogayogyam, tathA devAnAM daivam, prajApateH prajApatyam, brahmaNa idaM brAhmaM vA; yathAkarma yathAshrutamanyeShAMvA bhUtAnAM sambandhi sharIrAntaraM kuruta ityabhisambanyate  //4,4.4//

START BrhUp 4,4.5

#<sa vA ayam AtmA brahma vij~nAnamayo manomayo prANamayash cakShurmayaH shrotramayaH pR^ithivImaya Apomayo vAyumaya AkAshamayas tejomayo 'tejomayaH kAmamayo 'kAmamayaH krodhamayo 'krodhamayo dharmamayo 'dharmamayaH sarvamayaH |

BrhUpBh_4,4.5 yo 'sya bandhanasaMj~nakA upAdhibhUtAH, yaiH saMyuttkastanmaye 'yamiti vibhAvyate, te padArthAH puJNjIkR^ityehaikatra pratinirdishyante-sa vA ayaM ya evaM saMsaratyAtmA brahmaiva para eva yo 'shanAyAdyatIto, vij~nAnamayo vij~nAnaM budvistenopalaÇyamANastanmayaH /

tasmAtsarvamayatve 'sya saMsAritve ca kAma heturiti //4,4.5//

START BrhUp 4,4.6

#<tad eSha shloko bhavati --
tad eva saktaH saha karmaNaiti liN^gaM mano yatra niShaktam asya |
