BrhUpBh_4,4.6 tattasminnartha eSha shloko mantropi bhavati /
tadevaiti tadeva gacchati sakta AsaktastatrodbhUtAbhilAShaH sannityarthaH /
kathameti /
saha karmaNA yatkarmaphalAsaktaH sannakarottena karmaNA sahaiva tadeti tatphalameti /
kiM talliN^gamanaH /
manaH pradhAnatvAlliN^gasya mano liN^gamityucyate /
athavA liN^gayate 'vagamyate 'vagacchati yena talliN^gaM tanmano yatra yasminniShaktaM nishcayena saktamudbhUtAbhilAShamasya saMsAriNaH /
tadabhilASho hi tatkarma kR^itavAn /
tasmAttanmano 'bhiShaN^gavashAdevAsya tena karmaNA tatphalaprAptiH /
tenaitasidvaM bhavati kAmo mUlaM saMsArasyeti /
ata ucchinnakAmasya vidyamAnAnyapi karmANi brahmavido vandhyaprasavAni bhavanti /
"paryAptakAmasaya kR^itAtmanashca ihaiva sarve pravilItanti kAmAH"iti shruteH /
kiJNca prApyAntaM karmaNaH prApya bhuktvAntamavasAnaM tasya karmaNaH phalaM bhuktvAntaM prApya tasmAllokAtpunaraityAgacchatyasmai lokAya karmaNe 'yaM hi lokaH karmapradhAnastenA'ha karmaNa iti /
punaH karmakaraNAya punaH karma kR^itvA phalAsaN^gavashAtpunaramuM lokaM yAtItyevam /
iti nvevaM nu kAmayamAnaH saMsarati /
ya mAtkAmayamAna evaivaM saMsaratyatha tasmAdakAmayamAno na kvacitsaMsarati /
phalAsaktasya hi gatiruktA /
akAmasya hi kriyAnupapatterakAmayamAno mucyata eva /
kathaM punakAmayamAno bhavati /
yo 'kAmo bhavatyasAvakAmayamAnaH kathamakAmatetyucyate--yo niShTakAmo yasmAnnirgatAH kAmAH so 'yaM niShkAmaH /
kathaM kAmA nirgacchanti /
ya AptakAmo bhavatyAptAH kAmA yena sa AptakAmaH /
kathamApyante kAmA AtmakAmatvena yasyA'maiva nAnyaH kAmayitavyo vastvantarabhUtaH padArtho bhavati /
AtmaivAnantaro 'bAhyaH kR^itsnaH praj~nAnaghana ekaraso nordhva na tiryaÇnAdha Atmano 'nyatkAmayitavyaM vastvantaram /
yasya sarvamAtmaivAbhUttatkena kaM pashyecchR^iNuyAnmanvIta vijAnIyAdvaivaM vijAnankaM kAmayeta /
j~nAyamAno hyanyatvena padArthaH kAmayitavyo bhavati /
na cAsAvanyo brahmavida AptakAmasyAsti /
ya evA'tmakAmatayA'ptakAmaH sa niShkAmo 'kAmo 'kAmayamAnashceti mucyate /
na hi yasyA'tmaiva sarvaM bhavati tasyAnAtmA kAmayitavyo 'sti /
anAtmA cAnyaH kAmayitavyaH sarvaM cA'tmaivAbhUditi vipratiShidvam /
sarvAtmadarshinaH kAmayitavyAbhAvAtkarmAnupapattiH /
ye tu pratyavAyaparihArArthaM karma kalpayanti brahmavido 'pi teShAM sarva bhavati /
pratyavAyasya jihAsitavyasyA'tmano 'nyasyAbhipretatvAt /
yena cAshanAyAdyatIto nityaM pratyavAyasaMbadvo vidita AtmA taM vayaM brahmavidaM brUmaH /
nityamevAshanAyAdyatItamAtmanaM pashyati /
yasmAcca jihAsitavyamanyamupAdeyaM vA yo na pashyati tasya karma na shakyata eva saMbaddhu m /
yastvabrahmavitasya bhavatyeva pratyavAyaparihArArthaM karmeti na virodhaH /
ataH kAmAbhAvAdakAmayamAno na jAyate mucyata eva /
tasyaivamakAmayamAnasya karmAbhAve gamanakAraNAbhAvAtprANA vAgAdayo notkrAmanti nordhva krAmanti dehAt /
sa ca vidvAnAptakAma AtmakAmatayehaiva brahmabhUtaH /
sarvAtmano hi brahmaNo dR^iShTAntatvena pradarshitametadrUpaM tadvA asyaitadAptakAmamAtmakAmamakAmaM rUpamiti /
tasya hi dArShTAntikabhUto 'yamartha upasaMhriyate 'thAkAmayamAna ityAdinA /
sa kathamevaMbhUto mucyata ityucyate-yo hi suShuptAvasthamiva nirvisheShamadvaitamaluptacidrUpajyotiH svabhAvamAtmAnaM pashyati tasyaivAkAmayamAnasya karmabhAve gamanakAraNabhAvatprANA vAgAdayo notkrAmanti /
kintu vidvAnsaihaiva brahma, yadyapi dehAvAniva lakShyate sa brahmaiva sanbrahmApyeti /
yasmAnna hi tasyAbrahmatvaparicchedahetavaH kAmAH santi tasmAdihaiva brahmaiva sanbrahmApyeti na sharIrapAtettarakAlam /
na hi viduSho mR^itasya bhAvAntarApattirjIvato 'nyabhAvo dehAntarapratisaMdhAnAbhAvamAtreNova tu brahmApyetItyucyate /
bhAvAntarArApattau hi mokShasya sarvopaniShanidvivakShitor'tha AtmaikatvAkhyaH sa bAdhito bhavet /
karmahetukashca mokShaH prApnoti na j~nAnanimitta iti /
sa   cAniShTo 'nityatvaM ca mokShasya prApnoti /
na hi kriyAnirvR^ittor'tho nityo dR^iShTaH /
nityashca mokSho 'bhyupagamyate /
"eSha nityo mahimA"iti mantravarNAt /
na ca svAbhAvikAtsvabhAvAdanyannityaM kalpayituM shakyam /
svAbhAvikashcedagnyudAtmanaH svabhAvaH sa na shakyate puruShavyApArAnubhAvIti vaktum /
na hyagnerauShNyaM prakAsho vAgnuvyApArAnantarAnubhAvI /
agnivyApArAnubhAvI svAbhAvikashceti vipratiShiddham /
jvalanavyApAnAnubhAvitvamuShNaprAkAshaguNAbhyAmabhivyajyate tannAgnyepekShayA kiM tarhyanyadR^iShTeragnerauShNyaprakAshau dharmau vyavahitai kasyaciddR^iShTyA tvasaMbadhyamAnau jvalanApekShayA vyadhAnApagame dR^iShTerabhivyajyete tadapekShayA bhrAntirupajAyate jvalanapUrvakAvetAviShNaprAkAshau dharmau jAtAviti /
yadyuShNaprakAshayorapi svAbhAvikatvaM na syAt /
yaH svAbhAvaki'gnerdharmastamudAhariShyAmaH /
na ca svAbhAviko dharma eva nAsti padArthAnAmiti shakyaM vaktum /
na ca nigaDabhaN^ga ivAbhAvabhUto mokSho bandhananivR^ittirupapadyate /
paramAtmaikatvAbhyupagamAt 'ekamevAdvitIyam'iti shruteH /
na cAnyo baddho 'sti yasya nigaDanivR^ittivadbandhananivR^ittarmokShaH syAt /
paramAtmavyatirekeNAnyasyAbhAvaM vistareNAvAdiShma /
tasmAdavidyAnivR^ittimAtre mokShavyavahAra iti cAvocAma yathA rajjvAdau sarpAdyaj~nAnanivR^ittau sarpAdinivR^ittiH /
ye 'pyAcakShate mokShe vij~nAnAntaramAnandAntaraM cAbhivyajyata iti sairvaktavyo 'bhivyaktishabdArthaH /
yadi tAvatlaukikikyevopalabdhiviShayavyAptirabhivyaktishabdArthaH /
tato vaktavyaM kiM vidyamAnamabhivyajyate 'vidyamAnamiti vA /
vidyamAnaM cedyasya  muktasya tadabhivyajyate tasyA'tmabhUtameva tadityupalabdhivyavadhAnAnupapatternityAbhivyaktatvAnmuktasyAbhivyajyata iti visheShavacanamarthakam /
atha kadAcidevAbhivyajyata upalabdhivyavadhAnAdanAtmabhUtaM tadityanyato 'bhivyaktiprasaN^gaH /
tathA cAbhivyaktisAdhanApekShayA /
upalabdhisamAnAshrayatve tu vyavadhAnakalpanAnupapatteH sarvadAbhivyaktiprasaN^gaH /
tathA cAbhivyaktisAdhanApekShatA /
upalabdhisamAnAshrayatve tu vyavadhAnakalpanAnupapatteH sarvadAbhivyaktiranabhivyaktirvA /
natvantarAlakalpanAyA pramANamasti /
na ca samAnAshrayaNAmekasyA'tmabhUtAnAM dharmANAmitaretaraviShayaviShayitvaM saMbhavati /
vij~nAnasukhayoShca prAgabhivyakteH saMsAritvamabhivyaktyuttarakAlaM ca muktatvaMsya so 'nyaH parasmAnnityAbhivyaktaj~nAnasvarUpAdatyantavailakShaNyAcchaityamivauShNyAt /
paramAtmabhedakalpanAyAJNca vaidikaH kR^itAntaH parityaktaH syAt /
mokShasyedAnImiva nirvisheShatve tadarthAdhikayatnAnupapattiH shAstravaiyarthyaM ca prApnotIti cenna /
na, avidyAbhramApohApthatvAt /
na hi vastuto muktAmuktatvAvisheSho 'sti /
Atmano nityAkarUpatvAt /
kintu tadviShayAvidyApohyate shAstropadeshajanitavij~nAnena /
prAktadupadeshaprAptestadarthashca prayatna upapadyata eva /
avidyAvato 'vidyAnivR^ityanivR^ittikR^ito vesheSha AtmanaH syAditi cet /
avidyAkalpanAviShayatvAbhyupagamAdrajjUSharashuktakAgaganAnAM sarvodakarajatamalinatvAdivadadoSha ityavocAma /
timirAtimitaradR^iShTivadavidyAkartR^itvAkatR^itvAkR^ita Atmano visheShaH syAditi cet /
na /
dhyAtIva lelAyatIveti svato 'vidyAkartR^itvasva pratiShiddhatvA /
anekavyApArasannipAtajanitatvAccAvidyAbhramasya /
viShatvopapatteShca /

tasyApi vivekagrahaNAt /
na hi yo yasya vivekena grahItA sa tasminbhrAnta ityucyate /

na jAne mugdho 'smIti dR^ishyata iti bravIShi taddarshinashcAj~nAnaM mugdharUpatA dR^ishyata iti ca taddarshanasya viShayo bhavati karmatAmApadyata iti tatkathaM karmabhUtaM satkartR^isvarUpadR^ishivisheShaNaj~nAnamugdhate syAtAm /

START BrhUp 4,4.7

#<tad eSha shloko bhavati --
yadA sarve pramucyante kAmA ye 'sya hR^idi shritAH |
atha martyo 'mR^ito bhavaty atra brahma samashnuta iti |

BrhUpBh_4,4.7 svapnabuddhAntagamanadR^iShTAntasya dArShTAntikaH saMsAro varNitaH /
saMsArahetushca vidyAkarmapUrvapraj~nA varNitA /
yaishcopAdhibhUtaiH kAryakaraNalakShaNabhUtaiH pariveShTitaH saMsAritvamanubhavati tAni coktAni /
teShAM sAkShAtprayojakau dharmAdharvAviti pUrvapakShaM kR^itvA kAma evetyavadhAritam /
yathA ca brahmaNenAyamartho 'yavadhArita evaM mantreNApIti bandhaM bandhakAraNaM coktvopasaMhR^itaM prakaraNaM"iti na kAmayamAna"iti /
athAkAyamAna ityArabhya suShuptadR^iShTanAtasya dArShTAntikabhUtaH sarvAtmabhAvo mokSha uktaH /
mokShakAraNaM cA'tmakAmatayA yadAptakAmatvamuktaM tacca sAmarthAyadanAtmaj~nAnamantareNA'tmakAmayatayA'ptakAmatvamiti sAmarthyAdbrahmavidyaiva mokShakAraNamityuktam /
ato yadyapi kAmo mUlamityuktaM tathApi mokShakAraNaviparyayeNa bandhakAraNamavidyetyedapyuktameva bhavati /
atrApi mokSho mokShasAdhanaM ca brAhmaNenoktam /
tasyaiva dR^iDhIkaraNAya mantra udAhriyate shlokashabdavAcyaH-  tattasminnevArtha eSha shloko mantro bhavati /
yadA yasminkAle sarve samastAH kAmAstR^iShNAprabhedAH pramucyante /
AtmakAmya brahmavidaH samUlato vishIryante /
ye prasiddhA loka ihAmutrArthAH putravittalokaiShaNAlakShaNA asya prasiddhasya puruShasya hR^idi buddhau shritA AshritAH /
atha tadA martyo maraNadharmA sankAmaviyogAtsamUlato 'mR^ito bhavati /
atrAsminneva sharIre vartamAno brahma samashnute brahmabhAvaM mokShaM pratipadyata ityarthaH /
ato mokSho na deshAntaragamanAdyapekShate /
tasmAdviduSho notkrAmanti prANA yAvasthitA eva svakAraNe puruShe samavanIyante /
nAmamAtraM hyavashiShyata ityuktam /
kathaM punaH samanavIteShu prANeShu dehe ca svakAraNe pralIne vidvAnmukto 'traivasarvAtmA sanvartamAnaH punaH pUrvavaddehitvaM saMsAritvalakShaNaM na pratipadyata iti /
atrocyate-tattatrAyaM dR^iShTAnto yathA loke 'hiH sarpastasya nirlvayanI nirmekaH sAhinirlvayanI valmIke sarpAshraye valmIkAdAvityarthaH /

evameva yathAyaM dR^iShTAnta idaM sharIraM sarpasthAnIyena muktenAnAtmabhAvena parityaktaM mR^itamiva shete /
athetaraH sarpasthAnIyo muktaH sarmAtamabhUtaH sarpavattatraiva vartamAno 'pyasharIra eva na pUrvavtupanaH sasharIro bhavati /
kAmakarmaprayuktasharIrAtmabhAvena hi pUrvaM sharIro martyashca /
tadviyogAdathedAnImasharIro 'ta eva cAmR^itaH /
prANaH prANitIti prANaH /
prANasya prANamiti hi vakShyamANe shloke /
"prANabandhanaM hi somya manaH"iti ca shrutyantare /
prakaraNavAkyasamArthAcca para evA'tmAtra prANashabdavAcyaH /
brahmaiva paramAtmaiva /
kiM punastatteja eva vij~nAnaM jyotiryenA'tmajyotiShA jagadavabhAsyamAnaM praj~nAnetraM vij~nAnajyotiShmatsadavibraMshadvartate /
yaH kAmaprashno vimokShArtho yAj~navalkyena varo datto janakAya sahetuko bandhamokShArthalakShaNo dR^iShTAntikabhUtaH sa eSha nirNItaH savistaro janakayAj~navalkyAkhyAyikArUpadhAriNyA shrutyA /
saMsAravimokShopAya uktaH prANibhyaH /
idAnIM shrutiH svayamevA'ha vidyAniShkriyArthaM janakenaivamuktamiti /
kathaM? so 'hamovaM vimokShitastvayA bhagavate tubhyaM vidyAniShkriyArthaM sahasraM dadAmIti haiva kilovAcoktavAJNjanako vaidehaH /
atra kasmdAvimokShapadArthe nirNIte videharAjyamAtmAnameva ca na nivedayatyekadeshoktAviva sahasrameva dadAti tatra ko 'bhiprAya iti /
atra kecidvarNayanti-adhyAtmavidyArasiko janakaH shrutamapyartaM punarmantraiH shushrUShati /
ato na sarvameva nivedayati /
shrutvAbhipretaM yAj~navalkyAtpunarante nivedayiShyAmIti hi manyate /
yadi cAtraiva sarva nivedayAmi nivR^ittAbhilASho 'yaM shravaNAditi matvA shlokAnnavakShyatIti ca bhayAtsahasradAnaM shushrUShAliN^gaj~nApanAyeti /
sarvamapyetadasat /
puruShasyeva pramANabhUtAyAH shrutervyAjAnupapatteH /
arthasheShopapatteshca /
vimokShapadArtha ukte 'pyAtmaj~nAnasAdhana Atmaj~nAnasheShabhUtaH sarveShaNAparityAgaH saMnyAsAkhyo vaktavyor'thasheSho vidyate /

nityo hyAtmabhAvaH sarvasyAtadviShaya iva pratyavabhasate /

anyAtbhAvanivR^ittAvAtmabhAvaH svAtmani svAbhAviko yaH sa kevalo bhavatItyAtmA j~nAyata ityucyate /
svatashcAprameyaH pramANAntareNa na viShayIkriyata ityuccayate /
svatashcAprameyaH pramANAntareNa na viShayIkriyata ityubhayamapyaviruddhameva /
virajo vigatarajo rajo nAma dharmAdharmAdimalaM tadrahita ityetat /
paraH paro vyatiriktaH sUkShmo vyApI vA'kAshAdapyavyAkR^itAkhyAt /
ajo na jAyate janmapratiShedhAduttare 'pi bhAvavikArAH pratiShiddhAH /
sarveShAM janmAditvAt /
AtmA mahAnparimANato mahatatraH sarvasmAt /
dhruvo 'vinAshI //4,4.20//

BrhUpBh_4,4.22 sahetukau bandhamokShAvabhihitau mantrabrAhmaNabhyAM shlokaishca punarmokShasvarUpaM vistareNa pratipAditamevametasminnAtmaviShaye sarvo vedo yathopayukto bhavati tattathA vaktavyamiti tadartheyaM kaNDikA'rabhyate /

iti /

#<tad etad R^icAbhyuktam --
eSha nityo mahimA brAhmaNasya na karmaNA vardhate no kanIyAn |
tasyaiva syAt padavittaM viditvA na lipyate karmaNA pApakeneti |
tasmAd evaMvic chAnto dAnta uparatas titikShuH samAhito bhUtvAtmany evAtmAnaM pashyati |

nainaM pApmA tarati |

eSha brahmalokaH samrAT |
enaM prApito 'sIti hovAca yAj~navalkyaH |
so 'haM bhagavate videhAn dadAmi mAm cApi saha dAsyAyeti || BrhUp_4,4.23 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,4.23 tadetadvastu brAÇmaNenoktamR^icA mantreNAbhyuktaM prakAshitam /
eSha neti netyAdilakShaNo nityo mahimA /
anye tu mahimAnaH karmakR^itA ityanityAH /
ayaM tu tadvilakShaNo mahimA svAbhAvikatvAnnityo brahmavido brAhmaNasya tyaktasarveShaNasya /
kuto 'sya nityatvamiti hetumAha- karmaNA na vardhate shubhalakShaNena kR^itena vR^idvilakShaNAM vikriyAM na prApneti /
ashubhena karmaNA no kanIyAnnApyapakShayalakShaNAM vikriyAM prApnoti /
upacayApacayahetubhUtA eva hi sarvA vikriyA ityetAbhyAM pratiShidhyante /
ato 'vikriyatvAnnitya eSha mahimA /
tasmAttasyaiva mahimnaH syAdbhavetpadavitpadasya vettA padyate gamyate j~nAyata iti mahimnaH svarUpameva padaM tasya padasya veditA /
kiM tatpadavedanena syAdityucyate-taM viditvA mahimAnaM na lipyate na saMbadhyate karmaNA pApakena dharmAdharmalakShaNenobhayamapi pApakameva viduShaH /
tasmAdevamakarmasaMbandhyeSha brAhmaNasya mahimA neti netyAdilakShaNastasmAdevaMvicchAnto bAhyendriyavyApArata upashAntastathA dAnto 'ntaH karaNatR^iShNAto nivR^itta uparataH sarvaiShaNAvinirmuktaH saMnyAsI titikShurdvandvasahiShNuH samAhita indriyAntaH karaNAcalanarUpAdvyAvR^ityaikAgryarUpeNa samAhito bhUtvA /
tadetaduktaM purastAdbAlyaM ca pANDityaM ca nirvidyeti /
Atmanyeva sve kAryakaraNasaMghAta AtmAnaM pratyakcetayitAraM pashyati /
tatra kiM tAvanmAnnaM paricchinaM netyucyatesarvaM samastamAtmAnameva pashyati nAnyadAtmavyatiriktaM vAlAgramAnnamapyastItyevaM pashyati /
mananAnmunirbhavati jAgratsvapnasuShuptAkhyaM sthAnannayaM hitvA /
evaM pashyantaM brAhmaNaM nainaM pApmA puNyapApalakShaNastarati na prApneti /
ayaM tu brahmavitsarvaM pApmAnaM taratyAtmabhAvenaiva vyApnotyatikrAmati /
nainaM pApmA  kR^itAkR^italakShaNastapatIShTaphalapratyavAyotpAdanAbhyAm /
sarvaM pApmAnamayaM tapati brahmavitsarvatmadarshanavahrinA bhasmIkaroti /
sa eSha evaMvidvipAyo vigatadharmAdharmo birajo vigatarajo rajaHkAmo vigatakAmo 'vicikitsashchinnasaMshayo 'hamasmi sarvAtmA paraM brahmeti nishcitamatirbrAhmaNo bhavati /
ayaM tvevaMbhUta atasyAmavasthAyAM mukhyo brAhmaNaH prAgetasmAdbrahmasvarUpAvasthAnAdgauNamasya brAhmaNyam /
eSha brahmaloko brahmaiva loko brahmaloko mukhyo nirupacaritaH sarvAtmabhAvalakShaNo he smAraT /
enaM brahmalokaM pariprApito 'syabhayaM neti netyAdilakShaNamiti hovAca yAj~navalkyaH /
evaM brahmabhUto janako yAj~navalkyena brahmabhAvamApAditaH  pratyAha-so 'haM tvayA brahmabhAvamApAditaH sanbhagavate tubhyaM videhAndeshAnmama rAjya samastaM dadAmi mAM ca saha kartavyatAkA /
parisamAptaH paramapuruShArthaH /
etAvatpuruSheNa kartavyameShA niShThaiShA parA gatiretanniHshreyasametatprApya kR^itakR^ityo brAhmaNo bhavatyetatsarvavedAnushAsanamiti //4,4.23//

BrhUpBh_4,4.25 idAnIM samastasyaivA'raNyarakasya yor'tha uktaH sa samuccityAsyA kaNDikAyAM nirdishyata  etAvAnsamastAraNyakArtha iti /

START BrhUp 4,5.1

#<atha ha yAj~navalkyasya dve bhArye babhUvatur maitreyI ca kAtyAyanI ca |

START BrhUp 4,5.15

#<yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tad itara itaraM pashyati, tad itara itaraM jighrati, tad itara itaraM rasayate, tad itara itaram abhivadati, tad itara itaraM shR^iNoti, tad itara itaraM manute. tad itara itaraM spR^ishati, tad itara itaraM vijAnAti |

BrhUpBh_4,5.15 caturShvapi prapAThakeShveka AtmA tulyo nirdhAritaH paraM brahma /
upAyavisheShastu tasyAdhigame 'nyashcAnyashca /

punaH paJNcamasamAptau /
punarjanakayAj~navalkyasaMvAde /
punarihopaniShatsamAptau /
caturNAmapi prapAThakAnAmetadAtmaniShThatA nAnyo 'ntarAle kashcidapi vivakShiter'tha ityetatpradarshanAyAnta upasaMhAraH sa eSha neti netyAdiH /
yasmAtprakArashatenApi nirUpyamANe tattave neti netyAtmaiva niShThA nAnyopalabhyate tarkeNa vA'gamena vA tasmAdetadevAmR^itatvasAdhanaM yadetanneti netyAtmaparij~nAnaM sarvasaMnyAsashcetyetamarthamupasaMjihIrShannAha-etAvadetAvanmAtraM  yadetanneti netyadvaitAtmadarshanamidaM cAnyasahakArikAraNanirapekShamevAre maitreyyamR^itatvasAdhanam /
yatpR^iShTatyasi yadeva bhagavAnveda tadeva me brUhyamR^itatvasAdhanamiti tadetAvadevetu vij~neyaM tvayeti haivaM kilAmR^itatvasAdhanamAtmaj~nAnaM priyAyai bhAryAyA uktvA saMnyAsaparyavasAnA /
etAvAnupadesha etadvedAnushAsanameShA paramaniShThaiSha puruShArthakartavyatAnta iti /
idAnIM vicAryate shAstrArthavivekapratipattaye /
yata AkulAni hi vAkyAni dR^ishyante"yAvajjIvamagnihotraM juhuyAt" "yAvajjIvaM darshapUrNamAsAbhyAM yajeta" "kurvanneveha karmANi jijIviShecchataM samAH" "etadvai jarAmaryaM sarvaM yadagnihotram"ityAdInyaikAshramyAj~nApakAnyAni cA'shramAntarapratipAdakAni vAkyAni"viditvA vyutthAya pravrajanti" "brahmacaryaM samApya gR^ihI bhavedgrahAdvanI bhUtvA pravrajet" "yadi vetarathA brahmacaryAdeva pravrajedgR^ihAdvA vanAdvA"iti /
"na karmaNA na prajayA dhanena tyAgenaikemR^itatvamAnashuH"ityAdIni /
tathA smR^itayashca-"brahmacaryavAnpravrajati" "avishIrNabrahmacaryo yamicchattamAvaseti"tasyA'shramamavikalpamekebruvate"tathA-"vaidAnanadhItya brahmacaryeNa putrapautrAnicchetpAvanArthaM pitR^iNAm /
agnInAdhAya vidhivacceShTayaj~no vanaM pravishyAtha munirbubhUShet" //
"prAjApatyAM nirupyeShTiM sarvavesadakShiNAm /
AtmanyagnInsamAropya brAhmaNaH pravrajedgR^ihAt" //
ityAdyAH /
evaM vyutthAnavikalpakramayateShTAshramapratipattipratApAdakAni hi shrutismR^itivAkyAni shatasha upalaMbhyanta itaretaraviruddhAni /
AcArashca tadvidAm /
vipratipattishca shAstrArthapratapattÌNAM bahuvidAmapi /
ato na shakyate shAstrArtho mandabuddhibhirvivekena pratipattum /
pariniShThatashAstranyAyabuddhibhireva hyoShAM vAkyAnAM viShayavibhAgaH shakyate 'vadhArayitum /
tasmAdeShAM viShayavibhAgaj~nApanAya yathAbuddhisAmarthaMya vicArayiShyAmaH /
yAvajjIvashrutyAdivAkyAnAmanyArthAsaMbhavAtkriyAvasAna ava vedArtha /
taM yaj~napAtrairdahantItyantyakarmashravaNAjjarAmaryashravaNAcca liN^gAcca bhasmAntaM sharIramiti /
na hi pArivrAjyapakShe bhasmAntatA sharIrasya syAt /
smR^itishca-"niShekAdishmashAnAnto mantrairyasyodito vidhiH /
tasyA shAstre 'dhikAro 'smiJNj~neyo nAnyasya kasyacit"iti /
samantrakaM hi yatkarma vedeneha vidhIyate tasya shmashAnAntatAM darshayati smR^itiH /
adhikArAbhAvapradarshanAccAtyantameva shrutyadhikArAbhAvo 'karmiNo gamyate /
agnyudvAsanApavAdAcca 'vIrahA vA eSha devAnAM yo 'gnimudvAsayate' iti /
nanu vyutthAnAdivijhadhAnAdvaikalpikaM kriyAvasAnatvaM vedArthasya /
na /
anyArthatvAdvyutthAnAdishrutInAm /
'yAvajjIvamannihotraM juhoti'"yAjjIvaM darshapUrNamAsAbhyAM yajeta"ityevamAdInAM shrutInAM jIvanamAtranimittatvAdyadA na shakyate 'nyArthatA kalpayituM tadA vyutthAnAdivAkyAnAM karmAnadhikR^itaviShayatvasaMbhavAt /
"kurvanneveha karmANi jijIvaShecchataM samAH"iti ca mantravarNAjjarayA vA hyevAsmAnmucyate mR^ityunA veti ca jarAmR^ityubhyAmanyatra karmaviyogAcchidrAsaMbhavAtkarmiNAM shmashAnAntatvaM na vaikalpikam /
kANakubjAdayo 'pi karmaNyanadhikR^itA anugrAhyA eva shrutyeti vyutthAnAdyAshramAntaravidhAnaM nAnupapannam /
pArivrAjyAkramavidhAnasyAnavakAshatvamiti cet /
na /
vishvajitsarvamedhayoryAvajjIvavidhyapavAdatvAt /
yAvajjIvAgnihotrAdividhervishvajitsarvamedhayorevApavAdastatra ca kramapratipattisaMbhavo"brahmacaryaM samApya gR^ihI bhavedgR^ihAdvanI bhutvA pravrajedi"ti  virodhAnupapatteH /
na hyevaMviShayatve pArivrAjyakamavidhAnavAkyasya kashcidvirodhaH kramapratipatteH /
anyaviShayaparikalpanAyAM kashcidbAdhaH /
nA'tmaj~nAnasyAmR^itatvahetutvAbhyupagamAt /
yattAvadAtmetyevopAsItetyArabhya sa eSha neti netyetadantena granthena yadupasaMhR^itamAtmaj~nAnaM tadamR^itatvasAdhanamityabhyupagataM bhavatA /
tatraitAvadevAmR^itatvasAdhanamanyanirapekShamityetanna mR^iShyate /
tatra bhavantaM pR^icchAmi kimarthamAtmaj~nAnaM marShayati bhavAniti /
shR^iNu tatra kAraNaM yathAsvargakAmasya svargaprAptyupAyamajAnato 'gnihotrAdi svargasAdhanamabhyupagamyate tathehApyAtmaj~nAnam /
yathA j~nApyate tatAbhUtamevAmR^itatvasAdhanamAtmaj~nAnamabhyupagantuM yuktam tulyaprAmANyAdubhayatra /
yadyevaM kiM syAt /
sarvakarmahetUpamardakatvAdAtmaj~nAnasya vidyodbhave karmanivR^ittiH syAt /
dArAgnisaMbaddhAnAM tAvadagnihotrAdikarmaNAM bhedabuddhiviShayasaMpradAnakArakasAdhyatvam /
anyabuddhiparacchedyAM hyagnyAdidevatAM saMpradAnakArakabhUtAmantreNa na hi tatkarma nirvartyate /
yayA hi saMpradAnakArakabuddhyA saMpradAnakArakaM karmasAdhanatvenopadishyate seha vidyayA nivartyate"anyo 'sAvanyo 'hamasmIti na sa veda" "devAstaM parAduryo 'nyatrA'tmano devAnveda" "mR^ityo sa mR^ityumApnoti ya iha nAneva pashyati" "ekadhaivAnudraShTavyaM sarvamAtmAnaM pashyati"ityAdishrutibhyaH /
na ca deshakAlanimitta dyapekShatvaM vyavasthitAtmavastuviShayatvAdAtmaj~nAnasya /
kriyAyAstu puruShatantratvAtsyAddeshakAlanimittAdyepekShatvam /
j~nAnaM tu vastutantratvAnna deshakAlanimittAdyapekShate /
yathAgniruShNa AkAsho 'mUrta iti tathA'tmavij~nAnamapu /
nanvevaM sati prAmANabhUtasya karvidhernirodhaH syAt /
na ca tulyapramANayoritaretaranirodho yuktaH /
na /
svAbhAvikabhedabuddhimAtranirodhakatvAt /
na hi vidhyantaranirodhakamAtmaj~nAnam svAbhAvikabhedabuddhimAtraM niruNaddhi /
tathApi hetvapahArAtkarmAnupapattervidhainirodha eva syAditi cet /
na /
kAmapratiShedhAtkAmyapravR^ittinirodhavadadoShAt /
yathA svargakAmo yajeteti svargasAdhane yAge pravR^ittasya kAmapratiShevidheH kAme vihate kAmyayAgAnuShThAnapravR^ittirnirudhyate /
na caitAvatA kAmyavidhirniruddho bhavati /
kAmapratiShedhavidhinA kAmyavidheranarkatvaj~nAnAtpravR^ityanupapattiriti cet /
ananuShTheyatve 'nuShThAturabhAvAdanuShThAnavidhyAnarthakyAdaprAmANyameva karmavidhInAmiti cet /
na /
prAgAtmaj~nAnAtpravR^ityupapatteH svAbhAvikasya kriyAkArakaphalabhedavij~nAnasya prAgAtmaj~nAnAtkarmahetutvamupapadyata eva /
yathA kAmaviShaye doShavij~nAnotpatteH prAkkAmyakarmapravR^ittihetutvaM syAdeva svargAdIcchAyAH svAbhAvikyAstadvAt /
tathA satyanarthArtho veda iti cet /
na /
arthAnarthayorabhiprAtatantratvAt /
mokShamekaM varjayitvAnyasyAvidyAviShayatvAta /
puruShAbhiprAyatantrau hyArthAnarthau /
maraNAdikAmyeShTadarshanAt /
tasmAdyAvadAtmaj~nAnavidherAbhimukhyaM tAvadeva karmavidhaya /
tasmAnnA'tmaj~nAnasahabhAvitvaM karmaNAmityataH siddhamAtmaj~nAnamevAmR^itatvasAdhanametAvadare khalvamR^itatvamiti /
karmanirapekShatvAjj~nAnasya /
ato viduShastAvatpArivrAjyaM  siddhaM saMpradAnAdikarmakArakajAtyAdishUnyAvikriyabrahmAtmadR^iDhapratipattimAtreNa vacanamantareNApyuktanyAyataH /
tathAca vyAkhyAtametat"yeShAM no 'yamAtmAyaM loka"iti hotuvacanena /
pUrve vidvAsaH prajAmakAmayamAnA vyuttiShThantIti pArivrAjyaM viduShAmAtmalokAvabodhAdeva /
tathAca vividiShorapu siddhaM pArivrAjyam /
"etamevA'tmAnaM lokamicchantaH pravrajanti"iti vacanAt /
karmaNAM cAvidvadviShayatvamavocAma /
avidyAviShaye cotpatyAptivikArasaMskArthAni karmANItyataH AtmasaMskAradvaireNA'tmaj~nAnasAdhanatvamapi karmaNAmavocAma yaj~nAdibhirvividaShantIti /
athaita satyavidviShayANAmAshramakarmaNAM balAbalavicAraNAyAmAtmaj~nAnotpAdanaM prati yamapradhAnAnAmamAnitvAdInAM mAnasAnAM ca dhyAnaj~nAnavairAgyAdInAM sannipatyopakAratvam /
hiMsArAgadveShAdibAhulyAdbahukliShTakarmavimishritA itara ityataH pArivrAjyaM mumukShUNAM prashaMsanti-"tyAga eva hi sarveShAmuktAnAmapi karmaNAm /
vairAgyaM punaretasya mokShasya paramo 'vadhiH" //
"kiM te dhanena kimu bandhubhiste kiM te dArairbrAhmaNa yo mariShyasi /
AtmAnamanviccha guhA praviShTaM pitAmahAste kva gatAH pitA ca //
"evaM sAkhyayogashAstreShu ca saMnyAso j~nAnaM prati pratyAsanna ucyate /
kAmapravR^ittyabhAvAcca /
kAmapravR^itterhi j~nAnapratikUlatA sarvashAstreShu prasiddhA /
tasmAdviraktasya mumukShorvinApi j~nAnena brahmacaryAdeva pravrajedityAdyUpapannam /
nanu sAvakAshatvAdanadhikR^itaviShayametadityuktaM yAvajjIvashrutyuparodhAt /
naiSha doShaH /
nitarAM sAvakAshatvAdyAvajjIvashrutInAm /
avadvitkAmikartavyatA hyavocAma sarvakarmaNAm /
na tu nirapekShameva jIvananimittameva kartavyaM karma /
prAyeNahi puruShAH kAmabahulAH /
kAmashcAnekaviShayo 'nekakarmasAdhanasAdhyashca /
anekaphalasAdhanAni ca vaidikAni  karmANi dArAgnisaMbandhapuruShakartavyAnu punaH punashcAnuShThIyamAnAnu bahuphalAnu kR^iShyAdivadvarShashatasamAptIni ca gArhasthye vAraNye vAtastadapekShayA yAvajjIvashrutayaH /
'kurvanneveha karmANi' iti ca mantravarNaH /
tasmiMshca pakShe vishvajitsarvamedhayoH karmaparityAgaH /
yasmiMshca pakShe yAvajjIvAnuShThAnaM tadA shmashAnAntatvaM bhasmAntatA ca sharIrasya /
itaravarNApekShayA vA yAvajjIvashrutiH /
na hi kShattriyavaishyayo pArivrAjyapratipattirasti /
tathA 'mantrairyasyodito vidhiH' /
'aikAshramyaM tvAcAryA' ityevamAdInAM kShatriyavaishyApekShatvam /
tasmAtpurushasAmarthayaj~nAnavairAgyakAmAdyapekShayA vyutthAnavikalpakramapArivrAjyapripattaprakArA na virudhyante /
anadhikR^itAnAM ca pR^ithagvidhAnAtpArivrAjyas 'snAtako vAsnAtako votsannAgniranagniko ve'tyAdinA /
tasmAtsiddhAshramAntarANyadhikR^itAnAmeva //4,5.15//

iti paJNcamaM brAhmaNam //

#<pUrNam adaH pUrNam idaM pUrNAt pUrNam udacyate |

BrhUpBh_5,1.1 pUrNamadaH pUrNaM na kutashcid vyAvR^ittaM vyApItyetat /
niShThA ca kartari draShTavyA /
ada iti parokShAbhidhAyi sarvanAma, tatparaM brahmetyarthaH /
tat sampUrNamAkAshavad vyApi nirantaraM nirupAdhikaM ca tadevedaM sopAdhikaM nAmarUpasthaMvyavahArApannaM pUrNaM svena rUpeNa paramAtmanA vyApyeva nopAdhiparicchinnena visheShAtmanA /
tadidaM visheShApannaM kAryAtmakaM brahma pUrNAt kAraNAtmana udacyata udricyata udgacchatItyetat /
yadyapi kAryAtmanodricyate tathApi yat svarUpaM pUrNatvaM paramAtmabhAvaM tanna jAhAti pUrNamevodricyate /
pUrNasya kAryAtmano brahmaNaH pUrNa pUrNatvamAdAya gR^ihItvA AtmasvarUpaikarasatvamApadya, vidyayA avidyAkR^itaM bhUtamAtropAdhisaMsargajamanyatvAvabhAsaM tiraskR^itya pUrNamevAnantaramavAhyaM praj~nAnaghanaikarasasvabhAvaM kevalaM brahmAvashiShyate /
yaduktaM brahma vA idamagra AsIttadAtmAnamevAvettasmAttatsarvamabhavadityeSho 'sya mantrasyArthaH /
tatra brahmetyasyArthaH pUrNamada iti /
idaM pUrNamiti brahma vA idamagra AsIdityasyArthaH /
tathA ca shrutyantaram-"yadeveha tadamutrayadamutra tadanviha"iti /
ato 'daHshabdavAcyaM pUrNaM brahma tadevedaM pUrNaM kAryasthaM nAmarUpopAdhisaMyuktamavidyayodriktam /
tasmAdeva paramArthasvarUpAdanyadiva pratyavabhAsamAnam /
tadyadAtmAnameva paraM pUrNaM brahma viditvAhamadaH pUrNaM brahmAsmItyevaM pUrNamAdAya tiraskR^ityApUrNasvarUpatAmavidyAkR^itAM nAmarUpopAdhisaMparkajAmetayA brahmavidyayA pUrNameva kevalamavashiShyate /
tathA coktam"tasmAttatsarvamabhavat"iti /
yaH sarvopaniShadartho brahma sa eSho 'nena mantreNAnUdyata uttarasambandhArtham /
brahmavidyAsAdhanatvena hi vakShyamANAni sAdhanAnyoN^kAradamadAnadayAkhyAni vidhitsitAni khilaprakaraNasambandhAtsarvopAsanAN^gabhUtAni ca /
atraike varNayanti-pUrNAtkAraNAtpUrNaM kAryamudricyate /
udriktaM kAryaM vartamAnakAle 'pi pUrNameva paramArthavastubhUtaM dvaitarUpeNa /
punaH pralayakAle pUrNasya kAryasya pUrNatAmAdAyA'tmani dhitvA pUrNamevAvashiShyate kAraNarUpam /
evamutpattisthitipralayeShu triShvapi kAleShu kAryakAraNayoH pUrNataiva /
sA caikaiva pUrNatA kAryakAraNayorbhedena vyapadishyate /
evaM ca dvaitAdvaitAtmakamekaM brahma /
yathA kila samudro jalataraN^gaphenabudbudAdyAtmaka eva /
yathA ca jalaM satyaM tadudbhavAshca taraN^gaphelabudbudAdayaH samudrAtmabhUtA evA'virbhAvatirobhAvadharmiNaH paramArthasatyA eva /
evaM sarvamidaM dvaitaM paramArthasatyameva jalataraN^gAdisthAnIyaM samudrajalasthAnIyaM tu paraM brahma /
evaM ca kila dvaitasya satyatve karmakANDasya prAmANyaM yadA punardvaitaM dvaitamivAvidyAkR^itaM mR^igatR^iShNikAvadanR^itamadvaitameva paramArthatastadA kila karmakANDaM viShayAbhAvAdapramANaM bhavati /
tathA ca virodha eva syAt /
vedaikadeshabhUtopaniShatpramANaM paramArthAdvaitavastupratipAdakatvAdapramANaM karmakANDamasaddvaitaviShayatvAt /
tadvirodhaparijihIrShayA shrutyaitaduktaM kAryakAraNayoH satyatvaM samudravatpUrNamada ityAdineti /
tadasat /
vishiShTaviShayApavAdavikalpayorasambhavAt /
na hIyaM suvivakShitA kalpanA /
kasmAt /
yathA kriyAviShaya utsargaprAptasyaikadeshe 'pavAdaH kriyate /
yathAhiMsansarvabhUtAnyanyatra tIrthebhya iti hiMsA sarvabhUtaviShayotsargeNa nivAritA tIrthe vishiShTaviShaye jyotiShTomAdAvanuj~nAyate /
na ca tathA vastuviShaya ihAdvaitaM brahmotsargeNa pratipAdya punastadekadeshe 'pavadituM shakyate /
brahmaNo 'dvaitatvAdevaikadeshAnupapatteH /
tathA vikalpAnupapatteshca /
yathAtirAtre ShoDashinaM gR^ihNAti nAtirAtre ShoDashinaM gR^ihNAtIti grahaNAgrahaNayoH puruShAdhInatvAdvikalpo bhavati /
na tviha tathA vastuviShaye dvaitaM vA syAdadvaitaM veti vikalpaH sambhavatyapuruShatantratvAdAtmavastunaH /
virodhAcca dvaitAdvaitatvayorekasya /
tasmAnna suvivakShiteyaM kalpanA /
shrutinyAyavirodhAcca /
saindhavaghanavatpraj~nAnaikarasaghanaM nirantaraM pUrvAparabAhyAbhyantarabhedavivarjitaM sabAhyAbhyantaramajaM neti netyasthUlamanaNvajamajaramabhayamamR^itamityevamAdyAH shrutayo nishcitArthAH saMshayaviparyAsAshaN^kArahitAH sarvAH samudre prakShiptAH syurakiJNcitkaratvAt /
tathA nyAyavirodho 'pi sAvayavasyAnekAtmakasya kriyAvato nityatvAnupapatteH /
nityatvaM cA'tmanaH smR^ityAdidarshanAdanumIyate /
tadvirodhashca prApnotyanityatve /
bhavatkalpanAnarthakyaM ca /
sphuTameva cAsminpakShe karmakANDAnarthakyam /
akR^itAbhyAgamakR^itavipraNAshaprasaN^gAt /
nanu brahmaNo dvaitAdvaitAtmakatve samudrAdidR^iShTAntA vidyante kathamucyate bhavataikasya dvaitAdvaitatvaM viruddhamiti /
na /
anyaviShayatvAt /
nityAniravayavavastuviShayaM hi viruddhatvamavocAma dvaitAdvaitatvasya na kAryaviShaye sAvayave /
tasmAcchrutismatinyAyavirodhAdanupapanneyaM kalpanA /
asyAH kalpanAyA varamupaniShatparityAga eva /
adhyeyatvAcca na sAstrArtheyaM kalpanA /
na hi jananamaraNAdyanarthashatasahasrabhedasamAkulaM samudravanAdivatsAvayavamanekarasaM brahma dhyeyatvena vij~neyatvena vA shrutyopadishyate /
praj~nAnaghanatAM copadishati /
ekadhaivAnudraShTavyamiti ca /
anekadhAdarshanApavAdAcca"mR^ityoH sa mR^ityumApnoti ya iha nAneva pashyati"iti /
yacca shrutyA ninditaM tanna kartavyam /
yacca na kriyate na sa shAsrArthaH /
brahmaNo 'nekarasatvamanekadhAtvaM ca dvaitarUpaM ninditatvAnna draShTavyam /
ato na shAsrArthaH /
yattvekarasatvaM brahmaNastaddraShTavyatvAtprashastaM prashastatvAcca shAstrArtho bhavitumarhati /
yattUktaM vedaikadeshasyAprAmANyaM karmaviShaye dvaitAbhAvAdadvaite ca prAmANyamiti /
tanna /
yathAprAptopadeshArthatvAt /
na hi dvaitamadvaitaM vA vastu jAtamAtrameva puruShaM j~nApayitvA pashcAtkarma vA brahmavidyAM vopadishati shAsram /
na copadeshArhaM dvaitaM jAtamAtraprANibuddhigamyatvAt /
na ca dvaitasyAnR^itatvabuddhiH prathamameva kasyAcitsyAt /
yena dvaitasya satyatvamupadishya pashcAdAtmanaH prAmANyaM pratipAdayecchAsram /
nApi pAShaNDibhirapi prasthApitAH shAsrasya prAmANyaM na gR^ihNIyuH /
tasmAdyathAprAptameva dvaitamavidyAkR^itaM svAbhAvikamupAdAya svAbhAvikyaivAvidyayA yuktAya rAgadveShAdidoShavate yathAbhimatapuruShArthasAdhanaM karmopadishatyagre pashcAtprasiddhakriyAkArakaphalasvarUpadoShadarshanavate tadbiparItaudAsInyasvarUpAvasthAnaphalArthine tadupAyabhUtAmAtmaikatvadarshanAtmikAM brahmavidyAmupadishati /
athaivaM sati tadaudAsInyasvarUpAvasthAne phale prApte shAsrasya prAmANyaM pratyarthitvaM nivartate /
tadabhAvAcchAsrasyApi shAsratvaM taM prati nivartata eva /
tathA pratipuruShaM parisamAptaM shAsramiti na shAsravirodhagandho 'pyasti /
advaitaj~nAnAvasAnatvAcchAsrashiShyashAsanAdidvaitabhedasya /
anyatamAvasthAne hi virodhaH syAdavasthitasyetaretarApekShatvAttu shAsrashiShyashAsanAnAM nAnyatamo 'pyavatiShThate /
sarvasamAptau tu kasya viredha AshaN^kyetAdvaite kevale shive siddhe /
nApyavirodhatAta eva /
athApyabhyupagamya brUmaH-dvaitAdvaitAtmakatve 'pi shAsravirodhasya tulyatvAt /
yadApi samudrAdivaddvaitAtmakamekameva brahma nAnyadastIti virudhyate /
yasmindvaitaviShaye 'nyonyopadeshaH so 'nyo dvaitaM cAnyadeveti samudradR^iShTAnto viruddhaH /
na ca samudrodakaikatvavadvij~nAnaikatve brahmaNo 'nyatropadeshagrahaNAdikalpanA sambhavati /
na hi hastAdidvaitAdvaitAtmake devadatte vAkkarNayordevadattaikadeshabhUtayorvAgupadeShTrI karNaH kevala upadeshasya grahItA devadattastu nopadeShTA nApyupadeshasya grahIteti kalpayituM shakyate /
samudraikodakAtmatvavadekavij~nAnavatvAddevadattasya /
tasmAcchratinyAyavirodhashcAbhipretArthAsiddhishcaivaN^kalpanAyAM syAt /
tasmAdyathAvyAkhyAta evAsmAbhiH pUrNamada ityasya mantrasyArthaH /
oM khaM brahmeti mantro 'yaM cAnyatrAviniyukta iha brAhmaNena dhyAnakarmaNi viniyujyate /
atra ca brahmeti visheShyAbhidhAnaM khamiti visheShaNam /
visheShaNavisheShyayoshca sAmAnAdhikaraNyena nirdesho nIlotpalavat khaM brahmeti /
brahmashabdo bR^ihadvastumAtrAspado 'visheShito 'to visheShyate khaM brahmeti /
yattatkhaM brahma tadoMshabdavAcyamoMshabdasvarUpamevavobhayathApi sAmAnAdhikaraNyamaviruddham /
iha ca brahmopAsanasAdhanatvArthamoMshabdaH prayuktaH /
tathA ca shrutyantarAt"etadAlambanaM shreShThametadAlambanaM param" "omityAtmAnaM yuJNjIta" "omityetenaivAkShareNa paraM puruShamabhidhyAyIta""omityevaM dhyAyatha AtmAnam"ityAdeH /
anyArthAsaMbhavAccopadeshasya /
yathA'nyatromiti shaMsatyomityudgAyatItyevamAdau svAdhyAyArambhApavargayoshcoN^kAraprayogo viniyogAdavagamyate na ca tathAr'thAntaramihAvagamyate /
tasmAddhyAnasAdhanatvenaivehoN^kArashabdasyopadeshaH /
yadyapi brahmAtmAdishabdA brahmaNo vAcakAstathApi shrutiprAmANyAdbrahmaNo nediShThamabhidhAnamoN^kAraH /
ata eva brahmapratipattAvidaM paraM sAdhanam /
tacca dviprakAreNa pratIkatvenAbhidhAnatvena ca /
pratIkatvena yathA viShNvAdipratimAbhedena, evamoN^kAro brahmeti pratipattavyaH /
tathA hyoN^kArAlambanasya brahma prasIdati /
"etadAlambanaM shreShThametadAlambanaM param /
etadAlambanaM j~nAtvA brahmaloke mahIyate"iti shruteH /
tatra khamiti bhautike khe pratItirmA bhUdityAha-khaM purANaM ciratanaM khaM paramAtmAkAshamityarthaH /
yattatparamAtmAkAshaM purANaM khaM taccakShurAdyaviShayatvAnnirAlambanamashakyaM grahItumiti shraddhAbhaktibhyAM bhAvavisheSheNa coN^kAra Aveshayati /
yathA viShNvaN^gAN^kitAyAM shilAdipratimAyAM viShNuM loka evam /
vAyuraM khaM vAyurasminvidyata iti vAyuraM khaM khamAtraM khamityucyate na purANaM khamityevamAha sma /
ko 'sau /
kauravyAyaNIputraH /
vAyure hi khe mukhyaH svashabdavyavahArastasmAnmukhe saMpratyayo yukta iti manyate /
tatra yadi purANaM khaM brahma nirUpAdhisvarUpaM yadi vA vAyuraM khaM sopAdhikaM brahma sarvathApyoN^kAraH pratIkatvenaiva pratimAvatsAdhanatvaM pratipadyate /
etadvai satyakAma paraM cAparaM ca brahma yadoN^kAraH iti shrutyantarAt /
kevalaM svashabdArthe vipratipattiH /
vedo 'yamoN^kAro veda vijAnAtyanena yadveditavyam /
tasmAdveda oN^kAro vAcako 'bhidhAnam /
tenAbhidhAnena yadveditavyaM brahma prakAshyamAnamabhidhIyamAnaM veda sAdhako vijAnAtyupalabhate /
tasmAdvedo 'yamiti brAhmaNA viduH /
tasmAdbrAhyaNAnAmabhidhAnatvena sAdhanatvamabhipretamoN^kArasya /
athavA vedo 'yamityAdyarthavAdaH /

oM khaM brahmeti sAmAnAdhikaraNyAttasya stutiridAnIM vedatvena /

itarasyApi vedasya vedatvamata eva /
tasmAdvishiShTo 'yamoN^kAraH sAdhanatvena pratipattavya iti /
athavA vedaH saH /
ko 'sau /
yaM brAhmaNA viduroN^kArAt /
brAhmaNAnAM hyasau praNavodgothAdivikalpairvij~neyaH /
tasminhi prayujyamAne sAdhanatvena sarvo vedaH prayukto bhavatIti //1//

#<iti shrIbR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadbhAShye paJNcamAdhyAyasya prathamaM brAhmaNam //1//>#

BrhUpBh_5,2.1 adhunA damAdisAdhanatrayavidhAnArthoM'yamArambhaH - trayAstrisaMkhyAkAH prajApatyAH prajApaterapatyAni prAjApatyAste kiM prajApattau pitari brahmacaryaM shiShyatvavR^itterbrahmacaryasya prAdhAnyAcchiShyAH santo brahmacaryamUShuruShitavanta ityarthaH /

BrhUpBh_5,2.3 tathAsurA dayadhvamiti /

kAmaH krodhastathA lobhastasmAdetat trayaM tyajet iti /
asya hi vidheH sheShaH pUrvaH /
tathApi devAdInuddishya kimarthaM dakAratrayamuccAritavAnprajApatiH pR^ithaganushAsanArthibhyaH /
te vA kathaM vivekena pratipannAH prajApatermanogataM samAnenaiva dakAravarNamAtreNeti parAbhiprAyaj~nA vikalpayanti /
atraika AhuradAntatvAdAnAtvAdayAsutvairaparAdhitvamAtmano manyamAnAH shaN^kitA eva prajApatAvUShuH kiM no vakShyatIti /
teShAM ca dakArashravaNamAtrAdevA'tmAshaN^kAvashena tadarthapratipattirabhUt /

ato yuktaM prajApaterdakAramAtroccAraNam /

atrocyate - pUrvairdaivAdibhirapyekaikamevopAdeyamadyatve 'pi na tu trayaM manuShyaiH shikShitavyamiti /

tathA ca smR^itiH kAmaH krodhastathA lobhastasmAdetat trayaM tyajet iti //3//

START BrhUp 5,3.1

#<eSha prajApatir yad dhR^idayam |

START BrhUp 5,4.1

katham /

START BrhUp 5,5.2

#<tad yat tat satyam asau sa AdityaH |
ya eSha etasmin maNDale puruSho yash cAyaM dakShiNe 'kShan puruShas tAv etAv anyo 'nyasmin pratiShThitau |
rashmibhir eSho 'smin pratiShThitaH prANair ayam amuShmin |
sa yadotkramiShyan bhavati shuddham evaitan maNDalaM pashyati |
nainam ete rashmayaH pratyAyanti || BrhUp_5,5.2 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_5,5.2 asyAdhunA satyasya brahmaNaH saMsthAnavisheSha upAsanamucyate-tadyat /
kiM tatsatyaM brahma prathamajaM kimasau saH /
ko 'sAvAdityaH kaH punarasAvAdityo ya eSha ka eSha ya etasminnAdityamaNDale puruSho 'bhimAnI so 'sau satyaM brahma /
yashcAyamadhyAtmaM yo 'yaM dakShiNe 'kShannakShaNi puruShaH /
cashabdAtsa ca satyaM brahmeti saMbandhaH /
tAvetAvAdityAkShisthau puruShAvekasya satyasya brahmaNaH saMsthAnavisheShau yasmAttasmAdanyonyasminnitaretarasminnAdityashcAkShuShe cAkShuShashcA'ditye pratiShThitau /
adhyAtmAdhidaivatayoranyonyopakAryopakArakatvAt /
kathaM pratiShThitAvityucyate rashmibhiH prakAshenAnugrahaM kurvanneSha Adityo 'smiMshcAkShuShe 'dhyAtme pratiShThitaH /
ayaM ca cAkShuShaH prANairAdityamanugR^ihNannamuShminnAditye 'dhidaive pratiShThitaH /
so 'smiJNcharIre vij~nAnamayo bhoktA yadA yasminkAla utkramiShyanbhavati tadAsau cAkShuSha AdityapuruSho rashmInupasaMhR^itya kevalenaudAsInyena rUpeNa vyavatiShThate /
tadAyaM vij~nAnamayaH pashyati shuddhameva kevalaM virashmyetanmaNDalaM candramaNDalamiva /
tadetadariShTadarshanaM prAsahgikaM pradarshayate /
kathaM nAma puruShaH karaNIye yatnavAnsyAditi /
nainaM cAkShuShaM puruShamurarIkR^itya taM pratyanugrahAyaite rashmayaH svAmikartavyavashAtpUrvamAgacchanto 'pi punastatkarmakShayamanurudhyamAnA iva nopayanti na pratyAgacchantyenam /
ato 'vagamyate parasparopakAryopakArakabhAvAtsatyasyaivaikasyA'tmanoM'shA vetAviti //2//

START BrhUp 5,5.3

#<ya eSha etasmin maNDale puruShas tasya bhUr iti shiraH |
ekaM shira ekam etad akSharam |
bhuva iti bAhU |
dvau bAhU dve ete akShare |
svar iti pratiShThA |
dve pratiShThe dve ete akShare |
tasyopaniShad ahar iti |
hanti pApmAnaM jahAti ca ya evaM veda || BrhUp_5,5.3 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_5,5.3  tatra yo 'sau ko ya eSha etasminmaNDale puruShaH satyanAmA tasya vyAhR^itayo 'vayavAH /
katham /
bhUriti yeyaM vyAhR^itiH sA tasya shiraH /
prAthamyAt /
tatra sAmAnyaM svayamevAha shruti-ekamekasaMkhyAyiktaM shirastathaitadakSharamekaM bhUriti /
bhuva iti bAhU dvitvasAmAnyAddvau bAhU dve ete akShare /
tathA svariti pratiShThA dve pratiShThe dve ete akShare /
pratiShThe pAdau pratitiShThatyAbhyAmiti /
tasyAsya vyAhR^ityavayavasya satyasya brahmaNa upaniShadrahasyamabhidhAnam /
yenAbhidhAnenAbhidhIyamAnaM tadbrahmAbhimukho bhavati lokavat /
kAsAvityAha - ahariti ahariti caitadrUpaM hanterjahAteshceti yo veda sa hanti jahAti ca pApmAnaM ya evaM veda //3//

START BrhUp 5,5.4

#<yo 'yaM dakShiNe 'kShan puruShas tasya bhUr iti shiraH |

dvau bAhU dve ete akShare |

__________


BrhUpBh_5,5.4 evaM yo 'yaM dakShiNe 'kShanpuruShastasya bhUriti shira ityAdi sarvaM samAnam /

START BrhUp 5,6.1

#<manomayo 'yaM puruSho bhAHsatyaH |
tasminn antar hR^idaye yathA vrIhir vA yavo vA |
sa eSha sarvasyeshAnaH sarvasyAdhipatiH sarvam idaM prashAsti yad idaM kiJNca || BrhUp_5,6.1 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_5,6.1 upAdhInAmanekatvAdanekavisheShaNatvAcca tasyaiva prakR^itasya brahmaNo manaupAdhivishiShTasyopAsanaM vidhitsannAhamanomayo manaHprAyo manasyupalabhyamAnatvAt /
manasA copalabhata iti manomayo 'yaM puruSho bhAH satyo bhA eva satyaM sadbhAvaH svarUpaM yasya so 'yaM bhAH satyo bhAsvara ityetat /

sa eSha sarvasyeshAnaH sarvasya svabhedajAtasyeshAnaH svAmI /
svAmitve 'pi sati kashcidamAtyAditantro 'yaM tu na tathA kiM tarhyadhipatiradhiShThAya pAlayitA /

START BrhUp 5,7.1

#<vidyud brahmety AhuH |

BrhUpBh_5,7.1 tathaivopAsanAntaraM satyasya brahmaNo vishiShTaphalamArabhyate - vidyudbrahmetyAhuH /

START BrhUp 5,8.1

#<vAcaM dhenum upAsIta |
tasyAsh catvAraH stanAH |
svAhAkAro vaShaTkAro hantakAraH svadhAkAraH |
tasyai dvau stanau devA upajIvanti |
svAhAkAraM ca vaShaTkAraM ca |
hantakAraM manuShyAH |
svadhAkAraM pitaraH |
tasyAH prANa R^iShabho mano vatsaH || BrhUp_5,8.1 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_5,8.1 punarupAsanAntaraM tasyaiva brahmaNo vAgvai brahmeti vAgiti shabdasrayI tAM vAcaM dhenuM dhenuriva dhenuryathA dhenushcaturbhiH stanaiH stanyaM payaH kSharati vatsAyaivaM vAgdhenurvakShyamANaiH stanaiH paya ivAnnaM kSharati devAdibhyaH /
ke punaste stanA ye vA te yebhyaH kSharati /
tasyA etasyA vAco dhenvA dvau stanau devA upajIvanti vatsasthAnIyAH /
kau tau /
svAhAkAraM ca vaShaTkAraM ca /
AbhyAM hi havirdIyate devebhyaH /
hantakAraM manuShyAH /
hanteti manuShyebhyo 'nnaM prayacchanti /
svadhAkAraM ca vaShaTkAraM ca /
AbhyAM hi havirdIyate devebhyaH /
hantakAraM manuShyAH /
hanteti manuShyebhyo 'nnaM prayacchanti svadhAkAraM ca vaShaTkAraM ca /
AbhyAM hi havirdIyate devebhyaH /
hantakAraM manuShyAH /
hanteti manuShyebhyo 'nnaM prayacchanti /
svadhAkAraM pitaraH /
svadhAkAreNa hi pitR^ibhyaH svadhAM prayacchanti /
tasyA dhenvA vAcaH prANa R^iShabhaH /
prANena hi vAkprasUyate /
mano vatsaH /
manasA hi prasrAvyate /
manasA hyAlocite viShaye vAkpravartate /
tasmAnmano vatsasthAnIyam /
evaM vAgdhenUpAsakastAdbhAvyameva pratipadyate //1//

#<iti shrImadbR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadbhAShye paJNcamAdhyAyasyAShTamaM brAhmaNam //8//>#

START BrhUp 5,9.1

#<ayam agnir vaishvAnaro yo 'yam antaH puruShe |
yenedam annaM pacyate |
yad idam adyate |
tasyaiSha ghoSho bhavati |
yam etat karNAv apidhAya shR^iNoti |

BrhUpBh_5,9.1 ayamagnirvaishvAnanaraH pUrvavadupAsanAntaramayamagnirvaishvAnaraH /

tatra prAsaN^gikamidamariShTalakShaNamucyate-so 'tra sharIre bhoktA yadotkramiShyanbhavati nainaM ghoShaM shR^iNoti //1//

#<iti shrImadbR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadbhAShye paJNcamAdhyAyasya navamaM brAhmaNam //9//>#

START BrhUp 5,10.1

#<yadA vai puruSho 'smAl lokAt praiti sa vAyum Agacchati |
tasmai sa tatra vijihIte yathA rathacakrasya kham |
tena sa Urdhva Akramate |
sa Adityam Agacchati |
tasmai sa tatra vijihIte |
yathA lambarasya kham |
tena sa Urdhva Akramate |
sa candramasam Agacchati |
tasmai sa tatra vijihIte |
yathA dundubheH kham |
tena sa Urdhva Akramate |
sa lokam Agacchaty ashokam ahimam |
tasmin vasati shAshvatIH samAH || BrhUp_5,10.1 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_5,10.1 sarveShAmasminprakaraNa upAsanAnAM gatiriyaM phalaM cocyate-yadA vai puruSho vidvAnasmAllokAtpraiti sharIraM parityajati sa tadA vAyumAgacchatyantarikShe tiryagbhUto vAyuH stimito 'bhedyastiShThati /
sa vAyustatra svAtmani tasmai samprAptAya vijihote svAtmAvayavAnvigamayati cchidrIkarotyAtmAnamityarthaH /
kiMparimAmaM chidramiti /
ucyate-yathA ratha vakrasya khaM chidraM prasiddhaparimANam /
tena chidreNa sa vidvAnUrdhva Akramata UrdhvaH sangacchati sa AdityamAgacchati /
Adityo brahmalokaM jigamiShormArganirodhaM kR^itvA sthitaH so 'pyevaMvida upAsakAya dvAraM prayacchati /
tasmai sa tatra vijihote /
yathA lambarasya khaM vAditravisheShasya cchidraparimAmaM tena sa Urdhva Akramate sa candramasamAgacchati /
so 'pi tasmai tatra vijihIte /
yathA dundubheH khaM prasiddhaM tena sa Urdhva Akramate sa lokaM prajApatilokamAgacchati /
kiMvishiShTam /
ashokaM mAnasena duHkhena vivarjitamityetat /
ahimaM himavarjitaM shArIraduHkhavarjitamityarthaH /
taM prApya tasminvasati shAshvatIrnityAH samAH saMvatsarAnityarthaH /
brahmaNo bahUnkalpAnvasatItyetat //1//

#<iti shrImadbR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadbhAShye paJNcamAdhyAyasya dashamaM brAhmaNam //10//>#

START BrhUp 5,11.1

#<etad vai paramaM tapo yad vyAhitas tapyate |

paramaM haiva lokaM jayati ya evaM veda |

BrhUpBh_5,11.1 etadvai paramaM tapaH /

START BrhUp 5,12.1

#<annaM brahmety eka AhuH |
tan na tathA |
pUyati vA annam R^ite prANAt |
prANo brahmety eka AhuH |
tan na tathA |
shuShyati vai praNa R^ite 'nnAt |
ete ha tv eva devate ekadhAbhUyaM bhUtvA paramatAM gacchataH |
tad dha smAha prAtR^idaH pitaram |
kiM svid evaivaM viduShe sAdhu kuryAM kim evAsmA asAdhu kuryAm iti |
sa ha smAha pANinA mA prAtR^ida |
kas tv enayor ekadhAbhUyaM bhUtvA paramatAM gacchatIti |

anne hImAni sarvANi bhUtAni viShTAni |
ram iti |

BrhUpBh_5,12.1 annaM brahmeti /

anye cA'huH prANo brahmeti tacca tathA na grahItavyam /
kimarthaM punarannaM brahmeti na grAhyam /
yasmAtpUyati klidyate pUtibhAvamApadyata R^ite prANAttatkathaM brahma bhavitumarhati /
brahma hi nAma tadyadavinAshi /
astu tarhi prANo brahma /
naiva /
yasmAcchuShyati vai prANa R^ite 'nnAt /
attA hi prANaH /
ato 'nnenA'dyena vinA na shaknotyAtmAnaM dhArayitum /
tasmAcchruShyati vai prANa R^ite 'nnAt /
ata ekaikasya brahmatA nopapadyate yasmAttasmAdete ha tvevAnnaprANadevate ekadhAbhUyamekadhAbAvaM bhUtvA gatvA paramatAM paramatvaM gacchato brahmatvaM prApnutaH /
tadetadevamadhyavasya ha smA'ha sma prAtR^ido nAma pitarAtmanaH kiMsviditisviditi vitarke /
yathA mayA brahma parikalpitamevaM viduShe kiMsvitsAdhu kuryAM sAdhu shobhanaM pUjAM kAM tvasmai kuryAmityabhiprAyaH /
kinevAsmai viduShe 'sAdhu kuryAM kR^itakR^ityo 'sAvityabhiprAyaH /
annaprANau sahabhUto brahmeti vidvAnnAsAvasAdhukaramena khaNDito bhavati /
nApi sAdhukaraNena mahIkR^itaH /
tadevaMvAdinaM sa pitA ha smA'ha pANinA hastena nivArayanmA prAtR^ida maivaM vocaH /
kastvenayorannaprANayorekadhAbhUyaM bhUtvA paramatAM kastu gacchati na kashcidapi vidvAnanena brahmadarshanena paramatAM gacchati /
tasmAnnaivaM vaktumarhasi kR^itakR^ityo 'sAviti /
yadyevaM bravItu bhavAnkathaM paramatAM gacchatIti /
tasmA u haitadvakShyamANaM vaca uvAca /
kiM tat /
vIti /
kiM tadvIti /
ucyate-annaM vai vi /
anne hi yasmAdimAni sarvANi bhUtAni viShTAnyAshritAnyato 'nnaM vItyucyate /
kiJNca ramiti /
ramiti coktavAnpitA /
kiM punastadram /
prANo vai ram /
kuta ityAha /
prANe hi kashcidanAyatano nirAshrayo ramate /
nApi satyapyAyatane 'prANo durbalo ramate /
yadA tvAyatanavAnprANI balavAMshca tadA kR^itArthamAtmAnaM manyamAno ramate lokaH /
"yuvA syAtsAdhuyuvAdhyAyakaH"ityAdishruteH /
idAnImevaMvidaH phalamAha - sarvANi ha vA asminbhUtAni vishantyannaguNaj~nAnAtsarvANi bhUtAni ramante prANaguNaj~nAnAdya evaM veda //1//

#<iti shrImadbR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadbhAShye paJNcamAdhyAyasya dvAdashaM brAhmaNam //12//>#

START BrhUp 5,13.1

#<uktham |

START BrhUp 5,13.4

#<kShatram |

START BrhUp 5,14.1

#<bhUmir antarikShaM dyaur ity aShTAv akSharANi |
aShTAkSharaM ha vA ekaM gAyatryai padam |
etad u haivAsyA etat |
sa yAvad eShu triShu lokeShu tAvad dha jayati yo 'syA etad evaM padaM veda || BrhUp_5,14.1 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_5,14.1 brahmaNo hR^idayAdyanekopAdhivishiShTasyopAsanamuktamathedAnIM gAyatryupAdhivishiShTasyopAsanaM vaktavyamityArabhyate /
sarvacchandasAM hi gAyatrIcchandaH pradhAnabhUtam /
tatprayoktR^igayatrANAdgAyatrIti vakShyati /
na cAnyeShAM chandasAM prayoktR^iprANatrANasAmarthyam /
prANAtmabhUtA ca sA sarvacchandasAM cA'tmA prANaH /
prANashca kShatatrANAtkShattramityuktam /
prANashca gAyatrI /
tasmAttadupAsanameva vidhitsyate /
dvijottamajanmahetutvAcca /
gAyatryA brAhmaNamasR^ijata triShTubhA rAjanyaM jagatyA vaishyamati dvijottamasya dvitIyaM janma gAyatrInimittam /
tasmAtpradhAnA gAyatrI brAhmaNA vyutthAya brAhmaNA abhivadanti sa brAhmaNo vipApo virajo 'vicikitso brAhmaNo bhavatItyuttamapuruShArthasaMbandhaM brAhmaNasya darshayati /
tacca brAhmaNatvaM gAyatrIjanmamUlamato vaktavyaM gAyatryAH satattvam /
gAyatryA hi yaH sR^iShTo dvijottamo niraN^kusha evottamapuruShArthasAdhane 'dhikriyate 'tastanmUlaH paramapuruShArthasaMbandhaH /
tasmAttadupAsanavidhAnAyA'ha-bhUmirantarikShaM dyaurityetAnyaShTAvakSharANi /
aShTAkSharamaShTAvakSharANi yasya tadidamaShTAkSharam /
ha vai prasiddhAvadyotakau /
ekaM prathamaM gAyatryai gAyatryAH padam /
yakAreNaivAShTatvapUraNam /
etadu haivaitadevAsyA gAyatryAH padaM pAdaH prathamo bhUmyAdilakShaNasrailokyAtmA /
aShTAkSharatvasAmAnyAt /
evametattrailokyAtmakaM gAyatryAH prathamaM padaM yo vedatasyaitatphalam-sa vidvAnyAvatkiJNcideShu triShu jetavyaM tAvatsarvaM ha jayati yo 'syA etadevaM padaM veda //1//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 5,14.2

#<R^ico yajUShi sAmAnIty aShTAv akSharANi |
aShTAkSharaM ha vA ekaM gAyatryai padam |
etad u haivAsyA etat |
sa yAvatIyaM trayI vidyA tAvad dha jayati yo 'syA etad evaM padaM veda || BrhUp_5,14.2 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_5,14.2 tadarco yajUMsi sAmAnIti trayIvidyAnAmAkSharANyetAnyapyaShTAveva tathaivAShTAkSharaM ha vA ekaM gAyatryai padaM dvitIyametadu haivAsyA etadR^igyajuHsAmalakShaNamaShTAkSharatvasAmAnyAdeva /
sa yAvatIyaM trayI vidyA trayyA vidyayA yAvatphalajAtamApyate tAvaddha jayati yo 'syA etadgAyatryAsraividyalakShaNaM padaM veda //2//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 5,14.3

#<prANo 'pAno vyAna ity aShTAv akSharANi |
aShTAkSharaM ha vA ekaM gAyatryai padam |
etad u haivAsyA etat |
sa yAvad idaM prANi tAvad dha jayati yo 'syA etad evaM padaM veda |
athAsyA etad eva turIyaM darshataM padaM parorajA ya eSha tapati |
yad vai caturthaM tat turIyam |
darshataM padam iti dadR^isha iva hy eShaH |
parorajA iti sarvam u hy evaiSha raja upary upari tapati |
evaM haiva shriyA yashasA tapati yo 'syA etad evaM padaM veda || BrhUp_5,14.3 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_5,14.3 tathA prANo 'pAno vyAna etAnyapi prANAdyabhidhAnAkSharANyaShTau /
tacca gAyatryAstR^itIyaM padaM yAvadidaM prANijAtaM tAvaddha jayati yo 'syA etadevaM gAyatryAstR^itIyaM padaM veda /
athAnantaraM gAyatryAsripadAyAH shabdAtmikAyAsturIyaM padamucyate 'bhidheyabhUtamasyAH prakR^itAyA gAyatryA etadeva vakShyamAmaM turIyaM darshataM padaM parorajA ya eSha tapati /
turIyamityAdivAkyapadArthaM svameva vyAcaShTe shrutiH-yadvai caturthaM prasiddhaM loke tadidaM turIyashabdenAbhidhIyate /
darshataM padamityasya kor'tha ityucyate-dadR^isha iva dR^ishyata iva hyeSha maNDalasthaH puruSho rajo rajojAtaM samastaM lokamityarthaH /
uparyuparyAdhipatyabhAvena sarvaM lokaM rajojAtaM tapati /
uparyuparIti vIpsA sarvalokAdhipatyakhyApanArthA /
nanu sarvashabdenaiva siddhatvAdvIpsAnarthikA /
naiSha doShaH /
yeShAmupariShTAtsavitA dR^ishyate tadviShaya eva sarvashabdaH syAdityAshaN^kAnivR^ittyarthA vIpsA /
"ye cAmuShmAtparAJNco lokAsteShAM ceShTe devakAnAM ca"iti shrutyanrAt /
tasmAtsarvAvarodhArthA vIpsA /
yathAsau savitA sarvAdhipatyalakShaNayA shriyA yashasA ca khyAtyA tapatyevaM haiva shriyA yashasA ca tapati yo 'syA etadevaM turIyaM darshataM padaM veda //3//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 5,14.4

#<saiShA gAyatry etasmiMs turIye darshate pade parorajasi pratiShThitA |
tad vai tat satye pratiShThitam |
cakShur vai satyam |
cakShur hi vai satyam |
tasmAd yad idAnIM dvau vivadamAnAv eyAtam aham adarsham aham ashrauSham iti |
ya evaM brUyAd aham adarsham iti |
tasmA eva shraddadhyAma |
tad vai tat satyaM bale pratiShThitam |
prANo vai balam |
tat prANe pratiShThitam |
tasmAd Ahur balaM satyAd ogIya iti |
evaM v eShA gAyatry adhyAtmaM pratiShThitA |
sA haiShA gayAMs tatre |
prANA vai gayAH |
tat prANAs tatre |
tad yad gayAMs tatre tasmAd gAyatrI nAma |
sa yAm evAmUM sAvitrIm anvAhaiShaiva sA |
sa yasmA anvAha tasya prANAMs trAyate || BrhUp_5,14.4 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_5,14.4 saiShA tripadoktA yA trailokyatraividyaprANalakShaNA gAyatryetasmiMshcaturthe turIye darshate pade parorajasi pratiShThitA /
mUrtAmUrtarasatvAdAdityasya /
rasApAye hi vastu nIrasamapratiShThitaM bhavati /
yathA kAShThAdi dagdhasAraM tadvat /
tathA mUrtAmUrtarasatvAdAdityasya /
rasApAye hi vastu nIrasamapratiShThitaM bhavati /
yathA kAShThAdi dagdhasAraM tadvat /
tathA mUrtAmUrtAtmakaM jagattripadA gAyatryAditye pratiShThitA tadrasatvAtsaha tribhiH pAdaiH /
tadvai turIyaM padaM satye pratiShThitam /
kiM punastatsatyamityucyate-cakShurvai satyam /
kathaM cakShuH satyamityAha-prasiddhametaccakShurhi vai satyam /
kathaM prasiddhatetyAha-tasmAdyadidAnImeva dvau vivadamAnau viruddhaM vadamAnAveyAtAmAgaccheyAtAmahamadarshaM dR^iShTavAnanasmItyanya AhAhamashrauShaM tvayA dR^iShTaM na tathA tadvastviti tayorya evaM brUyAdahamadrAkShamiti tasmA eva shraddadhyAma napunaryo brUyAdahamashrauShamiti /
shroturmR^iShA shravaNamapi saMbhavati na tu cakShuSho mR^iShA darshanam /
tasmAnnAshrauShamityuktavate shraddadhyAma /
tasmAtsatyapratipattihetutvAtsatyaM cakShustasminsatye cakShuShi saha tribhiritaraiH pAdaisturIyaM padaM pratiShThitamityarthaH /
uktaM ca sa AdityaH kasminpratiShThita iti cakShuShIti /
tadvai turIyapadAshrayaM satyaM bale pratiShThitam /
kiM punastadbalamityAha-prANo vai balaM tasminprANe bale pratiShThitaM satyam /
tathA coktaM sUtre tadotaM ca protaM ceti /
yasmAdbale satyaM pratiShThitaM tasmAdAhurbalaM satyAdogIya ojIya ojastaramityarthaH /
loke 'pi yasminhi yadAshritaM bhavati tasmAdAshritAdAshrayasya balavattaratvaM prasiddham /
na hi durbalaM balavataH kvacidAshrayabhUtaM dR^iShTam /
evamuktanyAyena u eShA gAyatryadhyAtmamadhyAtme prANe pratiShThitA /
saiShA gAyatrI prANaH /
ato gAyatryAM jagatpratiShThitam /
yasminprANe sarve devA ekaM bhavanti /
sarvaM vedAH karmANi phalaM ca saivaM gAyatrI prANarUpA satI jagata AtmA /
sA haiShA gayAMstatre trAtavatI /
ke punargayAH prANA vAgAdayo vai gayAH /
shabdakaramAt /
tAMstatre saiShA gAyatrI /
tattatra yadyasmAdgayAMstatre tasmAdgAyatrI nAma /
gAyatrANAdgAyatrIti prathitA /
sa AcArya upanIya mANavakamaShTavarShaM yAmevAmUM gAyatrIM sAvitrIM savitR^idevatAkAmanvAha pacchordharcashaH samastAM ca /
eShaiva sA sAkShAtprANo jagata AtmA mANavakAya samarpitehedAnIM vyAkhyAtA nAnyA sa AcAryo yasmai mANavakAyAnvAhAnuvakti tasya mANavakasya gayAnprANAMsrAyate narakAdipatanAt //4//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 5,14.5

#<tAM haitAm eke sAvitrIm anuShTubham anvAhuH |
vAg anuShTup |
etad vAcam anubrUma iti |
na tathA kuryAt |
gAyatrIm eva sAvitrIm AnubrUyAt |
yadi ha vA apy evaMvid bahv iva pratigR^ihNAti na haiva tad gAyatryA ekaM cana padaM prati || BrhUp_5,14.5 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_5,14.5 tAmetAM sAvitrIM haike shAkhino 'nuShTupchandaskAmanvAhurupanItAya /
tadabhiprAyamAha-vAganuShTup /
vAkca sharIre sarasvatI tAmeva hi vAcaM sarasvatIM mANavakAyAnubrUma ityetadvadantaH /
na tathA kuryAnna tathA vidyAdyatta AhurmR^iShaiva tat /
kiM tarhi gAyatrImeva sAvitrImanubrUyAt /
kasmAt /
yasmAtprANo gAyatrItyuktam /
prANa ukte vAkca sarasvatI cAnye ta prANAH sarvaM mANavakAya samarpitaM bhavati /
kiJNcedaM prAsaN^gikamuktvA gAyatrIvidaM stauti-yadi ha vA apyevaMvidbahviva na hi tasya sarvAtmano bahu nAmAsti kicitsarvAtmakatvAdviduShaH pratigR^ihNAti na haiva tatpratigrahajAtaM gAyatryA ekaJNcanaikamapi padaM prati paryAptam //5//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 5,14.6

#<sa ya imAMs trIMl lokAn pUrNAn pratigR^ihNIyAt so 'syA etat prathamaM padam ApnuyAt |
atha yAvatIyaM trayI vidyA yas tAvat pratigR^ihNIyAt so 'syA etad dvitIyaM padam ApnuyAt |
atha yAvad idaM prANi yas tAvat pratigR^ihNIyAt so 'syA etat tR^itIyaM padam ApnuyAt |
athAsyA etad eva turIyaM darshataM padaM parorajA ya eSha tapati |
naiva kena canApyam |
kuta u etAvat pratigR^ihNIyAt || BrhUp_5,14.6 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_5,14.6 sa ya imAMsrInsa yo gAyatrIvidimAnbhUrAdIMsrIngo 'shvAdidhanapUrNAMllokAnpratigR^ihNIyAtsa pratigraho 'syA gAyatryA etatprathamaM padaM yadvyAkhyAtamApnuyAtprathamapadavij~nAnaphalaM tena bhuktaM syAnna tvadhikadoShotpAdakaH sa pratigrahaH /
atha punaryAvatIyaM trayI vidyA yastAvatpratigR^ihNIyAtso 'syA etattR^itIyaM padamApnuyAt /
tena tR^itIyapadavij~nAnaphalaM bhuktaM syAt /
kalpayitvedamicyate /
pAdatrayasamamapi yadi kashcitpratigR^ihNIyAttatpAdatrayavij~nAnaphalasyaiva kShayakAraNaM na tvanyasya doShasya kartR^itve kShamam /
na caivaM dAtA pratigrahItA vA /
gAyatrIvij~nAnastutaye kalpyate /
dAtA pratigrahItA ca yadyapyevaM saMbhAvyate nAsau pratigraho 'parAdhakShamaH /
kasmAdyato 'bhyadhikamapi puruShArthavij~nAnamavashiShTameva caturthapAdaviShayaM gAyatryAstaddarshayati /
athAsyA etadeva turIyaM darshataM padaM parorajA ya eSha tapati /
yaccaitannaiva kenacana kenacidapi pratigraheNA'pyaM naiva prApyamityarthaH /
yathA pUrvoktAni trINi padAni /
etAnyapi naivA'pyAni kenacitkalpayitvaivamuktaM paramArthataH kuta u etAvatpratigR^ihNoyAttrailokyAdisamam /
tasmAdgAyatryevaMprakAropAsyetyarthaH //6//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 5,14.7

#<tasyA upasthAnam |
gAyatry asy ekapadI dvipadI tripadI catuShpadi |
apad asi |
na hi padyase |
namas te turIyAya darshatAya padAya parorajase |
asAv ado mA prApad iti |
yaM dviShyAd asAv asmai kAmo mA samardhIti vA |
na haivAsmai sa kAmaH samR^idhyate yasmA evam upatiShThate |
aham adaH prApam iti vA || BrhUp_5,14.7 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_5,14.7 tasyA upasthAnaM tasyA gAyatryA upasthAnamupetya sthAnaM namaskaraNamanena mantreNa /
kau'sau mantra ityAha-he gAyatryasi bhavasi trailokyapAdenaikapadI trayIvidyArUpeNa dvitIyena dvipadI /
prANAdinA tR^itIyena tripadyasi /
caturthena turIyeNa catuShpadyasi /
evaM caturbhiH pAdairupAsakaiH padyase j~nAyase 'taH paraM pareNa nirupAdhikena svenA'tmanApadasi /
avidyamAnaM padaM yasyAstava yena padyase sA tvamapadasi yasmAnnahi padyase neti netyAtmatvAt /
ato vyavahAraviShayAya namabhte turIyAya darshatAya padAya poradase /
asau shatruH pApmA tvatprAptivighnakaro 'dastadAtmanaH kAryaM yattvatprAptivighnakartR^itvaM mA prApanmaiva prApnotu /
itishabdo mantraparisamAptyarthaH /
yaM dviShyAdyaM prati dveShaM kuryAtsvayaM vidvAMstaM pratyanenopasthAnamasau shatruramukanAmeti nAma gR^ihNIyAdasmai yaj~nadattAyAbhipretaH kAmo mA samR^iddhi samR^iddhiM mA prApnotviti vopatiShThate /
na haivAsmai devadattAya sa kAmaH samR^idhyate /
kasmai /
yasmA evamupatiShThate /
ahamado devadattAbhipretaM prApamiti vopatiShThate /
asAvado mA prApadityAditrayANAM mantrapadAnAM yathAkAmaM vikalpaH //7//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 5,14.8

#<etad dha vai taj janako vaideho buDilam AshvatarAshvim uvAca -- yan nu ho tad gAyatrIvid abrUthAH |
atha kathaM hastIbhUto vahasIti |
mukhaM hy asyAH samrAN na vidAM cakareti hovAca |
tasyA agnir eva mukham |
yadi ha vA api bahv ivAgnAv abhyAdadhati sarvam eva tat saMdahati |
evaM haivaivaMvid yady api bahv iva pApaM kurute sarvam eva tat saMpsAya shuddhaH pUto 'jaro 'mR^itaH saMbhavati || BrhUp_5,14.8 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_5,14.8 gAyatryA mukhavidhAnAyArthavAda ucyate-etaddha kila vai smaryate /
tattatra gAyatrIvij~nAnaviShaye janako vaideho buDilo nAmato 'shvatarAshvasyApatyamAshvatarAshvistaM kiloktavAn /
yannu iti vitarke ho aho ityetattadyattvaM gAyatrIvidbrUthA gAyatrIvidasmIti yadabrUthAH kimidaM tasya vacaso 'nanurUpam /
atha kathaM yadi gAyatrIvitpratigrahadoSheNa hastobhUto vahasIti /
sa pratyAha rAj~nA smArito mukhaM gAyatryA hi yasmAdasyA he samrANna vidAJNcakAra na vij~nAtavAnasmIti hovAca /
ekAhgavikalatvAdgAyatrIvij~nAnaM mamAphalaM jAtam /
shR^iNu tarhi tasyA gAyatryA agnireva mukham /
yadi ha vA api bahvivendhanamagnAvabhyAdadhati laukikAH sarvameva tatsaMdahatyevendhanamagnirevaM haivaivaMvidgAyatryA agnirmukhamityevaM vettItyevaMvitsyAtsvayaM gAyatryAtmAgnimukhaH san /
yadyapi bahviva pApaM kurute pratigrahAdidoShaM tatsarvaM pApajAtaM saMpsAya bhakShayitvA shuddho 'gnivatpUtashca tasmAtpratigrahadoShAdgAyatryAtmAjaro 'mR^itashca saMbhavati //8//

#<iti shrImadbR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadbhAShye paJNcamAdhyAyasya caturdashaM brAhmaNam //14//>#

START BrhUp 5,15.1

#<hiraNmayena pAtreNa satyasyApihitaM mukham |
tat tvam pUShann apAvR^iNu satyadharmAya dR^iShTaye |
pUShann ekarShe yama sUrya prAjApatya vyUha rashmIn samUha tejaH |
yat te rUpaM kalyANatamam tat te pashyAmi yo 'sAv asau puruShaH so 'ham asmi |
vAyur anilam amR^itam athedaM bhasmAntaM sharIram |
oM krato smara kR^itaM smara krato smara kR^itaM smara |
agne naya supathA rAye 'smAn vishvAni deva vayunAni vidvAn |
yuyodhy asmaj juhurANam eno bhUyiShThAM te namauktiM vidhema || BrhUp_5,15.1 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_5,15.1 yo j~nAnakarmasamuccayakArI so 'ntakAla AdityaM prArthayati /
asti ca prasaN^go gAyatryAsturIyaH pAdo hi saH /
tadupasthAnaM prakR^itamataH sa eva prArthyate /
hiraNyamayena jyotirmayena pAtreNa yathA pAtreNeShTaM vastvapidhIyata evamidaM satyAkhyaM brahma jyotirmayena maNDalenApihitamivAsamAhitacetasAmadR^ishyatvAttaducyate /
satyasyApihitaM mukhaM mukhyaM svarUpaM tadapidhAnaM pAtramapidhAnamiva darshanapratibandhakAraNaM tattvaM he pUShaJNjagataH poShaNatpUShA savitApAvR^iNvapAvR^itaM kuru darshanapratibandhakAraNamapanayetyarthaH /
satyadharmAya satyaM dharmo 'sya mama so 'haM satyadharmA tasmai tvadAtmabhUtAyetyarthaH /
dR^iShTaye darshanAya /
pUShannityAdIni nAmAnyAmantraNArthani savituH /
ekarSha ekashcAsAvR^iShishcaikarShirdarshanAdR^iShiH /
sa hi sarvasya jagata AtmA cakShushca sansarvaM pashyatyeko vA gacchatItyekarShiH"sUrya ekAkI carati"iti mantravarNAt /
yama sarvaM hi jagataH saMyamanaM tvatkR^itam /
sUrya suShThu vIrayate rasAnrashmInprANAndhiyo vA jagata iti /
prAjApatya prajApaterIshvarasyApatyaM hiraNyagarbhasya vA he prAjApatya vyUha vigamaya rashmIn /
samUha saMkShipA'tmanastejo yenAhaM shaknuyAM tvatsvarUpamaJNjasA draShTam /
vidyotana iva rUpANAmata upasaMhara tejaH /
yatte tava rUpaM sarvakalyANAnAmatishayena kalyANaM kalyANatamaM tatte pashyAmi /
pashyAmo vayaM vacanavyatyayena /
yo 'sau bhUrbhuvaHsvarvyAhR^ityavayavaH puruShaH puruShAkR^ititvAtpuruShaH so 'hamasmi bhavAmi /
aharamiti copaniShada uktatvAdAdityacAkShuShayostadevedaM parAmR^ishyate so 'hamasmyamR^itamiti saMbandhaH /
mamAmR^itasya satyasya sharIrapAte sharIrastho yaH prANo vAyuH so 'nilaM bAhyaM vAyumeva pratigacchatu /
tathAnyA devatAH svAM svAM prakR^itiM gacchantu /
athedamapi bhasmAntaM satpR^ithivIM yAtu sharIram /
athedAnImAtmanaH saMkalpabhUtAM manasi vyavasthitAmagnidevatAM prArthayate-oM krato /
oMmiti krato iti ca saMbodhanArthaveva /
oN^kArapratIkatvAdom /
manomayatvAcca kratuH /
he oM he krato smara smartavyamantakAle hi tvatsmaraNavashAdiShTA gatiH prApyate 'taH prArthyate yanmayA kR^itaM tatsmara punaruktirAdarArthA /
kiJNca he 'gne naya prApaya supathA shobhanena mArgeNa rAye dhanAya karmaphalaprAptaya ityarthaH /
na dakShiNena kR^iShNena punarAvR^ittiyuktena kiM tarhi shuklenaiva supathAsmAnvishvAni sarvANi he deva vayunAni praj~nAnAni sarvaprANinAM vidvAn /
kiJNca yuyodhyapanaya viyojayAsmadasmatto juhurANaM kuTilamenaH pApaM pApajAtaM sarvam /
tena pApena viyuktA vayameShyAma uttareNa pathA tvatprasAdAt /
kintu vayaM tubhyaM paricaryAM kartuM na shaknumo bhUyiShThAM bahutamAM te tubhyaM namauktiM namaskAravacanaM vidhema namaskAroktyA paricaremetyarthaH /
anyatkartumashaktAH santa iti //1 // //

iti shrImadbR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadi paJNcamAdhyAyasya paJNcadashaM brAhmaNam //15 //

#<iti bR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadi paJNcamodhyAyaH //5//>#

ADHYAYA 6



#<atha ShaShTho 'dhyAyaH>#
#<atha ShaShThAdhyAyasya prashamaM brAhmaNam>#



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,1.1

#<yo ha vai jyeShThaM ca shreShThaM ca veda jyeShThash ca shreShThash ca svAnAM bhavati |
prANo vai jyeShThash ca shreShThash ca |
jyeShThash ca shreShThash ca svAnAM bhavati |
api ca yeShAM bubhUShati |
ya evaM veda || BrhUp_6,1.1 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,1.1 oM prANo gAyatrItyuktam /
kasmAtpunaH kAraNAtprANabhAvo gAyatryA na punarvAgAdibhAva iti yasmAjjyeShThashca shreShThashca prANo na vAgAdayo jyaiShThyashraiShThyabhAjaH /
kathaM jyeShThatvaM shreShThatvaM ca prANasyoti tannirdidhArayiShayedamArabhyate /
athavokthayajuH sAmakShattrAdibhAvaiH prANasyaivopAsanamabhihitaM satsvapyanyeShu cakShurAdiShu /
tatra hetumAtramihA'nantaryeNa saMbadhyate /
na punaH pUrvasheShatA /
vivakShitaM tu khilatvAdasya kANDasya pUrvatra yadanuktaM vishiShTaphalaM prANaviShayamupAsanaM tadvaktavyamiti /
yaH kashciddha vA ityAvadhAraNarchai /
yo jyeShThashreShThaguNaM vakShyamANaM yo vedAsau bhavatyeva jyeShThashca shreShThashca /
evaM phalena pralobhitaH sanprashnAyAmukhIbhUtastasmai cA'ha-prANo vai jyeShThashca shreShThashceti /
kathaM punaravagamyate prANo jyeShThashca shreShThashceti /
yasmAnniShekakAla eva shukrashoNitasaMmbandhaH prANAdikalApasyAvishiShTaH /
tathApi nAprANaM shukraM virohatIti prathamo vR^ittilAbhaH prANasya cakShurAdibhyaH /
ataH jyeShTho vayasA prANaH /
niShekakAladArabhya garbhaM puShyati prANaH /
prANe hi labdhavR^ittau pashcAccakShurAdInAM vR^ittilAbhaH /
atoyuktaM prANasya jyeShThatvaM cakShurAdiShu /
bhavati tu kashcitkule jyeShTho guNahInatvAttu na shreShThaH /
madhyamaH kaniShTho vA guNADhyatvAdbhavecchreShTho na jyeShThaH /
na tu tathehetyAha-prANa eva tu jyeShThashca shreShThashca /
kathaM punaH shraiShThyamavagamyate prANasya tadiha saMvAdenadarshayiShyAmaH /
sarvathApi tu prANaM jyeShThashreShThaguNaM yo vedopAste sa svAnAM j~nAtInAM jyeShThashca shreShThashca bhavati /
jyeShThashreShThaguNopAsanasAmarthyAtsvavyatirekeNApi ca yeShAM madhye jyeShThashca shreShThashca bhaviShyAmIti bubhUShati bhavitumicchati teShAmapi jyeShThashreShThaprANadarshI jyeShThashca shreShThashca bhavati /
nanu vayenimittaM jyeShThatvaM tadicchAtaH kathaM bhavatItyucyate /
naiSha doShaH /
prANavadvR^ittilAbhasyaiva jyeShThatvasya vivakShitatvAt //1//

BrhUpBh_6,1.2 yo ha vai vasiShThAM veda vasiShThaH svAnAM bhavati /

yeShAM ca j~nAtivyatirekeNa vasiShTho bhavitumicchati teShAM ca vasiShTho bhavati /
ucyatAM tarhi kAsau vasiShTheti /
vAgvai vasiShThA /

START BrhUp 6,1.3

#<yo ha vai pratiShThAM veda pratitiShThati same |

BrhUpBh_6,1.3 yo ha vai pratiShThAM veda pratitiShThatyanayeti pratiShThA tAM pratiShThAM pratiShThAguNavatIM yo veda tasyaitatphalaM pratitiShThati same deshe kAle ca /

START BrhUp 6,1.13

#<atha ha prANa utkramiShyan yathA mahAsuhayaH saindhavaH paDvIshashaN^khUnt saMvR^ihed evaM haivemAn prANAnt saMvavarha |

BrhUpBh_6,1.13 atha ha prANa utkramiShyannutkramamaM kariShyaMstadAnImeva svasthAnAtpracalitA vAgAdayaH /
kimivetyAha-yathA loke mahAMshcAsau suhayashca mahAsuhayaH shobhano hayo lakShaNopeto mahAnparimANataH sindhudeshe bhavaH saindhavo 'bhijanataH paDvIshashaN^kUnpAdabandhanashaN^kUnpaDvIshAshca te shaN^kavashca tAn saMvR^ihedudyacchedyugapadutkhanedashvAroha ArUDhe parIkShaNAya /

START BrhUp 6,1.14

#<sA ha vAg uvAca -- yad vA ahaM vasiShThAsmi tvaM tad vasiShTho 'sIti |
yad vA ahaM pratiShThAsmi tvaM tat pratiShTho 'sIti cakShuH |

BrhUpBh_6,1.14 sA ha vAkprathamaM balidAnAya pravR^ittA ha kilovAcoktavatI yadvA ahaM vasiShThAsmi yanmama vasiShThatvaM tattavaiva tena vasiShThaguNena tvaM tadvasiShTho 'sIti /
yadvA ahaM pratiShThAsmi tvaM tatpratiShTho 'si yA mama pratiShThA sA tvamasIti /
cakShuH /
samAnamanyat /
sampadAyatanaprajAtitvagiNAnkrameNa samarpitavantaH /
yadyevaM sAdhu baliM dattavanto bhavanto brUta tasya u ma evaN^guNavishiShTasya kimannaM kiM vAsa iti /
Ahuritare-yadidaM loke kiJNca kiJNcidannaM nAmApyA shvabhya A kR^imibhya A kITapataN^gebhyaH /
yacca shvAnnaM kR^ibhyannaM kITapataN^gAnnaM ca tena saha sarvameva yatkiJNcitprANibhiradyamAnamannaM tatsarvaM tavAnnaM sarvaM prANasyAnnamiti dR^iShTiratra vidhIyate /
kecitu sarvabhakShaNe doShAbhAvaM vadanti prANAnnavidaH /
tadasat /
shAsrAntareNa pratiShiddhatvAt /
tenAsya vikalpa iti cet /
na /
avidhAyakatvAt /
na ha vA asyAnannaM jagdhaM bhavatIti sarvaM prANasyAnnamityetasya vij~nAnasya vihitasya stutyarthametat /
tenaikavAkyatApatteH /
na tu shAsrAntaravihitasya bAdhane sAmarthyamanyaparatvAdasya /
prANamAtrasya sarvamannamityetaddarshanamihi vidhitsitaM na tu sarvaM bhakShayediti /
yattu sarvabhakShaNe doShAbhAvaj~nAnaM sanmithyaiva pramANAbhAvAt /
viduShaH prANatvAtsarvAnnopapatteH sAmarthyAdadoSha eveti cet /
na /
asheShAnnatvAnupapatteH /
satyaM yadyapi vidvAnprANo yena kAryatakaraNasaMghAtena vishiShTasya vidvattA tena kAryakaraNasaMghAtena kR^imikITadevAdyasheShAnnabhakShaNaM nopapadyate /
tena tatrAsheShAnnabhakShaNe doShAbhAvaj~nApanamanarthakam /
aprAptatvAdasheShAnnabhakShaNadoShasya /
nanu prANaH sanbhakShayatyeva kR^imikITAdyannamapi /
bADham /
kintu na tadviShayaH pratiShedho 'sti /
tasmAddaivaraktaM kiMshukaM tatra doShAbhAvaH /
atastadrUpeNa doShAbhAvaj~nApanamanarthakam /
aprAptatvAdasheShAnnabhakShaNadeShasya /
yena tu kAryakaraNasaMghAtasambandhena pratiShedhaH kriyate tatsambandhena tviha naiva pratiprasavo 'sti /
tasmAttatpratiShedhAtikrame doSha eva syAdanyaviShayatvAnna ha vA ityAdeH /
na ca brAhmaNAdisharIrasya sarvAnnatvadarshanamiha vidhIyate kintu prANamAtrasyaiva /
yathA ca sAmAnyena sarvAnnasya prANasya kiJNcidannajAtaM kasyacijjIvanahetuH /
yathA viShaM viShajasya krimestadevAnyasya prANAnnamapi saddR^iShTameva doShamutpAdayati maraNAdilakShaNam /
tathA sarvAnnasyApi prANasya pratiShiddhAnnabhakShaNe brAhmaNatvAdidehasaMbandhAddoSha eva syAt /
tasmAnmithyAj~nAnamevAbhakShyabhakShaNe doShAbhAvaj~nAnam /
Apo vAsa ityApo bhakShamANA vAsaHsthAnIyAstava /
atra ca prANasyA'po vAsa ityetaddarshanaM vidhIyate /
na tu vAsaHkArye Apo viniyoktuM shakyAH /
tasmAdyathAprApte 'bbhakShaNe darshanamAtraM kartavyam /
na ha vA asya sarvaM prANasyAnnamityevaMvido 'nannamanadanIyaM jagdhaM bhuktaM na bhavati ha /
yadyapyanenAnadanIyaM bhuktamadanIyameva bhuktaM syAnna tu tatkR^itadoSheNa lipyata ityetadvidyAstutirityavocAma /
tathA nAnannaM pratigR^ihItaM yadyapyapratighrAhyaM hastyAdi pratigR^ihItaM syAttadapyannameva pratigrAhyaM syAttatrApyapratigrAhyapratigrahadoSheNa na lipyata iti stutyarthameva ya evametadanasya prANasyAnnaM veda /
phalaM tu prANAtmabhAva eva na tvetatphalAbhiprAyeNa kiM tarhi stutyabhiprAyeNeti /
nanvetadeva phalaM kasmAnna bhavati /
na prANAtmadarshinaH prANAtmabhAva eva phalam /
tatra ca prANAtmabhUtasya sarvAtmano 'nadanIyamapyAdyameva /
tathApratigrAhyamapi pratigrAhyameveti yathAprAptamevopAdAya vidyA stUyate /
ato naiva phalavidhisarUpatA vAkyasya /
yasmAdApo vAsaH prANasya tasmAdvidvAMso brAhmaNAH shrotriyA adhItavedA ashiShyanto bhokShyamANA AcAmantyapo 'shitvA'cAmanti bhuktyA cottarakAlamapo bhakShayanti /
tatra teShAmAcAmatAM ko 'bhiprAya ityAha-etamevAnaM prANamanagnaM kurvanto manyante /
asti caitadyoyasmai vAso dadAti sa tamanagnaM karomIti hi manyate /
prANasya cA'po vAsa iti hyuktam /
yadapaH pibAmi tatprANasya vAso dadAmIti vij~nAnaM kartavyamityevamarthametat /
nanu bhokShyamANo bhuktavAMshca prayato bhaviShyAmItyAcAmati /
tatra ca prANasyAnagnatAkaraNArthatve ca dvikAryatA'camanasya syAt /
na ca kAryadvayamAcamanasyaikasya yuktam /
yadi prAyatyArthaM nAnagnatArthamathAnagnatArthaM na prAyatyArtham /
yasmAdevaM tasmAddvitIyamAcamanAntaraM prANasyAnagnatAkaraNAya bhavatu /
na /
kriyAdvitvopapatteH /
dve hyete kriye bhotryamANasya bhuktavatashca yadAcamanaM smR^itivihitaM tatprAyatyArthaM bhavati /
kriyAmAtrameva na tu tatra prAyatyaM darshanAdyapekShate /
tatra cA'camanAN^gabhUtAsvapsu vAsovij~nAnaM prANasyetikartavyatayA codyate na tu tasminkriyamANa Acamanasya prAyatyarthatA vAdhyate kriyAntaratvAdAcamanasya /
tasmAdbhokShyamANasya bhuktavatashca yadAcamanaM tatrA /
Apo vAsaH prANasyeti darshanamAtraM vidhIyate /
aprAptatvAdanyataH //14//

#<iti bR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadi ShaShThAdhyAyasya prathamaM brAhmaNam //1//>#

START BrhUp 6,2.1

#<shvetaketur vA AruNeyaH pancAlAnAM pariShadam AjagAma |
sa AjagAma jaivaliM pravAhaNaM paricArayamANam |
tam udIkShyAbhyuvAda kumArA3 iti |
sa bho3 iti pratishushrAva |
anushiShTo nv asi pitreti |
om iti hovAca || BrhUp_6,2.1 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.1 shvetaketurha vA AruNeyaH ityasya saMbandhaH /
khilAdhikAro 'yaM tatra yadanuktaM taducyate /
saptamAdhyAyAnte j~nAnakarmasamuccayakAriNAgnermArgayAcanaM kR^itam-agne naya supatheti /
tatrAnekeShAM pathAM sadbhAvo mantreNa sAmarthyAtpradarshitaH /
supatheti visheShaNAt /
panthAnashca kR^itavipAkapratipattimArgAH /
vakShyati ca yatkR^itvetyAdi /
tatra ca kati karmavipAkapratipattimArgA iti sarvasaMsAragatyupasaMhArArtho 'yamArambhaH /
etAvatI hi saMsAragatiH /
etAvAnkarmaNo vipAkaH svAbhAvikasya shAsrIyasya ca savij~nAnasyeti /
yadyapi dvayA ha prAjApatyA ityatra svAbhAvikaH pApmA sUcitaH /
na ca tasyedaM kAryamiti vipAkaH pradarshitaH /
shAsrIyasyaiva tu vipAkaH pradarshitastryannAtmapratipattyantena /
brahmavidyArambhe tadvairAgyasya vivakShitatvAt /
tatrApi kevalena karmaNA pitR^iloko vidyayA vidyAsaMyuktena ca karmaNA devaloka ityuktam /
tatra kena mArgeNa pitR^ilokaM pratipadyate kena vA devalokamiti noktam /
tacceha khilaprakaraNe 'sheShato vaktavyamityata Arabhyate /
ante ca sarvopasaMhAraH shAsrasyeShTaH /
api caitAvadamR^itatvamityuktaM na karmaNo 'mR^itatvAshAstIti ca tatra heturnoktastadarthashcAyamArambhaH /
yasmAdiyaM karmaNo gatirna nitye 'mR^itatve vyApAro 'sti tasmAdetAvadevAmR^itatvasAdhanamiti sAmarthyAddhetutvaM saMpadyate /
api coktamagnihotre na tvevainayostvamutkrAtiM na gatiM na pratiShThAM na tR^iptiM na punarAvR^itiM na lokaM pratyutthAyinaM vettheti /
tatra prativacane te vA ete AhutI hute utkrAmata ityAdinA AhuteH kAryamuktam /
taccaitatkarturAhutilakShaNasya karmaNaH phalam /
na hi kartAramanAshrityA'hutilakShaNasya karmaNaH svAtantryeNotkrAntyAdikAryArambha upapadyate /
kartrarthatvAtkarmaNaH kAryArambhasya /
sAdhanAshrayatvAcca karmaNaH /
tatrAgnihotrastutyarthatvAdagnihotrasyaiva kAryamityuktaM ShaT prakAramapi /
iha tu tadeva kartuH phalamityupadishyate /
ShaTprakAramapi karmaphalavij~nAnasya vivakShitatvAt /
taddvAreNa ca paJNcAgnidarshanamihottaramArgapratipattisAdhanaM vidhitsitam /
evamasheShasaMsAragatyupasaMhAraH /
karmakANDasyaiShA niShThetyetaddvayaM didarshayiShurAkhyAyikAM praNayati /
shvetaketurnAmato 'ruNasyApatyamAruNistasyApatyamAruNeyaH /
hashabda aitihyArthaH /
vai nishcayArthaH /
pitrAnushiShTaH sannAtmano yashaHprathanAya paJNcAlAnAM pariShadamAgatya jitvA rAj~no 'pi pariShadaM jeShyAmIti garveNa sa AjagAma /
jIvalasyApatyaM jevaliM paJNcAlarAjaM pravAhaNanAmAnaMsvabhR^ityaiH paricArayamANamAtmanaH paricaraNaM kArayantamityetat /
sa rAjA pUrvameva tasya vidyAbhimAnagarvaM shrutvA vinetavyo 'yamiti matvA tamudIkShyotprekShyA'gatamAtramevAbhyuvAdAbhyuktavAnkumArA3iti saMbodhya /
bhartsanArthA plutiH /
evamuktaH sa pratishushrAva bho3iti /
bho3ityapratirUpamapi kShattriyaM pratyuktavAnkruddhaH san /
anushiShTo 'nushAsito 'si bhavasi kiM pitretyuvAca rAjA /
pratyAhetara oMmiti bADhamanushiShTo 'smi pR^iccha yadi saMshayaste //1//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,2.2

#<vettha yathemAH prajAH prayatyo vipratipadyantA3 iti |
neti hovAca |
vettho yathemaM lokaM punar ApadyantA3 iti |
neti haivovAca |
vettho yathAsau loka evaM bahubhiH punaH punaH prayadbhir na saMpUryatA3 iti |
neti haivovAca |
vettho yatithyAm AhutyAM hutAyAm ApaH puruShavAco bhUtvA samutthAya vadantI3 iti |
neti haivovAca |
vettho devayAnasya vA pathaH pratipadaM pitR^iyANasya vA |
yat kR^itvA devayAnaM vA panthAnaM pratipadyante pitR^iyANaM vA |
api hi na R^iSher vacaH shrutaM --
dve sR^itI ashR^iNavaM pitÌNAm ahaM devAnAm uta martyAnAm |
tAbhyAm idaM vishvam ejat sameti yad antarA pitaraM mAtaraM ceti |
nAham ata ekaM cana vedeti hovAca || BrhUp_6,2.2 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.2 yadyevaM vettha vijAnAsi kiM yathA yena prakAreNemAH prajAH prasiddhAH prayatyo mriyamANA vipratipadyantA3iti vipratipadyante vicAraNArthA plutiH /
samAnena mArgeNa gacchantInAM mArgadvaividhyaM yatra kAshcitprajA anyena mArgeNa gacchanti kAshcidanyeneti vipratipattiH /
yathA tAH prajA vipratipadyante tatkiM vetthetyarthaH /
neti hovAcetaraH /
tarhi vettha u yathemaM lokaM punarApadyantA3iti punarApadyante yathA punarAgacchantImaM lokam /
neti haivovAca shvetaketuH /
vettho yathAsau lokaH evaM prasiddhena nyAyena punaH punarasakR^itprayadbhirmariyamANairyathAyena prakAreNa na saMpUryatA3iti na saMpUryate 'sau lokastatkiM vettha /
neti haivovAca /
vettho yatithyAM yatsaMkhyAkAyAmAhutyAmAhutau hutAyAmApaH puruShavAcaH puruShasya yA vAksaiva yAsAM vAktAH puruShavAco bhUtvA puruShashabdavAcyA vA bhUtvA /
yadA puruShAkArapariNatAstadA puruShavAco bhavanti /
samutthAya samyagutthAyodbhUtAH satyo vadantI3iti /
neti haivovAca /
puruShAkArapariNatAstadA puruShavAco bhavanti /
samutthAya samyagutthAyodbhUtAH satyo vadantI3iti /
neti haivovAca /
yadyevaM vettha u devayAnasya patho mArgasya pratipadaM pratipadyate yena sA pratipattAM pratipadaM pitR^iyANasya vA pratipadaM pratipacchabdavAcyamarthamAha /
yatkarma kR^itvA yathAvishiShTaM karma kR^itvetyarthaH /
devayAnaM vA panthAnaM mArgaM pratipadyante pitR^iyANaM vA yatkarma kR^itvA pratidyante tatkarma pratipadicyate tAM pratipadaM kiM vettha devalokapitR^ilokapratipattisAdhanaM kiM vetthetyarthaH /
apyatrAsyArthasya prakAshakamR^iShermantrasya vaco vAkyaM naH shrutamasti /
mantro 'pyasyArthasya prakAshako vidyata ityarthaH /
ko 'sau mantra iti /
ucyate-dve sR^itI dvau mArgAvashR^iNavaM shR^itavAnasmi tayorekA pitR^iNAM prApikA pitR^ilokasaMbaddhA tayA sR^ityA pitR^ilokaM prApnotItyarthaH /
ahamashR^iNavamiti vyavahitena saMbandhaH /
devAnAmutApi devAnAM saMbandhinyanyA devAnprApayati sA /
ke punarubhAbhyAM sR^itibhyAM pitÌndevAMshca gacchantIti /
ucyate-utApi martyAnAM manuShyANAM saMbandhinyau manuShyA eva hi sR^itibhyAM gacchantItyarthaH /
tAbhyAM sR^itihyAmidaM vishvaM samastametadgacchatsameti saMgacchate /
te ca dve sR^itI yadantarA yayorantarA yadantarA pitaraM mAtaraM ca mAtApitrorantarA madhya ityarthaH /
kau tau mAtApitarau dyAvApR^ithivyAvaNDakapAle /
iyaM vai mAtAsau piteti hi vyAkhyAtaM brAhmaNena /
aNDakapAlayormadhye saMsAraviShaye evaite sR^itI nA'tyantikAmR^itatvagamanAya /
itara Aha-nAhamato 'smAtprashnasamudAyAdekaJNcanaikamapi prashnaM na veda nAhaM vedeti hovAca shvetaketuH //2//

START BrhUp 6,2.3

#<athainaM vasatyopamantrayAM cakre |
anAdR^itya vasatiM kumAraH pradudrAva |
sa AjagAma pitaram |
taM hovAca -- iti vAva kila no bhavAn purAnushiShTAn avoca iti |
katham sumedha iti |
paJNca mA prashnAn rAjanyabandhur aprAkShIt |
tato naikaM cana vedeti |
katame ta iti |
ima iti ha pratIkAny udAjahAra || BrhUp_6,2.3 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.3 athAnantaramapanIya vidyAbhimAnagarvamenaM prakR^itaM shvetaketuM vasatyA vasatiprayojanenopamantrayAJNcakre /
iha vasantu bhavantaH pAdyamarpyaM cA'nIyatAmityupamantraNaM kR^itavAnrAjA /
anAdR^itya tAM vasatiM kumAraH shvetaketuH pradudrAva pratigatavAnpitaraM prati /
sa cA'jagAma pitaramAgatya covAca taM kathamiti vAva kilaivaM kila no 'smAnbhavAnpurA samAvagatavAnpitaraM prati /
sa cA'jagAma pitaramAgatya covAca taM kathamiti vAva kilaivaM kila no 'smAnbhavAnpurA samAvartanakAle 'nushiShTAnsarvAbhirvidyAbhiravoco 'vocaditi /
sopAlambhaM putrasya vacaH shrutvA'ha pitA /
katha kena prakAreNa tava duHkhamupajAtaM he sumedhaH shobhanA medhA yasyeti sumedhAH /
shR^iNu mama yathA vR^ittaM paJNca paJNcasaMkhyAkAnprashnAnmA mAM rAjanyabandhU rAjanyA bandhavo yasyeti /
paribhavavacanametadrAjanyabandhuriti /
aprAkShItpR^iShTavAMstatastasmAnnaikaJNcanaikamapi na veda na vij~nAtavAnasmi /
katame te rAj~nAH pR^iShTAH prashnA iti pitroktaH putra ime ta iti ha pratIkAni mukhAni prashnAnAmudAjahArodAhR^itavAn //3//
