START BrhUp 6,2.4

#<sa hovAca -- tathA nas tvaM tata jAnIthA yathA yad ahaM kiMca veda sarvam ahaM tat tubham avocam |
prehi tu tatra |
pratItya brahmacaryaM vatsyAva iti |
bhavAn eva gacchatv iti |
sa AjagAma gautamo yatra pravAhaNasya jaivaler Asa |
tasmA Asanam AhR^ityodakam AhArayAM cakAra |
atha hAsmA arghyaM cakAra |
taM hovAca -- varaM bhagavate gautamAya dadma iti || BrhUp_6,2.4 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.4 sa hovAca pitA putraM kruddhamupashamayaMstathA tena prakAreNa no 'smAMstvaM he tAta vatsa jAnIthA gR^ihNIthA yathA yadahaM kiJNca vij~nAnajAtaM veda sarvaM tatubhyamavocamityeva jAnIthAH /
ko 'nyo mama priyataro 'sti tvatto yadarthaMrakShiShye /
ahamapyetanna jAnAmi yadrAj~nA pR^iShTam /
tasmAtprehyAgaccha tatra pratItya gatvA rAj~ni brahmacaryaM vatsyAvo vidyArthamiti /
sa Aha bhavAneva gacchatviti nAhaM tasya mukhaM nirIkShitumutsahe /
sa AjagAma gautamo gotrato gautama AruNiryatra pravAhaNasya jaivalerAsA'sanamAsthAyikA ShaShThIdvayaM prathamamAsthAne /
tasmai gautamAyA'gatAyA'sanamanurUpamAhR^ityodakaM bhR^ityairAhArayAJNcakAra /
atha hAsmA ardhyaM purodhasA kR^itavAnmantravanmadhuparkaM ca /
kR^itvA caivaM pUjAM taM hovAca varaM bhagavate gautamAya tubhyaM dadbha iti goshvAdilakShaNam //4//

START BrhUp 6,2.5

#<sa hovAca -- pratij~nato ma eSha varaH |
yAM tu kumArasyAnte vAcam abhAShathAs tAM me brUhIti || BrhUp_6,2.5 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.5 sa hovAca gautamaH pratij~nAto me mamaiSha varastvayAsyAM pratij~nAyAM dR^iDhI kurvAtmAnaM yAM tu vAcaM kumArasya mama putrasyAnte samIpe vAcamabhAShathAH prashnarUpAM tAmeva me brUhi sa eva no vara iti //5//

START BrhUp 6,2.6

#<sa hovAca -- daiveShu vai gautama tad vareShu |
mAnuShANAM brUhIti || BrhUp_6,2.6 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.6 sa hovAca rAjA daiveShu vareShu tadvai gautama yastvaM prArthayase mAnuShANAmanyatamaM prArthaya varam //6//

START BrhUp 6,2.7

#<sa hovAca -- vij~nAyate hAstihiraNyasyApAttaM goashvAnAM dAsInAM pravArANAM paridhAnasya |
mA no bhavAn bahor anantasyAparyantasyAbhyavadAnyo bhUd iti |
sa vai gautama tIrthenecchasA iti |
upaimy ahaM bhavantam iti |
vAcA ha smaiva pUrva upayanti |
sa hopAyanakIrtyovAsa || BrhUp_6,2.7 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.7 sa hovAca gautamo bhavatApi vij~nAyate ha mamAsti saH /
na tena prArthitena kR^ityaM mama yaM tvaM ditsasi mAnuShaM varam /
yasmAnmamApyasti hiraNyasya prabhUtasyApAttaM prAptaM go'ashvAnAnAmApAttamastIti sarvatrAnuShaN^go dAsInAM pravArANAM parivArANAM paridhAnasya ca /
na ca yanmama vidyamAnaM tattvattaH prArthanIyaM tvayA vA deyam /
pratij~nAtashca varastvayA tvameva jAnIShe yadatra yuktaM pratij~nA rakShaNIyA taveti /
mama punarayamabhiprAyo mA bhUnno 'smAnabhyasmAneva kevalAnprati bhavAnsarvatra vadAnyo bhUtvAvadAnyo mA bhUtkadaryo mA bhUdityarthaH /
bahoH prabhUtasyAnantasyAnantaphalasyetyetat /
aparyantasyAparisamAptikasya putrapautrAdigAmikasyetyetat /
IdR^ishasya vittasya mAM pratyeva kevalamAdAtA mA bhUdbhavAn /
na cAnyatrAdeyamasti bhavataH /
evamukta Aha-sa tvaM vai he gautama tIrthena nyAyena shAsravihitena vidyAM matta icchAsA icchAnvAptumityukto gautama Aha-upaimyupagacchAmi shiShyatvenAhaM bhavantamiti /
vAcA ha smaiva kila pUrva brAhmaNAH kShattriyAnvidyArthinaH santo vaishyAnvA kShattriyA vA vaishyAnApadyupayanti shiShyavR^ittyA hyupacchanti nopAyanashushrUShAdibiH /
ataH /
sa gautamo hopAyanakortyopagamanakIrtanamAtreNaivovAsoShitavAnnopAyanaM cakAra //7//

START BrhUp 6,2.8

#<sa hovAca -- tathA nas tvam gautama mAparAdhAs tava ca pitAmahAH |
yatheyaM vidyetaH pUrvaM na kasmiMsh cana brAhmana uvAsa |
tAM tv ahaM tubhyaM vakShyAmi |
ko hi tvaivaM bruvantam arhati pratyAkhyAtum iti || BrhUp_6,2.8 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.8 evaM gautamenA'padantara ukte sa hovAca rAjA pIDitaM matvA kShAmayaMstathA no 'smAnprati mAparAdhA aparAdhaM mA kArShIrasmadIyo 'parAdho na grahItavya ityarthaH /
tava ca pitAmahA asmatpitAmaheShu yatAparAdhaM na jagR^ihustathA pitAmahAnAM vR^ittamasmAsvapi bhavatA rakShaNIyamityarthaH /
yatheyaM vidyA tvayA prArthitetastvatsaMpradAnAtpUrvaM prAÇna kasminnapi brAhmaNa uvAsoShitavatItathA tvamapi jAnIShe sarvadA kShattriyaparamparayeyaM vidyA'gatA sA sthitirmayApi rakShaNIyA yadi shakyata ityuktaM daiveShu gautama tadvareShu mAnuShANAM brUhIti na punastavAdeyo vara itItaH para na shakyate rakShitum /
tAmapi vidyAmahaM tubhyaM vakShyAmi ko hyanyo 'pi hi yasmAdevaM bruvantaM tvAmarhati pratyAkhyAtuM na vakShyAmIti /
ahaM punaH kathaM na vakShye tubhyamiti //8//

START BrhUp 6,2.9

#<asau vai loko 'gnir gautama |
tasyAditya eva samit |
rashmayo dhUmaH |
ahar arciH |
disho 'N^gArAH |
avAntaradisho viShphuliN^gAH |
tasminn etasminn agnau devAH shraddhAM juhvati |
tasyA Ahutyai somo rAjA saMbhavati || BrhUp_6,2.9 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.9 asau vai loko 'gnirgotametyAdicaturthaH prashnaH prAthamyena nirNIyate /
kramabhaN^gastvetannirNayAyattatvAditaraprasnanirNayasya /
asau dyaurloko 'gnirhe gautama dyuloke 'gnidR^iShTiranagnau vidhIyate yathA yoShitpuruShayostasya dyulokAgnerAditya eva samitsamindhanAt /
Adityena hi samidhyate 'sau lokaH /
rashmayo dhUmaH samidha uththAnasAmAnyAt /
AdityAddhi rashmayo nirgatAH /
samidhashca dhUmo loka uttiShThati /
ahararciH prakAshasAmAnyAt /
disho 'N^gArA upashamasAmAnyAt /
avAntaradiSho visphuliN^gA visphuliN^gavadvikShepAt /
tasminnetasminnevaN^guNavishiShTe dyulokAgnau devA indrAdayaH shraddhAM juhvatyAhutidravyasthAnIyAM prakShipanti /
tasyA AhutyA AhuteH somo rAjA pitÌNAM brAhmaNAnAM ca saMbhavati /
tatra ke devAH kathaM juhvati kiMvA shraddhAkhyaM havirityata uktamasmAbhiH saMbandhe /
na tvevainayostvamutkrAntimityAdipadArthaShaTkanirNayArthamagnihotra uktam /
te vA ete agnihotrAhutI hute satyAvutkrAmataH /
te antarikShamAvishataH /
te antarikShamAhavanIyaM kurvAte vAyuM samidhaM marIcIreva shukrAmAhutim /
te antarikShantarpayataH /
te tata utkrAmataH /
te divamAvishataH /
te divamAhavanIyaM kurvAte AdityaM samidhamityevamAdyuktam /
tatrAgnihotrAhutI sasAdhane evotkrAmataH /
yatheha yaiH sAdhanairvishiShTe ye j~nAyete AhavanIyAgnisamiddhUmAN^gAravisphuliN^gAhutidravyaiste tathaivotkrAmato 'smAllokAdamuM lokam /
tatrAgniragnitvena samitsamittvena dhUmo dhUmatvenAN^gArA aN^gAratvena visphuliN^gatvenA'hutidravyamapi paya AdyAhutidravyatvenaiva sargAdAvavyAkR^itAvasthAyAmapi pareNasUkShmeNA'tmanA vyavatiShThate /
tadvidyamAnameva sasAdhanamagnihotralakShaNaM karmApUrveNA'tmanA vyavasthitaM sattatpunarvyAkaraNakAle tathaivAntarikShAdInAmAhavanIyAdyagnyAdibhAvaM kurvadvipariNamate /
tathaivedAnImapyagnihotrAkhyaM karma /
evamagnihotrAhutyapUrvavipariNAmAtmakaM jagatsarvamityAhutyoreva stutyarthatvenotkrAntyAdyA lokaM pratyutthAyinAntAH ShaT padArthAH karmaprakaraNe 'dhastAnnirNItAH /
iha tu kartuH karmavivakShAyAM dyulokAgnyAdyArabhya paJNcAgnidarshanamuttaramArgapratipattisAdhanaM vishiShTakarmaphalopabhogAya vidhitsitamiti dyulokAgnyAdidarshanaM prastUyate /
tatra ya AdhyAtmikAH prANA ihAgnihotrasya hotArasta evA'dhidaivikatvena pariNatAH santa indrAdayo bhavanti ta eva tatra hotAro dyulokAgnau /
te cehAgnihotrasya phalabhogAyAgnihotraM hutavantaH /
ta eva phalapariNAmakAle 'pi tatphalabhoktR^itvAttatra tatra hotR^itvaM pratipadyante tathA tathA vipariNamamAnA devashabdavAcyAH santaH /
atra ca yatpayodravyamagnihotrakarmAshrayabhUtamihA'havanIye prakShiptamagninA bhakShitamadR^iShTena sUkShmema rUpeNa vipariNataM saha kartrA yajamAnenAmuM lokaM dhUmAdikrameNAntarikShAddyulokamAvishati /
tAH sUkShmA Apa AhutikAryabhUtA agnihotrasamavAyinyaH kartR^isahitAH shraddhAshabdavAcyAH somaloke kartuH sharIrAntarArambhAya dyulokaM pravishantyo hUyante ityucyante /
tAstatra dyulokaM pravishya somamaNDale kartuH sharIramArabhante /
tadetaducyate devAH shraddhAM juhvati tasyA Ahutyai somo rAjA saMbhavatIti /
"shraddhA vA ApaH"iti shruteH /
vettha yatithyAmAhutyAM hutAyAmApaH puruShavAco bhUtvA samutthAya vadantoti prashnastasya ca nirNayaviShaye 'sau vai loko 'gniriti prastutam /
tasmAdApaH karmasamAvAyinyaH kartuH sharIrArambhikAH shraddhAshabdavAcyA iti nishcIyate /
bhUyastvAdApaH puruShavAca iti vyapadesho na tvitarANi bhUtAni na santIti /
karmaprayuktashca sharIrArambhaH /
karma cApsamavAyi /
tatashcApAM prAdhAnyaM sharIrakartR^itve /
tena cA'paH puruShavAca iti vyapadeshaH /
karmakR^ito hi janmArambhaH sarvatra /
tatra yadyapyagnihotrAhutistutidvAreNotkrAntyAdayaH prastutAH ShaTpadArthA agnihotre tathApi vaidikAni sarvANyeva karmANyagnihotraprabhR^itIni lakShyante /
dArAgnisaMbaddhaM hi pAN^ktaM karma prastutyoktam-karmaNA pitR^iloka iti /
vakShyati ca-atha ye yaj~nena dAnena tapasA lokAJNjayantIti //9//

START BrhUp 6,2.10

#<parjanyo vA agnir gautama |
tasya saMvatsara eva samit |
abhrANi dhUmaH |
vidyud arciH |
ashanir aN^gArAH |
hrAdunayo viShphuliN^gAH |
tasminn etasminn agnau devAH somaM rAjAnaM juhvati |
tasyA Ahutyai vR^iShTiH saMbhavati || BrhUp_6,2.10 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.10 parjanyo vA agnirgautama dvitIya AhutyAdhAra AhutyorAvR^ittikrameNa /
parjanyo nAma vR^iShTyupakaraNAbhimAnI devatAtmA /
tasya saMvatsara eva samit /
saMvatsareNa hi sharadAdibhirgrIShmAntaiH svAvayavairvaparivartamAnena parjanyo 'gnirdIpyate /
abhrANi dhUmaH /
dhUmaprabhavatvAddhUmavadupalakShyatvAdvA /
vidyudarciH /
prakAshasAmAnyAt /
ashaniraN^gArAH /
upashAntakAThinyasAmAnyAbhyAm /
hrAdunayo hlAdunayaH stanayitnushabdA visphuliN^gAH /
vikShepAnekatvasAmAnyAt /
tasminnetasminnityAhutyadhikaraNanirdeshaH /
devA iti ta eva hotAraH somaM rAjAnaM juhvati /
yo 'sau dyulokAgnau shraddhAyAM hutAyAmabhinirvR^ittaH somaH sa dvitIye parjanyAgnau hUyate /
tasyAshca somAhutervR^iShTiH saMbhavati //10//

START BrhUp 6,2.11

#<ayaM vai loko 'gnir gautama |
tasya pR^ithivy eva samit |
agnir dhUmaH |
rAtrir arciH |
candramA aN^gArAH |
nakShatrANi viShphuliN^gAH |
tasminn etasminn agnau devA vR^iShTiM juhvati |
tasyA AhutyA annaM saMbhavati || BrhUp_6,2.11 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.11 ayaM vai loko 'gnirgotama /
ayaM loka iti prANijanmopabhogAshrayaH kriyAkArakaphalavishiShTaH sa tR^itIyo 'gniH /
tasyAgneH pR^ithivyeva samit /
pR^ithivyA hyayaM loko 'nekaprANyupabhogasaMpannayA samidhyate /
agnirdhUmaH /
pR^ithivyAshrayotthAnasAmAnyAt /
pArthivaM hIndhanadravyamAshrityAgniruttiShThati /
yathA samidAshrayena dhUmaH /
rAtrirarciH /
samitsaMbandhaprabhavasAmAnyAt /
agneH samitsaMbandhena hyarciH saMbhavati /
tathA pR^ithivIsamitsaMbandhena sharvarI /
pR^ithivIchAyAM hi shArvaraM taM AcakShate /
candramA aN^gArAH /
tatprabhavatvasAmAnyAt /
arciSho hyaN^gArAH prabhavanti tathA rAtrau candramAH /
upashAntatvasAmAnyAdvA /
nakShatrANi visphuliN^gAH /
bisphuliN^gavadvikShepasAmAnyAt /
tasminnetasminnityAdi pUrvavat /
vR^iShTiM juhvati tasyA AhuterannaM saMbhavati /
vR^iShTiprabhavatvasya prasiddhatvAdvrIhiyavAderannasya //11//

START BrhUp 6,2.12

#<puruSho vA agnir gautama |
tasya vyAttam eva samit |
prANo dhUmaH |
vAg arciH |
cakShur aN^gArAH |
shrotraM viShphuliN^gAH |
tasminn etasminn agnau devA annaM juhvati |
tasyA Ahutyai retaH saMbhavati || BrhUp_6,2.12 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.12 puruSho vA agnirgautama prasiddhaH shiraHpANyAdimAnpuruShashcaturtho 'gnistasya vyAttaM vivR^itaM mukhaM samit /
vivR^itena hi mukhena dIpyate puruSho vacanasvAdhyAyAdau /
yathA samidhAgniH prANo dhUmastadutthAnasAmAnyAt /
mukhAddhi prANa uttiShThati /
vAkyashabdo 'rcirvyaJNjakatvasAmAnyAt /
arcishca vyaJNjakam /
tathA vAkshabdo 'bhidheyavyaJNjakaH /
cakShuraN^gArA upashamasAmAnyAtprakAshAshrayatvAdvA /
shrotraM visphuliN^gA vikShepasAmAnyAt /
tasminnannaM juhvati /
nanu naiva devA annamiha juhvato dR^ishyante /
naiSha doShaH /
prANAnAM devatvopapatteH /
adhidaivamindrAdayo devAsta evAdhyAtmaM prANAste cAnnasya puruShe prakSheptAraH /
tasyA Ahute retaH saMbhavati /
annapariNAmo hi retaH //12//

START BrhUp 6,2.13

#<yoShA vA agnir gautama |
tasyA upastha eva samit |
lomAni dhUmaH |
yonir arciH |
yad antaH karoti te 'N^gArAH |
abhinandA viShphuliN^gAH |
tasminn etasminn agnau devA reto juhvati |
tasyA Ahutyai puruShaH saMbhavati |
sa jIvati yAvaj jIvati |
atha yadA mriyate || BrhUp_6,2.13 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.13 yoShA vA agnirgautama /
yoSheti srI paJNcamo homAdhikaraNo 'gnistasyA upastha eva samit /
tena hi sA samidhyate /
lomAni dhUmastadutthAnasAmAnyAt /
yonirarcirvarNasAmAnyAt /
yadantaH karoti te 'N^gArA antaH karaNaM maithunavyApAraste 'N^gArA vIryopashamahetutvasAmAnyAt /
vIryAdyupashamakAraNaM maithunam /
tathAN^gArabhAvo 'gnerupashamakAraNam /
abhinandAH sukhalavAH kShudratvasAmAnyAdvisphuliN^gAH /
tasminreto juhvati /
tasyA AhuteH puruShaH saMbhavati /
evaM dyuparjanyAyaMlokapuruShayoShAgniShu kramema hUyamAnAH shraddhAsomavR^iShTyannaretobhAvena sthUlatAratamyakramamApadyamAnAH shraddhAshabdavAcyA ApaH puruShashabdamArabhante /
yaH prashnashcaturtho vettha yatithyAmAhutyAM hutAyAmApaH puraShavAco bhUtvA samutthAya vadantI3iti sa eSha nirNItaH /
paJNcamyAmAhutau yoShAgnau hutAyAM retobhUtA ApaH puruShavAco bhavantIti /
sa puruSha evaM krameNa jAto jIvati /
kiyantaM kAlamiti /
ucyate-yAvajjIvati yAvadasmiJNcharIre sthitinimittaM karma vidyate tAvadityarthaH /
atha tatkShaye yadA yasmikAle mriyate //13//

START BrhUp 6,2.14

#<athainam agnaye haranti |
tasyAgnir evAgnir bhavati |
samit samit |
dhUmo dhUmaH |

aN^gArA aN^gArAH |

__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.14 atha tadainaM mR^itamagnaye 'gnyarthamevAntyAhutyai haranti shratvijastasyA'hutibhUtasya prasiddho 'gnireva homAdhikaraNaM na parikalpyo 'gniH /
prasiddhaiva samitsamiddhUmo dhUmo 'rcirarciraN^gArA aN^gArA visphuliN^gA visphuliN^gA yathAprasiddhameva sarvamityarthaH /
tasminpuruShamantyAhutiM juhvati tasyA AhutyA AhuteH puruSho bhAsvaravarNo 'tishayadIptimAnniShekAdibhirantyAhutyantaiH karmabhiH saMskR^itatvAtsaMbhavati niShpadyate //14//

START BrhUp 6,2.15

#<te ya evam etad vidur ye cAmI araNye shraddhAM satyam upAsate te 'rcir abhisaMbhavanti |
arciSho 'haH |
ahna ApUryamANapakSham |
ApUryamANapakShAd yAn ShaN mAsAn udaÇÇ Aditya eti |
mAsebhyo devalokam |
devalokAd Adityam |
AdityAd vaidyutam |
tAn vaidyutAn puruSho mAnasa etya brahmalokAn gamayati |
te teShu brahmalokeShu parAH parAvato vasanti |
teShAM na punar AvR^ittiH || BrhUp_6,2.15 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.15 idAnIM prathamaprashnanirAkaraNArthamAha-te /
ke /
ya evaM yathoktaM paJNcAgnidarshanametadviduH /
evaM shabdAdagnisamiddhUmArciraN^gAravisphuliN^gashraddhAdivishiShTAH paJNcAgnayo nirdiShTAstAnevametAnpaJNcAgnInvidurityarthaH /
nanvagnihotrAhutidarshanaviShayamevaitaddarshanam /
tatra hyuktamutkrAntyAdipadArthaShaTkanirNaye divamevA'havanIyaM kurvAte ityAdi /
ihApyamuShya lokasyAgnitvamAdityasya ca samittvamityAdi bahu sAmyam /
tasmAttaccheShamevaitaddarshanamiti /
na, yatithyAmiti prasnaprativacanaparigrahAt /
yatithyAmityasya prashnasya prativacanasya yAvadeva parigrahastAvadevaivaMshabdena parAmraShTuM yuktam /
anyathA prashnAnarthakyAnnirj~nAtatvAcca saMkhyAyA agnaya eva vaktavyAH /
atha nirj~nAtamapyanUdyate /
yathAprAptasyaivAnuvadanaM yuktaM na tvasau loko 'gniriti /
athopalakShaNArthaH tathApyAdyenAntyena copalakShaNaM yuktam /
shrutyantarAcca /
samAne hi prakaraNe chAndogyashrutau paJNcAgnInvedeti paJNcasaMkhyAyA evopAdAnAdanagnihotrasheShametat /
paJNcAgnidarshanam /
yattvagnisamidAdisAmAnyaM tadagnihotrastutyarthamityavocAma /
tasmAnnotkrAntyAdipadArthaShaTkaparij~nAnAdarcirAdipratipattiH /
evamiti prakR^itopAdAnenArcirAdipratipattividhAnAt /
ke punaste ya evaM vidurgR^ihasthA eva /
nanu teShAM yaj~nAdisAdhanena dhUmAdipratipattirvidhitsita /
na, anevaMvidAmapi gR^ihasthAnAM yaj~nAdisAdhanopapatteH /
bhikShuvAnaprasthayoshcAraNyasaMbandhena grahaNAt /
gR^ihasthakarmasaMbaddhatvAccapaJNcAgnidarshanasya /
ato nApi brahmacAriNa evaM viduriti gR^ihyante /
teShAM tUttare pathi praveshaH smR^itiprAmANyAt-"aShTAshItisahasrANAmR^iShINAmUrdhvaretasAm /
uttareNAryamNaH panthAste 'mR^itatvaM hi bhejire"iti /
tasmAdye gR^ihasthA evamagnijo 'hamagnyapatyamityevaM krameNAgnibhyo jAto 'gnirUpa ityevaM ye viduste ca ye cAmI araNye vAnaprasthAH parivrAjakAshcAraNyaniShThAH shraddhAM shraddhAyuktAH snataH satyaM brahma hiraNyagarbhAtmAnamupAsate na punaH shraddhAM copAsate te sarve 'rcirabhisaMbhavanti /
yAvadgR^ihasthAH paJNcAgnividyAM satyaM vA brahma na vidustAvacchraddhAdyAhutikrameNa paJNcamyAmAhutau hutAyAM tato yoShAgnerjAtAH punarlokaM pratyutthAyino 'gnihotrAdikarmAnuShThAtAro bhavanti /
tena karmaNA dhUmAdikrameNa punaH pitR^ilokaM punaH parjanyAdikrameNemamAvartante /
punaryoShAgnerjAtAH punaH karma kR^itvetyevameva ghaTIyantravadgatyAgatibhyAM punaH punarAvartante /
yadA tvevaM vidustato ghaTIyantrabhramaNAdvinirmuktAH santo 'rcirabhisaMbhavanti /
arciriti nAgnijvAlAmAtraM kiM tarhyarcirabhimAninyarciH shabdavAcyA devatottaramArgalakShaNA vyavasthitaiva tAmabhisaMbhavanti /
na hi parivrAjakAnAmagnyarciShaiva sAkShAtsaMbandho 'sti /
tena devataiva parigR^ihyate 'rciHshabdavAcyA /
ato 'hardevatAm /
maraNakAlaniyamAnupapatterahaHshabdo 'pi devataiva /
AyuShaH kShaye hi maraNam /
na hyevaMvidAhanyeva martavyamityaharmaraNakAlo niyantuM shakyate /
na ca rAtrau pretAH santo 'haH pratIkShante /
"sa yAvatkShipyenmanastAvadAdityaM gacchati"iti shrutyantarAt /
ahna ApUryamANapakShamahardevatayAtivAhitA ApUryamANapakShadevatAM pratipadyante shuklapakShadevatAmityetat /
ApUryamANapakShAdyAnShaNmAsAnudaÇÇuttarAM dishamAdityaH savitaiti tAnmAsAnpratipadyante shuklapakShadevatayAtivAhitAHsantaH /
mAsAniti bahuvacanAtsaMghacAriNyaH ShaDuttarAyaNadevatAstebhyo mAsebhyaH ShaNmAsadevatAbhirativAhitA devalokAbhimAninIM devatAM pratipadyante /
devalokAdAdityamAdityAdvaidyutaM vidyudabhimAninIM devatAM pratipadyante /
vidyuddevatAM prAptAnbrahmalokavAsI puruSho brahmaNA manasA sR^iShTo mAnasaH kashcidetyA'gatya brahmalokAngamayati /
brahmalokAnityadharottarabhUmibhedena bhinnA iti gamyante /
bahuvacanaprayogAt /
upAsanatAratamyopapatteshca /
te tena puruSheNa gamitAH santasteShu brahmalokeShu parAH prakR^iShTAH santaH svayaM parAvataH prakR^iShTAH samAH saMvatsarAnanekAnvasanti /
brahmaNo 'nekAnkalpAnvasantItyarthaH /
teShAM brahmalokaM gatAnAM nAsti punarAvR^ittirasminsaMsAre na punarAgamanamiheti shAkhAntarapAThAt /
ihetyAkR^itimAtragrahaNamiti cecchvobhUte paurNamAsImiti yadvat /
na, ihetivisheShaNAnarthakyAt /
yadi hi nA'vartanta evehagrahaNamanarthakameva syAt /
shvobhUte paurNamAsImityatra paurNamAsyAH shvobhUtatvamanuktaMna j~nAyata iti yukta visheShayitum /
na hi tatra shvaAkR^itiH shabdArtho vidyata iti shvashabdo virarthaka eva prayujyate /
yatra tu visheShaNashabde prayukte 'nviShyamANe visheShaNaphalaM cenna gamyate tatra yukto nirarthakatvenotsraShTuM visheShaNashabdo na tu satyAM visheShaNaphalAvagatau /
tasmAdasmAtkalpAdUrdhvamAvR^ittirgamyate //15//

START BrhUp 6,2.16

#<atha ye yaj~nena dAnena tapasA lokA¤ jayanti te dhUmam abhisaMbhavanti |
dhUmAd rAtrim |
rAtrer apakShIyamANapakSham |
apakShIyamANapakShAd yAn ShaN mAsAn dakShiNAditya eti |
mAsebhyaH pitR^ilokam |
pitR^ilokAc candram |
te candraM prApyAnnaM bhavanti |
tAMs tatra devA yathA somaM rAjAnam ApyAyasvApakShIyasvety evam enAMs tatra bhakShayanti |
teShAM yadA tat paryavaity athemam evAkAsham abhiniShpadyante |
AkAshAd vAyum |
vAyor vR^iShTim |
vR^iShTeH pR^ithivIm |
te pR^ithivIM prApyAnnaM bhavanti |
te punaH puruShAgnau hUyante tato yoShAgnau jAyante |
lokAn pratyuthAyinas ta evam evAnuparivartante |
atha ya etau panthAnau na vidus te kITAH pataN^gA yad idaM dandashUkam || BrhUp_6,2.16 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,2.16 atha punarye naivaM vidurutkrAntyAdyagnihotrasaMbandhapadArthaShaTkasyaiva veditAraH kevalakarmiNo yaj~nenAgnihotrAdinA dAnena bahirvedi bhikShamANeShu dravyasaMvibhAgalakShaNena tapasA bahirvedyeva dIkShAdivyatiriktena kR^icchracAndrAyaNAdinA lokAJNjayanti /
lokAniti bahuvacanAttatrApi phalatAramyamabhipretam /
te dhUmamabhisaMbhavanti /
uttaramArga ivehApi devatA eva dhUmAdishabdavAcyAH /
dhUmadevatAM pratipadyanta ityarthaH /
AtivAhikatvaM ca devatAnAM tadvadeva /
dhUmAdrAtriM rAtridevatAM tato 'pakShIyamANapakShadevatAM tato yAnShaNmAsAndakShiNAM dishamAditya eti tAnmAsadevatAvisheShAnpratipadyante /
mAsebhyaH pitR^ilokaM pitR^ilokAccandram /
te candraM prApyAnnaM bhavanti tAMstatrAnnabhUtAnyathA somaM rAjAnamiha yaj~na R^itvija ApyAyasvApakShIyasveti bhakShayantyevamenAMshcandraM prAptAnkarmiNo bhR^ityAniva svAmino bhakShayantyupabhuJNjate devAH ApyAyasvApakShIyasveti na mantraH kiM tarhyApyAyyA'pyAyya camasasthaM bhakShaNenApakShayaM ca kR^itvA punaH punarbhakShayantItyarthaH /
evaM devA api somaloke labdhasharIrAnkarmiNa upakaraNabhUtAnpunaH punarvishrAmayantaH karmAnurUpaM phalaM prayacchantaH /
taddhi teShAmApyAyanaM somasyA'pyAyanamivopabhuJNjata upakaraNabhUtAndevAH teShAM karmiNAM yadA yasminkAle tadyaj~nadAnAdilakShaNaM somalokaprApakaM karma paryavaiti parigacchati parikShIyata ityarthaH /
atha tademameva prasiddhamAkAshamabhiniShpadyante /
yAstAH shraddhAshabdavAcyA dyulokAgnau hutA ApaH somAkArapariNatA yAbhiH somaloke karmiNAmupabhogAya sharIramArabdhamammayaM tAH karmakShayAddhimapiNDa ivA'tapasaMparkAtpravilIyante /
pravilInAH sUkShmA AkAshabhUtA iva bhavanti tadidamucyata imamevA'kAshamabhiniShpadyanta iti /
te punarapi karmiNastaccharIrAH santaH purovAtAdinA itAshcAmutashca nIyante 'ntarikShagAstadAha-AkAshAdvAyumiti /
vAyorvR^iShTiM pratipadyante /
taduktam-parjanyAgnau somaM rAjAnaM juhvatIti /
tato vR^iShTibhUtA imAM pR^ithivIM patanti /
te pR^ithivIM prApya vrIhiyavAdyannaM bhavanti /
taduktamasmiMlloke 'gnau vR^iShTiM juhvati tasyA AhutyA annaM saMbhavatIti /
te punaH puruShAgnau hUyante 'nnabhUtA retaHsici /
tato retobhUtA yoShAgnau hUyante tato jAyante lokaM pratyutthAyinaste lokaM pratyuttiShThanto 'gnihotrAdikarmAnutiShThanti /
tato dhUmAdinA punaH punaH somalokaM punarimaM lokamiti /
ta evaM karmiNo 'nuparivartante ghaTIyantravaccakrIbhUtA baMbhramantItyarthaH /
uttaramArgAya sadyomuktaye vA yAvadbrahma na viduH /
iti nu kAmayamAnaH saMsaratItyuktam /
atha punarya uttaraM dakShiNaM caitau panthAnau na viduruttarasya dakShiNasya vA pathaH pratipattaye j~nAnaM karma vA nAnutiShThantItyarthaH /
te kiM bhavantIti /
ucyate-te kITAH pataN^gA yadidaM yaccedaM dandashUkaM daMshamashakamityetadbhavanti /
evaM hIyaM saMsAragatiH kaShTAsyAM nimagnasya punaruddhAra eva durlabhaH /
tathA ca shrutyantaram-"tAnImAni kShudrANyasakR^idAvartIni bhUtAni bhavanti jAyasva mriyasva"iti /
tasmAtsarvotsAhena yathAshakti svAbhAvikakarmaj~nAnahAnena dakShiNottaramArgapratipattisAdhanaM shAsrIyaM karma j~nAnaM vAnutiShThediti vAkyArthaH /
tathA coktam"ato vai khalu durniShprapataraM tasmAjjugupseta"iti shrutyantarAnmokShAya prayatetetyarthaH /
atrApyuttaramArgapratipattisAdhana eva mahAnyatnaH kartavya iti gamyate /
evamevAnuparivartanta ityuktatvAt /
evaM prashnAH sarve nirNItAH /
esau vai loka ityArabhya puruShaH saMbhavatIticaturthaH prashno yatithyAmAhutyAmityAdiH prathamyena /
paJNcamastu dvitIyatvena devayAnasya vA pathaH pratipadaM  pitR^iyANasya veti dakShiNottaramArgapratipattisAdhanakathanena /
tenaiva ca prathamo 'pyagnerAbhya kecidarciH pratipadyante keciddhUmamiti vipratipattiH /
punarAvR^ittishca dvitIyaH prashna AkAshAdikrameNemaM lokamAgacchantIti /
tenaivAsau loko na saMpUryate kITapataN^gAdipratipatteshca keShAJNciditi tR^itIyo 'pi prashno nirNItaH16 //
#<iti bR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadi ShaShThAdhyAyasya dvitIyaM brAhmaNam //2//>#

START BrhUp 6,3.1

#<sa yaH kAmayeta -- mahat prApnuyAm ity udagayana ApUryamANapakShasya puNyAhe dvAdashAham upasadvratI bhUtvaudumbare kaMse camase vA sarvauShadhaM phalAnIti saMbhR^itya parisamuhya parilipyAgnim upasamAdhAya paristIryAvR^itAjyaM saMskR^itya puMsA nakShatreNa manthaM saMnIya juhoti --
yAvanto devAs tvayi jAtavedas tiryaJNco ghnanti puruShasya kAmAn |
tebhyo 'haM bhAgadheyaM juhomi te mA tR^iptAH sarvaiH kAmais tarpayantu svAhA |
yA tirashcI nipadyase 'haM vidharaNI iti |
tAM tvA ghR^itasya dhArayA yaje saMrAdhanIm ahaM svAhA || BrhUp_6,3.1 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,3.1 sa yaH kAmayeta /
j~nAnakarmaNorgatiruktA /
tatra j~nAnaM svatantraM karma tu daivamAnuShavittadvayAyattaM tena karmArthaM vittamupArjanIyam /
taccApratyavAyakAriNopAyeneti tadarthaM manthAkhyaM karmA'rabhyate mahattvaprAptaye /
mahattve ca satyarthasiddhaM hi vittam /
taducyate-sa yaH kAmayeta sa yo vittArthI karmaNyadhikR^ito yaH kAmayeta /
kim /
mahanmahattvaM prApnuyAM mahAnsyAmitItyarthaH /
tatra manthakarmaNo vidhitsitasya kAlo 'bhidhIyate-udagayana Adityasya tatra sarvatra prAptAvApUryamANapakShasya shuklapakShasya /
tatrApi sarvatra prAptau puNyAhe 'nukUla AtmanaH karmasiddhikara ityarthaH /
dvAdashAhaM yasminpuNye 'nukUle karma cikIrShati tataH prAkpuNyAhamevA'rabhya dvAdashAhamupasadvratI /
upasatsu vratamupasadaH prasiddhA jyotiShTome /
tatra ca stanopacayApacayadvAreNa payobhakShaNaM tadvratam /
atra ca tatkarmAnupasaMhArAtkevalamitikartavyatAshUnyaM payobhakShaNamAtramupAdIyate /
nanUpasado vratamiti yadA vigrahastadA sarvamitikartavyatArUpaM grAhyaM bhavati tatkasmAnna parigR^ihyata iti /
ucyate-smArtatvAtkarmaNaH /
smArtaM hIdaM manthakarma /
nanu shrutivihitaM satkathaM smArtaM bhavitumarhati /
smR^ityanuvAdinIhi shrutiriyam /
shrautatve hi prakR^itivikArabhAvastatashca prAkR^itadharmagrAhitvaM vikArakarmaNo na tviha shrautatvam /
ata eva cA'vasathyAgnAvetatkarma vidhIyate /
sarvA cA'vR^itsmArtaiveti /
upasadvratI bhUtvA payovratI sannItyarthaH /
audumbara udumbaravR^ikShamaye kaMse camase vA tasyaiva visheShaNaM kaMsAkAre camasAkAre vaudumbara eva /
AkAre tu vikalpo naudumbaratve /
etra sarvauShadhaM sarvAsAmoShadhInAM samUhaM yathAsambhavaM yathAshakti ca sarvA oShadhIH samAhR^itya tatra grAmyANAM tu dasha niyamena grAhyA vrIhiyavAdyA vakShyamANAH /
adhikagrahaNe tu na doShaH /
grAmyANAM phalAni ca yathAsambhavaM yathAshakti ca /
itishabdaH samastasambhAropacayapradarshanArthaH /
anyadapi yatsambharaNIyaM tatsarvaM saMbhR^ityetyarthaH /
kramastatra gR^ihyokto draShTavyaH /
parisamUhanaparilepane bhUmisaMskAraH /

START BrhUp 6,4.14

#<sa ya icchet -- putro me shuklo jAyeta vedam anubruvIta sarvam Ayur iyAd iti kShIraudanaM pAcayitvA sarpiShmantam ashnIyAtAm |
Ishvarau janayitavai || BrhUp_6,4.14 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.14 sa ya icchetputro me shuklo varNato jAyeta vedamekamanubruvIta sarvamAyuriyAdvarShashataM kShIraudanaM pAcayitvA sarpiShmantamashnIyAtAmAshvarau samarthau janayitavai janayitum //14//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,4.15

#<atha ya icchet -- putro me kapilaH piN^galo jAyeta dvau vedAv anubruvIta sarvam Ayur iyAd iti dadhyodanaM pAcayitvA sarpiShmantam ashnIyAtAm |
Ishvarau janayitavai || BrhUp_6,4.15 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.15 dadhyodanaM dadhnA caruM pAcayitvA dvidevaM cedicchati putraM tadaivamashananiyamaH //15//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,4.16

#<atha ya icchet -- putro me shyAmo lohitAkSho jAyeta trIn vedAn anubruvIta sarvam Ayur iyAd iti udaudanaM pAcayitvA sarpiShmantam ashnIyAtAm |
Ishvarau janayitavai || BrhUp_6,4.16 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.16 kevalameva svAbhAvikamodanam /
udagrahaNamanyaprasaN^ganivR^ittyatham //16//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,4.17

#<atha ya icched -- duhitA me paNDitA jAyeta sarvam Ayur iyAd iti tilaudanaM pAcayitvA sarpiShmantam ashnIyAtAm |
Ishvarau janayitavai || BrhUp_6,4.17 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.17 duhituH pANDityaM gR^ihatantraviShayameva vede 'nadhikArAt /
tilaudanaM kR^itaram //17//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,4.18

#<atha ya icchet -- putro me paNDito vigItaH samitiMgamaH shushrUShitAM vAcaM bhAShitA jAyeta sarvAn vedAn anubruvIta sarvam Ayur iyAd iti mAMsaudanaM pAcayitvA sarpiShmantam ashnIyAtAm |
Ishvarau janayitavAi |
aukSheNa vArShabheNa vA || BrhUp_6,4.18 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.18 vividhaM gIto vigItaH prakhyAta ityarthaH /
samitiN^gamaH sabhAM gacchatIti pragalbha ityarthaH /
pANDityasya pR^ithaggrahaNAt /
shushrUShitAM shrotumiShTAM ramaNIyAM vAcaM bhAShitA saMskR^itAyA arthavatyA vAco bhAShitetyarthaH /
mAMsamishramodanaM mAMsaudanam /
tanmAMsaniyamArthamAha-aukSheM vA mAMsena /
ukShA secanasamarthaH puN^gavastadIyaM mAMsam /
R^iShabhastato 'pyadhikavayAstadIyamArShabhaM mAMsam //17//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,4.19

#<athAbhiprAtar eva sthAlIpAkAvR^itAjyaM ceShTitvA sthAlIpAkasyopaghAtaM juhoty agnaye svAhAnumataye svAhA devAya savitre satyaprasavAya svAheti |
hutvoddhR^itya prAshnAti |
prAshyetarasyAH prayacchati |
prakShAlya pANI udapAtraM pUrayitvA tenainAM trir abhyukShati --
uttiShThAto vishvAvaso 'nyAm iccha prapUrvyAm |
saM jAyAM patyA saheti || BrhUp_6,4.19 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.19 athAmiprAtareva kAle 'vaghAtanirvR^ittAMstaNDulAnAdAya sthAlIpAkAvR^itA sthAlIpAkavidhinA'jyaM ceShTitvA'jyasaMskAraM kR^itvA caruM shrapayitvA sthAlIpAkasyA'hutIrjuhotyupaghAtamupahatyopahatyAgnaye svAhetyAdyAH /
gArhyaH sarvo vidhirdraShTavyo 'tra hutvoddhR^itya carusheShaM prAshnAti svayaM prAshyetarasyAH patnyai prayacchatyucchiShTam /
prakShAlya pANI AcamyodapAtraM pUrayitvA tenodakenainAM trirabhyukShatyena mantreNottiShThAta iti sakR^inmantroccAraNam //19//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,4.20

#<athainAm abhipadyate -- amo 'ham asmi sA tvam |
sA tvam asy amo 'ham |
sAmAham asmi R^ik tvam |
dyaur aham pR^ithivI tvam |
tAv ehi saMrabhAvahai saha reto dadhAvahai |
puMse putrAya vittaya iti || BrhUp_6,4.20 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.20 athainAmabhimantrya kShIraudanAdi yathApatyakAmaM bhuktveti kramo draShTavyaH /
saMveshanakAle 'mo 'hamasmItyAdimantreNAbhipadyate //20//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,4.21

#<athAsyA UrU vihApayati -- vijihIthAM dyAvApR^ithivI iti |
tasyAm arthaM niShThAya mukhena mukhaM saMdhAya trir enAm anulomAm anumArShTi --
viShNur yoniM kalpayatu tvaShTA rUpANi piMshatu |
A siJNcatu prajApatir dhAtA garbhaM dadhAtu te |
garbhaM dhehi sinIvAli garbhaM dhehi pR^ithuShTuke |
garbhaM te ashvinau devAv AdhattAM puShkarasrajau || BrhUp_6,4.21 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.21 athAsyA UrU vihApayati vijihIthAM dyAvApR^ithivI ityanena /
tasyAmarthamityAdi pUrvavat /
trirenAM shiraH prabhR^ityanulomAmanumArShTi viShNuryonimityAdi pratimantram //21//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,4.22

#<hiraNmayI araNI yAbhyAM nirmanthatAm ashvinau |
taM te garbhaM havAmahe dashame mAsi sUtaye |
yathAgnigarbhA pR^ithivI yathA dyaur aindreNa garbhiNI |
vAyur dishAM yathA garbha evaM garbhaM dadhAmi te 'sAv iti || BrhUp_6,4.22 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.22 ante nAma gR^ihNAtyasAviti tasyAH //22//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,4.23

#<soShyantIm adbhir abhyukShati --
yathA vAyuH puShkariNIM samiN^gayati sarvataH |
evA te garbha ejatu sahAvaitu jarAyuNA |
indrasyAyaM vrajaH kR^itaH sArgalaH saparishrayaH |
tam indra nirjahi garbheNa sAvarAM saheti || BrhUp_6,4.23 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.23 soShyantImadbhirabhyukShati prasavakAle sukhaprasavanArthamanena mantreNa /
yathA vAyuH puShkariNIM samiN^gayati sarvataH /
evA te garbha ejatviti //23//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,4.24

#<jAte 'gnim upasamAdhAyAN^ka AdhAya kaMse pR^iShadAjyaM saMnIya pR^iShadAjyasyopaghAtaM juhoti --
asminsahasraM puShyAsam edhamAnaH sve gR^ihe |
asyopasandyAM mA chaitsIt prajayA ca pashubhish ca svAhA |
mayi prANAMs tvayi manasA juhomi svAhA |
yat karmaNAtyarIricam yad vA nyUnam ihAkaram |
agniShTat sviShTakR^id vidvAn sviShTaM suhutaM karotu naH svAheti || BrhUp_6,4.24 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.24atha jAtakarma /
jAte 'gnimupasamAdhAyAN^ka AdhAya putraM kaMse pR^iShadAjyaM saMmIya saMyojya dadhi ghR^ite pR^iShadAjyasyopaghAtaM juhotyasminsahasramityAdyAvApasthAne //24//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,4.25

#<athAsya dakShiNaM karNam abhinidhAya vAg vAg iti triH |
atha dadhi madhu ghR^itaM saMnIyAnantarhitena jAtarUpeNa prAshayati |
bhUs te dadhAmi bhuvas te dadhAmi svas te dadhAmi bhUr bhuvaH svaH sarvaM tvayi dadhAmIti || BrhUp_6,4.25 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.25 athAsya dakShiNaM karNamabhinidhAya svaM mukhaM vAgvAgiti trirjapet /
atha dadhi madhu ghR^itaM saMnIyAnantarhitenAvyavahitena jAtarUpeNa hiraNyena prAshayatyetairmantraiH pratyekam //25//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,4.26

#<athAsya nAma karoti vedo 'sIti |
tad asyaitad guhyam eva nAma bhavati || BrhUp_6,4.26 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.26 athAsya nAmadheyaM karoti vedo 'sIti /
tadasya tadguhyaM nAma bhavati veda iti //26//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,4.27

#<athainaM mAtre pradAya stanaM prayacchati -- yas te stanaH shashayo yo mayobhUr yo ratnadhA vasuvid yaH sudatraH |
yena vishvA puShyasi vAryANi sarasvati tam iha dhAtave kar iti || BrhUp_6,4.27 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.27 athainaM mAtre pradAya svAN^kasthaM stanaM prayacchati yaste stana ityAdimantreNa //27//



_______________________________________________________________________

START BrhUp 6,4.28

#<athAsya mAtaram abhimantrayate -- ilAsi maitrAvaruNI vIre vIram ajIjanat |
sA tvaM vIravatI bhava yAsmAn vIravato 'karad iti |
taM vA etam AhuH -- atipitA batAbhUH |
atipitAmaho batAbhUH |
paramAM bata kAShThAM prApa shriyA yashasA brahmavarcasena |
ya evaMvido brAhmaNasya putro jAyata iti || BrhUp_6,4.28 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,4.28 athAsya mAtaramabhimantrayata ilAsItyanena /
taM vA etamAhurityanena vidhinA jAtaH putraH pitaraM pitAmahaM cAtisheta iti shriyA yashasA brahmavarcasena paramAM niShThAM prApadityevaM stutyo bhavatItyarthaH /
yasya caivaMvido brAhmaNasya putro jAyate sa caivaM bhavatItyadhyAhAryam //28//

#<iti bR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadi ShaShThAdhyAyasya caturthaM brAhmaNam //4//>#

START BrhUp 6,5.1-4

#<atha vaMshaH |
pautimAShIputraH kAtyAyanIputrAt |
kAtyAyanIputro gautamIputrAt |
gautamIputro bhAradvAjIputrAt |
bhAradvAjIputraH pArAsharIputrAt |
pArAsharIputra aupasvastIputrAt |
aupasvastIputraH pArAsharIputrAt |
pArAsharIputraH kAtyAyanIputrAt |
kAtyAyanIputraH kaushikIputrAt |
kaushikIputra AlambIputrAc ca vaiyAghrapadIputrAc ca |
vaiyAghrapadIputrah kANvIputrAc ca kApIputrAc ca |
kApIputraH || BrhUp_6,5.1 ||>#



#<AtreyIputrAt |
AtreyIputro gautamIputrAt |
gautamIputro bhAradvAjIputrAt |
bhAradvAjIputraH pArAsharIputrAt |
pArAsharIputro vAtsIputrAt |
vAtsIputraH pArAsharIputrAt |
pArAsharIputro vArkArunIputrAt |
vArkAruNIputro vArkAruNIputrAt |
vArkAruNIputra ArtabhAgIputrAt |
ArtabhAgIputraH shauN^gIputrAt |
shauN^gIputraH sAnkR^itIputrAt |
sAÇR^itIputra AlambAyanIputrAt |
AlambAyanIputra AlambIputrAt |
AlambIputro jAyantIputrAt |
jAyantIputro mANDUkAyanIputrAt |
mANDUkAyanIputro mANDUkIputrAt |
mANDUkIputraH shANDilIputrAt |
shANDilIputro rAthItarIputrAt |
rAthItarIputro bhAlukIputrAt |
bhAlukIputraH krauJNcikIputrAbhyAm |
krauJNcikIputrau vaidabhR^itIputrAt |
vaidabhR^itIputraH kArshakeyIputrAt |
kArshakeyIputraH prAcInayogIputrAt |
prAcInayogIputraH sAJNjIvIputrAt |
sAJNjIvIputraH prAshnIputrAd AsurivAsinaH |
prAshnIputra AsurAyaNAt |
AsurAyaNa AsureH |
AsuriH| BrhUp_6,5.2 ||>#



#<yAj~navalkyAt |
yAj~navalkya uddAlakAt |
uddAlako 'ruNAt |
aruNa upavesheH |
upaveshiH kushreH |
kushrir vAjashravasaH |
vAjashravA jIhvAvato bAdhyogAt |
jIhvAvAn bAdhyogo 'sitAd vArShagaNAt |
asito vArShagaNo haritAt kashyapAt |
haritaH kashyapaH shilpAt kashyapAt |
shilpaH kashyapaH kashyapAn naidhruveH |
kashyapo naidhruvir vAcaH |
vAg ambhiNyAH |
ambhiNy AdityAt |
AdityAnImAni shuklAni yajUMShi vAjasaneyena yAj~navalkyenAkhyayante || BrhUp_6,5.3 ||>#



#<samAnam A sAJNjIvIputrAt |
saJNjivIputro mANDUkAyaneH |
mANDUkAyanir mANDavyAt |
mANDavyaH kautsAt |
kautso mAhittheH |
mAhitthir vAmakakShAyaNAt |
vAmakakShAyaNaH shANDilyAt |
shANDilyo vAtsyAt |
vAtsyaH kushreH |
kushrir yaj~navacasaH rAjastambAyanAt |
yaj~navacA rAjastambAyanaH turAt kAvaSheyAt |
turaH kAvaSheyaH prajApateH |
prajApatir brahmaNaH |
brahma svayaMbhu |
brahmaNe namaH || BrhUp_6,5.4 ||>#


__________


BrhUpBh_6,5.1-4 athedAnIM samastapravacanavaMshaH /
srIprAdhAnyAt guNavAnputro bhavatIti prastutam /
ataH srIvisheShaNenaiva putravisheShaNAdAcAryaparamparA kIrtyate /
tAnImAni shuklAnItyavyAmishrANi brAhmaNena /
athavA yAnImAni yajUMShi tAnI shuklAni shuddhAnItyetat /
prajApatimArabhya yAvatpautimAShIputrastAvadadhomukho niyatAcAryapUrvakramo vaMshaH samAnamAsAMjIvIputrAt /
brahmaNaH pravacanAkhyasya /
taccaitadbrahma prajApatiprabandhaparamparayA'gatyAsmAsvanekadhAviprasR^itamanAdyanantaM svayaMbhu brahma nityaM tasmai brahmaNe namaH /
namastadanuvartibhyo gurubhyaH //1-4 //


iti bR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadi ShaShThAdhyAyasya paJNcamaM brAhmaNam //5//

iti vAjasaneyake bR^ihadAraNyakopaniShadi ShaShThodhyAyaH //6//

iti vAjasaneyakebR^ihadAraNyakakrameNAShTamo 'dhyAyaH //8//

iti shuklayajurvedIyA bR^ihadAraNyakopaniShat saMpUrNA 

oM pUrNamadaH pUrNamidaM pUrNAtpUrNamudacyate /
pUrNasya pUrNamAdAya pUrNamevAvashiShyate //

oM shAntiH shAntiH shAntiH
